### [1] [Collective response and noise of a levitated ferromagnet lattice for ultralight dark matter detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17417)
*Dongyi Yang,Xiao Yang,Chenxi Sun,Jianwei Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper proposes a levitated ferromagnet lattice as a scalable detector for ultralight dark matter, showing enhanced sensitivity across axion-electron, dark-photon, and axion-photon couplings due to collective effects and coherent signal amplification in the axion-photon channel.\n\n本文提出了一种悬浮铁磁体晶格作为超轻暗物质的可扩展探测器，由于集体效应以及在轴子-光子通道中的相干信号放大，该方案在轴子-电子、暗光子和轴子-光子耦合方面均展现出增强的灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Single levitated ferromagnets used in precision magnetometry for ultralight dark matter searches suffer from limited total polarized spin and suboptimal readout performance. The authors aim to overcome these limitations by exploring a scalable array—specifically, a levitated ferromagnet lattice—that leverages collective spin responses while managing noise and interaction effects.\n\n用于超轻暗物质搜索的精密磁力测量中，单个悬浮铁磁体受限于总极化自旋量不足和读出性能不佳。作者旨在通过探索一种可扩展阵列——即悬浮铁磁体晶格——来克服这些限制，该阵列利用集体自旋响应，同时有效管理噪声与相互作用效应。

Method: The authors develop a theoretical model of the collective response of a fully trapped ferromagnet lattice, incorporating dipole-dipole interactions, finite-size effects, and boundary-induced mode mixing. They analyze the collective noise budget, identifying thermal-noise amplification as the dominant interaction effect that creates a narrow blind zone. Sensitivity projections for axion-electron ($g_{ae}$), dark-photon ($\\epsilon$), and axion-photon ($g_{a\\gamma}$) couplings are derived by evaluating signal-to-noise ratios in this lattice configuration.\n\n作者构建了一个完全囚禁状态下铁磁体晶格集体响应的理论模型，纳入了偶极-偶极相互作用、有限尺寸效应和边界诱导的模式混合。他们分析了集体噪声预算，指出热噪声放大是主要的相互作用效应，会产生一个狭窄的盲区。通过评估该晶格构型中的信噪比，推导了对轴子-电子耦合（$g_{ae}$）、暗光子耦合（$\\epsilon$）和轴子-光子耦合（$g_{a\\gamma}$）的灵敏度预期。

Result: The lattice detector improves sensitivity over a single-ferromagnet setup in all three coupling channels. In the axion-photon channel, an additional coherent enhancement arises from the electromagnetic background generated by the lattice itself. Interaction effects induce only a narrow blind zone due to thermal-noise amplification, while elsewhere the system retains favorable $1/\\sqrt{N}$ collective noise scaling (with $N$ the number of ferromagnets).\n\n晶格探测器在所有三种耦合通道中均优于单铁磁体方案。在轴子-光子通道中，晶格自身产生的电磁背景带来了额外的相干增强。相互作用效应仅因热噪声放大而引入一个狭窄的盲区，而在其他区域系统仍保持有利的集体噪声标度 $1/\\sqrt{N}$（其中 $N$ 为铁磁体数量）。

Conclusion: A levitated ferromagnet lattice is a promising scalable architecture for ultralight dark matter detection, offering improved sensitivity across multiple interaction channels and demonstrating that collective effects can be harnessed without significant noise penalty outside a narrow frequency band.\n\n悬浮铁磁体晶格是一种有前景的可扩展架构，可用于超轻暗物质探测，在多个相互作用通道中提供更高的灵敏度，并表明除狭窄频带外，集体效应可在不显著增加噪声代价的情况下被有效利用。

Abstract: Ultralight dark matter can induce weak oscillating magnetic-like signals and can therefore be searched for with precision magnetometry. Levitated ferromagnets provide a sensitive platform for such searches, but a single ferromagnet is limited in total polarized spin and readout performance. We investigate a levitated ferromagnet lattice as a scalable detector for ultralight dark matter. We develop a theoretical description of the collective lattice response in the fully trapped regime, incorporating dipole-dipole interactions, finite-size effects, and boundary-induced mode mixing. We further analyze the collective noise budget and show that interaction effects mainly produce a narrow blind zone through thermal-noise amplification, while away from this region, the lattice preserves favorable collective noise scaling. We then derive projected sensitivities to axion-electron, dark-photon, and axion-photon couplings. We find that the lattice improves the reach in all three channels relative to a single-ferromagnet detector, with an additional coherent signal enhancement in the axion-photon channel from the lattice-generated electromagnetic background.

</details>


### [2] [Higher excited charmed and charmed-strange mesons in an unquenched quark model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17832)
*Ru-Hui Ni,Jia-Jun Wu,Xian-Hui Zhong*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper extends a prior study by analyzing the mass spectra and OZI-allowed strong decays of higher orbital and radial excitations ($3S$, $2P$, $2D$, $1F$) of charmed and charmed-strange mesons using a unified unquenched quark model. Coupled-channel effects significantly lower most predicted masses. The LHCb state $D_{s1}(2933)^+$ is interpreted as the low-mass mixed axial-vector $D_s(2P_1)$, while the BABAR structure $D_{sJ}(3040)^+$ likely corresponds to $D_s(3^1S_0)$. The LHCb $D(3000)^0$ does not match any considered assignment. Predictions are provided for missing states to guide future experiments.
\n\n
本文作为前期工作的延续，采用统一的非淬火夸克模型系统研究了粲介子和粲奇异介子高激发态（$3S$、$2P$、$2D$、$1F$）的质量谱和OZI允许的强衰变。耦合道效应显著降低了大部分激发态的质量。LHCb合作组新观测到的 $D_{s1}(2933)^+$ 可被解释为低质量轴矢量混合态 $D_s(2P_1)$；而早先由BABAR合作组观测到的宽结构 $D_{sJ}(3040)^+$ 更可能对应于 $D_s(3^1S_0)$ 态而非高质量混合态 $D_s(2P_1^\prime)$。LHCb观测到的 $D(3000)^0$ 信号无法用任何 $3S$、$2P$、$2D$ 或 $1F$ 态解释。文中对尚未观测到的高激发 $D$ 和 $D_s$ 介子的质量与衰变性质进行了预测，可为未来实验提供参考。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from recent experimental discoveries of new charmed and charmed-strange meson resonances (e.g., $D_{s1}(2933)^+$ by LHCb and $D_{sJ}(3040)^+$ by BABAR) whose quantum numbers and internal structures remain ambiguous. A systematic theoretical framework accounting for coupled-channel (unquenched) effects is needed to clarify their nature and to predict properties of yet-unobserved higher excitations in the $D$ and $D_s$ families.
\n\n
动机源于近期实验上发现的新粲及粲奇异介子共振态（如LHCb发现的 $D_{s1}(2933)^+$ 和BABAR发现的 $D_{sJ}(3040)^+$），其量子数和内部结构尚不明确。亟需一个能系统计入耦合道（非淬火）效应的理论框架，以厘清这些态的本质，并预测 $D$ 与 $D_s$ 家族中尚未观测到的高激发态的性质。

Method: The authors employ a unified unquenched quark model that incorporates coupled-channel effects via a $^3P_0$ decay kernel. This approach modifies the bare quark-model spectrum by including meson-meson continuum contributions through self-energy corrections. They compute masses and OZI-allowed strong decay widths for $3S$-, $2P$-, $2D$-, and $1F$-wave $D$ and $D_s$ mesons, taking into account $2^1P_1$-$2^3P_1$ mixing for axial-vector states. The model parameters are fixed from previous studies to ensure consistency.
\n\n
作者采用统一的非淬火夸克模型，通过 $^3P_0$ 衰变核引入耦合道效应。该方法通过自能修正将介子-介子连续谱贡献纳入，从而修正裸夸克模型谱。他们计算了 $3S$、$2P$、$2D$ 和 $1F$ 波 $D$ 与 $D_s$ 介子的质量及OZI允许的强衰变宽度，并考虑轴矢量态中的 $2^1P_1$-$2^3P_1$ 混合。模型参数沿用前期工作以保证一致性。

Result: Coupled-channel effects cause substantial downward mass shifts for most higher charmed meson excitations. The $D_{s1}(2933)^+$ is identified as the low-mass mixed $D_s(2P_1)$ state. The broad $D_{sJ}(3040)^+$ is better described as $D_s(3^1S_0)$ than as the high-mass mixed $D_s(2P_1^\prime)$. The $D(3000)^0$ cannot be accommodated within the considered $3S$, $2P$, $2D$, or $1F$ assignments. Predictions are made for masses and decay widths of several missing higher $D$ and $D_s$ states.
\n\n
耦合道效应对大多数高激发粲介子引起显著的质量下移。$D_{s1}(2933)^+$ 被认定为低质量混合态 $D_s(2P_1)$；宽结构 $D_{sJ}(3040)^+$ 更倾向于被解释为 $D_s(3^1S_0)$ 而非高质量混合态 $D_s(2P_1^\prime)$；$D(3000)^0$ 无法用所考虑的 $3S$、$2P$、$2D$ 或 $1F$ 态描述。文中还对多个尚未观测到的高激发 $D$ 和 $D_s$ 介子的质量与衰变宽度作出了预测。

Conclusion: The unquenched quark model successfully accounts for the observed spectrum of higher charmed mesons by incorporating coupled-channel dynamics, resolving ambiguities in the interpretation of recent experimental signals. It provides robust predictions for undiscovered states, emphasizing the critical role of continuum coupling in heavy-light meson spectroscopy.
\n\n
非淬火夸克模型通过引入耦合道动力学，成功解释了高激发粲介子的观测谱，澄清了近期实验信号的物理解释。该模型对未发现态提供了可靠预测，凸显了连续谱耦合在重轻介子谱学中的关键作用。

Abstract: In this paper, as a continuation of our previous work, we systematically study the mass spectra and OZI-allowed strong decays of the higher $3S$-, $2P$-, $2D$-, and $1F$-wave charmed and charmed-strange mesons within a unified unquenched quark model. It is found that for most of the higher excitations, the masses are significantly shifted down by the coupled-channel effects. The newly observed $D_{s1}(2933)^+$ reported by the LHCb collaboration could be identified as the low-mass axial-vector state $D_s(2P_1)$ via the $2^1P_1-2^3P_1$ mixing. For the broad structure $D_{sJ}(3040)^+$ observed earlier by the \emph{BABAR} collaboration, the $D_s(3^1S_0)$ assignment seems to be favored over the high-mass mixed state $D_s(2P_1^\prime)$. Meanwhile, the $D(3000)^0$ signals observed at LHCb cannot be well understood with any $3S$, $2P$, $2D$, or $1F$ assignments in the $D$-meson family. Our predicted masses and decay properties of the missing higher $D$ and $D_s$ mesons may provide useful information for future experimental searches.

</details>


### [3] [MAGE-HEP: Monte Carlo Analysis and Graphical Environment for High-Energy Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17871)
*Rishabh Gupta,Kangkan Goswami,Suraj Prasad,Raghunath Sahoo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: MAGE-HEP is a GUI-driven workflow environment for reproducible Monte Carlo analyses in high-energy physics, introducing a project-study-run hierarchy and supporting exportable context bundles (.mcx) and project bundles (.mgp). Its beta version integrates PYTHIA8 and ROOT with features like background execution, manifest-based tracking, and live ROOT inspection.
\n\n
MAGE-HEP 是一个用于高能物理中可复现 Monte Carlo 分析的图形用户界面（GUI）驱动工作流环境，引入了 project-study-run 层级结构，并支持可导出的上下文包（.mcx）和项目包（.mgp）。其测试版集成了 PYTHIA8 和 ROOT，具备后台执行、基于清单（manifest-based）的运行追踪和实时 ROOT 检查等功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional Monte Carlo workflows in high-energy physics rely on handwritten scripts, which become unwieldy when managing multiple generator models, tune variations, run configurations, and output formats—hindering reusability, modifiability, and reproducibility. MAGE-HEP addresses these challenges by providing a structured, GUI-based environment to standardize and streamline analysis workflows.
\n\n
高能物理中的传统 Monte Carlo 工作流依赖手写脚本，在管理多个生成器模型、tune 变体、运行配置和输出格式时变得难以维护，阻碍了可重用性、可修改性和可复现性。MAGE-HEP 通过提供一个结构化的图形用户界面（GUI）环境来标准化并简化分析工作流，以应对这些挑战。

Method: MAGE-HEP implements a hierarchical organization (project–study–run) where: projects store the workspace state; studies encapsulate reusable analysis contexts (including generator configurations, observables, selections, and output rules); and runs represent individual executions. The system provides a Node API to define analysis components and auto-generates C++/ROOT code. Contexts can be exported as .mcx bundles and full projects as .mgp bundles. The beta version uses PYTHIA8 for event generation and ROOT for analysis, with support for background execution, manifest-based run tracking, live ROOT histogram/tree inspection, and particle-table summaries.
\n\n
MAGE-HEP 实现了一种层级化组织结构（project–study–run）：project 存储工作区状态；study 封装可重用的分析上下文（包括生成器配置、观测量、选择条件和输出规则）；run 表示单次执行。系统提供 Node API 用于定义分析组件并自动生成 C++/ROOT 代码。上下文可导出为 .mcx 包，完整项目可导出为 .mgp 包。测试版使用 PYTHIA8 进行事例生成，ROOT 进行分析，支持后台执行、基于清单（manifest-based）的运行追踪、实时 ROOT 直方图/树检查以及粒子表摘要。

Result: The beta implementation successfully demonstrates the core architecture of MAGE-HEP using a PYTHIA8–ROOT workflow. It enables users to build, inspect, execute, and export reproducible Monte Carlo analyses through a GUI, with features including background job execution, persistent run manifests, live visualization of ROOT outputs, and standardized particle summaries—all while maintaining portability via .mcx and .mgp bundles.
\n\n
测试版成功通过 PYTHIA8–ROOT 工作流验证了 MAGE-HEP 的核心架构。它使用户能够通过图形界面构建、检查、执行和导出可复现的 Monte Carlo 分析，具备后台任务执行、持久化运行清单、ROOT 输出的实时可视化以及标准化粒子摘要等功能，并通过 .mcx 和 .mgp 包保持可移植性。

Conclusion: MAGE-HEP offers a novel, GUI-based framework that enhances reproducibility, modularity, and usability in Monte Carlo analyses for high-energy physics. By abstracting complex workflow management into an intuitive project–study–run model and enabling portable context sharing, it lays the groundwork for more collaborative and sustainable analysis practices. Future work will extend support to additional generators and analysis frameworks.
\n\n
MAGE-HEP 提供了一个新颖的基于 GUI 的框架，提升了高能物理中 Monte Carlo 分析的可复现性、模块化和易用性。通过将复杂的工作流管理抽象为直观的 project–study–run 模型并支持可移植的上下文共享，它为更协作和可持续的分析实践奠定了基础。未来工作将扩展对更多生成器和分析框架的支持。

Abstract: Monte Carlo event generators are central to high-energy physics analysis. However, workflows based on handwritten scripts can be difficult to reuse, modify, and reproduce when multiple Monte Carlo models, tune variations, run variations, and output formats are involved. We present MAGE-HEP, short for Monte Carlo Analysis and Graphical Environment for High-Energy Physics, a Graphical User Interface (GUI) driven workflow environment for reproducible Monte Carlo-based analyses in high-energy physics. MAGE-HEP organizes analysis workflows through a project-study-run hierarchy. The project stores the workspace, the study stores the reusable analysis context, and each run represents a controlled execution of that context.
  The MAGE-HEP Node API provides the analysis-building layer for defining generator configurations, observables, selections, output rules, and generated C++/ROOT analysis code. A study context can be inspected, reused, or exported as a \texttt{.mcx} context bundle, while the project state can be exported as a portable \texttt{.mgp} bundle. The current beta implementation validates the core idea using a PYTHIA8 and ROOT workflow. It includes background execution, manifest-based run tracking, live ROOT inspection, and particle-table summaries for supported output layouts. This paper describes the architecture, workflow, and current beta implementation of MAGE-HEP.

</details>


### [4] [Branching ratios and CP violations of $B \toρ(ω) γ$ decays in the modified perturbative QCD approach and the relevant dark photonic decays of $B\to ρ(ω) γ^\prime $](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17943)
*Shang Qi,Mao-Zhi Yang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates the radiative decays $B \to \rho(\omega)\gamma$ using a modified perturbative QCD (pQCD) approach that retains transverse momenta and includes Sudakov suppression to control infrared endpoint divergences. A critical infrared cutoff separates soft and hard contributions, leading to decomposed form factors—hard (calculable in pQCD) and soft (extracted from data). The total form factors agree with nonperturbative methods like light-cone sum rules. These form factors are then applied to constrain $B \to \rho(\omega)\gamma'$ decays involving a dark photon $\gamma'$ from a $U(1)$ extension, yielding upper limits on branching ratios.
\n\n
本文采用改进的微扰QCD（pQCD）方法研究辐射衰变过程 $B \to \rho(\omega)\gamma$，其中保留了夸克和胶子的横向动量，并引入Sudakov因子以压低红外端点发散。通过引入一个关键的红外动量截断尺度，将QCD贡献分为软硬两部分，相应的形状因子也被分解为可微扰计算的硬部分和需从实验数据拟合的软部分。总形状因子与光锥求和规则等非微扰方法结果一致。作者进一步利用这些形状因子研究 $B \to \rho(\omega)\gamma'$ 衰变（其中 $\gamma'$ 是由额外 $U(1)$ 对称性模型引入的暗光子），并给出了分支比的上限估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The standard perturbative QCD treatment of exclusive $B$-meson radiative decays suffers from large uncertainties due to infrared (IR) endpoint singularities. To address this, the authors adopt a modified pQCD framework that incorporates transverse momentum dependence and Sudakov resummation, which tames these divergences. Furthermore, they aim to connect theoretical predictions with experimental data by separating nonperturbative soft dynamics from perturbative hard dynamics, and subsequently apply this framework to probe physics beyond the Standard Model—specifically, dark photon scenarios via $B \to \rho(\omega)\gamma'$ decays.
\n\n
标准微扰QCD在处理 $B$ 介子辐射衰变时面临严重的红外（IR）端点奇异性问题，导致理论不确定性较大。为此，作者采用一种改进的pQCD框架，引入横向动量依赖和Sudakov重求和以抑制这些发散。此外，他们希望将非微扰的软动力学与微扰的硬动力学分离，通过与实验数据对照提取软贡献，并将此框架应用于超出标准模型的新物理探索——特别是通过 $B \to \rho(\omega)\gamma'$ 衰变来研究暗光子（dark photon）情景。

Method: The authors employ a modified perturbative QCD approach where partonic transverse momenta $k_T$ are retained and Sudakov factors $e^{-S}$ are included to suppress the IR-sensitive endpoint region. They introduce an infrared cutoff scale $k_{\text{cut}}$ to separate the amplitude into hard ($k_T > k_{\text{cut}}$) and soft ($k_T < k_{\text{cut}}$) components. The hard form factors are computed perturbatively at leading order, while the soft form factors are treated as nonperturbative parameters fitted to experimental branching ratios of $B \to \rho(\omega)\gamma$. The total form factor is $F = F_{\text{hard}} + F_{\text{soft}}$. This combined form factor is validated against light-cone sum rules. The same form factors are then used to compute $B \to \rho(\omega)\gamma'$ decay rates, where $\gamma'$ couples via kinetic mixing with the standard photon, and constraints on its branching ratios are derived.
\n\n
作者采用改进的微扰QCD方法，保留部分子横向动量 $k_T$ 并引入Sudakov因子 $e^{-S}$ 以压低对红外敏感的端点区域。他们引入一个红外截断尺度 $k_{\text{cut}}$，将振幅分为硬部分（$k_T > k_{\text{cut}}$）和软部分（$k_T < k_{\text{cut}}$）。硬形状因子在领头阶微扰计算，而软形状因子作为非微扰参数，通过拟合 $B \to \rho(\omega)\gamma$ 的实验分支比确定。总形状因子为 $F = F_{\text{hard}} + F_{\text{soft}}$，并与光锥求和规则结果进行比对验证。随后，利用该形状因子计算 $B \to \rho(\omega)\gamma'$ 衰变率，其中 $\gamma'$ 通过与标准光子的动力学混合耦合，并由此推导其分支比的上限。

Result: The total form factors obtained by summing hard and soft contributions show good agreement with those from nonperturbative methods such as QCD light-cone sum rules. Using these calibrated form factors, the authors compute the branching ratios for $B \to \rho(\omega)\gamma'$ decays mediated by a dark photon $\gamma'$ arising from a $U(1)$ gauge extension. They derive upper limits on these branching ratios, which depend on the dark photon mass and kinetic mixing parameter $\epsilon$, providing constraints on the parameter space of the dark photon model.
\n\n
将硬软形状因子相加得到的总形状因子与QCD光锥求和规则等非微扰方法的结果高度一致。利用这些标定后的形状因子，作者计算了由额外 $U(1)$ 规范对称性引入的暗光子 $\gamma'$ 所介导的 $B \to \rho(\omega)\gamma'$ 衰变分支比，并给出了其上限。该上限依赖于暗光子质量及其与标准光子的动力学混合参数 $\epsilon$，从而对暗光子模型的参数空间施加了限制。

Conclusion: The modified pQCD framework successfully reconciles perturbative calculations with nonperturbative inputs by separating soft and hard dynamics via an IR cutoff, yielding reliable form factors for $B \to \rho(\omega)\gamma$ decays. This approach not only validates the theoretical consistency with light-cone sum rules but also provides a robust tool to explore new physics, particularly setting meaningful bounds on dark photon couplings through rare $B$-meson decays.
\n\n
改进的pQCD框架通过引入红外截断将软硬动力学分离，成功结合了微扰计算与非微扰输入，为 $B \to \rho(\omega)\gamma$ 衰变提供了可靠的形状因子。该方法不仅在理论上与光锥求和规则一致，还为探索新物理提供了有力工具，特别是通过对稀有 $B$ 介子衰变过程设定了对暗光子耦合的有意义限制。

Abstract: In this work we study the radiative decays of $B\to ρ(ω)γ$ processes in the modified perturbative QCD approach, where the transverse momenta of the quark and gluons envolved in the interaction process are kept, and the Sudakov factor is incorporated in the theoretical calculation, which are helpful to suppress the infrared end-point contribution. A critical infrared momentum cutoff scale is introduced, which is used to separate the soft and hard contributions in QCD. Then the form factors envolved in the radiative decays should be separated as hard and soft form factors. The hard form factors can be calculated with the perturbative QCD approach, while the soft form factors should be viewed as soft input parameters. The soft form factors can be obtained by confronting the theoretical calculation of the branching ratios of the radiative decay of $B$ meson with the experimental data. Summing the soft and hard form factors, we find that the total form factors are in fine agreement with that obtained by nonperturbative theoretical method, such as the light-cone sum rules of QCD. We also study $B\to ρ(ω) γ^\prime$ decays by using the form factors obtained in the $B\to ρ(ω)γ$ decay processes, where $γ^\prime$ is the dark photon introduced by the extra $U(1)$ symmetry model. The upper limit of the branching ratios of thes decays are estimated.

</details>


### [5] [Freeze-in Warm Dark Matter via Dimension-6 Operators in 3-3-1 Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16465)
*Fuwei Liu,Fujun Liu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper resolves the fine-tuning issue in freeze-in dark matter by embedding a sterile singlet into a 3-3-1 electroweak extension with an exact $Z_{13}$ gauge symmetry, which restricts SM–dark sector interactions to a dimension-six operator. The required tiny coupling arises naturally from the hierarchy between the electroweak scale and the Peccei-Quinn scale, yielding a keV-scale warm dark matter candidate consistent with Lyman-alpha bounds and small-scale structure observations.
\n\n
本文通过将惰性单态嵌入具有精确 $Z_{13}$ 规范对称性的 3-3-1 电弱扩展模型，解决了 freeze-in 暗物质机制中的精细调节问题。该对称性将标准模型（SM）与暗区之间的相互作用严格限制为六维算符，所需极小耦合自然源于电弱能标与Peccei-Quinn对称性破缺能标之间的巨大层级。由此产生的 keV 能标温暗物质候选者满足 Lyman-alpha 森林约束，并可缓解星系尺度上的 cusp-core 与 missing satellites 等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The freeze-in mechanism for dark matter typically requires unnaturally small couplings, leading to a fine-tuning problem. Additionally, reconciling dark matter production with solutions to the strong CP problem—such as the Peccei-Quinn mechanism—often involves ad hoc assumptions. This work aims to construct a theoretically robust framework where both the relic abundance and the strong CP solution emerge naturally without fine-tuning.
\n\n
freeze-in 暗物质机制通常需要非自然的小耦合，导致精细调节问题。此外，将暗物质产生与强CP问题的解决方案（如 Peccei-Quinn 机制）相协调往往依赖于人为假设。本文旨在构建一个理论自洽的框架，使暗物质遗迹丰度与强CP问题的解决均能自然出现，无需精细调节。

Method: The authors embed a sterile singlet dark matter candidate within a 3-3-1 electroweak gauge extension of the Standard Model and impose an exact discrete $Z_{13}$ gauge symmetry. This symmetry forbids all renormalizable and dimension-five portals, allowing only a dimension-six operator to mediate interactions between the dark sector and the SM. The small coupling governing freeze-in production is then tied to the ratio of the electroweak scale $v \\sim 246$ GeV and the ultra-high Peccei-Quinn symmetry breaking scale $f_a \\gg v$, yielding $g \\sim v^2 / f_a^2$. The Boltzmann equations are numerically solved to compute the relic density via infrared freeze-in.
\n\n
作者将惰性单态暗物质候选者嵌入标准模型的 3-3-1 电弱规范扩展中，并施加一个精确的离散 $Z_{13}$ 规范对称性。该对称性禁止所有可重整及五维算符门户，仅允许六维算符作为暗区与标准模型之间的相互作用媒介。主导 freeze-in 产生的微小耦合由电弱能标 $v \\sim 246$ GeV 与极高 Peccei-Quinn 对称性破缺能标 $f_a \\gg v$ 的比值决定，即 $g \\sim v^2 / f_a^2$。通过数值求解玻尔兹曼方程，计算红外 freeze-in 机制下的遗迹密度。

Result: The model successfully produces the observed dark matter relic abundance $\\Omega_S h^2 = 0.12$ through infrared freeze-in. The resulting dark matter mass lies in the keV range, classifying it as warm dark matter. It satisfies current Lyman-alpha forest constraints and alleviates small-scale structure issues like the cusp-core and missing satellites problems. Crucially, the axion associated with the Peccei-Quinn symmetry simultaneously solves the strong CP problem, with no need for parameter tuning.
\n\n
该模型通过红外 freeze-in 成功产生观测到的暗物质遗迹丰度 $\\Omega_S h^2 = 0.12$。所得暗物质质量处于 keV 量级，属于温暗物质。它满足当前 Lyman-alpha 森林约束，并可缓解 cusp-core 和 missing satellites 等小尺度结构问题。关键在于，与 Peccei-Quinn 对称性相关的轴子同时解决了强CP问题，且无需任何参数调节。

Conclusion: This work presents a unified, natural framework that simultaneously addresses dark matter genesis via freeze-in and the strong CP problem via the Peccei-Quinn mechanism, embedded in a 3-3-1 gauge extension with a $Z_{13}$ symmetry. The required tiny coupling emerges from a physical scale hierarchy rather than fine-tuning, and the resulting keV-scale warm dark matter is phenomenologically viable.
\n\n
本文提出了一个统一且自然的理论框架，将 freeze-in 暗物质产生机制与 Peccei-Quinn 强CP问题解决方案相结合，嵌入于具有 $Z_{13}$ 对称性的 3-3-1 规范扩展中。所需极小耦合源于物理能标层级而非人为调节，所产生的 keV 能标温暗物质在现象学上是可行的。

Abstract: We propose a natural resolution to the fine-tuning problem inherent in the freeze-in dark matter paradigm by embedding a sterile singlet within a 3-3-1 electroweak extension. By imposing an exact $Z_{13}$ discrete gauge symmetry, we formally suppress all low-dimensional portals to ensure that the dark sector communicates with the Standard Model (SM) exclusively through a dimension-six operator. This theoretical structure allows the extraordinarily small coupling required for dark matter production to emerge naturally from the profound hierarchy between the electroweak scale and the ultra-high Peccei-Quinn symmetry breaking scale. Detailed numerical integration of the Boltzmann equations demonstrates that the sterile singlet can be produced via the infrared freeze-in mechanism to match the observed relic abundance of $Ω_S h^2 = 0.12$. The resulting keV-scale warm dark matter candidate remains consistent with stringent Lyman-alpha forest constraints while offering a viable solution to galactic-scale discrepancies such as the cusp-core and missing satellites problems. Ultimately, this framework provides a self-consistent unification of dark matter genesis and the strong CP solution that is completely independent of ad hoc parameter adjustments.

</details>


### [6] [Helicity effects in the dynamically assisted Schwinger mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18027)
*A. I. Baksheev,V. A. Bokhan,A. Kudlis,I. A. Aleksandrov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates helicity-resolved electron-positron pair production via the dynamically assisted Schwinger effect in a bichromatic, circularly polarized electric field using the quantum-kinetic formalism for fermions. It demonstrates that dynamical assistance enhances both total particle yield and helicity asymmetry, with opposite helicities preferentially emitted into opposite momentum half-spaces. The helicity ratio depends primarily on the polar angle relative to the field axis and weakly on momentum magnitude and azimuthal angle, becoming more pronounced at higher frequencies of the weak field component.
\n\n
本文在量子动力学（quantum-kinetic）框架下研究了双色圆偏振电场中真空电子-正电子对产生过程的螺旋度分辨可观测量，重点关注动态辅助Schwinger效应。研究表明，动态辅助不仅增强了总产额，还显著增强了螺旋度不对称性：右旋和左旋电子优先占据相反的动量半空间。在所考虑的参数范围内，相反螺旋度的动量分布之比主要由相对于传播轴的极角决定，而对动量大小和方位角的依赖较弱；随着弱场分量频率的提高，这种不对称性更加明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how structured strong-field backgrounds—specifically bichromatic circularly polarized fields mimicking counterpropagating laser pulses—affect nonperturbative QED processes like vacuum pair production, with particular emphasis on helicity-resolved observables. While the total yield in the dynamically assisted Schwinger effect is known to be enhanced, the behavior of spin/helicity degrees of freedom in such time-dependent, rotating fields remains poorly explored. This work aims to uncover whether helicity carries a distinct signature of dynamical assistance.
\n\n
动机在于理解结构化的强场背景（特别是模拟对向传播激光脉冲的双色圆偏振场）如何影响非微扰QED过程（如真空对产生），尤其关注螺旋度分辨的可观测量。尽管动态辅助Schwinger效应中的总产额增强已被认知，但在这种含时且旋转的场中，自旋/螺旋度自由度的行为仍鲜有研究。本文旨在揭示螺旋度是否携带动态辅助的独特信号。

Method: The authors employ the quantum-kinetic framework for fermions, which describes pair production via a transport equation for the phase-space distribution function $f_{\\mathbf{p},s}(t)$. The external field is modeled as a spatially uniform bichromatic electric field: $\\mathbf{E}(t) = \\mathcal{E}_1 \\cos(\\omega_1 t) (\\hat{x} \\cos \\omega_1 t + \\hat{y} \\sin \\omega_1 t) + \\mathcal{E}_2 \\cos(\\omega_2 t) (\\hat{x} \\cos \\omega_2 t - \\hat{y} \\sin \\omega_2 t)$, representing two counterpropagating circularly polarized waves. They solve the kinetic equations numerically across three regimes: multiphoton (weak-field), tunneling (strong-field), and their combination (dynamical assistance). Helicity eigenstates are constructed from solutions of the Dirac equation in the background field, and momentum-resolved helicity asymmetries are computed as ratios $R(\\mathbf{p}) = f_{+}(\\mathbf{p}) / f_{-}(\\mathbf{p})$, where $\\pm$ denote helicity.
\n\n
作者采用费米子的量子动力学框架，通过相空间分布函数 $f_{\\mathbf{p},s}(t)$ 的输运方程描述对产生过程。外场被建模为空间均匀的双色电场：$\\mathbf{E}(t) = \\mathcal{E}_1 \\cos(\\omega_1 t) (\\hat{x} \\cos \\omega_1 t + \\hat{y} \\sin \\omega_1 t) + \\mathcal{E}_2 \\cos(\\omega_2 t) (\\hat{x} \\cos \\omega_2 t - \\hat{y} \\sin \\omega_2 t)$，代表两束对向传播的圆偏振波。他们在三个区域（多光子弱场区、隧穿强场区及其组合的动态辅助区）数值求解动力学方程。螺旋度本征态由Dirac方程在外场中的解构造，并计算动量分辨的螺旋度不对称性比值 $R(\\mathbf{p}) = f_{+}(\\mathbf{p}) / f_{-}(\\mathbf{p})$，其中 $\\pm$ 表示螺旋度。

Result: The key results are: (i) Dynamical assistance significantly enhances the helicity asymmetry in addition to the total pair yield; (ii) Right- and left-handed electrons are preferentially produced in opposite hemispheres defined by the field propagation axis ($p_z > 0$ vs. $p_z < 0$); (iii) The helicity ratio $R(\\mathbf{p})$ is dominantly a function of the polar angle $\\theta$ and exhibits weak dependence on the magnitude $|\\mathbf{p}|$ and azimuthal angle $\\phi$; (iv) This angular dependence sharpens as the frequency $\\omega_2$ of the weak high-frequency component increases. These findings hold across the transition between multiphoton and tunneling regimes.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(i) 动态辅助不仅显著增强总对产额，还大幅增强螺旋度不对称性；(ii) 右旋与左旋电子优先产生于由场传播轴定义的相反半球（$p_z > 0$ 与 $p_z < 0$）；(iii) 螺旋度比值 $R(\\mathbf{p})$ 主要依赖于极角 $\\theta$，而对动量大小 $|\\mathbf{p}|$ 和方位角 $\\phi$ 的依赖较弱；(iv) 随着弱高频分量频率 $\\omega_2$ 的增加，这种角度依赖性变得更加尖锐。这些结论在多光子与隧穿区域之间的过渡中均成立。

Conclusion: The paper establishes that the dynamically assisted Schwinger effect in rotating bichromatic fields imprints a robust and compact helicity signature on the produced electron-positron pairs. The dominance of polar-angle dependence in the helicity ratio provides a clean observable for experimental identification and theoretical modeling, suggesting that helicity-resolved measurements could serve as a sensitive probe of nonperturbative strong-field QED dynamics beyond total yields.
\n\n
本文确立了在旋转双色场中的动态辅助Schwinger效应对所产生的电子-正电子对施加了一个稳健且简洁的螺旋度印记。螺旋度比值对极角的主导依赖性提供了一个清晰的可观测量，可用于实验识别和理论建模，表明螺旋度分辨测量可作为超越总产额的非微扰强场QED动力学的灵敏探针。

Abstract: We study vacuum electron-positron pair production in a spatially uniform bichromatic electric field within the quantum-kinetic framework for fermions. The external background models the superposition of two counterpropagating circularly polarized laser pulses and combines a strong slowly varying component with a weak rapidly oscillating one. We analyze the weak-field multiphoton regime, the strong-field tunneling regime, and their combination corresponding to the dynamically assisted Schwinger effect. Our main focus is on helicity-resolved observables. We show that dynamical assistance enhances not only the total yield but also the helicity asymmetry: right- and left-handed electrons preferentially populate opposite momentum half-spaces. Most importantly, within the parameter range considered here, the ratio of the momentum distributions for opposite helicities is governed predominantly by the polar angle with respect to the propagation axis and depends only weakly on the momentum magnitude and azimuthal angle. The corresponding asymmetry becomes more pronounced as the weak-field frequency is increased. These results identify a clear helicity signature of the dynamically assisted Schwinger effect in rotating strong-field backgrounds and provide a compact characterization of the associated helicity-resolved spectra.

</details>


### [7] [Compact $cs\bar{s}\bar{s}$ Tetraquarks in the Charm--Strange Sector: Mass Spectra, Rearrangement Decays and Regge Trajectories with $D_s$ Threshold Inputs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18075)
*Chetan Lodha,Ajay Kumar Rai*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates the spectroscopy of the compact tetraquark $cs\bar{s}\bar{s}$ modeled as an axial diquark-antidiquark system $[cs][\bar{s}\bar{s}]$, computing its mass spectrum using Cornell potentials under semi-relativistic and non-relativistic treatments, analyzing strong decays via rearrangement into $D_s^{(*)}η$, $D_s^{(*)}η'$, and $D_s^{(*)}φ$ channels, and constructing Regge trajectories to characterize excitations—using the conventional $D_s$ meson spectrum for calibration.
\n\n
本文研究了被建模为轴向二夸克-反二夸克系统 $[cs][\bar{s}\bar{s}]$ 的紧致四夸克态 $cs\bar{s}\bar{s}$ 的谱学性质，采用Cornell势在半相对论与非相对论框架下计算其质量谱，通过重排衰变机制分析其强衰变至 $D_s^{(*)}η$、$D_s^{(*)}η'$ 和 $D_s^{(*)}φ$ 末态，并构建Regge轨迹以刻画激发模式——利用常规 $D_s$ 介子谱进行参数校准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to systematically explore exotic hadrons beyond the quark model, particularly multi-strange open-charm tetraquarks like $cs\bar{s}\bar{s}$, which are poorly constrained experimentally and theoretically. By treating it as a compact diquark-antidiquark state and leveraging Pauli symmetry constraints due to identical $\bar{s}$ antiquarks, the work aims to provide a robust phenomenological framework for identifying such states in hidden-strangeness open-charm final states.
\n\n
该工作的动机源于系统探索超出传统夸克模型的奇异强子（特别是多奇异开粲四夸克态如 $cs\bar{s}\bar{s}$）的必要性，这类态在实验和理论上均缺乏充分约束。通过将其视为紧致二夸克-反二夸克态，并利用因两个相同 $\bar{s}$ 反夸克导致的Pauli对称性限制，本研究旨在为在隐奇异开粲末态中识别此类态提供坚实的唯象学框架。

Method: The authors employ a Cornell-potential-based quark model with both semi-relativistic and non-relativistic kinematics to compute the mass spectrum of the $cs\bar{s}\bar{s}$ tetraquark, distinguishing between $\bar{\mathbf{3}}-\mathbf{3}$ and $\mathbf{6}-\bar{\mathbf{6}}$ color configurations. The $[\bar{s}\bar{s}]$ antidiquark is constrained by Pauli exclusion to axial-vector ($J^P=1^+$) states, forming $J^P=0^+,1^+,2^+$ tetraquark multiplets. Strong decays are treated via rearrangement topology $cs\bar{s}\bar{s}\rightarrow(c\bar{s})(s\bar{s})$, with decay amplitudes derived from spin-color Fierz transformations and normalized using QCD sum rules (two-point and three-point correlators). Regge trajectories (orbital and radial) are constructed and benchmarked against the calibrated $D_s$ meson spectrum.
\n\n
作者采用基于Cornell势的夸克模型，在半相对论与非相对论运动学下计算 $cs\bar{s}\bar{s}$ 四夸克态的质量谱，并区分 $\bar{\mathbf{3}}-\mathbf{3}$ 与 $\mathbf{6}-\bar{\mathbf{6}}$ 色构型。由于Pauli不相容原理，$[\bar{s}\bar{s}]$ 反二夸克被限制为轴矢量（$J^P=1^+$）态，从而构成 $J^P=0^+,1^+,2^+$ 四夸克多重态。强衰变通过重排拓扑 $cs\bar{s}\bar{s}\rightarrow(c\bar{s})(s\bar{s})$ 处理，衰变振幅由自旋-色Fierz变换导出，并利用QCD求和规则（两点与三点关联函数）进行归一化。构建轨道与径向Regge轨迹，并以校准后的 $D_s$ 介子谱为基准进行比对。

Result: The study yields a predicted mass spectrum for the $cs\bar{s}\bar{s}$ tetraquark in both color configurations, with the $\bar{\mathbf{3}}-\mathbf{3}$ channel favored as lower-lying. Dominant decay modes are identified as $D_s^{(*)}η$, $D_s^{(*)}η'$, and $D_s^{(*)}φ$, with partial widths estimated via QCD-sum-rule-normalized amplitudes. Orbital and radial Regge trajectories exhibit linear behavior, consistent with quark-model expectations, and align reasonably with the $D_s$ reference spectrum, supporting the compact tetraquark interpretation.
\n\n
研究给出了 $cs\bar{s}\bar{s}$ 四夸克态在两种色构型下的质量谱预测，其中 $\bar{\mathbf{3}}-\mathbf{3}$ 通道更可能对应低质量态。主导衰变道被确定为 $D_s^{(*)}η$、$D_s^{(*)}η'$ 和 $D_s^{(*)}φ$，部分宽度通过QCD求和规则归一化的振幅估算。轨道与径向Regge轨迹呈现线性行为，符合夸克模型预期，并与 $D_s$ 参考谱合理一致，支持紧致四夸克态的诠释。

Conclusion: The paper establishes a self-consistent spectroscopic and decay framework for the compact $cs\bar{s}\bar{s}$ tetraquark, demonstrating that axial diquark-antidiquark configurations naturally accommodate the Pauli principle and yield testable predictions for masses, decay patterns, and Regge behavior. This provides a targeted theoretical basis for experimental searches in channels like $D_s^{(*)}η$ and $D_s^{(*)}φ$ at facilities such as LHCb and Belle II.
\n\n
本文为紧致 $cs\bar{s}\bar{s}$ 四夸克态建立了一个自洽的谱学与衰变框架，表明轴向二夸克-反二夸克构型自然满足Pauli原理，并对质量、衰变模式及Regge行为给出可检验的预言。这为LHCb和Belle II等实验装置在 $D_s^{(*)}η$ 和 $D_s^{(*)}φ$ 等道中的搜寻提供了明确的理论依据。

Abstract: This work presents a spectroscopy-focused study of the compact open-charm, multi-strange tetraquark configuration \(cs\bar{s}\bar{s}\), modeled as an axial diquark-antidiquark system \([cs][\bar{s}\bar{s}]\). The conventional \(D_s\) meson spectrum is retained as a calibration sector for the model parameters and as a reference for the dominant two-meson thresholds; however, the primary emphasis is placed on the mass spectrum, threshold structure, rearrangement decay mechanisms, and Regge systematics of the \(cs\bar{s}\bar{s}\) tetraquark. The spectrum is computed within a Cornell-potential framework using both semi-relativistic and non-relativistic treatments, with the \(\bar{\mathbf{3}}-\mathbf{3}\) and \(\mathbf{6}-\bar{\mathbf{6}}\) color configurations analyzed separately. Owing to the presence of two identical strange antiquarks, Pauli symmetry imposes restrictions on the \([\bar{s}\bar{s}]\) antidiquark, favoring axial-vector building blocks as the natural low-lying degrees of freedom for the \(J^P=0^+,1^+,2^+\) tetraquark multiplet. The strong-decay sector is formulated in terms of the rearrangement topology \(cs\bar{s}\bar{s}\rightarrow(c\bar{s})(s\bar{s})\), with the \(D_s^{(*)}η\), \(D_s^{(*)}η'\), and \(D_s^{(*)}φ\) modes identified through spin-color Fierz recoupling and normalized using two-point and three-point QCD-sum-rule amplitudes. Orbital and radial Regge trajectories are constructed to characterize the excitation patterns of the compact tetraquark and to benchmark them against the calibrated \(D_s\) spectrum. This framework provides a dedicated phenomenological basis for identifying \(cs\bar{s}\bar{s}\) candidates in hidden-strangeness open-charm final states.

### [8] [The Triadic Texture: Neutrino Predictions, Viable Vacuum, and Phenomenological Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18154)
*Sagar Tirtha Goswami,Pralay Chakraborty,Subhankar Roy*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A minimal Majorana neutrino mass matrix texture is proposed that predicts normal mass hierarchy, the octant of $\\theta_{23}$, constraints on the Dirac CP phase $\\delta$, bounds on absolute neutrino masses, and ranges for the two Majorana phases. The texture is embedded in a Type-I seesaw mechanism and a Weinberg-like dimension-6 operator under an extended flavor symmetry $SU(2)_L \\otimes U(1)_Y \\otimes A_4 \\otimes Z_{10} \\otimes Z_7 \\otimes Z_5 \\otimes Z_3$. Viable vacuum alignments are constrained by scalar sector consistency, and the model suppresses conventional leptogenesis while restricting charged lepton flavor violation channels.
\n\n
本文提出了一种极简的Majorana中微子质量矩阵结构，该结构预言了中微子质量的正常层级、$\\theta_{23}$ 的八分象限、Dirac CP 相位 $\\delta$ 的约束、绝对中微子质量的界限，以及两个 Majorana 相位的取值范围。该结构在 Type-I seesaw 机制和 Weinberg 型维度-6 算符框架下实现，并基于扩展的对称群 $SU(2)_L \\otimes U(1)_Y \\otimes A_4 \\otimes Z_{10} \\otimes Z_7 \\otimes Z_5 \\otimes Z_3$。可行的标量场真空对齐受到标量扇区自洽性的限制，且该模型抑制了常规轻子生成机制（leptogenesis），同时限制了带电轻子味破坏（charged lepton flavour violation）的可能通道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to address the lack of predictivity in generic neutrino mass models by constructing a highly constrained and minimal texture for the Majorana neutrino mass matrix. This is motivated by current and upcoming precision measurements of neutrino oscillation parameters (e.g., $\\theta_{23}$ octant, $\\delta_{CP}$) and the need to link low-energy observables to high-scale flavor symmetries and UV-complete mechanisms like the Type-I seesaw.
\n\n
本文旨在通过构建一个高度受限且极简的 Majorana 中微子质量矩阵结构，解决一般中微子质量模型缺乏预言能力的问题。其动机源于当前及未来对中微子振荡参数（如 $\\theta_{23}$ 八分象限、$\\delta_{CP}$）的高精度测量需求，并试图将低能可观测量与高能标味对称性及 Type-I seesaw 等紫外完备机制联系起来。

Method: The authors construct a specific zero-texture or constrained form of the Majorana neutrino mass matrix that is compatible with observed mixing angles. They embed this texture within a Type-I seesaw framework supplemented by a Weinberg-like dimension-6 operator. The structure is enforced by an extended discrete and continuous gauge symmetry: $SU(2)_L \\otimes U(1)_Y \\otimes A_4 \\otimes Z_{10} \\otimes Z_7 \\otimes Z_5 \\otimes Z_3$. Different vacuum expectation value (VEV) alignments of flavon fields are considered, but only those yielding a consistent scalar potential and phenomenologically viable fermion masses are retained. Predictions for oscillation parameters, Majorana phases, and lepton flavor violation rates are derived from diagonalizing the resulting mass matrices.
\n\n
作者构建了一种与已观测混合角相容的特定零结构（或受约束形式）的 Majorana 中微子质量矩阵。该结构被嵌入到 Type-I seesaw 框架中，并辅以 Weinberg 型维度-6 算符。该形式由扩展的离散与连续规范对称性 $SU(2)_L \\otimes U(1)_Y \\otimes A_4 \\otimes Z_{10} \\otimes Z_7 \\otimes Z_5 \\otimes Z_3$ 所保证。文中考虑了不同味标量场（flavon）的真空期望值（VEV）对齐方式，但仅保留那些能产生自洽标量势和现象学上可行的费米子质量的构型。通过对所得质量矩阵进行对角化，推导出对振荡参数、Majorana 相位及轻子味破坏率的预言。

Result: The model successfully predicts normal neutrino mass hierarchy, fixes the octant of $\\theta_{23}$ (likely upper octant), constrains the Dirac CP-violating phase $\\delta$ to a limited range, provides upper and lower bounds on the lightest neutrino mass, and yields allowed intervals for the two Majorana phases. It also restricts possible charged lepton flavor violation processes (e.g., $\\mu \\to e\\gamma$) and leads to a suppressed baryon asymmetry via thermal leptogenesis due to small CP asymmetry parameters.
\n\n
该模型成功预言了中微子质量的正常层级，固定了 $\\theta_{23}$ 的八分象限（可能为上八分象限），将 Dirac CP 破坏相位 $\\delta$ 限制在较窄范围内，给出了最轻中微子质量的上下界，并确定了两个 Majorana 相位的允许区间。此外，它还限制了可能的带电轻子味破坏过程（如 $\\mu \\to e\\gamma$），并由于 CP 不对称参数较小，导致通过热轻子生成机制（thermal leptogenesis）产生的重子不对称性被压低。

Conclusion: The proposed minimal texture, when realized under a rich flavor symmetry structure, offers a predictive and testable framework for Majorana neutrino masses. It connects high-scale symmetry breaking to low-energy observables, including CP violation and absolute mass scales, while simultaneously addressing flavor violation and leptogenesis. Future neutrino experiments can directly test its predictions for $\\theta_{23}$, $\\delta$, and the mass hierarchy.
\n\n
所提出的极简质量矩阵结构在丰富的味对称性框架下实现，为 Majorana 中微子质量提供了一个具有预言性和可检验性的理论框架。它将高能标对称性破缺与包括 CP 破坏和绝对质量标度在内的低能可观测量联系起来，同时兼顾味破坏与轻子生成机制。未来的中微子实验可直接检验其对 $\\theta_{23}$、$\\delta$ 和质量层级的预言。

Abstract: A minimal and predictive neutrino mass matrix texture for Majorana neutrino is proposed. The texture favours the normal hierarchy of neutrino mass eigenvalues. It further predicts the octant of $θ_{23}$, constraints $δ$, gives bounds on neutrino mass eigenvalues and also gives ranges for the two Majorana phases.The texture is realised in the framework of a Type-I seesaw and a Weinberg like dimension 6 operator under an extended symmetry of $SU(2)_L \otimes U(1)_Y \otimes A_4 \otimes Z_{10} \otimes Z_7 \otimes Z_5 \otimes Z_3$. The texture can be realised with different sets of vacuum expectation values of the associated scalar fields, but not all such sets lead to a viable scalar sector. The model also constrains the allowed channels of charged lepton flavour violation and leads to a suppressed baryon asymmetry generation through conventional leptogenesis.

</details>


### [9] [Positivity of the effective range for finite range attractive potentials with a repulsive core](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18207)
*Davide Germani*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates that for single-channel local finite-range potentials with a repulsive core and attractive tail, the effective range $r_0$ is strictly positive when the scattering length exceeds the potential range ($a > R$), challenging the use of $r_0 < 0$ as a universal indicator of compact multiquark states.
\n\n
本文证明，对于具有排斥核和吸引尾的单通道局域有限程势，当散射长度超过势程（$a > R$）时，有效程 $r_0$ 严格为正，从而对将 $r_0 < 0$ 作为紧致多夸克态普适判据的做法提出挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from phenomenological claims in exotic hadron spectroscopy that a negative effective range ($r_0 < 0$) signals compact multiquark states, whereas a positive effective range ($r_0 > 0$) indicates loosely bound hadronic molecules. The authors aim to examine whether such sign-based classification holds under rigorous theoretical constraints for local, finite-range interactions.
\n\n
动机源于奇特强子谱学中的唯象主张：负的有效程（$r_0 < 0$）标志紧致多夸克组态，而正的有效程（$r_0 > 0$）对应松散束缚的强子分子态。作者旨在检验在局域、有限程相互作用的严格理论约束下，这种基于符号的分类是否成立。

Method: The authors employ rigorous scattering theory for single-channel quantum mechanical systems with local, finite-range potentials featuring a repulsive core at short distances and an attractive tail at longer ranges. They analyze the low-energy expansion of the phase shift and derive bounds on the effective range $r_0$ using integral representations and properties of the Jost function, under the condition $a > R$, where $a$ is the scattering length and $R$ the potential range.
\n\n
作者采用单通道量子力学系统的严格散射理论，研究具有短程排斥核和长程吸引尾的局域有限程势。他们分析相移的低能展开，利用Jost函数的积分表示及其性质，在条件 $a > R$（$a$ 为散射长度，$R$ 为势程）下推导有效程 $r_0$ 的严格界限。

Result: The paper proves that for any finite-range, local potential with a repulsive core and attractive tail, if the scattering length satisfies $a > R$, then the effective range must be strictly positive: $r_0 > 0$. This result contradicts the naive identification of $r_0 < 0$ with compact multiquark states in such systems.
\n\n
论文证明：对于任何具有排斥核和吸引尾的有限程局域势，若散射长度满足 $a > R$，则有效程必严格为正：$r_0 > 0$。该结果与将 $r_0 < 0$ 简单等同于紧致多夸克态的观点相矛盾。

Conclusion: The sign of the effective range alone cannot reliably distinguish between compact multiquark states and hadronic molecules in systems governed by local finite-range interactions. The condition $r_0 < 0$ is not generally attainable under physically motivated potential structures when $a > R$, implying that more sophisticated criteria beyond the effective range sign are needed in exotic hadron classification.
\n\n
仅凭有效程的符号无法可靠区分由局域有限程相互作用支配系统中的紧致多夸克态与强子分子态。在物理上合理的势结构下，当 $a > R$ 时，条件 $r_0 < 0$ 通常无法实现，这表明奇特强子分类需要超越有效程符号的更精细判据。

Abstract: In the phenomenological study of exotic hadrons, the sign of the effective range, $r_0$, is invoked as a criterion to distinguish between compact multiquark configurations (associated with $r_0 < 0$) and loosely bound hadronic molecules ($r_0 > 0$). Motivated by this, we investigate the fundamental constraints on the sign of the effective range for single-channel local interactions. We rigorously prove that for finite-range potentials, characterized by an inner repulsive core and an outer attractive tail, the effective range remains strictly positive provided that the scattering length is greater than the range of the potential ($a > R$).

</details>


### [10] [An EFT Map of Axion Dark Radiation from Reheating](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17178)
*Yong Xu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Light axions produced during reheating contribute to dark radiation ($ΔN_{\rm eff}$) via two channels—direct inflaton decay and inflaton annihilation—encoded in a shift-symmetric EFT with an inflaton-dependent axion kinetic term. These channels scale oppositely with reheating temperature $T_{\rm rh}$, enabling combined constraints on Wilson coefficients and yielding both upper and lower bounds on $T_{\rm rh}$ from $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ measurements.
\n\n
在再加热期间产生的轻轴子通过两种机制——直接暴胀子衰变和暴胀子湮灭——对暗辐射（$ΔN_{\rm eff}$）产生贡献，这些机制被编码在一个具有暴胀子依赖的轴子动能项的平移对称EFT中。这两种机制对再加热温度 $T_{\rm rh}$ 的依赖关系相反，使得结合 $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ 测量可同时约束Wilson系数，并对 $T_{\rm rh}$ 给出上下限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Current and future measurements of dark radiation ($ΔN_{\rm eff}$) offer a unique probe of physics beyond the Standard Model during the early universe, particularly during reheating. Light, weakly coupled axion-like particles can be produced during this epoch and retain memory of the cosmological background. However, previous analyses often consider only one production mechanism (e.g., decay or scattering), potentially missing crucial interference or complementary sensitivity. A systematic EFT framework is needed to unify and compare all leading-order production channels consistently.
\n\n
当前和未来的暗辐射（$ΔN_{\rm eff}$）测量为探测早期宇宙（尤其是在再加热时期）超出标准模型的物理提供了独特窗口。轻且弱耦合的类轴子粒子可在该时期产生并保留宇宙学背景的信息。然而，以往分析通常只考虑单一产生机制（如衰变或散射），可能遗漏关键的干涉效应或互补敏感性。因此需要一个系统的EFT框架来统一并一致地比较所有主导的产生通道。

Method: The authors construct a shift-symmetric Effective Field Theory (EFT) where the axion kinetic term depends on the inflaton field: $\\mathcal{L} \\supset -\\frac{1}{2} Z(\\phi) (\\partial_\\mu a)^2$, with $Z(\\phi) = 1 + \\sum_n c_n \\phi^n / M^{n}$. Expanding around the oscillating inflaton background after inflation generates time-dependent couplings that source axion production. They compute two leading contributions: (1) direct inflaton decay $\\phi \\to a a$, governed by the branching fraction $\\text{Br}_{\\rm inv}$, and (2) inflaton annihilation $\\phi \\phi \\to a a$ from coherent inflaton oscillations, controlled by a combination of Wilson coefficients $c_n$. The resulting phase-space distribution is integrated to obtain $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ as a function of reheating temperature $T_{\rm rh}$ and EFT parameters.
\n\n
作者构建了一个平移对称的有效场论（EFT），其中轴子动能项依赖于暴胀子场：$\\mathcal{L} \\supset -\\frac{1}{2} Z(\\phi) (\\partial_\\mu a)^2$，其中 $Z(\\phi) = 1 + \\sum_n c_n \\phi^n / M^{n}$。在暴胀结束后围绕振荡的暴胀子背景展开，会产生含时耦合，从而激发轴子产生。他们计算了两个主导贡献：(1) 直接暴胀子衰变 $\\phi \\to a a$，由不可见分支比 $\\text{Br}_{\\rm inv}$ 主导；(2) 来自相干暴胀子振荡的暴胀子湮灭 $\\phi \\phi \\to a a$，由Wilson系数 $c_n$ 的特定组合控制。通过对相空间分布积分，得到 $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ 作为再加热温度 $T_{\rm rh}$ 和EFT参数的函数。

Result: The decay channel contributes $ΔN_{\rm eff}^{\\rm dec} \\propto T_{\rm rh}^{-2}$, while the annihilation channel gives $ΔN_{\rm eff}^{\\rm ann} \\propto T_{\rm rh}^{4/3}$. Their opposite scalings imply a crossing point in $T_{\rm rh}$ where both mechanisms are equally important—a feature absent in single-channel analyses. Using current (e.g., Planck) and future (CMB-S4, CMB-HD) $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ sensitivities, the authors map constraints onto the two-dimensional space of Wilson coefficients $(c_1, c_2)$ in the kinetic function $Z(\\phi)$. This yields nontrivial exclusion regions and, importantly, simultaneous upper and lower bounds on $T_{\rm rh}$ for fixed EFT parameters.
\n\n
衰变通道的贡献满足 $ΔN_{\rm eff}^{\\rm dec} \\propto T_{\rm rh}^{-2}$，而湮灭通道满足 $ΔN_{\rm eff}^{\\rm ann} \\propto T_{\rm rh}^{4/3}$。二者相反的标度行为意味着存在一个 $T_{\rm rh}$ 的交叉点，此时两种机制同等重要——这一特征在单通道分析中被遗漏。利用当前（如Planck）和未来（CMB-S4、CMB-HD）对 $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ 的灵敏度，作者将限制映射到动能函数 $Z(\\phi)$ 中Wilson系数 $(c_1, c_2)$ 的二维参数空间上。这给出了非平凡的排除区域，并且更重要的是，对于固定的EFT参数，可同时得出 $T_{\rm rh}$ 的上限和下限。

Conclusion: Light axion production during reheating, when treated within a consistent shift-symmetric EFT, reveals a rich interplay between multiple production channels whose relative importance depends strongly on the reheating temperature. Dark radiation measurements thus do not merely constrain axion couplings but can also provide robust, two-sided bounds on the reheating history of the universe. This establishes $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ as a powerful indirect probe of reheating dynamics through axion relics.
\n\n
在一致的平移对称EFT框架下处理再加热期间的轻轴子产生，揭示了多种产生机制之间的丰富相互作用，其相对重要性强烈依赖于再加热温度。因此，暗辐射测量不仅约束轴子耦合，还能对宇宙再加热历史给出稳健的双向限制。这确立了 $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ 作为通过轴子遗迹间接探测再加热动力学的强大工具。

Abstract: Light, weakly coupled sectors can retain information about the cosmological background in which they are produced. We study light axions produced during reheating and their contribution to dark radiation, $ΔN_{\rm eff}$. We develop a shift-symmetric EFT in which an inflaton-dependent axion kinetic term systematically organizes the leading production channels. The same kinetic function generates both direct inflaton decay and inflaton annihilation from the oscillating inflaton background. Direct decay is described by an invisible inflaton branching fraction, while annihilation is a genuinely reheating-sensitive source controlled by a coherent combination of Wilson coefficients. We derive the contribution to $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ from both channels and show that they scale oppositely with the reheating temperature: the decay contribution falls as $T_{\rm rh}^{-2}$, whereas the annihilation contribution grows approximately as $T_{\rm rh}^{4/3}$. Their crossing is missed by treatments that keep only one production channel. We translate current and projected $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ sensitivities into constraints on the Wilson coefficients of the kinetic function, obtaining a two-dimensional EFT map of axion dark radiation from reheating. This map can imply both lower and upper bounds on the reheating temperature, showing that light axion relics can turn dark radiation measurements into constraints on reheating.

</details>


### [11] [Two-body decays of radially excited $η(1295)$ and $η(1475)$ mesons in the extended NJL model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18270)
*M. K. Volkov,A. A. Pivovarov,K. Nurlan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates two-body strong decays of the radially excited pseudoscalar mesons $η(1295)$ and $η(1475)$ within the extended Nambu–Jona-Lasinio (NJL) model. It finds that for $η(1475)$, dominant decay channels are $η(1475)\to K_0^*K$ and $a_0π$, while $η(1475)\to K^*K$ is suppressed; in contrast, all two-body decays of $η(1295)$ contribute negligibly to its total width.
\n\n
本文在扩展的Nambu–Jona-Lasinio（NJL）模型中研究了径向激发赝标量介子$η(1295)$和$η(1475)$的两体强衰变。结果表明，对于$η(1475)$，主导衰变道为$η(1475)\to K_0^*K$和$a_0π$，而$η(1475)\to K^*K$被压低；相比之下，$η(1295)$的所有两体衰变对其总宽度的贡献均可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the decay patterns and total widths of the poorly characterized radially excited pseudoscalar mesons $η(1295)$ and $η(1475)$ by employing a non-perturbative effective field theory—the extended NJL model—which incorporates quark dynamics and chiral symmetry breaking.
\n\n
动机在于通过采用一种非微扰有效场论——扩展的NJL模型（该模型包含夸克动力学和手征对称性破缺），来理解尚未充分刻画的径向激发赝标量介子$η(1295)$和$η(1475)$的衰变模式及其总宽度。

Method: The authors use the extended Nambu–Jona-Lasinio (NJL) model to compute amplitudes for two-body strong decays of $η(1295)$ and $η(1475)$. This approach includes quark loop diagrams with constituent quark masses generated dynamically via spontaneous chiral symmetry breaking, and accounts for intermediate scalar and vector meson states such as $K_0^*$, $a_0$, and $K^*$.
\n\n
作者使用扩展的Nambu–Jona-Lasinio（NJL）模型计算$η(1295)$和$η(1475)$的两体强衰变振幅。该方法包含由自发手征对称性破缺动态生成的组分夸克质量的夸克圈图，并考虑了如$K_0^*$、$a_0$和$K^*$等中间标量与矢量介子态。

Result: The calculation shows that the dominant contributions to the total decay width of $η(1475)$ come from $η(1475)\to K_0^*K$ and $a_0π$, while $η(1475)\to K^*K$ is significantly suppressed. In contrast, all considered two-body decay channels for $η(1295)$ yield negligible partial widths, implying its width must arise from other mechanisms (e.g., three-body decays or mixing effects).
\n\n
计算结果表明，$η(1475)$总衰变宽度的主要贡献来自$η(1475)\to K_0^*K$和$a_0π$，而$η(1475)\to K^*K$被显著压低。相比之下，$η(1295)$所有考虑的两体衰变道给出的分宽度均可忽略，意味着其宽度必须源于其他机制（例如三体衰变或混合效应）。

Conclusion: The extended NJL model successfully explains the observed hierarchy in decay widths of radially excited $η$ mesons, highlighting the importance of scalar meson intermediate states and suggesting that $η(1295)$ may not be dominantly a radial excitation of the ground-state $η$ meson, or that its decay dynamics require inclusion of additional channels beyond two-body processes.
\n\n
扩展的NJL模型成功解释了径向激发$η$介子衰变宽度的层级结构，凸显了标量介子中间态的重要性，并暗示$η(1295)$可能并非基态$η$介子的纯径向激发态，或者其衰变动力学需要引入超出两体过程的额外道。

Abstract: In the extended NJL model, two-body strong decays of the radially excited $η(1295)$ and $η(1475)$ mesons are described. It is shown that the two-body decays $η(1475)\to K_0^*K, a_0π$ play a dominant role in determining the width of the radially excited meson $η(1475)$. At the same time, the decays $η(1475)\to K^*K$ make a significantly smaller contribution to the total width. It is shown that two-particle decays give only a negligible contribution to the total width of the $η(1295)$.

### [12] [Gravitational form factors of light mesons from Basis Light-Front Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18350)
*Amrita Sain,Sreeraj Nair,Chandan Mondal,Xingbo Zhao,James P. Vary*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper computes the gravitational form factors (GFFs) $A(Q^2)$ and $D(Q^2)$ for the pion and kaon using light-front wave functions derived from a Basis Light-Front Quantization (BLFQ) framework with a confining Hamiltonian and Nambu–Jona-Lasinio interaction. While $A(Q^2)$ agrees with lattice QCD and dispersive methods, $D(Q^2)$ shows significant low-$Q^2$ enhancement due to sensitivity to small-$x$ dynamics and zero-mode effects. The GFFs are used to extract mass and mechanical radii and to study pressure and shear-force distributions.
\n\n
本文在Basis Light-Front Quantization（BLFQ）框架下，利用包含三维禁闭势和Nambu–Jona-Lasinio相互作用的轻前有效哈密顿量求解π介子和K介子的轻前波函数，并由此计算其引力形状因子（GFFs）$A(Q^2)$和$D(Q^2)$。结果表明，$A(Q^2)$与格点QCD及色散方法总体一致，而$D(Q^2)$在低$Q^2$区域显著增强，这源于使用QCD能量-动量张量横向分量提取$D$项时对小$x$区域和轻前零模效应的敏感性。作者进一步利用所得GFFs确定了π介子和K介子的质量（物质）半径与力学半径，并分析了其压力与剪切力分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the internal mechanical structure of hadrons—such as pressure and shear-force distributions—requires knowledge of their gravitational form factors (GFFs), particularly the $D$-term. However, nonperturbative calculations of GFFs remain challenging. This work aims to provide a first-principles-inspired computation of pion and kaon GFFs within a light-front Hamiltonian approach that incorporates both confinement and chiral symmetry breaking via an effective Nambu–Jona-Lasinio interaction.
\n\n
理解强子内部力学结构（如压力与剪切力分布）需要掌握其引力形状因子（GFFs），尤其是$D$项。然而，GFFs的非微扰计算仍具挑战性。本文旨在通过一个结合禁闭与手征对称性破缺（通过有效Nambu–Jona-Lasinio相互作用）的轻前哈密顿量方法，对π介子和K介子的GFFs进行基于第一性原理启发的计算。

Method: The authors employ the Basis Light-Front Quantization (BLFQ) framework to solve for the light-front wave functions of the pion and kaon. The effective Hamiltonian includes a three-dimensional harmonic confinement potential and a color-singlet Nambu–Jona-Lasinio (NJL) interaction between the valence quark and antiquark. Gravitational form factors $A(Q^2)$ and $D(Q^2)$ are extracted from matrix elements of the QCD energy–momentum tensor, specifically using its transverse components in the light-front formalism. The $D$-term is isolated via the Fourier transform of the $D(Q^2)$ form factor to obtain spatial pressure and shear-force distributions.
\n\n
作者采用Basis Light-Front Quantization（BLFQ）框架求解π介子和K介子的轻前波函数。有效哈密顿量包含三维谐振子禁闭势以及价夸克-反夸克之间的color-singlet Nambu–Jona-Lasinio（NJL）相互作用。引力形状因子$A(Q^2)$和$D(Q^2)$通过QCD能量-动量张量矩阵元提取，特别在轻前形式中使用其横向分量。$D$项通过$D(Q^2)$的傅里叶变换分离，以获得空间压力与剪切力分布。

Result: The computed $A(Q^2)$ for both pion and kaon agrees well with recent lattice QCD and dispersive results. However, the $D(Q^2)$ form factor exhibits a pronounced enhancement at low momentum transfer ($Q^2 \\to 0$) compared to those same references. This discrepancy is attributed to the use of transverse components of the energy–momentum tensor, which amplify contributions from the small-$x$ region and light-front zero modes—effects not fully captured in the current truncated Fock space. From the GFFs, the authors extract the mass radius $\\sqrt{\\langle r^2 \\rangle_{\\text{mass}}}$ and mechanical radius $\\sqrt{\\langle r^2 \\rangle_{\\text{mech}}}$, and reconstruct the radial pressure $p(r)$ and shear-force $s(r)$ distributions, revealing a repulsive core and confining pressure shell.
\n\n
计算得到的π介子和K介子的$A(Q^2)$与近期格点QCD及色散结果吻合良好。然而，$D(Q^2)$形状因子在低动量转移（$Q^2 \\to 0$）区域相比这些参考结果显著增强。这一差异归因于使用能量-动量张量的横向分量，该分量放大了小$x$区域和轻前零模的贡献——这些效应在当前截断的Fock空间中未被完全捕捉。作者从GFFs中提取了质量半径$\\sqrt{\\langle r^2 \\rangle_{\\text{mass}}}$和力学半径$\\sqrt{\\langle r^2 \\rangle_{\\text{mech}}}$，并重构了径向压力$p(r)$与剪切力$s(r)$分布，揭示出排斥核心与禁闭压力壳层结构。

Conclusion: The BLFQ approach provides a viable nonperturbative framework for computing hadronic gravitational form factors and mechanical properties. The observed enhancement of the $D$-term underscores the importance of small-$x$ physics and zero-mode contributions in light-front formulations. Future improvements—such as inclusion of higher Fock sectors and refined treatment of zero modes—are necessary to achieve quantitative agreement with lattice and dispersive methods for the $D(Q^2)$ form factor.
\n\n
BLFQ方法为计算强子引力形状因子及其力学性质提供了一个可行的非微扰框架。所观测到的$D$项增强突显了小$x$物理和零模贡献在轻前表述中的重要性。未来需通过引入更高阶Fock态及改进零模处理，以实现$D(Q^2)$形状因子与格点及色散方法的定量一致。

Abstract: We compute the gravitational form factors (GFFs) of the pion and kaon using their light-front wave functions within the Basis Light-Front Quantization framework. The wave functions are obtained by solving a light-front effective Hamiltonian that incorporates three-dimensional confinement along with a color-singlet Nambu--Jona-Lasinio interaction between the constituent quark and antiquark. The form factor $A(Q^2)$ is found to be in overall agreement with recent lattice QCD and dispersive results. In contrast, $D(Q^2)$ is enhanced in magnitude at low $Q^2$ relative to both lattice QCD and dispersive determinations. This behavior arises from extracting the $D$-term using transverse components of the QCD energy--momentum tensor, which are more sensitive to the small-$x$ region and to light-front zero-mode effects in the present truncated framework. Using the resulting GFFs, we determine the mass (matter) and mechanical radii of the pion and kaon and analyze their mechanical structure through the corresponding pressure and shear-force distributions.

</details>


### [13] [Nested-GPT for variable-multiplicity parton showers: A case study in the resummation of non-global logarithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18360)
*Wanchen Li,Ding Yu Shao,Hao-Zhe Shi,Yu-Xuan Sun*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We propose Nested-GPT, a hierarchical autoregressive Transformer that dynamically generates variable-multiplicity parton-shower histories by enforcing ordered Markovian branching and learning a sequence-termination condition. It outperforms a flow-matching Transformer baseline—which requires fixed multiplicity—on gap fraction observables in the leading-logarithmic large-$N_c$ limit, demonstrating physical consistency and potential for extension to subleading logarithms and finite-$N_c$.
\n\n
我们提出了 Nested-GPT，一种分层自回归 Transformer 架构，通过强制有序的马尔可夫分支结构并学习序列终止条件，动态生成可变多重性的 parton shower 历史。在大 $N_c$ 极限下的领头对数近似中，它在 gap fraction 观测量上优于需要固定多重性的流匹配（flow-matching）Transformer 基线，展现出物理一致性，并为推广到次领头对数和有限 $N_c$ 色演化提供了动机。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional parton showers rely on stochastic Monte Carlo methods that are computationally expensive and lack differentiability. Recent machine learning approaches, such as flow matching, can model fixed-multiplicity emission distributions but fail to dynamically generate the number of emissions—a core feature of physical showers. The authors aim to develop a generative model that respects the causal, ordered structure of parton branching while allowing variable final-state multiplicities, enabling both efficiency and physical fidelity.
\n\n
传统的 parton shower 依赖于计算昂贵且不可微的随机蒙特卡洛方法。近期的机器学习方法（如流匹配）虽能建模固定多重性的辐射分布，但无法动态生成辐射次数——这是物理 shower 的核心特征。作者旨在开发一种既能尊重 parton 分支的因果有序结构，又能允许末态多重性可变的生成模型，从而兼顾计算效率与物理保真度。

Method: The paper introduces Nested-GPT, a hierarchical autoregressive Transformer that sequentially predicts emissions in an ordered phase space (e.g., angular or energy ordering), mimicking the Markovian evolution of parton showers. At each step, it outputs kinematic variables and a learned termination probability, enabling dynamic determination of multiplicity. Training data comes from a leading-logarithmic dipole Monte Carlo shower in the large-$N_c$ limit. The model is compared against a flow-matching Transformer that models the joint distribution of emissions at fixed multiplicity using a continuous normalizing flow. Two training strategies are tested: (1) direct training on vetoed (gap-enforced) histories, and (2) inclusive training followed by post-hoc application of the gap veto at analysis level.
\n\n
本文提出 Nested-GPT，一种分层自回归 Transformer，按有序相空间（如角度或能量排序）依次预测辐射，模拟 parton shower 的马尔可夫演化。每一步输出运动学变量和一个学习得到的终止概率，从而动态确定多重性。训练数据来自大 $N_c$ 极限下领头对数精度的偶极子蒙特卡洛 shower。该模型与一个使用连续归一化流（continuous normalizing flow）建模固定多重性辐射联合分布的流匹配 Transformer 进行对比。测试了两种训练策略：(1) 直接在施加了 veto（gap 约束）的历史上训练；(2) 先进行包容性训练，再在分析阶段事后施加 gap veto。

Result: Both Nested-GPT and the flow-matching baseline reproduce reference Monte Carlo predictions for gap fraction observables within statistical uncertainties under both training regimes. However, only Nested-GPT naturally generates variable-multiplicity samples without requiring the final emission count as input. Its autoregressive structure enforces physical ordering and causality, making it a faithful surrogate for parton showers. The flow-matching approach, while accurate for fixed multiplicity, lacks intrinsic termination dynamics.
\n\n
在两种训练方案下，Nested-GPT 和流匹配基线均能在统计误差范围内复现参考蒙特卡洛对 gap fraction 观测量的预测。然而，只有 Nested-GPT 能自然生成可变多重性样本，无需预先指定最终辐射次数。其自回归结构强制实施了物理排序与因果性，使其成为 parton shower 的忠实代理。流匹配方法虽在固定多重性下准确，但缺乏内在的终止动力学。

Conclusion: Nested-GPT provides a physically consistent, differentiable, and autoregressive surrogate for parton showers with variable multiplicity, successfully capturing leading-logarithmic non-global logarithm resummation in the large-$N_c$ limit. This framework paves the way for extending machine-learned showers to subleading-logarithmic accuracy and finite-$N_c$ color correlations, potentially enabling fast, differentiable event generators for precision collider physics.
\n\n
Nested-GPT 为具有可变多重性的 parton shower 提供了一个物理自洽、可微且自回归的代理模型，成功捕捉了大 $N_c$ 极限下非全局对数的领头对数重求和。该框架为将机器学习 shower 推广至次领头对数精度和有限 $N_c$ 色关联铺平了道路，有望实现用于高精度对撞机物理的快速、可微事件生成器。

Abstract: We introduce Nested-GPT, a hierarchical autoregressive Transformer architecture for simulating the variable-multiplicity parton-shower histories. As a controlled benchmark, we study the leading-logarithmic resummation of non-global logarithms in the large-$N_c$ limit, utilizing a stochastic Monte Carlo dipole shower to generate reference training data. We systematically evaluate Nested-GPT against a Transformer flow-matching baseline. The flow-matching framework successfully parameterizes the joint distribution of emission kinematics at fixed multiplicity. Its phase-space representation, however, requires the final number of emissions to be specified externally rather than generated dynamically. Conversely, Nested-GPT strictly enforces the ordered Markovian branching structure, predicting emissions sequentially and dynamically evaluating a learned sequence-termination condition. We benchmark both approaches using gap fraction observables under two complementary training regimes: direct training on vetoed histories and inclusive training followed by an analysis-level veto. The resulting generated samples agree with the reference shower within statistical uncertainties for the observables considered. These results establish Nested-GPT as a physically consistent autoregressive surrogate for variable-multiplicity shower generator and motivate extensions to subleading-logarithmic resummation and finite-$N_c$ color evolution.

</details>


### [14] [Probing SMEFT Operators through $t\bar{t}t\bar{t}$ Production with Hyper-Graph Neural Networks at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18382)
*Amir Subba,Sanmay Ganguly*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents a phenomenological study of $t\bar{t}t\bar{t}$ production at $\sqrt{s} = 13$~TeV using a Hyper-Graph Neural Network (H-GNN) to distinguish signal from Standard Model backgrounds. The H-GNN models events as hypergraphs capturing higher-order kinematic correlations among jets and leptons, achieving superior discrimination performance (AUC = 0.951) and a statistical significance of $Z = 9.11$ at $\mathcal{L} = 140~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$, outperforming other ML baselines and the ATLAS analysis. The enhanced sensitivity is used to set 95% CL limits on several dimension-six SMEFT Wilson coefficients and project HL-LHC sensitivities.
\n\n
本文对质子-质子对撞中 $\sqrt{s} = 13$~TeV 下的 $t\bar{t}t\bar{t}$ 产生过程进行了唯象研究，采用超图神经网络（Hyper-Graph Neural Network, H-GNN）区分信号与标准模型（SM）主要背景。H-GNN 将每个事例表示为超图，节点对应重建的喷注和轻子，超边编码这些对象任意子集间的高阶关联，从而学习 $t\bar{t}t\bar{t}$ 末态特有的多体运动学结构。在 CMS 类似的事例选择下，结合同号双轻子、三轻子和四轻子道，H-GNN 对 $t\bar{t}t\bar{t}$ 信号的 ROC 曲线下面积达到 0.951，在积分亮度 $\mathcal{L} = 140~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ 下统计显著性为 $Z = 9.11$，优于 SPANet 基线（$Z = 8.62$）、Particle Transformer 基线（$Z = 7.37$）以及 ATLAS 分析结果（$Z = 5.13$）。利用该提升的信号提取能力，作者设定了多个维度六 SMEFT 算符 Wilson 系数的 95% 置信度上限，并投影了在高亮度 LHC（HL-LHC）积分亮度 $1000~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ 和 $3000~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ 下的预期灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The extremely rare $t\bar{t}t\bar{t}$ process is a sensitive probe of new physics beyond the Standard Model, particularly through modifications induced by dimension-six operators in the SMEFT framework. However, its observation is hindered by overwhelming SM backgrounds with similar multilepton final states. Traditional cut-based or shallow machine learning methods struggle to fully exploit the complex many-body kinematic correlations inherent in the $t\bar{t}t\bar{t}$ signal. This motivates the development of more powerful discriminators capable of modeling high-order relationships among final-state objects.
\n\n
极稀有的 $t\bar{t}t\bar{t}$ 过程是探测标准模型之外新物理的灵敏探针，尤其通过 SMEFT 框架中维度六算符引起的修正。然而，其观测受到具有相似多轻子末态的压倒性标准模型背景的阻碍。传统的基于切割或浅层机器学习方法难以充分利用 $t\bar{t}t\bar{t}$ 信号中固有的复杂多体运动学关联。这促使人们开发更强大的判别器，以建模末态对象之间的高阶关系。

Method: The authors employ a Hyper-Graph Neural Network (H-GNN), where each collision event is represented as a hypergraph: nodes correspond to reconstructed jets and leptons, and hyperedges connect arbitrary subsets of nodes to encode higher-order kinematic correlations beyond pairwise interactions. This architecture enables the network to learn the intricate many-body structure of the $t\bar{t}t\bar{t}$ final state. The analysis combines same-sign di-lepton, tri-lepton, and four-lepton channels under a CMS-like selection. Performance is benchmarked against SPANet, Particle Transformer, and the ATLAS analysis using identical event selections. Statistical significance is computed via the Asimov dataset method, and constraints on SMEFT Wilson coefficients are derived using a profile likelihood ratio.
\n\n
作者采用超图神经网络（Hyper-Graph Neural Network, H-GNN），其中每个对撞事例被表示为一个超图：节点对应重建的喷注和轻子，超边连接节点的任意子集，以编码超越成对相互作用的高阶运动学关联。该架构使网络能够学习 $t\bar{t}t\bar{t}$ 末态复杂的多体结构。分析在 CMS 类似的选择下结合了同号双轻子、三轻子和四轻子道。在相同事例选择下，与 SPANet、Particle Transformer 和 ATLAS 分析进行性能基准比较。统计显著性通过 Asimov 数据集方法计算，并使用轮廓似然比推导 SMEFT Wilson 系数的约束。

Result: The H-GNN achieves an AUC of 0.951 for $t\bar{t}t\bar{t}$ signal versus combined SM backgrounds. At $\mathcal{L} = 140~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$, it yields a statistical significance of $Z = 9.11$, surpassing SPANet ($Z = 8.62$), Particle Transformer ($Z = 7.37$), and the ATLAS result ($Z = 5.13$). Using this improved sensitivity, the study sets 95% CL upper limits on the Wilson coefficients of five dimension-six SMEFT operators: $\mathcal{O}_{Φu}$, $\mathcal{O}^{(1)}_{tt}$, $\mathcal{O}^{(1)}_{qq}$, $\mathcal{O}^{(1)}_{qt}$, and $\mathcal{O}^{(8)}_{qt}$. Projections for HL-LHC with $\mathcal{L} = 1000$ and $3000~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ (assuming 50% background uncertainty) show significantly improved expected constraints.
\n\n
H-GNN 在 $t\bar{t}t\bar{t}$ 信号与组合标准模型背景之间达到了 0.951 的 AUC。在 $\mathcal{L} = 140~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ 下，其统计显著性为 $Z = 9.11$，优于 SPANet（$Z = 8.62$）、Particle Transformer（$Z = 7.37$）和 ATLAS 结果（$Z = 5.13$）。利用这一提升的灵敏度，本研究设定了五个维度六 SMEFT 算符——$\mathcal{O}_{Φu}$、$\mathcal{O}^{(1)}_{tt}$、$\mathcal{O}^{(1)}_{qq}$、$\mathcal{O}^{(1)}_{qt}$ 和 $\mathcal{O}^{(8)}_{qt}$——的 Wilson 系数的 95% 置信度上限。对高亮度 LHC（HL-LHC）在 $\mathcal{L} = 1000$ 和 $3000~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$（假设背景不确定性为 50%）下的投影显示出显著改善的预期约束。

Conclusion: The H-GNN framework demonstrates superior capability in capturing complex many-body kinematic features of rare multi-top processes, leading to significantly enhanced signal sensitivity compared to existing methods. This advancement enables stronger constraints on BSM physics parameterized by SMEFT, and the methodology is readily extendable to other high-multiplicity final states at the LHC and future colliders.
\n\n
H-GNN 框架在捕捉稀有多顶过程的复杂多体运动学特征方面展现出卓越能力，相比现有方法显著提升了信号灵敏度。这一进展使得对由 SMEFT 参数化的新物理（BSM）施加更强的约束成为可能，且该方法可直接推广至 LHC 及未来对撞机上的其他高多重数末态。

Abstract: We present a phenomenological study of $t\bar{t}t\bar{t}$ production in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s} = 13$~TeV, using a Hyper-Graph Neural Network (H-GNN) to discriminate multilepton signal events from the dominant SM backgrounds, namely $t\bar{t}W$, $t\bar{t}Z$, $t\bar{t}H$, $t\bar{t}VV$, single-top associated production, and diboson and triboson processes. In the H-GNN architecture each event is represented as a hypergraph whose nodes correspond to reconstructed jets and leptons and whose hyperedges encode higher-order correlations among arbitrary subsets of these objects, allowing the network to learn the many-body kinematic structures that characterize the $t\bar{t}t\bar{t}$ final state. Combining same-sign di-lepton, tri-lepton, and four-lepton channels following a CMS-like event selection, the H-GNN attains an area under the ROC curve of $0.951$ for the $t\bar{t}t\bar{t}$ signal and yields a statistical significance of $Z = 9.11$ at an integrated luminosity of $\mathcal{L} = 140~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$, to be compared with $Z = 8.62$ for a SPANet baseline, $Z = 7.37$ for a Particle Transformer baseline, and $Z = 5.13$ obtained by the ATLAS analysis, evaluated under identical event selection. We exploit the improved signal extraction to derive one- and two-parameter $95\%$ confidence level limits on the Wilson coefficients of the dimension-six operators $\mathcal{O}_{Φu}$, $\mathcal{O}^{(1)}_{tt}$, $\mathcal{O}^{(1)}_{qq}$, $\mathcal{O}^{(1)}_{qt}$, and $\mathcal{O}^{(8)}_{qt}$, and we project the expected sensitivity at the HL-LHC integrated luminosities of $1000~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ and $3000~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ with $50\%$ uncertainty on the background estimation.

### [15] [Quantum enhanced identification of boosted jets with quantum graph neural networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18416)
*Parichehr Kangaziankangazi,Abideh Jafari,Maurizio Pierini,Hamed Bakhshiansohi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We introduce a quantum-enhanced jet tagger using a convolutional quantum graph neural network (QGNN) to distinguish highly boosted Z boson jets from gluon jets. The input data are preprocessed via a noise-augmented convolutional autoencoder for dimensionality reduction, then formatted into graphs and processed by a 10-qubit QGNN. Training is performed both separately and jointly for the autoencoder and QGNN, with results showing competitive performance against classical graph neural networks.
\n\n
我们提出了一种量子增强的喷注标记器，使用卷积量子图神经网络（QGNN）来区分高度洛伦兹boosted的Z玻色子喷注与高动量胶子喷注。输入数据通过加入噪声的卷积自编码器进行降维预处理，随后转换为图结构并送入一个10量子比特的QGNN。自编码器与QGNN分别及联合训练，结果表明其性能可与经典图神经网络相媲美。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to efficiently identify highly boosted jets originating from electroweak bosons (like the Z boson) amidst overwhelming QCD backgrounds (e.g., gluon jets) at high-energy colliders. Classical machine learning methods have shown promise but may face limitations in expressivity or scalability; thus, exploring quantum-enhanced architectures like QGNNs offers a path toward potentially superior discrimination capabilities leveraging quantum computational advantages.
\n\n
动机源于在高能对撞机上高效识别来自电弱玻色子（如Z玻色子）的高度boosted喷注，以应对压倒性的QCD背景（例如胶子喷注）。经典机器学习方法虽已展现潜力，但在表达能力或可扩展性方面可能存在局限；因此，探索如QGNN等量子增强架构，有望利用量子计算优势实现更优的判别性能。

Method: The method employs a two-stage pipeline: first, a convolutional autoencoder performs unsupervised dimensionality reduction on raw jet data, with performance enhanced by injecting noise during training. The compressed latent representations are structured as graphs and fed into a 10-qubit convolutional Quantum Graph Neural Network (QGNN). Both components are trained in two configurations—separately and end-to-end—and benchmarked against a classical graph neural network baseline. No physics-motivated feature engineering is applied; the model relies purely on data-driven representation learning.
\n\n
该方法采用两阶段流程：首先，卷积自编码器对原始喷注数据进行无监督降维，并在训练中通过注入噪声提升性能；压缩后的潜在表示被构造成图结构，并输入到一个10量子比特的卷积量子图神经网络（QGNN）中。两个组件分别以分离训练和端到端联合训练两种配置进行训练，并与经典图神经网络基线进行对比。整个过程未使用任何物理驱动的特征工程，完全依赖数据驱动的表示学习。

Result: The QGNN achieves discrimination performance comparable to that of a classical graph neural network, despite using only ten qubits and no handcrafted features. Notably, the convolutional autoencoder’s robustness improves with added noise, and joint training yields better results than separate training. This demonstrates that even near-term quantum devices can match classical methods in high-energy physics classification tasks when integrated with appropriate classical preprocessing.
\n\n
尽管仅使用10个量子比特且无手工设计特征，QGNN仍实现了与经典图神经网络相当的判别性能。值得注意的是，卷积自编码器在加入噪声后鲁棒性增强，且联合训练优于分离训练。这表明即使在近期量子设备上，只要结合适当的经典预处理，也能在高能物理分类任务中媲美经典方法。

Conclusion: Quantum graph neural networks, when combined with classical dimensionality reduction techniques like noise-augmented autoencoders, show strong potential for jet tagging in collider physics. The results suggest that hybrid quantum-classical architectures can already rival purely classical models, paving the way for future applications of quantum machine learning in high-energy physics despite current hardware limitations.
\n\n
量子图神经网络结合经典降维技术（如加噪自编码器），在对撞机物理的喷注标记任务中展现出强大潜力。结果表明，混合量子-经典架构即便在当前硬件限制下，已可与纯经典模型竞争，为量子机器学习在未来高能物理中的应用铺平道路。

Abstract: We present a quantum enhanced tagger to identify jets with large Lorentz boost at colliders. For the first time, a convolutional quantum graph neural network (QGNN) is designed to discriminate boosted jets arising from hadronic decays of the Z boson, against those produced from gluons with large momentum. The network receives data without any physics-driven refinement, relying solely on the dimensionality reduction. The reduction is performed using a convolutional autoencoder whose performance is improved in the presence of added noise. The latent data are put into a graph format and fed to the QGNN of ten qubits. The autoencoder and the QGNN are trained separately, and simultaneously, and the resulting performances are compared with a classic algorithm based on graph networks. The findings indicate a strong potential of quantum graph networks to reproduce the performance of classical methods.
