### [16] [Quark and gluon tomography of the helium-4 nucleus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18519)
*V. Martínez-Fernández,B. Pire,P. Sznajder,J. Wagner*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents the first 3D tomography of a light nucleus (helium-4) using QCD collinear factorization, by computing elastic form factors and deeply virtual Compton scattering (DVCS) with next-to-leading order (NLO) precision in $α_s$, including kinematic twist corrections and full evolution equations. It reveals distinct transverse spatial distributions of quarks and gluons.
\n\n
本文利用QCD共线因子化方法，通过计算弹性形状因子和深度虚康普顿散射（DVCS），在$α_s$的次领头阶（NLO）精度下（包含运动学扭度修正和完整的演化方程），首次实现了对轻核（氦-4）的三维层析成像，揭示了夸克与胶子在横向空间分布上的显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to extend the tools of nucleon structure studies—specifically generalized parton distributions (GPDs) and 3D tomography—to light nuclei. Helium-4 serves as an ideal benchmark due to its simplicity and experimental accessibility, yet no prior theoretical framework achieved NLO precision with full kinematic and evolution effects for nuclear GPDs.
\n\n
动机是将核子结构研究的工具——特别是广义部分子分布（GPDs）和三维层析成像——拓展至轻核体系。氦-4因其结构简单且实验上可及，是理想的基准系统，但此前尚无理论框架能在包含完整运动学效应和演化效应的情况下，以次领头阶（NLO）精度处理原子核的GPDs。

Method: The authors employ QCD collinear factorization for coherent hard exclusive processes on nuclei. They compute elastic electromagnetic form factors and deeply virtual Compton scattering (DVCS) amplitudes on helium-4 at next-to-leading order in $α_s$. Their calculation incorporates kinematic higher-twist corrections and uses the full renormalization group evolution equations for GPDs. The spatial tomography is obtained via Fourier transform of the GPDs in the impact parameter space.
\n\n
作者采用QCD共线因子化方法处理原子核上的相干硬排他过程。他们在$α_s$的次领头阶（NLO）下计算氦-4的弹性电磁形状因子和深度虚康普顿散射（DVCS）振幅，包含了运动学高扭度修正，并使用GPDs的完整重整化群演化方程。空间层析图像通过在横向坐标（impact parameter）空间中对GPDs进行傅里叶变换获得。

Result: The study achieves unprecedented theoretical precision for a nuclear target, surpassing even typical proton analyses. It provides the first quantitative 3D tomographic images of helium-4, showing that quarks and gluons exhibit different transverse spatial profiles—gluons are more centrally concentrated than quarks.
\n\n
该研究在原子核靶上的理论精度前所未有，甚至超越了典型的质子分析。研究首次给出了氦-4的定量三维层析图像，表明夸克与胶子具有不同的横向空间分布轮廓——胶子比夸克更集中于中心区域。

Conclusion: This work establishes a rigorous QCD-based framework for nuclear tomography, demonstrating that light nuclei like helium-4 can serve as laboratories for probing quark-gluon spatial structure with high precision. The distinct spatial distributions of quarks and gluons underscore the importance of non-perturbative nuclear binding effects in shaping partonic structure.
\n\n
本工作建立了基于QCD的原子核层析严格框架，证明了氦-4等轻核可作为高精度探测夸克-胶子空间结构的实验室。夸克与胶子空间分布的差异凸显了非微扰核束缚效应对部分子结构形成的重要作用。

Abstract: QCD collinear factorization allows coherent hard exclusive reactions to reveal the quark-gluon structure of light nuclei, enabling their 3D tomography. We study elastic form factors and deeply virtual Compton scattering on a helium-4 target, achieving theoretical precision unprecedented even in proton studies. Constraining generalized parton distributions at next-to-leading order in $α_s$, incorporating kinematic twist corrections, and using full evolution equations, we provide the first tomography of a light nucleus, revealing distinct transverse spatial distributions of quarks and gluons.

</details>


### [17] [Final-state rescattering in $\bar{B}^{0}_{(s)}\to Λ^{+}_{c}\barΛ^{-}_{c}$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18574)
*Zhu-Ding Duan,Xiao Huang,Dong-Hao Li,Run-Hui Li,Jian-Peng Wang,Fu-Sheng Yu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper analyzes the baryonic B decays $\bar B^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$ and $\bar B_s^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$ using final-state re-scattering, successfully reproducing the LHCb-measured branching fractions and predicting near-zero direct CP asymmetries and a sizable longitudinal polarization in $\bar B^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$ as a key testable signature.
\n\n
该论文利用末态再散射（final-state re-scattering）框架分析重子型B介子衰变$\bar B^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$和$\bar B_s^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$，成功复现了LHCb测得的分支比，并预言这两种衰变的直接CP不对称性几乎为零，而$\bar B^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$具有显著的纵向极化，可作为未来实验检验该理论框架的关键可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Motivated by the recent LHCb observation of $\bar B_s^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$ and measurements of branching fractions for both $\bar B^0$ and $\bar B_s^0$ decays into $Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$, the authors aim to understand the underlying dynamics—particularly the role of long-distance final-state interactions—which are typically challenging to compute in perturbative QCD but may dominate in baryonic B decays.
\n\n
受LHCb合作组近期对$\bar B_s^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$衰变的首次观测以及对$\bar B^0$和$\bar B_s^0$衰变到$Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$分支比的测量所驱动，作者旨在理解其背后的动力学机制——尤其是长程末态相互作用（long-distance final-state interactions）的作用。这类效应在微扰QCD中难以计算，但在重子型B衰变中可能起主导作用。

Method: The authors employ a final-state re-scattering mechanism, where short-distance tree-level amplitudes generate intermediate meson-baryon states (e.g., $D^{(*)}\Lambda_c$), which then rescatter into the final $Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$ state via nonperturbative strong interactions. This approach effectively incorporates long-distance physics that is otherwise inaccessible in naive factorization or perturbative calculations.
\n\n
作者采用末态再散射机制：短程树图振幅首先产生中间介子-重子态（如$D^{(*)}\Lambda_c$），随后通过非微扰强相互作用再散射至末态$Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$。该方法有效纳入了朴素因子化或微扰计算无法处理的长程物理效应。

Result: The calculated branching fractions for both $\bar B^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$ and $\bar B_s^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$ agree with LHCb data. The predicted direct CP asymmetries are nearly zero ($\mathcal{A}_{CP} \approx 0$) for both modes. Additionally, $\bar B^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$ exhibits a sizable longitudinal polarization fraction ($f_L \sim \mathcal{O}(1)$), while $\bar B_s^0$ decay shows less polarization due to different quark-level dynamics.
\n\n
计算得到的$\bar B^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$和$\bar B_s^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$分支比与LHCb实验数据一致。两种衰变模式的直接CP不对称性均接近于零（$\mathcal{A}_{CP} \approx 0$）。此外，$\bar B^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$展现出显著的纵向极化分数（$f_L \sim \mathcal{O}(1)$），而$\bar B_s^0$衰变因不同的夸克层次动力学导致极化较弱。

Conclusion: Final-state re-scattering provides a viable and quantitatively successful description of baryonic B decays into charmed baryon pairs, highlighting the dominance of long-distance strong interactions. The prediction of near-zero CP violation and large longitudinal polarization offers clear experimental signatures to validate this mechanism in future high-precision measurements at LHCb and Belle II.
\n\n
末态再散射机制为含粲重子对的重子型B衰变提供了可行且定量成功的描述，凸显了长程强相互作用的主导地位。近零CP破坏和大纵向极化的预言为未来LHCb和Belle II的高精度实验提供了明确的检验信号，可用于验证该机制。

Abstract: The LHCb Collaboration has recently reported the first observation of the decay $\bar B_s^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$, along with measurements of the branching fractions for both $\bar B^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$ and $\bar B_s^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$. In this work, we investigate these two decays within the framework of final state re-scattering. Our results show that the predicted branching fractions are consistent with the experimental measurements, indicating the significant role of long-distance final-state interactions in such baryonic B decays. Furthermore, we present predictions for the direct CP asymmetries and the asymmetry parameters. Numerically, both decays exhibit nearly vanishing CP asymmetries, while $\bar B^0\to Λ_c^+\barΛ_c^-$ displays a sizable longitudinal polarization, providing a sensitive observable for testing our theoretical framework in future experimental measurements.

</details>


### [18] [Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) based Likelihood Extraction of Chiral-Odd Compton Form Factors from Deeply Virtual Exclusive Experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18589)
*Saraswati Pandey,Douglas Q. Adams,Simonetta Liuti*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A likelihood-based analysis of deeply virtual meson production data is performed to extract Compton form factors (CFFs) using combined cross-section and asymmetry measurements; Markov chain Monte Carlo methods are used to explore the resulting joint likelihoods.
\n\n
对深度虚介子产生过程的数据进行基于似然的分析，结合截面和不对称性测量提取Compton form factors (CFFs)；采用Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) 方法探索所得联合似然函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to rigorously constrain the Compton form factors (CFFs)—which encode non-perturbative QCD information about the proton’s 3D structure—using the most complete available experimental data from unpolarized deeply virtual exclusive meson production at Jefferson Lab, including both cross-section and beam/target asymmetry observables.
\n\n
动机是利用Jefferson Lab提供的最完整的非极化深度虚专属介子产生实验数据（包括截面和束流/靶不对称性观测量），严格约束Compton form factors (CFFs)——这些量编码了关于质子三维结构的非微扰QCD信息。

Method: The authors construct a joint likelihood function for the CFFs as a function of kinematic variables ($x_B$, $Q^2$, $t$, etc.), incorporating both unpolarized cross-section data and asymmetry measurements. Only three CFFs are constrained at twist-two accuracy. The posterior distributions of the CFFs are sampled using Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) techniques.
\n\n
作者构建了作为运动学变量（$x_B$、$Q^2$、$t$ 等）函数的CFFs联合似然函数，纳入了非极化截面数据和不对称性测量。在twist-two精度下仅有三个CFFs被约束。使用Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) 技术对CFFs的后验分布进行采样。

Result: The joint likelihood analysis successfully constrains three twist-two Compton form factors using combined cross-section and asymmetry data. The MCMC exploration provides statistically robust posterior distributions for these CFFs across the kinematic domain covered by Jefferson Lab experiments.
\n\n
联合似然分析成功利用组合的截面与不对称性数据约束了三个twist-two阶的Compton form factors。MCMC探索在Jefferson Lab实验覆盖的运动学区域内为这些CFFs提供了统计上稳健的后验分布。

Conclusion: Combining cross-section and asymmetry observables in a joint likelihood framework significantly improves the extraction of Compton form factors, offering a more complete and statistically sound determination of proton structure within the QCD factorization formalism.
\n\n
在联合似然框架中结合截面与不对称性观测量显著改进了Compton form factors的提取，在QCD因子化形式体系内实现了对质子结构更完整且统计上更可靠的确定。

Abstract: A likelihood analysis of the observables in deeply virtual exclusive meson production off a proton target is presented. We consider the unpolarized process for which the largest amount of data with all the kinematic dependences are available from corresponding datasets with unpolarized beams and unpolarized as well as longitudinally polarized targets from Jefferson Lab. We employ a method which derives a joint likelihood of the Compton form factors, which parameterize the deeply virtual Compton scattering amplitude in QCD, for each observed combination of the kinematic variables defining the reaction. The twist-two cross-section likelihood constrain only three of the Compton form factors (CFFs). The joint likelihood analysis of cross-section and Asymmetry information adds more sophistication to the Compton form factors (CFFs). The derived likelihoods are explored using Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) methods.

</details>


### [19] [NLO EW and QCD dimension-6 SMEFT results for Higgs and gauge boson decays in POPxf format](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18679)
*Luigi Bellafronte,Sally Dawson,Clara Del Pio,Matthew Forslund,Pier Paolo Giardino*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper computes next-to-leading-order (NLO) QCD and electroweak corrections within the dimension-6 Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT) for a comprehensive set of Higgs, $Z$, and $W$ boson decay processes, as well as the Higgstrahlung cross section at future lepton collider energies. Results are provided in the POPxf format, including the total Higgs width and differential distributions such as $d\\Gamma/dm_{Z^*}$ for off-shell Higgs decays.
\n\n
本文在维度-6标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）框架下，计算了希格斯玻色子、$Z$ 和 $W$ 玻色子衰变过程以及未来轻子对撞机能量下的Higgstrahlung过程的次领头阶（NLO）QCD和电弱修正。结果以POPxf格式提供，包括总希格斯宽度以及离壳希格斯衰变（如 $d\\Gamma/dm_{Z^*}$）的微分分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Precision measurements at future lepton colliders (e.g., ILC, FCC-ee, CEPC) require NLO SMEFT predictions for key electroweak and Higgs observables to constrain beyond-Standard Model physics. Existing calculations often lack complete NLO treatment across multiple channels or convenient formats for experimental use. This work addresses these gaps by providing consistent, high-precision SMEFT predictions for 2- and 4-body Higgs decays, gauge boson decays, electroweak precision observables, and $e^+e^- \\rightarrow ZH$ production.
\n\n
未来轻子对撞机（如ILC、FCC-ee、CEPC）上的高精度测量需要关键电弱与希格斯观测量的NLO SMEFT预言，以约束超出标准模型（BSM）的新物理。现有计算通常缺乏对多个过程的完整NLO处理，或缺少便于实验使用的格式。本文通过为2体与4体希格斯衰变、规范玻色子衰变、电弱精密观测量及 $e^+e^- \\rightarrow ZH$ 过程提供一致且高精度的SMEFT预言，填补了这些空白。

Method: The authors perform a full one-loop (NLO) calculation in the dimension-6 SMEFT, including both QCD and electroweak corrections. They compute amplitudes for all relevant 2- and 4-body Higgs decays, $Z$ and $W$ decays, electroweak precision observables (e.g., $S$, $T$, $U$ parameters), and the Higgstrahlung process $e^+e^- \\rightarrow ZH$ at center-of-mass energies of 240, 365, and 500 GeV. The results are encoded in the machine-readable POPxf format, which allows direct interfacing with experimental analysis frameworks. Special attention is given to the gauge-invariant treatment of off-shell effects in $H \\rightarrow l^+l^- Z^*$ decays, yielding the differential distribution $d\\Gamma/dm_{Z^*}$.
\n\n
作者在维度-6 SMEFT中执行完整的单圈（NLO）计算，包含QCD与电弱修正。他们计算了所有相关2体与4体希格斯衰变、$Z$ 与 $W$ 衰变、电弱精密观测量（如 $S$、$T$、$U$ 参数）以及质心能量为240、365和500 GeV下的Higgstrahlung过程 $e^+e^- \\rightarrow ZH$ 的振幅。结果以机器可读的POPxf格式编码，可直接与实验分析框架对接。特别关注了 $H \\rightarrow l^+l^- Z^*$ 衰变中离壳效应的规范不变处理，从而得到微分分布 $d\\Gamma/dm_{Z^*}$。

Result: The paper provides NLO SMEFT predictions for: (i) total and partial widths of Higgs decays including all dimension-6 operators; (ii) $Z$ and $W$ decay observables; (iii) electroweak precision observables; and (iv) Higgstrahlung cross sections at $\\sqrt{s} = 240$, 365, and 500 GeV. Crucially, the total Higgs width is computed consistently at NLO in SMEFT, enabling accurate branching ratio predictions. Additionally, the first NLO SMEFT result for the differential spectrum $d\\Gamma/dm_{Z^*}$ in $H \\rightarrow 4\\ell$ via off-shell $Z^*$ is presented.
\n\n
本文提供了以下NLO SMEFT预言：(i) 包含所有维度-6算符的希格斯总宽度与部分宽度；(ii) $Z$ 与 $W$ 衰变观测量；(iii) 电弱精密观测量；(iv) 在 $\\sqrt{s} = 240$、365 和 500 GeV 下的Higgstrahlung截面。关键的是，希格斯总宽度在SMEFT中被一致地计算至NLO，从而实现精确的分支比预言。此外，本文首次给出了通过离壳 $Z^*$ 的 $H \\rightarrow 4\\ell$ 过程中微分谱 $d\\Gamma/dm_{Z^*}$ 的NLO SMEFT结果。

Conclusion: This work delivers a complete and publicly usable NLO SMEFT dataset for Higgs and electroweak physics at future lepton colliders. By providing results in the POPxf format and including previously unavailable differential distributions and consistent total widths, it significantly enhances the capability of experimental collaborations to perform global SMEFT fits and probe new physics at the precision frontier.
\n\n
本工作为未来轻子对撞机上的希格斯与电弱物理提供了一套完整且公开可用的NLO SMEFT数据集。通过以POPxf格式提供结果，并包含此前不可得的微分分布与一致的总宽度，显著增强了实验合作组进行全局SMEFT拟合并在精度前沿探测新物理的能力。

Abstract: We present next-to-leading-order (NLO) QCD and electroweak (EW) results using the dimension-6 SMEFT for all 2- and 4- body Higgs decays, for $Z$ and $W$ decays along with the corresponding EW precision observables, and for the Higgstrahlung process $e^+e^-\rightarrow ZH$ at $\sqrt{s}=240$, $365$ and $500$ GeV. The results are presented in the POPxf format for ease of use in experimental and phenomenological studies. Of particular utility is the total Higgs width, including all dimension-6 contributions at NLO. In addition, we present the differential distributions $dΓ/dm_{Z*}$ for $H\rightarrow l^+l^- Z^*, Z^*\rightarrow l^+l^-$ at NLO in the SMEFT.

### [20] [Sensitivity of MAGIX@MESA to BSM effects via Bethe-Heitler pair production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18718)
*Aleksandr Pustyntsev,Marc Vanderhaeghen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates the sensitivity of the MAGIX experiment at MESA to light Beyond the Standard Model (BSM) mediators with masses between a few MeV and 100 MeV, using 55 MeV and 105 MeV electron beams on a $^{181}\text{Ta}$ target. It shows that by leveraging the Bethe-Heitler process and optimizing the double-spectrometer kinematics, MAGIX can probe mediator-electron couplings as small as $\mathcal{O}(10^{-4})$, providing strong constraints on sub-GeV dark sector models.
\n\n
本文研究了MESA装置上MAGIX实验对质量在几MeV至100 MeV范围内的轻质量Beyond the Standard Model (BSM)媒介粒子的灵敏度，利用55 MeV和105 MeV电子束轰击$^{181}\\text{Ta}$靶。通过Bethe-Heitler过程并优化双谱仪的非对称运动学接受度，MAGIX可探测小至$\\mathcal{O}(10^{-4})$量级的媒介粒子-电子耦合，从而对sub-GeV暗区模型提供强有力限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to explore light BSM mediators in the MeV–100 MeV mass window—a region poorly constrained by existing experiments but theoretically well-motivated for dark matter and dark sector scenarios. The MAGIX experiment, with its high-intensity electron beams and specialized spectrometer design, offers a unique opportunity to fill this gap by probing extremely weak couplings between electrons and new light mediators.
\n\n
动机源于探索MeV–100 MeV质量窗口内轻质量BSM媒介粒子的需求——该区域现有实验约束较弱，但在暗物质和dark sector理论中具有重要动机。MAGIX实验凭借其高强度电子束和专用谱仪设计，为探测电子与新轻媒介粒子之间极弱耦合提供了独特机会，填补当前实验空白。

Method: The authors simulate mediator production via the Bethe-Heitler process, where high-energy electrons scatter off a heavy $^{181}\text{Ta}$ nucleus and radiate scalar, pseudoscalar, vector, or axial vector mediators. They model the double-arm spectrometer acceptance of MAGIX and optimize its asymmetric kinematic configuration to maximize signal-to-background discrimination. Sensitivity projections are derived based on expected beam intensities, detector resolution, and background suppression capabilities.
\n\n
作者通过Bethe-Heitler过程模拟媒介粒子产生：高能电子在重核$^{181}\\text{Ta}$上散射并辐射标量、赝标量、矢量或轴矢量媒介粒子。他们建模了MAGIX双臂谱仪的接受度，并优化其非对称运动学构型以最大化信噪比。灵敏度预测基于预期束流强度、探测器分辨率及本底抑制能力得出。

Result: MAGIX is projected to reach mediator-electron coupling sensitivities of $\mathcal{O}(10^{-4})$ across the few–100 MeV mass range for all four mediator types (scalar, pseudoscalar, vector, axial vector). This performance rivals or exceeds that of current fixed-target and beam-dump experiments in the sub-GeV regime, particularly for vector and axial vector mediators.
\n\n
MAGIX预计在几MeV至100 MeV质量范围内，对所有四类媒介粒子（标量、赝标量、矢量、轴矢量）均可达到$\\mathcal{O}(10^{-4})$量级的媒介粒子-电子耦合灵敏度。该性能在sub-GeV能区与现有固定靶和束流dump实验相当甚至更优，尤其对矢量和轴矢量媒介粒子更具竞争力。

Conclusion: The MAGIX experiment at MESA represents a powerful near-future probe of light BSM physics in the MeV–100 MeV mass range. By exploiting precision electron scattering and optimized spectrometer kinematics, it can significantly advance our understanding of weakly coupled dark sectors and complement other experimental approaches targeting the same parameter space.
\n\n
MESA上的MAGIX实验是探测MeV–100 MeV质量范围内轻质量BSM物理的强有力近未来手段。通过利用高精度电子散射和优化的谱仪运动学，它可显著推进我们对弱耦合dark sector的理解，并与其他探索相同参数空间的实验方法形成互补。

Abstract: We explore the sensitivity of the upcoming MAGIX experiment at the MESA facility to light Beyond the Standard Model (BSM) mediators in the few to hundred MeV mass range. Utilizing high-intensity electron beams of 55 MeV and 105 MeV on a heavy $^{181}\text{Ta}$ target, we investigate the production of scalar, pseudoscalar, vector, and axial vector mediators via the Bethe-Heitler process. By optimizing the asymmetric kinematic acceptance of the double-spectrometer setup to enhance the signal over background ratio, we demonstrate that MAGIX can probe mediator-electron couplings down to $\mathcal{O}(10^{-4})$, offering a competitive probe of the dark sector in the sub-GeV mass range.

### [21] [Strong-coupling results in (non-)conformal $\mathcal{N}=2$ theories with fundamental flavors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16521)
*M. Billo,A. Lerda,A. Testa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper investigates 4D $\mathcal{N}=2$ SU($N$) gauge theories with two massless antisymmetric hypermultiplets and $0 \leq N_f \leq 4$ fundamental flavors. Using supersymmetric localization on $S^4$, the authors compute the free energy and $\frac{1}{2}$-BPS Wilson loop in the large-$N$ limit. They resum non-planar corrections at strong 't Hooft coupling $λ$ into an effective coupling $\widetilde{λ}$, yielding explicit planar results for non-conformal cases ($N_f < 4$) and suggesting a refined AdS/CFT dictionary where $\widetilde{λ}$ replaces $λ$ as the bulk string coupling in the superconformal case ($N_f = 4$).
\n\n
本文研究了具有两个无质量反对称超多重态和 $0 \leq N_f \leq 4$ 个基础味的四维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ SU($N$) 规范理论。作者利用 $S^4$ 上的超对称局域化方法，在大 $N$ 极限下计算了自由能和 $\frac{1}{2}$-BPS 圆形 Wilson loop。他们将强 ’t Hooft 耦合 $λ$ 下的非平面修正级数重求和为一个有效耦合 $\widetilde{λ}$，从而在非共形情形（$N_f < 4$）下首次获得了显式的平面极限结果，并在超共形情形（$N_f = 4$）下提出了一种改进的 AdS/CFT 对应字典，其中 $\widetilde{λ}$ 取代 $λ$ 成为体弦耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore strongly coupled regimes of 4D $\mathcal{N}=2$ gauge theories that are either asymptotically free or superconformal, using exact non-perturbative tools. Supersymmetric localization provides access to protected observables beyond perturbation theory, especially in the large-$N$ and strong coupling limits where traditional methods fail. A key goal is to understand how non-planar corrections organize themselves and whether they can be captured by a redefined coupling, which may have implications for holography.
\n\n
动机在于利用精确的非微扰工具探索四维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ 规范理论在强耦合区域的行为——这些理论要么是渐近自由的，要么是超共形的。超对称局域化方法能够获得受保护观测量的精确结果，特别是在传统方法失效的大 $N$ 和强耦合极限下。核心目标之一是理解非平面修正如何组织自身，以及是否能通过一个重新定义的有效耦合来刻画它们，这对全息对偶（holography）可能具有重要意义。

Method: The authors employ supersymmetric localization on the four-sphere $S^4$, which reduces the path integral for protected observables (like the partition function and Wilson loops) to a finite-dimensional matrix model. They analyze this matrix model in the large-$N$ limit using saddle-point techniques and perform a strong-coupling expansion in the 't Hooft coupling $λ = g_{\text{YM}}^2 N$. Crucially, they identify that the infinite series of $1/N$ (non-planar) corrections at large $λ$ can be resummed into a new effective coupling $\widetilde{λ}$, defined implicitly through an equation involving $λ$ and $N_f$.
\n\n
作者采用四维球面 $S^4$ 上的超对称局域化方法，将受保护观测量（如配分函数和 Wilson loop）的路径积分简化为有限维矩阵模型。他们在大 $N$ 极限下使用鞍点法分析该矩阵模型，并在 ’t Hooft 耦合 $λ = g_{\text{YM}}^2 N$ 的强耦合展开中进行计算。关键步骤在于识别出：在大 $λ$ 下，无穷级数的 $1/N$（非平面）修正可以重求和为一个新的有效耦合 $\widetilde{λ}$，该耦合通过一个包含 $λ$ 和 $N_f$ 的隐式方程定义。

Result: For all $0 \leq N_f \leq 4$, the large-$N$ free energy $F$ and the $\frac{1}{2}$-BPS Wilson loop expectation value $\langle W \rangle$ admit expansions in powers of $1/\widetilde{λ}^{1/2}$ rather than $1/λ^{1/2}$. In the non-conformal cases ($N_f < 4$), this yields the first explicit strong-coupling planar results from localization. In the superconformal case ($N_f = 4$), the result implies that the natural parameter controlling the $1/N$ expansion in the dual AdS$_5 \times S^5$ string theory is $\widetilde{λ}$, not the standard ’t Hooft coupling $λ$, suggesting a refinement of the AdS/CFT dictionary.
\n\n
对于所有 $0 \leq N_f \leq 4$，大 $N$ 自由能 $F$ 和 $\frac{1}{2}$-BPS Wilson loop 期望值 $\langle W \rangle$ 的展开是以 $1/\widetilde{λ}^{1/2}$ 的幂次进行的，而非 $1/λ^{1/2}$。在非共形情形（$N_f < 4$）下，这给出了首个来自局域化的显式强耦合平面极限结果。在超共形情形（$N_f = 4$）下，结果表明对偶的 AdS$_5 \times S^5$ 弦理论中控制 $1/N$ 展开的自然参数是 $\widetilde{λ}$ 而非标准的 ’t Hooft 耦合 $λ$，暗示了 AdS/CFT 字典的改进。

Conclusion: The resummation of non-planar corrections into an effective coupling $\widetilde{λ}$ reveals a hidden simplicity in the large-$N$, strong-coupling dynamics of these $\mathcal{N}=2$ theories. This not only provides new analytic control over asymptotically free gauge theories via localization but also indicates that the standard identification of the bulk string coupling with the boundary ’t Hooft coupling in AdS/CFT may need modification for non-maximally supersymmetric theories, with $\widetilde{λ}$ being the more appropriate holographic parameter.
\n\n
将非平面修正重求和为有效耦合 $\widetilde{λ}$ 揭示了这些 $\mathcal{N}=2$ 理论在大 $N$、强耦合动力学中的隐藏简洁性。这不仅通过局域化方法为渐近自由规范理论提供了新的解析控制手段，还表明在 AdS/CFT 中，体弦耦合与边界 ’t Hooft 耦合的标准对应关系在非极大超对称理论中可能需要修正，而 $\widetilde{λ}$ 才是更合适的全息参数。

Abstract: We study a class of four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=2$ SU($N$) gauge theories with two massless hypermultiplets in the rank-two antisymmetric representation and $0\leq N_f\leq 4$ fundamental flavors. These theories are superconformal for $N_f=4$ and asymptotically free otherwise. Supersymmetric localization on the four-sphere applies in both cases and leads to matrix-model representations for a broad class of protected observables. Within this framework, we compute the free energy and the expectation value of the $\frac{1}{2}$-BPS circular Wilson loop in the large-$N$ limit. For any $N_f$, we show that the infinite series of non-planar corrections at large 't Hooft coupling $λ$ can be resummed in terms of an effective coupling $\widetildeλ$. In the non-conformal window ($0\leq N_f<4$), this provides a first example in which localization leads to explicit results in the planar limit at strong 't Hooft coupling. In the superconformal case ($N_f=4$), the large-$N$ expansion in $\widetildeλ$ suggests a refined AdS/CFT dictionary in which $\widetildeλ$, rather than $λ$, plays the role of the bulk string coupling.

</details>


### [22] [Nonlinear response of the chiral magnetic effect in the D3/D7 holographic model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16931)
*Masataka Matsumoto,Mirmani Mirjalali,Ali Vahedi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper studies the nonlinear chiral magnetic current in a holographic D3/D7 brane model beyond the linear response regime, revealing a multi-valued current–magnetic field relation near the phase boundary between insulating and CME phases, and demonstrating cooperative stabilization of the insulating phase by axial chemical potential and magnetic field.
\n\n
本文在全息D3/D7膜模型中研究了手征磁电流在线性响应之外的非线性行为，揭示了在绝缘相与CME相之间的相边界附近电流与磁场关系的多值性，并证明了轴向化学势与外磁场协同稳定绝缘相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the nonlinear regime of the chiral magnetic effect (CME), which is typically studied only in linear response, and to explore how the interplay between axial chemical potential $\\mu_5$ and external magnetic field $B$ governs the phase structure and stability in strongly coupled gauge theories via gauge/gravity duality.
\n\n
动机在于理解手征磁效应（CME）的非线性区域——该效应通常仅在线性响应框架下研究——并探索轴向化学势 $\\mu_5$ 与外磁场 $B$ 如何通过规范/引力对偶共同决定强耦合规范理论中的相结构与稳定性。

Method: The authors employ the D3/D7 probe brane holographic setup, where rotating D7-branes encode an axial chemical potential. They solve the DBI action for the D7-brane embedding in the presence of both $B$ and $\\mu_5$, analyze equilibrium configurations near the insulator–CME phase boundary, and examine dynamical stability via small fluctuations around the insulating solution.
\n\n
作者采用D3/D7探针膜全息模型，其中旋转的D7膜对应于引入轴向化学势。他们在同时存在 $B$ 和 $\\mu_5$ 的情况下求解D7膜的DBI作用量，分析绝缘相与CME相边界附近的平衡构型，并通过围绕绝缘解的小扰动研究系统的动力学稳定性。

Result: Near the phase transition, the chiral magnetic current $J \\propto B$ becomes nonlinear and multi-valued as a function of $B$, signaling a breakdown of linear response. Additionally, the insulating phase—normally unstable under $B$ alone—is dynamically stabilized when both $B$ and $\\mu_5$ are present, indicating cooperative stabilization.
\n\n
在相变点附近，手征磁电流 $J \\propto B$ 随 $B$ 呈现非线性且多值依赖关系，表明线性响应失效。此外，原本仅在外磁场 $B$ 下不稳定的绝缘相，在同时存在 $B$ 和 $\\mu_5$ 时变得动力学稳定，显示出协同稳定效应。

Conclusion: The work reveals that nonlinear chiral transport in holographic models exhibits rich structure near phase boundaries, with axial chemical potential and magnetic field jointly shaping both thermodynamic phases and dynamical stability—offering new insights into non-equilibrium and strong-coupling aspects of the CME.
\n\n
该工作揭示了全息模型中的非线性手征输运在相边界附近具有丰富结构，轴向化学势与磁场共同塑造热力学相和动力学稳定性，为理解CME的非平衡与强耦合特性提供了新视角。

Abstract: We investigate the nonlinear response of the chiral magnetic current to an external magnetic field in a holographic setup. Using the D3/D7 brane system, where the chiral magnetic effect (CME) can be realized by considering rotating probe D7-branes, corresponding to introducing an axial chemical potential, we analyze the current-magnetic field relation beyond the linear regime. Focusing on the vicinity of the phase boundary between the insulating phase and the CME phase, we find that the chiral magnetic current exhibits a multi-valued dependence on the magnetic field, indicating a highly nonlinear response characteristic of this model. We further study the dynamical stability of the insulating phase near the transition point, and show that the presence of both an axial chemical potential and an external magnetic field cooperatively stabilize the system. Our results clarify the interplay between the axial chemical potential and the magnetic field in determining the phase structure and stability of the system, and reveal new nonlinear aspects of chiral transport in holographic gauge theories.

### [23] [Five legs @ three loops: slightly off-shell dual conformal integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17057)
*Andrei V. Belitsky,Leonid V. Bork,Roman N. Lee,Andrei I. Onishchenko,Vladimir A. Smirnov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper computes three-loop master integrals for the five-point amplitude in $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM on a special Coulomb branch, using dual conformal invariance (DCI)-preserving regularization. A novel method factors out DCI cross-ratio dependence per region, simplifying integrals via successive limits of vanishing external invariants. For 79 of 82 regions of the hardest integral $\mathcal{I}_5^{(3)}$, analytic results are obtained; the remaining 3 are evaluated via IBP reduction in parametric form and HyperInt.
\n\n
本文计算了特殊Coulomb分支上$\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM理论中五点振幅的三圈主积分，采用保持对偶共形不变性（DCI）的正规化方法。文中提出一种新方法，将每个区域对DCI交叉比的依赖因子化出来，并通过依次取外动量不变量趋于零的极限来简化剩余积分。对于最复杂的积分$\mathcal{I}_5^{(3)}$所涉及的82个区域中的79个，获得了解析结果；其余3个区域则通过参数表示下的IBP约化并利用HyperInt进行数值评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to compute higher-loop scattering amplitudes in maximally supersymmetric Yang–Mills theory ($\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM), particularly on the Coulomb branch where infrared divergences are regulated while preserving dual conformal invariance (DCI). Understanding the structure of multi-loop, multi-leg amplitudes is crucial for exploring hidden symmetries, integrability, and the connection to Wilson loops and correlation functions in the AdS/CFT correspondence.
\n\n
动机源于需要计算最大超对称Yang–Mills理论（$\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM）中更高圈阶的散射振幅，尤其是在Coulomb分支上——该设定可正规化红外发散同时保持对偶共形不变性（DCI）。理解多圈、多腿振幅的结构对于探索隐藏对称性、可积性以及AdS/CFT对偶中与Wilson圈和关联函数的联系至关重要。

Method: The authors employ a DCI-preserving regularization scheme as in Ref. [JHEP 12 (2025) 107]. They introduce a new technique to factorize the dependence on DCI cross ratios $u_{ij} = \\frac{x_{ij+1}^2 x_{i+1 j}^2}{x_{ij}^2 x_{i+1 j+1}^2}$ from each integration region. After factorization, they take successive limits where external invariants $x_{ij}^2 \\to 0$, drastically simplifying the integrands. For regions resistant to this approach (3 out of 82), they perform integration-by-parts (IBP) reduction in Feynman parametric representation and evaluate the resulting finite integrals using the HyperInt package, which handles hyperlogarithms over rational alphabets.
\n\n
作者采用参考文献[JHEP 12 (2025) 107]中的DCI保持正规化方案。他们提出一种新技术，将每个积分区域对DCI交叉比$u_{ij} = \\frac{x_{ij+1}^2 x_{i+1 j}^2}{x_{ij}^2 x_{i+1 j+1}^2}$的依赖因子化分离。因子化后，通过依次取外不变量$x_{ij}^2 \\to 0$的极限，显著简化被积函数。对于无法通过此方法处理的区域（82个中的3个），他们在Feynman参数表示下执行integration-by-parts（IBP）约化，并利用HyperInt软件包计算所得的有限积分——该工具可处理有理字母表上的hyperlogarithm函数。

Result: Analytic expressions are obtained for 79 out of 82 contributing regions of the most complex three-loop pentagon integral $\mathcal{I}_5^{(3)}$. The remaining three regions are computed numerically (or symbolically via HyperInt) after IBP reduction, confirming the feasibility of the combined strategy. The factorization method significantly reduces computational complexity by decoupling kinematic dependence from loop integration.
\n\n
对最复杂的三圈五边形积分$\mathcal{I}_5^{(3)}$所涉及的82个区域中的79个获得了解析表达式。其余三个区域在IBP约化后通过HyperInt进行数值（或符号）计算，验证了该组合策略的可行性。所提出的因子化方法通过将运动学依赖与圈积分解耦，显著降低了计算复杂度。

Conclusion: The paper demonstrates an efficient hybrid approach—combining analytic simplifications via DCI-preserving limits with modern symbolic integration tools—for computing previously inaccessible three-loop five-point master integrals in $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM. This paves the way for complete amplitude calculations at three loops and provides insights into the algebraic structure of Feynman integrals with dual conformal symmetry.
\n\n
本文展示了一种高效混合方法——结合基于DCI保持极限的解析简化与现代符号积分工具——用于计算$\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM中此前难以处理的三圈五点主积分。这为完成三圈振幅的完整计算铺平了道路，并深化了对具有对偶共形对称性的Feynman积分代数结构的理解。

Abstract: We calculate the three-loop master integrals contributing to the three-loop five-point amplitude on the special Coulomb branch of $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM theory. For the genuine pentagon integrals, we follow the approach of Ref. [JHEP 12 (2025) 107], which includes a regularization preserving dual conformal invariance (DCI). As a new ingredient, we introduce a simple method, allowing to factor out the dependence on the DCI cross ratios from the contribution of each region. The remaining integrals are then essentially simplified by taking successive limits of vanishing external invariants. For 3 out of 82 regions contributing to the most complicated integral $\mathcal{I}_5^{(3)}$ we were not able to perform the integration even after these simplifications. For these three regions, we perform the integration-by-parts (IBP) reduction in parametric representation and evaluate the resulting locally finite integrals using HyperInt.

</details>


### [24] [Covariant extrinsic curvature expansion of the nonlocal effective action for a massless scalar field on a manifold with boundary](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17124)
*A. Boasso,C. D. Fosco,B. C. Guntsche,F. D. Mazzitelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper computes the nonlocal effective action for a massless scalar field on a flat bulk with a curved boundary, using a heat-kernel method to obtain a covariant expansion quadratic in extrinsic curvature. This generalizes prior Monge-patch results to arbitrary boundaries and is applied to compute particle production from oscillating deformed rings (2+1D) and spheres (3+1D).
\n\n
本文利用热核方法计算了平直体空间中具有弯曲边界的无质量标量场的非局域有效作用量，得到了外曲率张量二次阶的协变展开式。该结果将先前仅适用于Monge-patch嵌入的情形推广至任意边界，并应用于计算2+1维振荡形变环和3+1维振荡形变球的粒子产生率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous studies of boundary-induced quantum effects relied on Monge-patch parameterizations, which restrict consideration to boundaries that can be globally expressed as single-valued height functions. The authors aim to develop a fully covariant geometric framework that applies to general curved boundaries without such restrictions, enabling broader applications in quantum field theory with boundaries.
\n\n
先前关于边界诱导量子效应的研究依赖于Monge-patch参数化，这限制了只能考虑可全局表示为单值高度函数的边界。作者旨在构建一个完全协变的几何框架，适用于无需此类限制的一般弯曲边界，从而拓展边界量子场论的应用范围。

Method: The authors employ a heat-kernel regularization technique to compute the one-loop effective action of a massless scalar field with Dirichlet boundary conditions on a flat manifold bounded by a curved hypersurface. They perform a covariant derivative expansion, retaining terms up to quadratic order in the extrinsic curvature $K_{ab}$, under the assumption that spatial gradients of $K_{ab}$ dominate over intrinsic curvature nonlinearities. The formalism is manifestly geometric and does not require a Monge gauge.
\n\n
作者采用热核正则化技术，计算在平直流形上、具有弯曲超曲面边界的无质量标量场（满足Dirichlet边界条件）的单圈有效作用量。他们在协变导数展开中保留外曲率张量 $K_{ab}$ 的二次项，假设 $K_{ab}$ 的空间梯度主导于内禀曲率的非线性效应。该形式体系是显式几何的，无需Monge规范。

Result: The nonlocal effective action is expressed as a covariant integral over the boundary involving operators like $K \\frac{1}{\\sqrt{-\\partial_\\parallel^2}} K$, where $\\partial_\\parallel$ denotes tangential derivatives. This reproduces known Monge-patch results as a special case and extends them to topologically nontrivial or multi-valued boundaries. Applied to dynamical boundaries, the formalism yields explicit particle-creation rates for an oscillating deformed ring in $2+1$ dimensions and a deformed sphere in $3+1$ dimensions.
\n\n
非局域有效作用量被表示为边界上的协变积分，包含如 $K \\frac{1}{\\sqrt{-\\partial_\\parallel^2}} K$ 的算符，其中 $\\partial_\\parallel$ 表示切向导数。该结果在特殊情形下复现了已知的Monge-patch结果，并推广至拓扑非平凡或多值边界。将此形式体系应用于动力学边界，得到了2+1维振荡形变环和3+1维形变球的显式粒子产生率。

Conclusion: The work establishes a general, covariant framework for computing quantum boundary effects beyond the Monge-patch approximation, valid in the gradient-dominated regime of extrinsic curvature. It opens the door to studying quantum vacuum phenomena—such as particle creation and Casimir-like forces—for arbitrarily shaped, time-dependent boundaries in any dimension.
\n\n
本工作建立了一个超越Monge-patch近似的通用协变框架，用于计算外曲率梯度主导区域中的量子边界效应。它为研究任意形状、含时边界下的量子真空现象（如粒子产生和类Casimir力）开辟了道路。

Abstract: We study the nonlocal effective action of a massless scalar field defined on a flat manifold with a curved boundary. Using a heat-kernel approach, we derive a covariant expansion of the nonlocal contribution to quadratic order in the extrinsic curvature tensor. Our construction provides a geometric framework that both reproduces earlier results obtained for Monge-patch embeddings and extends them to more general surfaces that need not admit a global Monge-patch description. The expansion is valid in the regime where gradients of the extrinsic curvature dominate over nonlinear curvature effects. As an application, we compute the particle-creation rate for an oscillating deformed ring in $2+1$ dimensions and an oscillating deformed sphere in $3+1$ dimensions.

</details>


### [25] [Emergent AdS Geometry and Black Hole Thermodynamics from Functional Renormalization Group](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17209)
*Ki-Seok Kim*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper constructs a non-perturbative holographic dual of the $O(N)$ vector model in $d$-dimensional Euclidean space using the functional renormalization group (FRG), identifying the RG scale as a radial bulk coordinate. It demonstrates that the emergent geometry is a regular $\text{AdS}_{d+1}$ spacetime at criticality, proves exact matching of Hawking and boundary temperatures by removing conical singularities, and derives the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy law from first principles via the First Law of Black Hole Thermodynamics.
\n\n
本文利用泛函重整化群（FRG）为 $d$ 维欧几里得空间中的 $O(N)$ 矢量模型构建了一个非微扰全息对偶，将 RG 标度识别为体时空的径向坐标。文章证明在临界点处涌现几何为无奇点的正则 $\text{AdS}_{d+1}$ 时空，通过消除锥形奇点严格证明了霍金温度与边界场论温度精确一致，并基于黑洞热力学第一定律从第一性原理推导出贝肯斯坦-霍金熵公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to establish a rigorous, non-perturbative realization of the holographic principle beyond the large-$N$ or strong-coupling limits typically assumed in AdS/CFT. The $O(N)$ vector model serves as a tractable yet nontrivial quantum field theory where such a bottom-up holographic emergence can be explicitly constructed within the FRG framework, bridging Wilsonian RG flow with gravitational dynamics in one higher dimension.
\n\n
动机源于在 AdS/CFT 中通常假设的大 $N$ 或强耦合极限之外，建立一个严格且非微扰的全息原理实现。$O(N)$ 矢量模型作为一个可处理但非平凡的量子场论，可在泛函重整化群（FRG）框架内显式构建这种自下而上的全息涌现，从而将威尔逊 RG 流与高一维的引力动力学联系起来。

Method: The authors employ the functional renormalization group (FRG) to implement continuous Wilsonian RG transformations on the $O(N)$ vector model. The RG scale $k$ is promoted to a radial coordinate in an emergent $(d+1)$-dimensional bulk. A bidirectional holographic dictionary is formulated by mapping non-perturbative FRG flow equations to gravitational constraints in the bulk, yielding warping factors of the metric. Regularity conditions at the thermal horizon are imposed to eliminate conical deficits, enabling a precise identification of temperature. Thermodynamic consistency is then verified via the First Law of Black Hole Thermodynamics.
\n\n
作者采用泛函重整化群（FRG）对 $O(N)$ 矢量模型实施连续的威尔逊 RG 变换，将 RG 标度 $k$ 提升为涌现 $(d+1)$ 维体时空中的径向坐标。通过将非微扰 FRG 流方程映射到体时空中的引力约束，构建双向全息字典，从而得到度规的弯曲因子。通过对热视界施加正则性条件以消除锥形亏格，实现温度的精确匹配。最后通过黑洞热力学第一定律验证热力学一致性。

Result: At the massless critical point, the emergent bulk geometry is shown to be a smooth, singularity-free $\text{AdS}_{d+1}$ spacetime satisfying all local energy conditions. The conical singularity at the Euclidean thermal horizon is removed by tuning the periodicity of imaginary time, leading to the exact equality $T_H = T$. Furthermore, the near-horizon thermodynamic potentials obey $dE = T dS$, and the entropy is derived as $S_{\text{horizon}} = \frac{N}{4} \mathcal{A}$, reproducing the Bekenstein-Hawking area law from first principles without assuming black hole microstates.
\n\n
在无质量临界点处，涌现体几何被证明是一个光滑、无奇点的 $\text{AdS}_{d+1}$ 时空，满足所有局域能量条件。通过调节虚时间周期性消除欧几里得热视界处的锥形奇点，得到精确关系 $T_H = T$。此外，近视界热力学势满足 $dE = T dS$，并推导出熵 $S_{\text{horizon}} = \frac{N}{4} \mathcal{A}$，从第一性原理复现了贝肯斯坦-霍金面积律，无需预设黑洞微观态。

Conclusion: This work provides a first-principles, non-perturbative derivation of emergent holography for the $O(N)$ vector model via FRG, demonstrating that AdS geometry, black hole thermodynamics, and the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy law can all arise intrinsically from RG flow without invoking string theory or supersymmetry. It establishes FRG as a powerful framework for bottom-up holography grounded in quantum field theory.
\n\n
本工作通过 FRG 为 $O(N)$ 矢量模型提供了首个基于第一性原理的非微扰全息涌现推导，表明 AdS 几何、黑洞热力学及贝肯斯坦-霍金熵律均可内生于 RG 流，无需引入弦论或超对称。该研究确立了 FRG 作为植根于量子场论的自下而上全息方法的强大框架。

Abstract: We present a non-perturbative holographic dual description for the \(O(N)\) vector model in \(d\)-dimensional Euclidean space within the functional renormalization group (FRG) framework. By continuously iterating Wilsonian RG transformations, the extra-dimensional scale coordinate is identified as the radial direction of an emergent \((d+1)\)-dimensional bulk spacetime. We construct a bidirectional holographic dictionary that maps non-perturbative fluctuations directly into the emergent bulk metric warping factors. Under the massless critical configuration, the emergent gravitational vacuum spontaneously organizes into a stable, regular Anti-de Sitter (\(\text{AdS}_{d+1}\)) geometry without coordinate singularities, satisfying all foundational local energy conditions. Near the thermal horizon, by systematically eliminating the conical deficit singularity, we rigorously prove that the semiclassical Hawking temperature identically matches the boundary field theory temperature (\(T_H \equiv T\)). Finally, we show that the near-horizon thermodynamic potentials exactly satisfy the First Law of Black Hole Thermodynamics, spontaneously generating the Bekenstein-Hawking area law (\(S_{\text{horizon}} = \frac{N}{4}\mathcal{A}\)) from a first-principles, bottom-up derivation.

### [26] [Functional Renormalization Group as a Ricci Flow: An $\mathcal{F}$-Entropy Perspective on Information Metric Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17215)
*Ki-Seok Kim*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper demonstrates that the Functional Renormalization Group (FRG) is equivalent to a diffeomorphism-modified Ricci flow on the information manifold of coupling constants. By recasting the Polchinski equation as an infinite-dimensional Fokker-Planck equation, the authors identify the Fisher information metric’s evolution as a Riemannian gradient flow driven by a field-theoretic $\mathcal{F}$-entropy functional—analogous to Perelman’s $\mathcal{F}$-functional in Ricci flow theory. The log of the effective action acts as a scalar potential generating necessary diffeomorphisms, and RG flow smooths the information geometry toward a Ricci soliton fixed point.
\n\n
本文证明了泛函重整化群（Functional Renormalization Group, FRG）等价于耦合常数信息流形上经微分同胚修正的Ricci流。通过将Polchinski方程重构为无穷维Fokker-Planck方程，作者指出Fisher信息度规的演化是由一个场论版本的$\mathcal{F}$-熵泛函驱动的黎曼梯度流——该泛函是Perelman在Ricci流理论中提出的$\mathcal{F}$-泛函的无穷维类比。有效作用量的对数作为标量势$Φ$生成必要的微分同胚，而重整化群流通过平滑信息几何结构，驱使系统趋向Ricci孤子不动点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the desire to uncover deep geometric structures underlying renormalization group (RG) flows in quantum field theory (QFT). Traditional RG formulations lack a manifestly geometric interpretation in terms of information geometry or differential geometry. Inspired by Perelman’s breakthrough in solving the Poincaré conjecture via Ricci flow with entropy functionals, the authors aim to establish a rigorous connection between FRG, information geometry (via the Fisher metric), and geometric flows, thereby providing new tools to analyze RG fixed point stability and universality classes.
\n\n
动机源于揭示量子场论（QFT）中重整化群（RG）流背后深层几何结构的愿望。传统RG表述缺乏在信息几何或微分几何框架下的显式几何诠释。受Perelman借助带有熵泛函的Ricci流解决庞加莱猜想的启发，作者旨在建立泛函重整化群（FRG）、信息几何（通过Fisher度规）与几何流之间的严格联系，从而为分析RG不动点稳定性与普适类提供新工具。

Method: The authors reformulate the Polchinski exact RG equation as an infinite-dimensional Fokker-Planck equation governing the probability distribution over field configurations. They define a field-theoretic $\mathcal{F}$-entropy functional:  
$$
\mathcal{F} = \int \mathcal{D}\phi\, P[\phi] \left( \Phi[\phi] + |\nabla \ln P[\phi]|^2 \right),
$$
where $P[\phi]$ is the field distribution and $\Phi = -\ln Z_{\text{eff}}$ is derived from the effective action. They show that the scale-dependent evolution of the Fisher information metric $g_{ij}(t)$ on the space of couplings $\{g_i\}$ satisfies a modified Ricci flow equation:
$$
\partial_t g_{ij} = -2 R_{ij} + 2 \nabla_i \nabla_j \Phi,
$$
which is precisely the Ricci flow coupled to a diffeomorphism generated by the gradient of $\Phi$. This identifies the RG flow as a Riemannian gradient flow of $\mathcal{F}$, with the parametric Hessian of $\mathcal{F}$ deforming the information metric.
\n\n
作者将Polchinski精确RG方程重构为支配场构型概率分布的无穷维Fokker-Planck方程。他们定义了一个场论版本的$\mathcal{F}$-熵泛函：
$$
\mathcal{F} = \int \mathcal{D}\phi\, P[\phi] \left( \Phi[\phi] + |\nabla \ln P[\phi]|^2 \right),
$$
其中$P[\phi]$为场分布，$\Phi = -\ln Z_{\text{eff}}$由有效作用量导出。他们证明：在耦合常数空间$\{g_i\}$上，Fisher信息度规$g_{ij}(t)$的尺度依赖演化满足修正的Ricci流方程：
$$
\partial_t g_{ij} = -2 R_{ij} + 2 \nabla_i \nabla_j \Phi,
$$
这正是与由$\Phi$梯度生成的微分同胚耦合的Ricci流。由此，RG流被识别为$\mathcal{F}$的黎曼梯度流，而$\mathcal{F}$的参数Hessian矩阵则导致信息度规的形变。

Result: The key results are: (1) the FRG flow is mathematically equivalent to a diffeomorphism-corrected Ricci flow on the information manifold; (2) the field-theoretic $\mathcal{F}$-entropy serves as a Lyapunov functional monotonically decreasing under RG flow; (3) the logarithm of the effective action $\Phi = -\ln Z_{\text{eff}}$ generates the compensating diffeomorphisms ensuring tensorial covariance of the flow equation; and (4) RG trajectories asymptotically approach Ricci solitons—geometric fixed points where curvature is balanced by diffeomorphism drift—providing a geometric characterization of stable RG fixed points.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(1) FRG流在数学上等价于信息流形上经微分同胚修正的Ricci流；(2) 场论$\mathcal{F}$-熵作为Lyapunov泛函，在RG流下单调递减；(3) 有效作用量的对数$\Phi = -\ln Z_{\text{eff}}$生成补偿性微分同胚，确保流方程的张量协变性；(4) RG轨迹渐近趋于Ricci孤子——即曲率与微分同胚漂移达到平衡的几何不动点——从而为稳定RG不动点提供了几何刻画。

Conclusion: This work establishes a profound link between quantum field theory, information geometry, and geometric analysis by identifying the FRG as a Perelman-type geometric flow. It reinterprets renormalization not merely as coarse-graining but as a curvature-driven geometric optimization on the space of theories. This framework opens new avenues for studying non-perturbative RG dynamics, classifying fixed points via geometric invariants, and potentially applying techniques from Ricci flow theory (e.g., singularity analysis) to understand phase transitions and universality in QFT.
\n\n
本工作通过将FRG识别为Perelman型几何流，在量子场论、信息几何与几何分析之间建立了深刻联系。它将重整化重新诠释为不仅是粗粒化过程，更是理论空间上由曲率驱动的几何优化。该框架为研究非微扰RG动力学、通过几何不变量分类不动点，以及潜在地应用Ricci流理论中的技术（如奇点分析）来理解QFT中的相变与普适性开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We establish an equivalence between the Functional Renormalization Group (FRG) and the Ricci flow modified by a diffeomorphism. By reformulating the Polchinski exact renormalization group equation into an infinite-dimensional Fokker-Planck framework, we show that the evolution of the Fisher information metric on the coupling constant space is a geometric optimization process. Central to this mapping is our construction of a field-theoretic $\mathcal{F}$-entropy functional - an infinite-dimensional analogue of Perelman's $\mathcal{F}$-entropy functional - which acts as a Lyapunov potential for the theory. We prove that the continuous scale evolution of the field distribution constitutes a Riemannian gradient flow of this $\mathcal{F}$-entropy, which in turn deforms the information metric on the coupling constant space via the parametric Hessian of the entropic landscape. Crucially, the log of the effective action serves as a scalar potential $Φ$ that generates the diffeomorphisms required to ensure the tensorial consistency of the flow. Our framework demonstrates that successive integration of high-energy degrees of freedom effectively smooths out the curvature of the information manifold, driving the system toward a Ricci soliton equilibrium. These results provide a novel foundation for characterizing the stability of RG fixed points and offer a first-principles bridge connecting quantum field theory, information geometry, and Perelman's theory of geometric evolution.

</details>


### [27] [Holographic entanglement entropy in the QCD phase diagram under external magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17438)
*Man-Man Sun,Man-Li Tian,Zhou-Run Zhu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper investigates holographic entanglement entropy in the QCD phase diagram under an external magnetic field using an Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton gravity dual. It identifies a swallow-tail structure in entanglement entropy for perpendicular magnetic field orientation, signaling a transition between connected and disconnected Ryu-Takayanagi surfaces, while parallel orientation shows no such transition. Entanglement entropy exhibits multivalued behavior at large chemical potential, which is suppressed by stronger magnetic fields, aligning with known QCD thermodynamics.
\n\n
本文利用爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量（Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton）引力对偶模型，研究了外加磁场下QCD相图中的全息纠缠熵。在垂直磁场取向下，纠缠熵呈现出燕尾（swallow-tail）结构，表明Ryu-Takayanagi曲面在连通与非连通构型之间发生跃迁；而平行取向下行为单调，无此类跃迁。在大化学势下，纠缠熵差呈现多值性，但随磁场增强恢复为单值，与已知QCD热力学一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how quantum entanglement, as captured by holographic entanglement entropy via the AdS/CFT correspondence, reflects non-perturbative features of the QCD phase diagram—particularly under extreme conditions like finite temperature, chemical potential, and external magnetic fields. The authors aim to test whether entanglement entropy can act as a diagnostic tool for confinement/deconfinement transitions and critical phenomena in strongly coupled gauge theories.
\n\n
动机在于通过AdS/CFT对偶所刻画的全息纠缠熵，理解量子纠缠如何反映QCD相图中的非微扰特征——尤其是在有限温度、化学势和外加磁场等极端条件下。作者旨在检验纠缠熵能否作为强耦合规范理论中禁闭/解禁闭相变及临界现象的有效探针。

Method: The authors employ a bottom-up Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton holographic model dual to a QCD-like theory. They compute the holographic entanglement entropy using the Ryu-Takayanagi prescription for a strip-shaped region, analyzing both perpendicular and parallel orientations of the external magnetic field relative to the entangling surface. They solve the bulk equations of motion numerically to obtain background geometries corresponding to specious-confinement and deconfined phases, then evaluate the area functional of minimal surfaces to extract entanglement entropy as a function of temperature $T$, chemical potential $\mu$, and magnetic field $B$.
\n\n
作者采用自下而上的爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量全息模型，该模型对偶于类QCD理论。他们利用Ryu-Takayanagi公式计算条带区域的全息纠缠熵，分别分析外加磁场相对于纠缠面的垂直与平行取向。通过数值求解体时空（bulk）运动方程，获得对应于“伪禁闭”（specious-confinement）与解禁闭相的背景几何，进而计算极小曲面的面积泛函，提取纠缠熵作为温度$T$、化学势$\mu$和磁场$B$的函数。

Result: For perpendicular magnetic field orientation, the relation between strip length and entanglement entropy exhibits three branches and a swallow-tail structure, indicating a first-order-like transition between connected and disconnected entanglement surfaces. In contrast, the parallel case shows monotonic behavior with no transition. At small $\mu$, the entanglement entropy difference varies smoothly with $T$, but becomes multivalued at large $\mu$, signaling non-analyticity associated with phase structure. Increasing $B$ suppresses this multivaluedness, restoring single-valued behavior. These features mirror those in black hole thermodynamics and the expected QCD phase diagram.
\n\n
在垂直磁场取向下，条带长度与纠缠熵的关系呈现三个分支及燕尾结构，表明连通与非连通纠缠曲面之间存在类一级相变。相比之下，平行取向下行为单调，无相变。在小$\mu$时，纠缠熵差随$T$平滑变化；但在大$\mu$时变为多值，反映出与相结构相关的非解析性。增强磁场$B$可抑制多值性，恢复单值行为。这些特征与黑洞热力学及预期的QCD相图一致。

Conclusion: Holographic entanglement entropy encodes rich information about the QCD phase structure under external magnetic fields. Its non-analytic behavior—such as swallow-tail structures and multivaluedness—correlates with thermodynamic phase transitions, confirming its utility as a probe of confinement/deconfinement dynamics. The dependence on magnetic field orientation further reveals anisotropic entanglement properties in strongly coupled plasmas.
\n\n
全息纠缠熵在外加磁场下编码了QCD相结构的丰富信息。其非解析行为（如燕尾结构和多值性）与热力学相变密切相关，证实了其作为禁闭/解禁闭动力学探针的有效性。对磁场取向的依赖性进一步揭示了强耦合等离子体中纠缠的各向异性特性。

Abstract: In this work, we explore holographic entanglement entropy in the QCD phase diagram under an external magnetic field using an Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton model. We consider both the specious-confinement and deconfined phases. In the perpendicular magnetic field orientation, the strip length shows three distinct branches, and the entanglement entropy develops a swallow-tail structure, indicating a transition between connected and disconnected entanglement surfaces. For the parallel orientation, the behavior is monotonic and no transition occurs. In addition, the difference in entanglement entropy changes smoothly with temperature at small chemical potential, but becomes multivalued at large chemical potential. Increasing the magnetic field restores single-valued behavior. These results are consistent with the black hole thermodynamics and the QCD phase diagram. Our findings show that entanglement entropy can serve as an effective probe of the QCD phase transition.

### [28] [Krylov Correlators in $\mathfrak{sl}(2,\mathbb R)$ Models: Exact Results and Holographic Complexity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17550)
*Eleonora Alfinito,Matteo Beccaria*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper extends the holographic complexity–momentum correspondence beyond the original Krylov complexity by analyzing higher-order Krylov correlators and showing their connection to proper radial momenta of infalling particles in the BTZ black hole background.
\n\n
本文通过分析高阶Krylov correlators，将全息complexity–momentum对应关系从原始的Krylov complexity推广出去，并展示了这些correlators与BTZ黑洞背景下落入粒子的proper radial momenta之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The original complexity–momentum correspondence was established for the BTZ black hole in AdS$_3$, linking the growth rate of Krylov complexity of the boundary quantum state to the momentum of a bulk particle falling into the black hole. The authors aim to generalize this duality by incorporating fluctuations and temporal correlations via higher Krylov complexities and Krylov correlators, which encode richer dynamical information about quantum state spreading.
\n\n
最初的complexity–momentum对应关系在AdS$_3$中的BTZ黑洞背景下建立，将边界量子态的Krylov complexity增长率与体空间中落入黑洞的粒子动量联系起来。作者旨在通过引入高阶Krylov complexities和Krylov correlators（编码量子态扩散的涨落和时间关联）来推广这一对偶关系，以捕捉更丰富的动力学信息。

Method: The authors derive exact analytic expressions for Krylov correlators in quantum systems possessing either $\\mathfrak{sl}(2,\\mathbb{R})$ or Heisenberg-Weyl symmetry. These correlators involve out-of-time-ordered products (OTOCs) of Krylov speed operators at multiple times. They then map these boundary correlators to bulk quantities by evaluating combinations of the proper radial momenta of a point particle falling into the BTZ black hole at corresponding times.
\n\n
作者推导了具有$\\mathfrak{sl}(2,\\mathbb{R})$或Heisenberg-Weyl对称性的量子系统中Krylov correlators的精确解析表达式。这些correlators包含多个时刻的Krylov speed算符的out-of-time-ordered乘积（OTOCs）。随后，他们将这些边界correlators映射到体空间量，即在相应时刻计算落入BTZ黑洞的点粒子的proper radial momenta的组合。

Result: The paper demonstrates that specific out-of-time-ordered correlators of Krylov speed operators are proportional to linear combinations of the proper radial momenta of an infalling particle in the BTZ geometry at different times. This provides an explicit generalization of the original complexity–momentum correspondence to include multi-time correlators encoding quantum fluctuations.
\n\n
论文证明了特定的Krylov speed算符的out-of-time-ordered correlators与BTZ几何中落入粒子在不同时刻的proper radial momenta的线性组合成正比。这为原始complexity–momentum对应关系提供了明确推广，纳入了编码量子涨落的多时correlators。

Conclusion: This work establishes a first concrete extension of the complexity–momentum correspondence beyond the leading-order Krylov complexity, revealing a deeper link between boundary quantum dynamics—captured by Krylov correlators—and bulk gravitational physics in AdS$_3$/CFT$_2$. It opens the door to exploring higher-moment diagnostics of quantum chaos and complexity through holography.
\n\n
本工作首次将complexity–momentum对应关系从主导阶的Krylov complexity明确推广出去，揭示了由Krylov correlators刻画的边界量子动力学与AdS$_3$/CFT$_2$中体空间引力物理之间的更深层联系。这为通过全息原理探索量子混沌与复杂性的高阶矩诊断开辟了道路。

Abstract: In holography, the complexity--momentum correspondence relates the increasing momentum of a point particle falling into an eternal black hole to the rate of growth of the Krylov complexity of the dual boundary state, a conjecture established exactly for the BTZ black hole in AdS$_{3}$ at the semiclassical level. We examine possible extensions of the correspondence by considering boundary higher Krylov complexities and Krylov correlators encoding fluctuations and temporal correlations of the spreading quantum state. To this end, we derive exact results for Krylov correlators in quantum systems with $\mathfrak{sl}(2,\mathbb{R})$ or Heisenberg-Weyl symmetry and apply them to the complexity--momentum correspondence. We show that certain out-of-time-ordered correlators of two or more Krylov speed operators at different times are proportional to combinations of the proper radial momenta of a particle falling into the BTZ black hole in AdS$_{3}$, evaluated at those times. This represents a first step in the generalization of the original complexity--momentum relation.

### [29] [Semi-classical Imprint of Horizon Induced Instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17586)
*Arnab Chakraborty,Onirban Islam,Arshad Momen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper computes the density of states for an inverted harmonic oscillator on the circle $L^{2}(\mathbb{S})$ using the stationary phase approximation applied to an oscillatory integral representation of the time-evolution kernel, thereby rigorously demonstrating thermalisation as a semi-classical consequence of classical Lyapunov instability and resolving prior conceptual and mathematical gaps.
\n\n
本文利用时间演化算符的振荡积分表示，并通过平稳相位近似计算了圆周上 $L^{2}(\mathbb{S})$ 空间中反向谐振子的态密度，从而严格证明了热化现象是经典Lyapunov不稳定性在半经典极限下的体现，并弥补了先前文献中的概念与数学缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous works [Phys. Rev. D 102, 044006; Phys. Rev. D 102, 124047] heuristically suggested that thermalisation in systems with an inverted harmonic oscillator arises from analytic continuation and is linked to classical Lyapunov instability, but lacked rigorous spectral analysis and suffered from conceptual and mathematical ambiguities. This paper aims to provide a mathematically sound foundation by explicitly computing the density of states in $L^{2}(\mathbb{S})$.
\n\n
先前的研究 [Phys. Rev. D 102, 044006; Phys. Rev. D 102, 124047] 通过启发式的解析延拓指出，反向谐振子系统中的热化现象源于经典Lyapunov不稳定性，但缺乏严格的谱分析，并存在概念与数学上的模糊性。本文旨在通过对 $L^{2}(\mathbb{S})$ 中态密度的显式计算，提供一个数学上严谨的基础。

Method: The authors employ an oscillatory integral representation of the Schwartz kernel of the time-evolution operator $U(t) = e^{-iHt}$, where $H$ is the Hamiltonian of the inverted harmonic oscillator on $\mathbb{S}$. They then apply the stationary phase approximation to evaluate the trace of $U(t)$ in the semi-classical limit, from which the density of states is extracted via Fourier transform.
\n\n
作者采用时间演化算符 $U(t) = e^{-iHt}$ 的Schwartz核的振荡积分表示，其中 $H$ 是定义在 $\mathbb{S}$ 上的反向谐振子哈密顿量。随后，他们在半经典极限下应用平稳相位近似来计算 $U(t)$ 的迹，并通过对该迹进行傅里叶变换提取出态密度。

Result: The computation yields an explicit expression for the density of states that exhibits exponential growth characteristic of thermal spectra, directly linking it to the classical Lyapunov exponent of the inverted oscillator. This provides a rigorous semi-classical derivation of thermalisation without relying on heuristic analytic continuation.
\n\n
计算得到了一个显式的态密度表达式，其呈现出热谱所特有的指数增长行为，并直接与反向谐振子的经典Lyapunov指数相关联。这为热化现象提供了无需依赖启发式解析延拓的严格半经典推导。

Conclusion: Thermalisation in the quantum inverted harmonic oscillator on the circle is rigorously established as a semi-classical manifestation of classical chaotic instability (Lyapunov instability). The work closes foundational gaps in earlier treatments by providing a precise spectral analysis grounded in oscillatory integrals and stationary phase methods.
\n\n
圆周上量子反向谐振子中的热化现象被严格确立为经典混沌不稳定性（Lyapunov不稳定性）的半经典体现。本文通过基于振荡积分和平稳相位方法的精确谱分析，弥补了早期处理中的基础性缺陷。

Abstract: We consider an inverted harmonic oscillator in the space $L^{2} (\mathbb{S})$ of square-integrable functions on the circle $\mathbb{S}$ and compute its density of states employing the stationary phase approximation. Our computation is based on an oscillatory integral representation of the Schwartz kernel of the time-evolution operator. This demonstrates thermalisation as a semi-classical manifestation of the classical Lyapunov instability -- reported earlier in [Phys. Rev. D 102, 044006; Phys. Rev. D 102, 124047] using heuristic analytic continuation. Our spectral analysis of the Hamiltonian points out and closes the conceptual and mathematical gaps in the preceding literature.

### [30] [Anomaly-Free Spectra, Unimodular Lattices and 6D R-Symmetry Gauged Supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17643)
*Katrin Becker,Qi You*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper discovers eleven new 6D $\mathcal{N}=(1,0)$ supergravity models with gauged $U(1)_R$ R-symmetry and one tensor multiplet that satisfy both local (Green–Schwarz) and global anomaly cancellation conditions. These models populate previously underexplored low-rank gauge groups and reveal a richer yet constrained landscape of consistent theories. The authors analyze arithmetic properties of anomaly coefficients—such as unimodular lattice embeddability, characteristic-vector constraints, and ghost-free conditions—and establish that $n_V \equiv 8 \pmod{12}$ is necessary and sufficient for rank-two unimodular embedding. They also detail the anomaly contribution from $D_4$ gauge algebras, sharpening connections to UV completions in string/F-theory.
\n\n
本文发现了十一个新的具有规范化的 $U(1)_R$ R-对称性和一个张量多重态的 6D $\mathcal{N}=(1,0)$ 超引力模型，这些模型同时满足局域（Green–Schwarz）和全局反常抵消条件。这些模型填补了此前文献中低秩规范群区域的研究空白，揭示了一个比以往认知更丰富但仍高度受限的一致理论景观。作者分析了反常系数的算术结构——包括幺模格嵌入性、特征向量条件和无鬼场条件——并证明在秩为二的情形下，$n_V \equiv 8 \pmod{12}$ 是幺模嵌入的充要条件。他们还详细讨论了 $D_4$ 规范代数对反常多项式的贡献，从而更清晰地刻画了无反常 6D 谱、全局一致性约束与弦论或 F-theory 中紫外实现之间的边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The classification of consistent 6D $\mathcal{N}=(1,0)$ supergravities is crucial for understanding quantum gravity constraints and the Swampland Program. While anomaly cancellation via the Green–Schwarz mechanism provides local consistency, recent work emphasizes additional global constraints (e.g., charge quantization, lattice embeddability). Models with gauged abelian R-symmetry ($U(1)_R$) are particularly subtle due to their coupling to the tensor multiplet and restricted matter content. Prior enumerations often assume high-rank gauge groups or ignore global subtleties, leaving low-rank $U(1)_R$-gauged models underexplored. This paper aims to fill this gap and test the robustness of proposed global consistency conditions.
\n\n
对一致的 6D $\mathcal{N}=(1,0)$ 超引力进行分类对于理解量子引力约束和 Swampland 纲领至关重要。尽管 Green–Schwarz 机制提供的反常抵消保证了局域一致性，但近期工作强调了额外的全局约束（例如电荷量子化、格嵌入性）。具有规范阿贝尔 R-对称性（$U(1)_R$）的模型尤其微妙，因其与张量多重态耦合并限制了物质内容。以往的枚举通常假设高秩规范群或忽略全局细节，导致低秩 $U(1)_R$ 规范模型研究不足。本文旨在填补这一空白，并检验所提出的全局一致性条件的稳健性。

Method: The authors construct explicit 6D supergravity models with gauge group $G_{\mathrm{non-Abelian}} \times U(1)_R$ and one tensor multiplet. They impose: (i) the local Green–Schwarz factorization condition on the 8-form anomaly polynomial $I_8$; (ii) global consistency conditions including integrality of the Dirac pairing on the charge lattice $\Lambda$, embeddability of $\Lambda$ into a rank-two unimodular lattice, the characteristic-vector condition (related to spin structure), and absence of ghosts in the gauge sector. They perform systematic scans over possible non-Abelian gauge algebras (including exceptional and $D_n$ series) and hypermultiplet representations, solving Diophantine equations arising from anomaly cancellation. Special attention is paid to cases involving the $D_4$ Lie algebra due to its triality symmetry. Arithmetic number theory (e.g., congruence conditions modulo 12) is used to characterize lattice embeddability.
\n\n
作者构造了具有规范群 $G_{\mathrm{non-Abelian}} \times U(1)_R$ 和一个张量多重态的显式 6D 超引力模型。他们施加了以下条件：(i) 8-形式反常多项式 $I_8$ 的局域 Green–Schwarz 因子化条件；(ii) 全局一致性条件，包括电荷格 $\Lambda$ 上 Dirac 配对的整性、$\Lambda$ 嵌入秩为二的幺模格的可能性、特征向量条件（与旋量结构相关），以及规范扇区中无鬼场。他们对可能的非阿贝尔规范代数（包括例外代数和 $D_n$ 系列）及超多重态表示进行系统扫描，求解由反常抵消导出的丢番图方程。由于 $D_4$ 李代数具有三重性（triality）对称性，作者对其情形给予特别关注。算术数论（例如模 12 的同余条件）被用于刻画格嵌入性。

Result: Eleven new consistent 6D $\mathcal{N}=(1,0)$ supergravity models with gauged $U(1)_R$ and one tensor multiplet are explicitly constructed. These satisfy all known local and global anomaly constraints. The models predominantly feature low-rank non-Abelian gauge groups (e.g., $SU(2)$, $SU(3)$, $G_2$, $D_4$), regions where prior automated classifications are less effective. Key theoretical results include: (1) proof that for rank-two charge lattices, unimodular embeddability holds iff $n_V \equiv 8 \pmod{12}$, where $n_V$ is the number of vector multiplets; (2) verification that the characteristic-vector condition is sufficient for the branches realized by their examples, while identifying an unrealized branch that may require further exclusion; (3) explicit computation of the $D_4$ contribution to the anomaly polynomial, clarifying its role in consistency conditions.
\n\n
作者显式构造了十一个新的具有一致性的 6D $\mathcal{N}=(1,0)$ 超引力模型，这些模型具有规范化的 $U(1)_R$ 和一个张量多重态，并满足所有已知的局域和全局反常约束。这些模型主要包含低秩非阿贝尔规范群（例如 $SU(2)$、$SU(3)$、$G_2$、$D_4$），而这些区域是以往自动化分类方法效果较弱的部分。关键理论成果包括：(1) 证明在秩为二的电荷格情形下，幺模嵌入性成立当且仅当 $n_V \equiv 8 \pmod{12}$，其中 $n_V$ 为矢量多重态数目；(2) 验证了特征向量条件对其示例所实现分支的充分性，并识别出一个尚未实现的分支可能需要进一步排除；(3) 显式计算了 $D_4$ 对反常多项式的贡献，澄清了其在一致性条件中的作用。

Conclusion: The landscape of anomaly-free 6D $\mathcal{N}=(1,0)$ supergravities with gauged $U(1)_R$ symmetry is more extensive than previously thought, especially in the low-rank regime, yet remains tightly constrained by arithmetic conditions on anomaly coefficients. The derived congruence $n_V \equiv 8 \pmod{12}$ and analysis of the characteristic-vector condition provide sharper criteria for distinguishing consistent low-energy theories from the Swampland. The detailed treatment of $D_4$ underscores the importance of Lie-algebra-specific data in anomaly cancellation. These results enhance the bridge between bottom-up supergravity constructions and top-down UV completions in F-theory, suggesting that global consistency conditions are essential for accurate classification.
\n\n
具有规范 $U(1)_R$ 对称性的无反常 6D $\mathcal{N}=(1,0)$ 超引力景观比以往认为的更为广阔，尤其是在低秩区域，但仍受到反常系数上算术条件的严格约束。所导出的同余条件 $n_V \equiv 8 \pmod{12}$ 及对特征向量条件的分析，为区分一致的低能理论与 Swampland 提供了更精确的判据。对 $D_4$ 的细致处理突显了李代数特异性数据在反常抵消中的重要性。这些结果加强了自下而上的超引力构造与 F-theory 中自上而下的紫外实现之间的联系，表明全局一致性条件对准确分类至关重要。

Abstract: We study the classification problem for anomaly-free 6D $\mathcal N=(1,0)$ supergravities with a gauged abelian R-symmetry and one tensor multiplet. We present eleven new models with gauge group $G_{\mathrm{non-Abelian}}\times U(1)_R$ that satisfy the local Green--Schwarz factorization condition, together with several recently proposed global consistency conditions. In particular, the low-rank models we found are precisely where some of the recent enumeration literature is least directly applicable. These examples suggest that the landscape of anomaly-free gauged $U(1)_R$ supergravities may be richer than previously recognized while still remaining highly constrained. We analyze the arithmetic structure of the anomaly coefficients, including their integral pairings, embeddability into rank-two unimodular charge lattices, the characteristic-vector condition and ghost-free gauge-field conditions. We show that $n_V \equiv 8 \pmod{12}$ is necessary and sufficient for the unimodular embeddability in the rank-two case. For the characteristic-vector condition we verify sufficiency for the branches realized by our examples and identify a remaining branch requiring additional exclusion. We also present a detailed discussion of the contribution to the anomaly polynomial when the $D_4$ Lie algebra is present. These results sharpen the boundary between anomaly-free 6D spectra, global-consistency constraints, and possible UV realization in string theory or F-theory.

</details>


### [31] [An Alternative Viewpoint on Kinematic Flow from Tubing Splitting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17751)
*Ji-Yuan Ke,Ping He*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper reinterprets the differential equations governing wavefunction coefficients of conformally coupled scalars in power-law cosmologies by reversing the evolution direction of graph tubings, revealing that kinematic flow and tubings may be more fundamental than the differential equations themselves.
\n\n
本文通过反转图管（graph tubings）的演化方向，重新诠释了幂律宇宙学中共形耦合标量场波函数系数所满足的微分方程，揭示出运动学流（kinematic flow）和图管可能比微分方程本身更为基本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional approaches describe the wavefunction coefficients via differential equations derived from cosmological time evolution. The authors seek a deeper understanding of the underlying structure by exploring whether the combinatorial and geometric data encoded in graph tubings—and their associated kinematic flow—can serve as more fundamental building blocks than the differential equations.
\n\n
传统方法通过从宇宙学时间演化导出的微分方程来描述波函数系数。作者试图通过探索图管及其关联的运动学流所编码的组合与几何数据，是否能作为比微分方程更基本的构建单元，从而获得对底层结构的更深刻理解。

Method: The authors reformulate the relations among basis functions by reversing the evolution direction of graph tubings. They construct splitting rules equivalent to the kinematic flow at tree level, which generate the original differential equations. An alternative time-ordered basis is also employed to examine how time emerges from kinematic space.
\n\n
作者通过反转图管的演化方向来重构基函数之间的关系，并在树图层级上构建等价于运动学流的分裂规则（splitting rules），这些规则可重现原始微分方程。同时采用一种基于时间排序的替代基底，以考察时间如何从运动学空间中涌现。

Result: The reversed tubing evolution leads to splitting rules that reproduce the differential equations while exposing richer structures such as singularities and local evolution. The framework applies beyond individual Feynman diagrams and extends to the tr $\\phi^3$ theory, suggesting tubings and kinematic flow are intrinsic objects independent of specific dynamical formulations.
\n\n
反转的图管演化导出了可重现微分方程的分裂规则，同时揭示了诸如奇点和局域演化等更丰富的结构。该框架不仅适用于单个费曼图，还可推广至 tr $\\phi^3$ 理论，表明图管和运动学流是独立于特定动力学表述的内在对象。

Conclusion: Graph tubings and their kinematic flow may represent more fundamental entities than the differential equations traditionally used to describe cosmological wavefunctions. Time itself may emerge from the structure of kinematic space, with implications extending beyond scalar theories to broader quantum field theoretic contexts.
\n\n
图管及其运动学流可能比传统用于描述宇宙学波函数的微分方程更为基本。时间本身或许从运动学空间的结构中涌现，其含义可超越标量理论，延伸至更广泛的量子场论语境。

Abstract: The differential equations satisfied by the wavefunction coefficients of conformally coupled scalars in a power-law cosmology can be recast into an iterative differential system of basis functions. These functions can be encoded within graph tubings, and are governed by a set of rules describing how they flow in kinematic space. In this paper we propose a new viewpoint on the kinematic flow by reformulating the relations among these basis functions through reversing the evolution direction of the tubings. The differential equations can then be derived by constructing appropriate splitting rules equivalent to the kinematic flow (at tree level). While the implementation of these rules can be somewhat complicated, they reveal richer physical structures underlying the differential equations, such as singularities and local evolution. Under an alternative basis based on time ordering, these rules offer important implications for how time emerges from kinematic space. This conclusion is even not restricted to individual Feynman diagrams, and can be generalized to the tr $φ^3$ theory. This suggests that the tubings, as well as the kinematic flow, might be more fundamental objects than the differential equations, and have a life of their own.
