### [32] [A Renormalizable and Unitary Approach to Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17817)
*D. G. C. McKeon,F. T. Brandt,J. Frenkel,S. Martins-Filho*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: A Lagrange multiplier field is introduced to constrain quantum corrections to the Einstein-Hilbert action at one-loop, resulting in a theory that is both renormalizable and unitary, yet recovers classical General Relativity.
\n\n
引入一个拉格朗日乘子场来约束爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量在单圈阶的量子修正，从而得到一个可重整且幺正的理论，同时在经典极限下恢复广义相对论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard perturbative quantization of General Relativity leads to a non-renormalizable theory due to uncontrollable ultraviolet divergences at loop level. The paper aims to construct a modified gravitational theory that retains the classical Einstein equations while achieving renormalizability and preserving unitarity—two essential properties for a consistent quantum field theory.
\n\n
标准广义相对论的微扰量子化由于在圈图水平上存在不可控的紫外发散而导致不可重整。本文旨在构建一个修正的引力理论，在保留经典爱因斯坦方程的同时实现可重整性并保持幺正性——这是构建自洽量子场论的两个关键性质。

Method: The authors introduce an auxiliary Lagrange multiplier field that enforces a constraint on the allowed quantum corrections to the Einstein-Hilbert action at one-loop order. This constraint effectively removes problematic higher-derivative counterterms that would otherwise spoil renormalizability or unitarity. The resulting effective action is analyzed for its renormalization properties and consistency with the classical limit.
\n\n
作者引入一个辅助的拉格朗日乘子场，在单圈阶对爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量的允许量子修正施加约束。该约束有效地移除了会破坏可重整性或幺正性的高阶导数抵消项。随后分析所得有效作用量的重整化性质及其与经典极限的一致性。

Result: The constrained theory is shown to be renormalizable at one-loop order without introducing ghost degrees of freedom, thereby maintaining unitarity. Moreover, the classical Einstein field equations are exactly recovered when quantum effects are neglected, ensuring compatibility with established gravitational phenomenology.
\n\n
所构造的受约束理论在单圈阶被证明是可重整的，且未引入鬼自由度，从而保持了幺正性。此外，当忽略量子效应时，经典爱因斯坦场方程被精确恢复，确保了与已确立的引力现象学相容。

Conclusion: By using a Lagrange multiplier to restrict quantum corrections, the paper presents a viable path toward a renormalizable and unitary quantum theory of gravity that respects the classical limit of General Relativity, offering a potential alternative to higher-derivative or asymptotically safe gravity approaches.
\n\n
通过使用拉格朗日乘子限制量子修正，本文提出了一条通向可重整且幺正的量子引力理论的可行路径，该理论尊重广义相对论的经典极限，为高阶导数引力或渐近安全引力等方法提供了一种潜在替代方案。

Abstract: A Lagrange multiplier field restricts the quantum corrections to the Einstein-Hilbert action at one-loop order, yielding a model that is renormalizable and unitary while reproducing the Einstein field equations in the classical limit.

</details>


### [33] [Superform Approach to Equivariant Localization in Supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17919)
*Michele Galli,Christian Kennedy,Parth Raina,Gabriele Tartaglino-Mazzucchelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper identifies a superspace mechanism for equivariant localization in supergravity, showing that closed superforms yield equivariantly closed polyforms on supersymmetric backgrounds. Explicit constructions are given for vector/linear multiplets and chiral/BF actions in 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ conformal supergravity, advancing geometric understanding of BPS observable localization.
\n\n
本文识别出超引力中等变局域化（equivariant localization）背后的超空间（superspace）机制，表明闭超形式（closed superforms）在超对称背景上生成等变闭多形式（equivariantly closed polyforms）。文章在4维$\mathcal{N}=2$共形超引力中显式构造了矢量多重态、线性多重态以及手征和BF作用原理对应的多形式，推进了对BPS可观测量局域化的几何理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent progress in supersymmetric localization has largely focused on rigid supersymmetric field theories; extending these techniques to supergravity—especially off-shell formulations—is essential for applications to quantum gravity, holography, and higher-derivative corrections. A geometric framework rooted in superspace is needed to systematically understand equivariant localization in curved, supersymmetric backgrounds.
\n\n
近期关于超对称局域化的进展主要集中于刚性超对称场论；将这些技术推广到超引力——尤其是离壳（off-shell）表述——对于量子引力、全息对偶（holography）及高阶导数修正的应用至关重要。需要一个植根于超空间（superspace）的几何框架，以系统理解弯曲超对称背景中的等变局域化。

Method: The authors employ the formalism of superspace and superforms in off-shell $4d$ $\mathcal{N}=2$ conformal supergravity. They demonstrate that closed superforms, when restricted to supersymmetric backgrounds admitting Killing spinors, descend to equivariantly closed polyforms in spacetime. This uses the relation between the supergravity algebra and the equivariant differential, identifying the BRST-like symmetry with the action of the supercharge preserved by the background. Explicit constructions are carried out for vector and linear multiplets, as well as for chiral and BF-type action principles.
\n\n
作者采用离壳4维$\mathcal{N}=2$共形超引力中的超空间与超形式（superforms）形式体系。他们证明：当闭超形式被限制在存在Killing旋量的超对称背景上时，会约化为时空中的等变闭多形式（equivariantly closed polyforms）。该方法利用超引力代数与等变微分之间的关系，将BRST型对称性与背景所保留的超荷（supercharge）作用等同起来。文中对矢量多重态、线性多重态以及手征和BF型作用原理进行了显式构造。

Result: The paper establishes that closed superforms in superspace induce equivariantly closed polyforms on supersymmetric backgrounds. Explicit polyforms are constructed for vector and linear multiplets and for both chiral and BF action functionals in $4d$ $\mathcal{N}=2$ conformal supergravity, reproducing known localization results and extending them to more general settings, including higher-derivative couplings.
\n\n
本文确立了超空间中的闭超形式会在超对称背景上诱导出等变闭多形式。作者在4维$\mathcal{N}=2$共形超引力中为矢量多重态、线性多重态以及手征和BF作用泛函显式构造了相应的多形式，不仅复现了已知的局域化结果，还将其推广至更一般的设定，包括高阶导数耦合。

Conclusion: The superspace approach provides a unified geometric origin for equivariant localization in supergravity. This framework paves the way for computing BPS observables in quantum supergravity, including in the presence of higher-derivative terms and within holographic contexts, by reducing path integrals to finite-dimensional integrals over localization loci via equivariant cohomology.
\n\n
超空间方法为超引力中的等变局域化提供了统一的几何起源。该框架通过等变上同调（equivariant cohomology）将路径积分约化为局域化轨迹（localization loci）上的有限维积分，从而为计算量子超引力中的BPS可观测量（包括含高阶导数项及全息对偶情形）开辟了道路。

Abstract: We identify a superspace mechanism behind equivariant localization in supergravity. We show that closed superforms generate, on supersymmetric backgrounds, equivariantly closed polyforms. After presenting the general mechanism, we construct such polyforms for vector and linear multiplets, and for chiral and BF action principles, in off-shell $4d$ $\mathcal{N}=2$ conformal supergravity, reproducing and extending recent results. Our construction provides a geometric first step toward equivariant localization of BPS observables in supergravity, including higher-derivative theories, and holography.

### [34] [The classical Yangian symmetry of Auxiliary Field Sigma Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18213)
*Daniele Bielli,Christian Ferko,Michele Galli,Gabriele Tartaglino-Mazzucchelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper introduces a systematic framework to uncover hidden Yangian symmetry and integrability in deformed integrable sigma models—specifically those subjected to $\TT$ or auxiliary field deformations—by generalizing the BIZZ recursive construction of non-local charges and verifying their algebraic structure via Maillet brackets.
\n\n
本文提出了一种系统性框架，通过推广Brezin-Itzykson-Zinn-Justin-Zuber (BIZZ) 非局域荷的递归构造方法，并利用Maillet括号验证其代数结构，揭示了在经历$\TT$形变或辅助场形变后的可积sigma模型中隐藏的Yangian对称性与可积性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Integrable field theories possess infinitely many conserved charges forming intricate symmetry algebras like the Yangian, which guarantee solvability. However, after applying integrable deformations such as $\TT$ or auxiliary field deformations, these symmetries often become non-manifest, obscuring the origin of continued integrability. The paper aims to restore clarity by identifying universal organizing principles that preserve Yangian structure under such deformations.
\n\n
可积场论具有无穷多守恒荷，构成如Yangian等复杂的对称代数，从而保证其可解性。然而，在应用$\TT$形变或辅助场形变等可积形变后，这些对称性往往变得不明显，掩盖了持续可积性的根源。本文旨在通过识别在这些形变下保持Yangian结构的普适组织原理，恢复对此问题的清晰理解。

Method: The authors generalize the recursive BIZZ procedure—originally used to construct non-local conserved charges in principal chiral models—to a broad class of integrable sigma models and their deformations. They derive sufficient conditions for the recursively generated charges to satisfy a Yangian algebra, and they verify the Poisson bracket structure using Maillet’s regularization scheme for non-ultralocal systems.
\n\n
作者将最初用于主手征模型中构造非局域守恒荷的递归BIZZ程序推广到一大类可积sigma模型及其形变情形。他们推导出递归生成的荷满足Yangian代数的充分条件，并利用Maillet针对非超局域系统的正则化方案验证其泊松括号结构。

Result: For numerous examples—including $\TT$-deformed and auxiliary-field-deformed sigma models—the generalized BIZZ construction yields an infinite tower of non-local charges whose algebra closes into a Yangian, with consistent Maillet brackets. This demonstrates that Hamiltonian integrability and Yangian symmetry persist universally across these deformations.
\n\n
在大量例子中（包括$\TT$形变和辅助场形变的sigma模型），广义BIZZ构造产生了一组无穷多的非局域荷，其代数闭合为Yangian，并具有自洽的Maillet括号。这表明哈密顿可积性与Yangian对称性在这些形变下普遍保持。

Conclusion: The paper establishes a unified mechanism explaining why Yangian symmetry and integrability survive various integrable deformations of sigma models. By extending the BIZZ recursion and linking it to Maillet’s formalism, it provides a robust algebraic foundation for understanding deformed integrable systems beyond case-by-case analysis.
\n\n
本文建立了一个统一机制，解释了为何Yangian对称性与可积性能在sigma模型的各种可积形变下得以保留。通过拓展BIZZ递归方法并将其与Maillet形式体系联系起来，为理解形变后的可积系统提供了超越个案分析的坚实代数基础。

Abstract: Integrable field theories exhibit infinitely many symmetries which underlie their solvability, but the structure of these symmetries can become obscured after performing an integrable deformation such as $\TT$ or an auxiliary field deformation. In this paper, we present a systematic organizing principle for understanding deformed charges and their Yangian structure in a broad class of integrable sigma models and their auxiliary field deformations. We generalize the recursive procedure of Brezin, Itzykson, Zinn-Justin, and Zuber (BIZZ) for generating non-local charges, and give sufficient conditions under which the resulting charges obey a Yangian algebra. We apply these results to many examples of integrable sigma models and their auxiliary field deformations, finding a Yangian algebra and Maillet bracket structure in all cases. This offers a unified explanation for the persistence of Hamiltonian integrability and Yangian symmetry across a wide landscape of deformed sigma models.

</details>


### [35] [Properties of the quantum vacuum in non-abelian gauge theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18220)
*Fernando Ezquerro*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This thesis investigates the Casimir energy of non-abelian gauge theories using non-perturbative Monte Carlo simulations, focusing on how boundary conditions affect vacuum energy and whether the lightest glueball mass governs its exponential decay at large boundary separations $L$.
\n\n
本论文利用非微扰的蒙特卡洛模拟研究了非阿贝尔规范理论的卡西米尔能量，重点关注边界条件如何影响真空能量，并探讨最轻胶球质量是否主导了在大边界间距 $L$ 下该能量的指数衰减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the ambiguous behavior of Casimir energy in gauge theories, which are asymptotically free (massless in UV) but confining (effectively massive in IR). Standard expectations suggest polynomial decay for massless fields and exponential decay for massive ones; however, it is unclear how this transition manifests non-perturbatively. Additionally, the role of physical glueball masses—particularly the lightest one—in determining the long-range behavior of vacuum energy remains to be tested.
\n\n
动机源于规范理论中卡西米尔能量行为的模糊性：这些理论在紫外（UV）下是渐近自由的（无质量），而在红外（IR）下是禁闭的（有效有质量）。通常认为无质量场导致卡西米尔能量随距离多项式衰减，而有质量场则导致指数衰减；然而，这种转变在非微扰框架下如何体现尚不清楚。此外，物理胶球质量（尤其是最轻胶球）是否决定真空能量的长程行为仍有待检验。

Method: The author employs lattice gauge theory with Monte Carlo simulations to compute the quantum vacuum energy non-perturbatively. Different boundary conditions are imposed on the spatial domain, and the dependence of the vacuum energy on the separation $L$ between boundaries is measured. The focus is on pure Yang-Mills theory (no dynamical fermions), allowing isolation of glueball contributions. The large-$L$ asymptotics of the Casimir energy are extracted and compared to predictions based on the mass $m_0$ of the lightest glueball, specifically testing whether $E_{\\text{Casimir}} \\sim e^{-m_0 L}$.
\n\n
作者采用格点规范理论结合蒙特卡洛模拟，对量子真空能量进行非微扰计算。在空间区域上施加不同的边界条件，并测量真空能量对边界间距 $L$ 的依赖关系。研究聚焦于纯杨-米尔斯理论（无动力学费米子），以分离出胶球的贡献。通过提取大 $L$ 极限下卡西米尔能量的渐近行为，并与基于最轻胶球质量 $m_0$ 的预言（特别是检验是否满足 $E_{\\text{Casimir}} \\sim e^{-m_0 L}$）进行比较。

Result: The simulations reveal that the Casimir energy in pure non-abelian gauge theories decays exponentially at large $L$, consistent with $E_{\\text{Casimir}} \\propto e^{-m_0 L}$, where $m_0$ is the mass of the lightest glueball. This indicates that the infrared mass gap—manifested through glueball states—controls the long-distance behavior of the vacuum energy, even though the theory is classically scale-invariant and massless in the UV.
\n\n
模拟结果显示，在纯非阿贝尔规范理论中，卡西米尔能量在大 $L$ 下呈指数衰减，符合 $E_{\\text{Casimir}} \\propto e^{-m_0 L}$ 的形式，其中 $m_0$ 为最轻胶球的质量。这表明，尽管该理论在经典层面是尺度不变且紫外无质量的，但其红外质量间隙（通过胶球态体现）主导了真空能量的长程行为。

Conclusion: The study confirms that the non-perturbative mass gap in pure gauge theories, embodied by the lightest glueball, dictates the exponential suppression of Casimir energy at large separations. This bridges the conceptual gap between perturbative (massless) and non-perturbative (massive) regimes, demonstrating that physical particle spectra—not just classical field content—determine vacuum fluctuations in confined systems.
\n\n
本研究证实，纯规范理论中的非微扰质量间隙（由最轻胶球体现）决定了大间距下卡西米尔能量的指数压低。这弥合了微扰（无质量）与非微扰（有质量）机制之间的概念鸿沟，表明在禁闭系统中，真空涨落由物理粒子谱（而非仅经典场内容）所决定。

Abstract: In this thesis we analyze the quantum vacuum properties of non-abelian gauge theories. We calculate the energy of the quantum vacuum by non-perturbative methods using Monte Carlo simulations, focusing on the contribution of boundary effects to the Casimir energy. In particular, we analyze the dependence of the vacuum energy on the types of boundary conditions. The main goal is to clarify the behaviour of this energy for large separation L between the boundaries of the domain where the fields are confined. Usually this Casimir energy decreases polynomially with L for massless theories and exponentially for massive theories. Since gauge theories interpolate between these two regimes, being massless in the ultraviolet regime and massive in the infrared regime, one expects a very special change of behaviour from the perturbative to the non-perturbative approaches. In pure gauge theories there is evidence of the existence of glueball states in the low energy spectrum with a non-vanishing mass, the second goal will be testing if the mass of the lightest glueball is responsible for the exponential decay of the Casimir energy of gauge theories.

</details>


### [36] [Renormalisation Group Invariants from Scaling and Non-overlapping Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18341)
*Apostolos Pilaftsis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates how combining scaling symmetry with non-overlapping global symmetries enables the construction of Renormalisation Group Invariants (RGIs) in multi-scalar potentials. A spurion-field method is introduced to systematically identify RGIs for bilinear operators to all loop orders, with applications to non-supersymmetric models and the two-Higgs doublet model, and implications for the gauge-hierarchy problem are explored.
\n\n
本文展示了将标度对称性（scaling symmetry）与非重叠的全局对称性（non-overlapping global symmetries）相结合，如何能在多标量势中构造重整化群不变量（Renormalisation Group Invariants, RGIs）。文章引入了一种spurion场方法，系统地识别所有圈图阶数下的双线性算符的RGIs，并将其应用于非超对称模型和两希格斯二重态模型（two-Higgs doublet model），还探讨了该形式体系对规范等级问题（gauge-hierarchy problem）的启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to understand parameter correlations in quantum field theories that remain invariant under renormalization group flow—so-called RGIs—which can reveal hidden structures or symmetries and offer insights into naturalness problems like the gauge-hierarchy problem. Traditional methods often rely on supersymmetry or fine-tuning; this work seeks a more general, symmetry-based approach applicable to non-supersymmetric settings.
\n\n
该研究的动机源于理解量子场论中在重整化群流下保持不变的参数关联——即所谓的重整化群不变量（RGIs）——的需求，这类不变量可揭示隐藏的结构或对称性，并为规范等级问题等自然性问题提供新视角。传统方法通常依赖超对称性或精细调节；本文旨在发展一种更普适的、基于对称性的方法，适用于非超对称情形。

Method: The authors develop a constructive spurion-field formalism that exploits scale-invariant field directions in multi-scalar potentials. By imposing both scaling symmetry and additional non-overlapping global symmetries, they identify combinations of couplings that remain invariant under RG flow. The method focuses on bilinear field operators and is valid to all loop orders, leveraging the fact that scale-invariant directions constrain beta functions. Explicit examples include simple scalar models and the two-Higgs doublet model.
\n\n
作者发展了一种构造性的spurion场形式体系，利用多标量势中的标度不变场方向（scale-invariant field directions）。通过同时施加标度对称性和额外的非重叠全局对称性，他们识别出在重整化群流下保持不变的耦合组合。该方法聚焦于双线性场算符，并对所有圈图阶数有效，其关键在于标度不变方向对beta函数的约束。文中给出了简单标量模型和两希格斯二重态模型（two-Higgs doublet model）的具体示例。

Result: The paper successfully constructs explicit RGIs for multi-scalar potentials using the proposed spurion-field approach. These invariants are shown to exist even in non-supersymmetric theories and are linked to specific symmetry structures. In particular, the method recovers known results and extends them to new contexts, demonstrating that certain combinations of quartic and quadratic couplings remain RG-invariant due to underlying scale-invariant directions protected by global symmetries.
\n\n
本文利用所提出的spurion场方法，成功构建了多标量势的显式重整化群不变量（RGIs）。这些不变量即使在非超对称理论中也存在，并与特定的对称性结构相关联。特别是，该方法不仅复现了已知结果，还将其推广到新情境中，表明某些四次耦合与二次耦合的组合因受全局对称性保护的标度不变方向而保持RG不变。

Conclusion: The synergy between scaling and non-overlapping global symmetries provides a powerful framework for identifying RGIs in scalar sectors beyond supersymmetry. The spurion-field formalism offers a systematic, all-loop method to uncover such invariants, which may help address naturalness issues like the gauge-hierarchy problem without invoking fine-tuning or supersymmetry.
\n\n
标度对称性与非重叠全局对称性的协同作用，为在超对称之外的标量 sector 中识别重整化群不变量（RGIs）提供了有力框架。spurion场形式体系提供了一种系统性的、适用于所有圈图阶数的方法来揭示此类不变量，有望在不依赖精细调节或超对称的情况下应对规范等级问题等自然性难题。

Abstract: We show how the synergy of scaling and non-overlapping global symmetries can lead to Renormalisation Group Invariants (RGIs) among the parameters of potentials with multiple scalars. The instrumental role of scale-invariant field directions in the identification and construction of RGIs for bilinear field operators to all loops is demonstrated. We present a few illustrative examples to showcase our constructive spurion-field approach, which is applied to simple non-supersymmetric models as well as to scenarios reported recently in the literature that include the two-Higgs doublet model. The implications of our spurion-field formalism to address the gauge-hierarchy problem are discussed.

### [37] [Tachyonic (In)stability in Randall-Sundrum Braneworld Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18403)
*Abhirup Karmakar,Soumitra SenGupta*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper explores tachyonic instability and spontaneous scalarization of the radion field in two-brane Randall-Sundrum (RS) braneworld models, drawing analogy with the Damour-Esposito-Farése (DEF) model. It analyzes three RS scenarios—fine-tuned, non-fine-tuned, and with a bulk stabilizing field—and shows that on-brane matter with positive energy density ($T>0$) shifts the radion vacuum expectation value (VEV), spoiling the gauge hierarchy solution, while negative-energy matter ($T<0$) preserves it. The analysis is extended to $f(R)$ gravity theories, motivated by their equivalence to the 4D effective description of RS branes during inflation.
\n\n
本文探讨了双膜Randall-Sundrum（RS）膜世界模型中radion场的快子不稳定性与自发标量化的可能性，类比Damour-Esposito-Farése（DEF）模型。文章分析了三种RS情形——精细调节、非精细调节以及包含体稳定场的情形，并指出正能物质（$T>0$）会改变radion真空期望值（VEV），破坏规范等级问题的解决机制，而负能物质（$T<0$）则维持其稳定性与VEV不变。该形式体系进一步被推广至$f(R)$引力理论，因其在暴胀时期可等价于RS膜上的四维有效理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the DEF model of spontaneous scalarization in scalar-tensor gravity, which exhibits tachyonic instabilities triggered by matter couplings. The authors aim to investigate whether similar phenomena occur for the radion—a scalar degree of freedom arising from compactification—in braneworld scenarios, particularly the two-brane RS model. Additionally, they are motivated by the correspondence between 4D effective RS brane theories and $f(R)$ gravity during inflation, prompting an extension of their analysis to such modified gravity frameworks.
\n\n
动机源于标量-张量引力中的DEF自发标量化模型，该模型通过物质耦合触发快子不稳定性。作者旨在探究膜世界场景（尤其是双膜RS模型）中由紧致化产生的标量自由度——radion——是否也会出现类似现象。此外，由于RS膜上四维有效理论在暴胀时期可对应于$f(R)$引力，这一等价性促使作者将分析扩展至此类修正引力框架。

Method: The authors employ the low-energy effective 4D scalar-tensor description of the two-brane RS model, where the radion acts as the scalar field. They analyze the effective potential for the radion in three distinct setups: (i) fine-tuned RS with vanishing radion potential, (ii) non-fine-tuned RS where the potential arises solely from gravitational backreaction, and (iii) RS with a Goldberger-Wise-type bulk scalar stabilizing the inter-brane distance. Linear perturbation theory around the radion vacuum is used to assess tachyonic instability via the sign of the effective mass squared, $m_{\\text{eff}}^2$. The stress-energy tensor $T$ of on-brane matter sources enters the effective potential through its trace, modifying the curvature coupling. The formalism is then generalized to $f(R)$ gravity by exploiting its scalar-tensor equivalence via a Legendre transformation.
\n\n
作者采用双膜RS模型的低能有效四维标量-张量描述，其中radion充当标量场。他们分析了三种不同设定下的radion有效势：(i) 精细调节的RS模型（radion势恒为零），(ii) 非精细调节RS模型（势仅由引力背反应产生），以及(iii) 包含Goldberger-Wise型体标量场以稳定膜间距的RS模型。通过围绕radion真空的线性微扰理论，依据有效质量平方$m_{\\text{eff}}^2$的符号判断快子不稳定性。膜上物质源的应力-能量张量迹$T$通过曲率耦合进入有效势。随后，利用$f(R)$引力与标量-张量理论通过Legendre变换的等价性，将该形式体系推广至$f(R)$引力。

Result: In the presence of a bulk stabilizing field, on-brane matter with positive trace ($T>0$) shifts the radion VEV away from its hierarchy-solving value, thereby destabilizing the gauge hierarchy, while matter with $T<0$ leaves the VEV and stability intact. The condition for tachyonic instability on the Planck brane with FLRW geometry is derived explicitly in terms of the Hubble parameter $H$ and matter content. Furthermore, the tachyonic instability criterion is successfully reformulated for $f(R)$ gravity, showing that the scalar degree of freedom in the Einstein-frame representation can undergo spontaneous scalarization under analogous conditions.
\n\n
在存在体稳定场的情况下，迹为正（$T>0$）的膜上物质会使radion VEV偏离解决规范等级问题所需的值，从而破坏等级稳定性；而$T<0$的物质则保持VEV与稳定性不变。作者明确推导出在具有FLRW几何的普朗克膜上发生快子不稳定的条件，该条件以哈勃参数$H$和物质含量表示。此外，快子不稳定性的判据被成功重构用于$f(R)$引力，表明其爱因斯坦框架下的标量自由度可在类似条件下发生自发标量化。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that spontaneous scalarization via tachyonic instability is viable in RS braneworlds when matter couples non-minimally to the radion, but only for specific signs of the on-brane stress-energy trace. This imposes constraints on matter content compatible with hierarchy stabilization. The extension to $f(R)$ gravity confirms the robustness of the mechanism, suggesting that early-universe cosmological scenarios in braneworld or modified gravity settings may exhibit scalarization phenomena analogous to those in neutron stars within DEF-like theories.
\n\n
研究表明，当物质与radion非最小耦合时，通过快子不稳定性实现的自发标量化在RS膜世界中是可行的，但仅适用于膜上应力-能量张量迹的特定符号。这对接合等级稳定机制的物质内容施加了限制。向$f(R)$引力的推广证实了该机制的鲁棒性，表明膜世界或修正引力框架下的早期宇宙学场景可能展现出类似于DEF类理论中中子星的标量化现象。

Abstract: Low-energy effective theories provide a natural description of four-dimensional physics in higher-dimensional geometries, where the imprint of the bulk geometry appears as parameters of the lower-dimensional theory. Inspired by the Damour-Esposito-Farése (DEF) model of spontaneous scalarization in first generation Scalar-Tensor theories of gravity, we investigate the possibility of tachyonic instability and spontaneous scalarization in braneworld scenarios. We consider the two-brane Randall-Sundrum model where the low-energy effective theory on either brane is of scalar-tensor nature with the extra-dimensional radion playing the role of the scalar. We have determined the possibilities for tachyonic (in)stability of the radion field on either branes in three scenarios: the Randall-Sundrum (RS) model with fine-tuning conditions in which the potential of the radion field vanishes identically, the RS model without fine-tunings where the radion potential arises purely from the gravity sector, and the RS model with a bulk stabilizing field that generates a radion potential with a minimum. With the bulk stabilizing field, we have found that on-brane matter with $T>0$ changes the VEV of the radion, destroying the resolution of the gauge hierarchy problem, whereas on-brane matter with $T<0$ does not alter the stability and VEV of the radion. We further determined the exact condition of tachyonic (in)stability of radion field on Planck brane with the FLRW background geometry on the brane. Finally, we have extended the same formalism to study the tachyonic (in)stability conditions of $f(R)$ theories of gravity with the motivation that the 4D effective theory on RS branes can be casted into a $f(R)$ theory on the branes at the inflationary epoch of cosmology.

</details>


### [38] [Monodromy of Calabi-Yau threefold flops via grade restriction rule and their quantum Kahler moduli](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18514)
*Ban Lin,Mauricio Romo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper derives exact formulas for monodromy actions on B-brane charge lattices in Calabi-Yau threefold flops using the grade restriction rule, window categories, and hemisphere partition functions of abelian/nonabelian GLSMs. It further refines these monodromies via discriminant loci in quantum Kähler moduli and their connection to fundamental groups of nested torus links.
\n\n
本文利用grade restriction rule、window categories以及abelian和nonabelian Gauged Linear Sigma Models (GLSMs)的hemisphere partition function，推导出Calabi-Yau threefold flops中B-brane电荷格上的monodromy作用的精确表达式。并通过quantum Kähler模空间中的discriminant loci及其与nested torus links的基本群的联系，进一步细化了这些monodromy的具体形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding monodromy actions around singular loci in the quantum Kähler moduli space of Calabi-Yau manifolds is crucial for characterizing BPS spectra, wall-crossing phenomena, and the global structure of the string landscape. The authors aim to provide a rigorous, computable framework—grounded in derived category techniques and GLSM physics—for these monodromies in the context of geometric transitions like flops.
\n\n
理解Calabi-Yau流形的quantum Kähler模空间中奇异点周围的monodromy作用，对于刻画BPS谱、wall-crossing现象以及弦景观的整体结构至关重要。作者旨在基于derived category技术与GLSM物理，为flop等几何过渡情形下的monodromy提供一个严格且可计算的框架。

Method: The authors employ the grade restriction rule and window subcategories from derived category theory to isolate admissible brane charges under analytic continuation. They compute the hemisphere partition function $Z_{\\text{hem}}$ for both abelian and nonabelian Gauged Linear Sigma Models (GLSMs), which encodes the central charges of B-branes and thus determines the monodromy action on the charge lattice. By analyzing the explicit form of the discriminant locus in the quantum Kähler moduli space, they relate monodromy matrices to the fundamental group $\\pi_1$ of complements of nested torus links, enabling concrete refinements in specific examples.
\n\n
作者采用derived category理论中的grade restriction rule和window subcategories来分离在解析延拓下允许的brane电荷。他们计算了abelian和nonabelian Gauged Linear Sigma Models (GLSMs)的hemisphere partition function $Z_{\\text{hem}}$，该函数编码了B-brane的central charges，从而确定了电荷格上的monodromy作用。通过分析quantum Kähler模空间中discriminant locus的具体形式，他们将monodromy矩阵与nested torus links补集的基本群 $\\pi_1$ 联系起来，从而在多个例子中实现了具体细化。

Result: The paper establishes a general formula for the monodromy action on the B-brane charge lattice in terms of the hemisphere partition function. In explicit Calabi-Yau threefold flop examples, the monodromy matrices are refined using the geometry of discriminant loci and shown to correspond to elements of the fundamental group of nested torus link complements. This yields exact, non-perturbative expressions for monodromies that agree with expectations from homological mirror symmetry and categorical wall-crossing.
\n\n
本文建立了以hemisphere partition function表示的B-brane电荷格上monodromy作用的一般公式。在具体的Calabi-Yau threefold flop例子中，利用discriminant loci的几何结构细化了monodromy矩阵，并证明其对应于nested torus link补集基本群的元素。由此得到了与homological mirror symmetry和categorical wall-crossing预期一致的精确非微扰monodromy表达式。

Conclusion: The interplay between GLSM techniques, derived category methods, and knot-theoretic structures in moduli space provides a powerful toolkit for computing exact monodromies in Calabi-Yau compactifications. This approach bridges physical constructions in string theory with deep mathematical structures in algebraic geometry and low-dimensional topology.
\n\n
GLSM技术、derived category方法与模空间中knot-theoretic结构之间的相互作用，为计算Calabi-Yau紧化中的精确monodromy提供了强有力的工具。这一方法架起了弦论中的物理构造与代数几何及低维拓扑中深层数学结构之间的桥梁。

Abstract: We present exact expressions, based on the grade restriction rule and window categories, for monodromies associated to certain Calabi-Yau threefold flops. We show a general formula for the monodromy action on the lattice of B-brane charges, based on the hemisphere partition function for abelian and nonabelian gauged linear sigma models. We exploit the explicit form of the discriminant in the quantum Kähler moduli to further refine the form of the monodromies, in several examples, using their relation to the fundamental group of nested torus links.

本文证明了最近提出的一种新的规范多重态在$(2, 2)$超对称sigma模型中等价于Large Vector Multiplet (LVM)的约束形式或部分对偶形式。使用该多重态进行规范作用会得到一个耦合的$(2, 2)$ $βγ$系统与sigma模型。

Abstract: The Large Vector Multiple (LVM) is the relevant gauge multiplet for gauging isometries acting on both the chiral and the twisted chiral fields in a $(2, 2)$ sigma model. Here we show that a recently proposed new gauge multiplet is a constrained or partially dualized version of the LVM. ### [40] [The Classical Gravitational Impulse at High Energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18544)
*Michael Saavedra*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper computes the all-orders-in-$G_N$ gravitational impulse for two ultrarelativistic massive scalars, resumming large $G_N s$ corrections via 4- and 5-point amplitudes in the small-mass regime ($-t \\sim m^2$), recovering classical high-energy results and predicting the leading high-energy behavior up to 11th post-Minkowski (PM) order.
\n\n
本文计算了两个超相对论性有质量标量粒子在牛顿常数 $G_N$ 中的全阶引力冲量，在固定 $G_N s/m b$ 下展开至 $O(m^4/s^2)$。通过在小质量区域（$-t \\sim m^2$）计算 4 点和 5 点散射振幅，对大 $G_N s$ 修正进行重求和，恢复了高能下的经典结果，并预测了后闵可夫斯基（post-Minkowski, PM）展开至第 11 阶的主导高能行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand classical gravitational dynamics in the ultrarelativistic regime through quantum scattering amplitudes, bridging quantum field theory with classical general relativity. Specifically, the authors aim to resum large $G_N s$ contributions that dominate at high energies and connect them to known classical results in the post-Minkowski expansion and gravitational radiation.
\n\n
动机是通过量子散射振幅理解超相对论区域中的经典引力动力学，从而在量子场论与经典广义相对论之间建立桥梁。作者特别旨在对高能下主导的大 $G_N s$ 贡献进行重求和，并将其与后闵可夫斯基展开中的已知经典结果及引力辐射联系起来。

Method: The method involves computing 4- and 5-point scattering amplitudes of massive scalars in the limit $-t \\sim m^2$, where $t$ is the Mandelstam variable and $m$ the particle mass. These amplitudes are used within the KMOC (Kosower–Maybee–O’Connell) formalism to compute the classical gravitational impulse. The large mass and high-energy limits are taken to isolate classical contributions, and a resummation of terms proportional to $(G_N s)^n$ is performed to all orders in $G_N$, yielding predictions for high-order PM coefficients.
\n\n
方法包括在极限 $-t \\sim m^2$（其中 $t$ 为 Mandelstam 变量，$m$ 为粒子质量）下计算有质量标量粒子的 4 点和 5 点散射振幅。这些振幅被用于 KMOC（Kosower–Maybee–O’Connell）形式中以计算经典引力冲量。通过取大质量与高能极限以分离出经典贡献，并对所有 $G_N$ 阶次中正比于 $(G_N s)^n$ 的项进行重求和，从而对高阶后闵可夫斯基（PM）系数做出预测。

Result: The resummed impulse agrees precisely with existing post-Minkowski results and reproduces known radiated energy in the massless limit. Moreover, the authors predict the leading high-energy scaling behavior of the gravitational impulse up to the eleventh post-Minkowski order, providing new data for the PM expansion beyond current computational reach via traditional methods.
\n\n
重求和后的冲量与现有的后闵可夫斯基结果精确一致，并在无质量极限下复现了已知的辐射能量。此外，作者预测了引力冲量在高能下的主导标度行为，直至第十一阶后闵可夫斯基（PM）展开，为传统方法目前无法企及的 PM 展开提供了新数据。

Conclusion: The work demonstrates that quantum scattering amplitudes, when combined with the KMOC framework and appropriate classical limits, can efficiently resum high-energy gravitational interactions and provide access to very high orders in the post-Minkowski expansion, offering a powerful tool for classical gravity from quantum principles.
\n\n
该工作表明，当结合 KMOC 框架并在适当经典极限下处理时，量子散射振幅能够高效地对高能引力相互作用进行重求和，并获得后闵可夫斯基展开中极高阶的信息，从而为从量子原理出发研究经典引力提供了一种强有力的工具。

Abstract: We compute the gravitational impulse for two classical massive scalars in the ultrarelativistic limit to all orders in Newton's constant $G_N$ at fixed $G_N s/m b$ to $O(m^4/s^2)$. By computing the 4 and 5-point scattering amplitudes in the small-mass regime of $-t\sim m^2$, we are able to resum all large $G_N s$ corrections. Applying the KMOC formula for the impulse and taking the large mass limit, we recover the classical result at high energies. This resummation is in complete agreement with known results in the post-Minkowski expansion, and in the massless limit we recover previous results for the radiated energy. We use this resummed amplitude to predict the leading high-energy behavior of the PM expansion to eleventh post-Minkowski order.

</details>


### [41] [Field Theory Models for a Holographic Superconductor in Two Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18628)
*Salvatore Santoro,Roberto Auzzi,Stefano Bolognesi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper studies holographic superconductors modeled by 2D CFTs with Robin boundary conditions inducing order parameter condensation. Using modular invariance and large-$c$ factorization, it analytically reproduces the phase diagram of the zero-winding sector and matches near-critical behavior to Ginzburg–Landau theory. It also proposes a field-theoretic toy model for fractional vortices, interpreted as a fractional Little–Parks effect.

本文研究由 Robin 边界条件诱导序参量凝聚的全息超导体模型，该模型基于二维共形场论（2D CFT）。利用模不变性（modular invariance）和大中心荷（large-$c$）因子化假设，解析复现了零绕数扇区（zero-winding sector）的相图，并将临界点附近的行为与 Ginzburg–Landau 理论匹配。此外，文章还提出了一个具有分数磁通涡旋的场论玩具模型，并将其解释为分数 Little–Parks 效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand holographic superconductors from a purely field-theoretic perspective, without relying on bulk gravitational computations. Specifically, the authors aim to derive the phase structure and critical behavior of such systems using CFT techniques like modular invariance and large-$c$ factorization, and to explore the origin of exotic features such as fractional flux vortices within boundary quantum field theory.
\n\n
动机在于从纯场论角度理解全息超导体，而不依赖于体时空（bulk）引力计算。作者特别希望利用共形场论（CFT）技术（如模不变性和大中心荷因子化）推导此类系统的相结构和临界行为，并在边界量子场论框架内探索分数磁通涡旋等奇异现象的起源。

Method: The authors consider a two-dimensional CFT deformed by a relevant double-trace operator, which implements a Robin boundary condition in the dual gravitational picture. They assume large central charge $c$ so that factorization holds, enabling a saddle-point analysis. Modular invariance of the torus partition function is used to relate low- and high-temperature regimes, yielding an analytic expression for the phase transition. Near-critical scaling of the condensate is matched to a Ginzburg–Landau effective action. Additionally, they construct a toy model exhibiting fractional vortices and analyze it as a fractional version of the Little–Parks effect.
\n\n
作者考虑一个被相关双迹算符（relevant double-trace operator）形变的二维 CFT，该形变在对偶引力图像中对应 Robin 边界条件。他们假设中心荷 $c$ 很大，使得因子化成立，从而可进行鞍点分析。通过环面配分函数的模不变性关联低温与高温区域，获得相变的解析表达式。将凝聚体在临界点附近的标度行为与 Ginzburg–Landau 有效作用量匹配。此外，他们构建了一个展现分数涡旋的玩具模型，并将其分析为 Little–Parks 效应的分数版本。

Result: The paper analytically reproduces the phase diagram of the zero-winding sector of the holographic superconductor using modular invariance, confirming the second-order phase transition at a critical temperature $T_c$. The condensate's near-critical behavior scales as $\\langle \\mathcal{O} \\rangle \\sim (T_c - T)^{1/2}$, consistent with mean-field Ginzburg–Landau theory. Furthermore, the proposed toy model demonstrates that fractional magnetic flux quantization can arise in field theory through topological sectors analogous to those in superconducting rings, interpreted as a fractional Little–Parks effect.
\n\n
本文利用模不变性解析复现了全息超导体零绕数扇区的相图，确认在临界温度 $T_c$ 处发生二级相变。凝聚体的临界行为满足 $\\langle \\mathcal{O} \\rangle \\sim (T_c - T)^{1/2}$，与平均场 Ginzburg–Landau 理论一致。此外，所提出的玩具模型表明，分数磁通量子化可通过类似于超导环中的拓扑扇区在场论中出现，被解释为分数 Little–Parks 效应。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that key features of holographic superconductors—such as condensation triggered by boundary conditions, second-order phase transitions, and fractional vortices—can be captured entirely within two-dimensional boundary CFTs using non-perturbative tools like modular invariance and large-$c$ factorization. \n\n
本研究表明，全息超导体的关键特征——如由边界条件触发的凝聚、二级相变以及分数涡旋——完全可以利用二维边界 CFT 中的非微扰工具（如模不变性和大-$c$ 因子化）来描述。这为全息超导性提供了纯场论基础，并为在不引入引力对偶的情况下建模奇异超导现象开辟了新路径。

Abstract: We investigate field theory models of holographic superconductors in which the condensation of the order parameter is induced by a Robin boundary condition. Assuming large-$c$ factorization, we study the phase diagram of a two-dimensional CFT deformed by a relevant double-trace perturbation. Using modular invariance, we relate the high- and low-temperature phases, reproducing analytically the results for the zero-winding sector of the holographic model. Moreover, we match the near-critical behaviour of the condensate with an effective Ginzburg--Landau field theory description. Another important feature of the holographic superconductor is the presence of vortices that carry fractional magnetic flux. We investigate a field theory toy model with similar properties and interpret it as a fractional Little--Parks effect.

### [42] [Five legs @ three loops: N=4 sYM amplitude near mass-shell](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17056)
*Andrei V. Belitsky,Leonid V. Bork,Roman N. Lee,Vladimir A. Smirnov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We compute the three-loop five-point scattering amplitude of nearly massless W-bosons in planar $\\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM using six-dimensional unitarity cuts and dimensional reduction. The result exhibits exponentiation of both infrared and finite parts, with the infrared double logarithm governed by the octagon anomalous dimension. Each of the three kinematic structures has its own 't Hooft coupling-dependent function.
\n\n
我们在平面 $\\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM 中利用六维幺正切割和维度约化方法，计算了近无质量 W 玻色子的三圈五点散射振幅。结果展现出红外和有限部分的指数化行为，其中红外双重对数由 octagon 异常维度控制。三种独立运动学结构各自具有依赖于 't Hooft 耦合的函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to extend the understanding of non-planar and multi-leg scattering amplitudes in maximally supersymmetric Yang-Mills ($\\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM) theory beyond two loops. Specifically, it investigates the structure of infrared divergences and finite terms in a five-point amplitude on the Coulomb branch, probing the universality of infrared behavior via the octagon anomalous dimension and exploring how kinematic dependence factorizes at higher loops.
\n\n
本文旨在将对最大超对称杨-米尔斯理论（$\\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM）中非平面及多腿散射振幅的理解从两圈推广到更高阶。特别地，它研究了Coulomb分支上五点振幅的红外发散与有限项的结构，通过 octagon 异常维度检验红外行为的普适性，并探索高圈下运动学依赖如何分解。

Method: The authors use the unitarity-cut sewing technique in six-dimensional $\\mathcal{N}=(1,1)$ super-Yang-Mills theory to construct a basis of master integrals. Dimensional reduction from six to four dimensions generates small masses for internal and external lines, allowing access to the Coulomb branch of $\\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM by taking the massless limit of propagators. Explicit integral results from a companion paper are used to assemble the full three-loop amplitude, which is then analyzed for exponentiation properties and kinematic dependence.
\n\n
作者在六维 $\\mathcal{N}=(1,1)$ 超杨-米尔斯理论中使用幺正切割缝合技术构建主积分基。通过从六维到四维的维度约化，为内线和外线生成小质量，再通过对传播子取无质量极限进入 $\\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM 的 Coulomb 分支。利用配套论文中计算出的显式积分结果，组装完整的三圈振幅，并分析其指数化性质与运动学依赖。

Result: The three-loop five-point amplitude is expressed in a compact form that confirms exponentiation of both infrared and finite contributions. The coefficient of the infrared double logarithm matches the octagon anomalous dimension, confirming universality. \n\n
三圈五点振幅被表示为一个简洁形式，确认了红外和有限部分的指数化。红外双重对数的系数与 octagon 异常维度一致，验证了普适性。与两圈情形不同，振幅的三个独立运动学张量结构各自携带不同的 't Hooft 耦合 $\\lambda = g_{\\text{YM}}^2 N_c$ 函数。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates that while infrared structure remains universal and governed by the octagon anomalous dimension, the finite part of multi-leg amplitudes at three loops exhibits richer kinematic dependence than previously observed. This suggests that the notion of a single coupling-dependent function per amplitude must be refined for amplitudes with more than four legs beyond two loops in $\\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM.
\n\n
本工作表明，尽管红外结构仍由 octagon 异常维度控制并保持普适性，但三圈多腿振幅的有限部分展现出比以往更丰富的运动学依赖性。这表明，在 $\\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM 中，对于超过四腿且高于两圈的振幅，每个振幅对应单一耦合函数的概念需要被修正。

Abstract: We present a three-loop analysis of the scattering amplitude of five nearly massless W-bosons in planar maximally supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory. The basis of the master integrals is established, making use of the unitarity-cut sewing technique in six-dimensional N=(1,1) super-Yang-Mills theory. Its dimensional reduction down to four allows us to generate masses for internal and external states. We descend on the special Coulomb branch of maximally supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory by setting all propagator masses to zero. Employing explicit expressions for all integrals that we calculated in a companion paper, we find a concise representation for this infrared-sensitive observable. We confirm its exponentiation, both for infrared and finite terms. The infrared double logarithm manifests the anticipated universality through the octagon anomalous dimension as its governing coefficient. Unlike our previous two-loop result, this consideration reveals that each of the three independent kinematic structures furnishing the amplitude possesses its own function of 't Hooft coupling.

### [43] [$J\bar{J}$-deformation as a Riemann bilinear dressing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18631)
*Kangning Liu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper reformulates conformal perturbation theory for $J\\bar{J}$-deformed CFTs by interpreting the deformation as a dressing of operators, enabled by the Riemann bilinear identity. This approach consistently reproduces both bare and renormalized perturbation theory, yields modular-invariant expressions for deformed partition functions on tori and higher-genus surfaces via kernel integrals, computes the flow of conformal weights and conserved charges, and proposes a criterion for constructing dressed operators using modular $S$-transformation—validated through $O(2, 2)$ theories and TsT string backgrounds.
\n\n
本文通过将 $J\\bar{J}$-deformed CFT 中的共形微扰理论重新表述为算符的 dressing，利用 Riemann bilinear identity 将形变转化为 dressing 和高亏格上的大环积分。该方法同时匹配裸微扰和重整化微扰理论，得到环面及高亏格黎曼面上保持模不变性（或协变性）的核积分形式的配分函数，计算了共形权重与守恒荷沿形变的流，并基于此流与模 $S$-变换提出构造 dressed 算符的判据，最后在 $O(2, 2)$ 理论和 TsT 背景下的弦理论中验证了该形式体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard conformal perturbation theory for $J\\bar{J}$-deformed CFTs faces challenges in maintaining consistency between bare and renormalized expansions, especially on higher-genus Riemann surfaces where modular properties are crucial. The authors aim to develop a unified framework that naturally incorporates modular invariance/covariance and provides a geometric interpretation of the deformation via operator dressing, thereby clarifying the structure of deformed correlation functions and partition functions beyond the sphere.
\n\n
标准的 $J\\bar{J}$-deformed CFT 共形微扰理论在裸展开与重整化展开之间的一致性上存在困难，尤其在高亏格黎曼面上，模性质至关重要。作者旨在构建一个统一框架，自然地纳入模不变性/协变性，并通过算符 dressing 对形变给出几何诠释，从而澄清形变后关联函数与配分函数在球面以外的结构。

Method: The core method employs the Riemann bilinear identity to re-express the $J\\bar{J}$ deformation as an operator dressing combined with a large-cycle integral on higher-genus surfaces. This reformulation allows the deformed partition function $Z(\\lambda)$ to be written as a kernel integral: $$Z(\\lambda) = \\int \\mathcal{K}(\\lambda; \\tau, \\bar{\\tau}) Z_{\\text{CFT}}(\\tau, \\bar{\\tau}) \\, d\\tau d\\bar{\\tau},$$ which preserves modular invariance or covariance. The flow equations for conformal weights $h(\\lambda), \\bar{h}(\\lambda)$ and conserved charges are derived from this dressed picture. A construction criterion for physical dressed operators is then proposed using the modular $S$-transformation property of the deformed theory.
\n\n
核心方法是利用 Riemann bilinear identity 将 $J\\bar{J}$ 形变重写为算符 dressing 与高亏格面上的大环积分之和。这一重构使得形变后的配分函数 $Z(\\lambda)$ 可表示为核积分：$$Z(\\lambda) = \\int \\mathcal{K}(\\lambda; \\tau, \\bar{\\tau}) Z_{\\text{CFT}}(\\tau, \\bar{\\tau}) \\, d\\tau d\\bar{\\tau},$$ 该表达式保持模不变性或协变性。从该 dressed 图像出发，推导出共形权重 $h(\\lambda), \\bar{h}(\\lambda)$ 与守恒荷的流方程，并基于形变理论的模 $S$-变换性质提出物理 dressed 算符的构造判据。

Result: The authors successfully compute deformed partition functions on torus and higher-genus Riemann surfaces as modular-covariant kernel integrals. They derive explicit flow equations for conformal dimensions and conserved charges under $J\\bar{J}$ deformation. Their proposed criterion for dressed operators is validated in solvable examples: $O(2, 2)$ current algebra models and string theory on TsT (T-duality–shift–T-duality) transformed backgrounds, confirming consistency with known results and modular symmetry.
\n\n
作者成功将环面及高亏格黎曼面上的形变配分函数计算为保持模协变性的核积分，推导出 $J\\bar{J}$ 形变下共形维数与守恒荷的显式流方程。所提出的 dressed 算符构造判据在可解模型（$O(2, 2)$ 流代数模型及 TsT（T-对偶–平移–T-对偶）变换背景下的弦理论）中得到验证，与已知结果及模对称性一致。

Conclusion: The dressing formalism provides a coherent and modular-symmetric framework for $J\\bar{J}$-deformed CFTs beyond perturbation theory on the sphere. By linking the deformation to geometric structures on Riemann surfaces via the Riemann bilinear identity, it resolves ambiguities in traditional perturbative approaches and offers a systematic method to construct physical observables in deformed theories, with broad applicability to integrable deformations and holographic duals like TsT backgrounds.
\n\n
该 dressing 形式体系为球面以外的 $J\\bar{J}$-deformed CFT 提供了一个自洽且具有模对称性的框架。通过 Riemann bilinear identity 将形变与黎曼面上的几何结构联系起来，解决了传统微扰方法中的模糊性，并为形变理论中物理可观测量的系统构造提供了方法，在可积形变及 TsT 背景等全息对偶中有广泛应用前景。

Abstract: We propose a reformulation of the conformal perturbation theory of the correlation functions in $J\bar{J}$-deformed CFTs as a dressing on the deformed operators, that matches both bare and renormalized perturbation theory. The key is to use the Riemann bilinear identity to convert the deformation into a dressing and a large-cycle integral for higher genus. Based on the proposal, we calculate the deformation of partition functions on the torus and higher genus Riemann surfaces, which can be written as kernel integrals that preserve modular invariance or covariance. We also calculate the flow of the conformal weights and conserved charges along the deformation. Based on this flow and the modular $S$-transformation, we propose a criterion for constructing dressed operators. We test our formalism and results by studying the $O(2, 2)$ theories and strings on the TsT background.

### [44] [Modular Lower Bounds on Reeh-Schlieder State Preparation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18640)
*Javier Blanco-Romero,Florina Almenares Mendoza*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This note establishes a quantitative, model-independent lower bound on the cost of preparing arbitrary target states from the vacuum using operators localized in arbitrarily small spacetime regions, based on the Reeh-Schlieder theorem. The bound is expressed via modular energy: states with deeply negative modular energy require large local operators or incur significant postselection overhead. Explicit forms are derived using known modular Hamiltonians (e.g., Bisognano-Wichmann for wedges, Casini-Huerta-Myers for CFT balls). Local unitaries cannot access negative modular energy sectors, necessitating nonunitary or postselected operations, thereby complementing results on vacuum embezzlement in type III von Neumann algebras.
\n\n
本文基于Reeh-Schlieder定理，建立了一个模型无关的、定量的下界，用于刻画使用任意小时空区域内局域算符从真空制备任意目标态所需的成本。该界限通过模能量（modular energy）表达：具有深度负模能量的目标态需要大的局域算符或导致显著的后选择（postselection）开销。利用已知的模哈密顿量（例如，Bisognano-Wichmann对应于楔形区域，Casini-Huerta-Myers公式对应于共形场论中的球形区域），可得到显式形式。局域幺正操作无法触及负模能量区域，必须借助非幺正或后选择操作，从而为III型冯·诺依曼代数中的真空窃取（vacuum embezzlement）现象提供了互补的制备成本界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Reeh-Schlieder theorem guarantees state approximability from the vacuum using arbitrarily localized operators but offers no quantitative measure of the operational cost. This work aims to fill that gap by deriving a universal, quantitative preparation cost bound rooted in Tomita-Takesaki theory, which applies across all quantum field theories with type III local algebras. Understanding this cost is crucial for quantum information tasks in QFT, such as state preparation, teleportation, and the limitations of local operations.
\n\n
Reeh-Schlieder定理保证了可以使用任意局域化的算符从真空逼近任意态，但并未提供操作成本的定量度量。本工作旨在通过Tomita-Takesaki理论导出一个普适的、定量的制备成本界限，以填补这一空白，该界限适用于所有具有III型局域代数的量子场论。理解这一成本对于QFT中的量子信息任务（如态制备、量子隐形传态以及局域操作的局限性）至关重要。

Method: The paper employs Tomita-Takesaki modular theory. It starts from the standard estimate $\\|\\Delta^{1/2} A \\Omega\\| \\leq \\|A \\Omega\\|$ for $A$ in a local algebra $\\mathcal{A}(\\mathcal{O})$, where $\\Delta$ is the modular operator and $\\Omega$ the vacuum. By decomposing a target state $|\\psi\\rangle$ into modular energy eigenstates, the norm constraint implies that components with modular energy $K < -\\kappa$ must be suppressed unless the operator norm $\\|A\\|$ is exponentially large in $\\kappa$. After rescaling $A$ to a contraction (e.g., via postselection), this translates into an exponential lower bound on the success probability (overhead). The method then specializes this general bound using explicit modular Hamiltonians: $K = 2\\pi H_{\\text{boost}}$ for Rindler wedges (Bisognano-Wichmann) and $K = 2\\pi \\int_B T_{00}^{\\text{CFT}} \\zeta^0 d^{d-1}x$ for spherical regions in CFTs (Casini-Huerta-Myers).
\n\n
本文采用Tomita-Takesaki模理论方法。从局域代数$\\mathcal{A}(\\mathcal{O})$中算符$A$的标准估计$\\|\\Delta^{1/2} A \\Omega\\| \\leq \\|A \\Omega\\|$出发，其中$\\Delta$是模算符，$\\Omega$是真空态。通过将目标态$|\\psi\\rangle$分解为模能量本征态，范数约束表明：除非算符范数$\\|A\\|$在$\\kappa$上呈指数级增长，否则模能量$K < -\\kappa$的分量必然被压低。将$A$重缩放为收缩算符（例如通过后选择）后，这转化为成功概率（开销）的指数级下界。随后，该方法利用显式的模哈密顿量对这一普适界限进行具体化：对于Rindler楔形区域，$K = 2\\pi H_{\\text{boost}}$（Bisognano-Wichmann）；对于共形场论中的球形区域，$K = 2\\pi \\int_B T_{00}^{\\text{CFT}} \\zeta^0 d^{d-1}x$（Casini-Huerta-Myers）。

Result: The main result is a quantitative preparation cost bound: to prepare a state with a component of modular energy less than $-\\kappa$, any local operator $A \\in \\mathcal{A}(\\mathcal{O})$ must satisfy $\\|A\\| \\geq e^{\\kappa/2} |\\langle \\psi | A \\Omega \\rangle|$. If $A$ is implemented as a physical operation with postselection, the success probability $p$ is bounded by $p \\leq e^{-\\kappa} \\|\\psi_{\\text{neg}}\\|^2$, where $\\|\\psi_{\\text{neg}}\\|$ is the norm of the negative-modular-energy part of $|\\psi\\rangle$. Explicitly, for a wedge, this becomes a statement about boost energy; for a CFT ball, it becomes a bound involving the integrated stress tensor. Furthermore, it is shown that the set of states reachable by local unitaries has nonnegative modular energy.
\n\n
主要结果是一个定量的制备成本界限：为了制备一个包含模能量小于$-\\kappa$分量的态，任何局域算符$A \\in \\mathcal{A}(\\mathcal{O})$必须满足$\\|A\\| \\geq e^{\\kappa/2} |\\langle \\psi | A \\Omega \\rangle|$。如果$A$通过带有后选择的物理操作实现，则成功概率$p$满足$p \\leq e^{-\\kappa} \\|\\psi_{\\text{neg}}\\|^2$，其中$\\|\\psi_{\\text{neg}}\\|$是$|\\psi\\rangle$中负模能量部分的范数。具体而言，对于楔形区域，该界限转化为关于boost能量的陈述；对于CFT中的球形区域，则转化为涉及积分应力张量的界限。此外，文中还证明了局域幺正操作所能到达的态集具有非负模能量。

Conclusion: The work provides a rigorous, information-theoretic quantification of the Reeh-Schlieder theorem's operational implications. It shows that the "cost" of accessing deep vacuum correlations is exponential in the depth of negative modular energy. This establishes a fundamental limitation on local state preparation in QFT and clarifies the role of postselection and nonunitarity. The results complement the phenomenon of vacuum embezzlement by providing a dual perspective: while embezzling allows approximate reuse of the vacuum, preparing states with negative modular energy is inherently costly.
\n\n
本工作为Reeh-Schlieder定理的操作含义提供了严格的信息论量化。研究表明，访问深层真空关联的“成本”随负模能量的深度呈指数增长。这确立了QFT中局域态制备的根本性限制，并阐明了后选择与非幺正性的作用。这些结果通过提供一个对偶视角补充了真空窃取（vacuum embezzlement）现象：尽管窃取允许近似重复利用真空，但制备具有负模能量的态本质上是高成本的。

Abstract: The Reeh-Schlieder theorem says that every target vector can be approximated from the vacuum by an operator localized in an arbitrarily small spacetime region, but it gives no quantitative cost for doing so. This note isolates a standard Tomita-Takesaki estimate as a model-independent preparation bound. Targets with deeply negative modular energy require large local operators. After rescaling such an operator to a physical contraction, the same estimate becomes a lower bound on postselection overhead. In geometries where the modular Hamiltonian is known, the bound becomes explicit. Bisognano-Wichmann turns it into a boost energy statement for wedges, and the Casini-Huerta-Myers formula gives a stress-tensor version for bounded regions of conformal field theories. Local unitaries can only reach states of nonnegative modular energy. Negative modular sectors require nonunitary or postselected outcomes, giving a preparation cost bound that complements vacuum embezzlement in type III local algebras.

</details>


### [45] [From classical Lax ODEs to quantum integrable theories: the moduli](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18695)
*Davide Fioravanti,Marco Rossi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper establishes a correspondence between classical integrable PDEs—specifically a generalized sinh-Gordon equation with $2N-1$ complex moduli—and quantum integrable systems via the ODE/IM (Ordinary Differential Equation/Integrable Model) correspondence. It shows that connection coefficients (Wronskians) of solutions to an associated linear problem satisfy functional relations identifying eigenvalues of Baxter $Q$ and $T$ operators, leading directly to Y-systems and thermodynamic Bethe ansatz (TBA) equations without invoking scattering theory. The dependence on moduli modifies these relations, and in the zero-momentum limit, the framework describes the quantum homogeneous sine-Gordon model, relevant to strong-coupling scattering amplitudes in $\mathcal{N} = 4$ SYM and dual Wilson loops in $AdS_3$. Two conjectures by Zamolodchikov are proven as corollaries.
\n\n
本文通过ODE/IM（常微分方程/可积模型）对应关系，建立了经典可积偏微分方程（特别是含 $2N-1$ 个复模的广义sinh-Gordon方程）与量子可积系统之间的联系。文章表明，相关线性问题解的联络系数（Wronskian）满足特定函数关系，在补充适当渐近行为后，可识别为Baxter算符 $Q$ 和转移矩阵 $T$ 的本征值，并直接导出Y-系统和热力学Bethe Ansatz（TBA）方程，而无需经过散射理论。这些关系因对模的依赖而被修正；在零动量极限下，该框架完整描述了量子齐次sine-Gordon模型，这对应于 $\mathcal{N} = 4$ SYM 在强耦合下的规范场散射振幅或其对偶的 $AdS_3$ 中零多边形类光Wilson圈。作为该对应关系的直接推论，Zamolodchikov的两个猜想也得以证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the desire to understand quantum integrable models through classical integrable structures, leveraging the ODE/IM correspondence. Traditional approaches often rely on scattering theory or Bethe ansatz techniques derived from S-matrices. This work seeks a more intrinsic, geometric characterization of quantum states via monodromy data of associated linear problems, especially in contexts like $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM where integrability plays a central role at strong coupling. The inclusion of moduli allows for a richer structure that captures physical deformations and enables direct access to observables such as scattering amplitudes.
\n\n
该工作的动机源于通过经典可积结构理解量子可积模型的愿望，特别是借助ODE/IM对应关系。传统方法通常依赖于散射理论或从S矩阵导出的Bethe Ansatz技术。本文旨在通过相关线性问题的单值性数据（monodromy data），对量子态给出一种更内在、几何化的刻画，尤其适用于 $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM 这类在强耦合下具有中心可积性的理论。引入模参数使得结构更加丰富，能够捕捉物理形变，并直接获得散射振幅等可观测量。

Method: The method centers on analyzing a generalized sinh-Gordon equation arising as the compatibility condition of a matrix linear differential system. The authors compute Wronskians (connection coefficients) between different solutions of this system. Using the ODE/IM correspondence, they interpret these Wronskians as eigenvalues of Baxter’s $Q$-operators and the transfer matrix $T$. By imposing suitable asymptotic conditions on the solutions, they derive functional relations that lead to the Y-system and, subsequently, the thermodynamic Bethe ansatz (TBA) equations. Crucially, all relations are modified by the presence of $2N-1$ complex moduli, which parametrize the space of monodromy data invariantly. In the zero-momentum sector, this construction is matched to the quantum homogeneous sine-Gordon model.
\n\n
该方法的核心是分析作为矩阵线性微分系统相容性条件出现的广义sinh-Gordon方程。作者计算该系统不同解之间的Wronskian（联络系数），并利用ODE/IM对应关系，将这些Wronskian解释为Baxter $Q$ 算符和转移矩阵 $T$ 的本征值。通过施加适当的渐近条件，他们导出函数关系，进而得到Y-系统及热力学Bethe Ansatz（TBA）方程。关键在于，所有关系都因 $2N-1$ 个复模的存在而被修正，这些模不变地参数化了单值性空间。在零动量扇区，该构造与量子齐次sine-Gordon模型相匹配。

Result: The paper derives modified functional relations for Wronskians that incorporate dependence on $2N-1$ complex moduli, yielding a monodromy-invariant parametrization of the solution space. From these, Y-system and TBA equations are obtained directly, bypassing scattering theory. In the zero-momentum limit, the framework exactly describes the quantum homogeneous sine-Gordon model, providing a non-perturbative formulation of scattering amplitudes in $\mathcal{N} = 4$ SYM at strong coupling and their holographic duals—null polygonal Wilson loops in $AdS_3$. Additionally, two long-standing conjectures by Zamolodchikov are rigorously proven as immediate consequences of the established correspondence.
\n\n
本文导出了包含 $2N-1$ 个复模依赖性的Wronskian修正函数关系，从而给出了单值性不变的解空间参数化。由此直接获得Y-系统和TBA方程，无需经过散射理论。在零动量极限下，该框架精确描述了量子齐次sine-Gordon模型，为 $\mathcal{N} = 4$ SYM 在强耦合下的散射振幅及其全息对偶——$AdS_3$ 中的零多边形Wilson圈——提供了非微扰表述。此外，Zamolodchikov提出的两个长期猜想也被作为该对应关系的直接推论而严格证明。

Conclusion: The work demonstrates that classical integrable PDEs with moduli provide a powerful and intrinsic route to quantum integrable models via the ODE/IM correspondence. By encoding quantum data in the monodromy of associated linear problems, it offers a scattering-free derivation of key structures like Y-systems and TBA equations. This approach not only deepens the understanding of integrability in gauge/gravity duality but also resolves foundational conjectures in integrable field theory, highlighting the unifying role of monodromy data and moduli spaces.
\n\n
本工作表明，带模的经典可积偏微分方程通过ODE/IM对应关系，为通向量子可积模型提供了一条强大且内在的路径。通过将量子数据编码在相关线性问题的单值性中，该方法无需散射理论即可导出Y-系统和TBA方程等关键结构。这一方法不仅深化了对规范/引力对偶中可积性的理解，还解决了可积场论中的基础性猜想，凸显了单值性数据与模空间的统一作用。

Abstract: The general idea of this paper is to start from a classical integrable (partial differential) equation which arises as a compatibility condition for a matrix linear differential problem. For definitiveness' sake, a generalised sinh-Gordon equation depending on $2N-1$ complex coefficients or moduli is considered. Then, the connexion coefficients (Wronskians) of different solutions to this problem satisfy, in the spirit of the Ordinary Differential Equation/Integrable Model correspondence, functional relations, which can be considered, -- if supplemented by suitable asymptotic behaviours --, as identifying a specific state of a quantum integrable model: in fact they are the eigenvalues of extensions of Baxter operators $Q$ and $T$, the transfer matrix. Moreover, Y-system and (implementing the asymptotic conditions) thermodynamic Bethe Ansatz equations originate from them, without any passage through the scattering theory, and providing an invariant parametrisation of the monodromy space. The crucial novelty is the modification of all the relations because of their dependence on the moduli. For zero momentum, they fully describe physically the quantum homogeneous sine-Gordon model, {\it i.e.} scattering amplitudes of gauge fields in $\mathcal{N} = 4$ SYM at strong coupling or their dual null polygonal light-like Wilson loops in $AdS_3$. As a direct consequence of the correspondence, two Zamolodchikov's conjectures, based on previous results, are also proven.

</details>


### [46] [Signatures of Quantum Chaos in the D1D5 System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18725)
*Haoyu Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper studies second-order lifting matrices in the D1D5 CFT and finds that at finite $N$, non-planar contributions induce mixing between single- and multi-cycle states, leading to level repulsion and random-matrix statistics; in contrast, the planar large-$N$ limit exhibits suppressed mixing and Poisson-like level spacing.
\n\n
本文研究了 D1D5 CFT 中的二阶 lifting 矩阵，发现在有限 $N$ 时，非平面贡献诱导单圈态与多圈态之间的混合，导致能级排斥和随机矩阵统计；相比之下，平面大 $N$ 极限下混合被抑制，呈现出类泊松的能级间距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how quantum chaos, as diagnosed by random-matrix statistics, emerges in holographic CFTs like the D1D5 system. Specifically, the authors aim to connect finite-$N$ effects—particularly non-planar corrections—to the transition from integrable (Poisson) to chaotic (random-matrix) spectral statistics in near-BPS sectors.
\n\n
动机在于理解量子混沌（通过随机矩阵统计诊断）如何在全息 CFT（如 D1D5 系统）中出现。作者特别旨在将有限 $N$ 效应——尤其是非平面修正——与近 BPS 区域中谱统计从可积（泊松）向混沌（随机矩阵）的转变联系起来。

Method: The authors compute second-order lifting matrices for low-energy near-BPS states in the D1D5 CFT at both finite $N=3$ and in the planar large-$N$ limit with fixed orbifold conformal weight and R charges. They resolve the spectra by symmetry sectors and analyze the resulting eigenvalue spacing distributions using tools from random matrix theory, comparing Poisson versus Wigner-Dyson statistics.
\n\n
作者在 D1D5 CFT 中对低能近 BPS 态计算了二阶 lifting 矩阵，分别在有限 $N=3$ 和固定轨道共形权重与 R 电荷的平面大 $N$ 极限下进行。他们按对称性分解谱，并利用随机矩阵理论工具分析所得本征值间距分布，比较泊松分布与 Wigner-Dyson 统计。

Result: In the planar large-$N$ limit, mixing between single-cycle and multi-cycle states is suppressed, yielding Poisson-like level statistics within symmetry-resolved sectors. At finite $N=3$, non-planar terms reintroduce this mixing, and the resulting level spacings exhibit repulsion consistent with random-matrix universality classes.
\n\n
在平面大 $N$ 极限下，单圈态与多圈态之间的混合被抑制，在对称性分解的子空间中产生类泊松的能级统计。而在有限 $N=3$ 时，非平面项重新引入该混合，导致能级间距表现出与随机矩阵普适类一致的排斥行为。

Conclusion: Non-planar cycle-structure mixing at finite $N$ drives the transition from integrable to chaotic spectral behavior in low-energy near-BPS sectors of the D1D5 CFT, linking finite-$N$ quantum gravity effects in the dual bulk to the emergence of random-matrix statistics in the boundary theory.
\n\n
在 D1D5 CFT 的低能近 BPS 区域中，有限 $N$ 下的非平面圈结构混合驱动了谱行为从可积向混沌的转变，将对偶体中的有限 $N$ 量子引力效应与边界理论中随机矩阵统计的出现联系起来。

Abstract: We investigate the emergence of random-matrix statistics in the D1D5 CFT by studying second-order lifting matrices in low-energy near-BPS sectors. We compare the $N=3$ finite-$N$ lifting problems with the planar large-$N$ limit at fixed orbifold conformal weight and R charges. In the planar large-$N$ limit at fixed orbifold energy, mixing between single-cycle and multi-cycle states is suppressed, and the symmetry-resolved lifting spectra display Poisson-like level statistics. At finite $N$, non-planar terms restore this mixing between different cycle structures. Within the resulting symmetry-resolved sectors, this finite-$N$ mixing is accompanied by level repulsion consistent with random-matrix behavior. These results suggest that, in the low-energy near-BPS sectors accessible to our analysis, non-planar cycle-structure mixing at finite $N$ is associated with the onset of level repulsion and random-matrix-like spacing statistics.

</details>


### [47] [Static electromagnetic Love tensors of 5-dimensional Myers-Perry black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16792)
*Boyang Yu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates electromagnetic and gravitational perturbations in five-dimensional Myers-Perry black holes, showing that in the static limit, their master equations reduce to Heun equations which belong to a solvable class expressible via hypergeometric functions. The authors reconstruct the gauge field, analyze its asymptotics, and compute the static tidal Love tensor that encodes angular momentum mixing in the response.
\n\n
本文研究了五维Myers-Perry黑洞中的电磁和引力微扰，发现在静态极限下，其主方程归结为一类可解的Heun方程，可用超几何函数精确表达。作者重构了规范场，分析其渐近行为，并计算了刻画角动量混合响应结构的静态潮汐Love张量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding perturbative dynamics of fields around higher-dimensional rotating black holes is crucial for testing general relativity in extra dimensions and exploring holographic dualities. The Myers-Perry solution provides a natural arena for such studies, yet analytic control over perturbations—especially for mixed polarizations—is limited. This work aims to fill this gap by leveraging the separability and exact solvability of the master equations in the static limit.
\n\n
理解高维旋转黑洞周围的场微扰动力学对于检验额外维度中的广义相对论和探索全息对偶至关重要。Myers-Perry解为此类研究提供了自然平台，但对微扰（尤其是混合极化情形）的解析控制仍有限。本文旨在通过利用静态极限下主方程的可分离性和精确可解性来填补这一空白。

Method: The authors separate variables in the master equations governing electromagnetic (Maxwell) and gravitational perturbations on the five-dimensional Myers-Perry background. In the static limit ($\\omega \\to 0$), they show that the electric polarization reduces to a scalar field equation, while magnetic and gravitational sectors yield coupled angular and radial Heun equations. They identify these as belonging to a special subclass solvable in terms of Gauss hypergeometric functions. Using these solutions, they reconstruct the full gauge potential and expand it in modified spherical harmonics to extract coupling between different angular momentum modes. The static tidal Love tensor is then computed iteratively from the asymptotic expansion.
\n\n
作者在五维Myers-Perry背景上对支配电磁（Maxwell）和引力微扰的主方程进行变量分离。在静态极限（$\\omega \\to 0$）下，他们证明电极化部分退化为标量场方程，而磁极化和引力部分则导出角向与径向耦合的Heun方程。他们识别出这些方程属于一类可用Gauss超几何函数求解的特殊子类。利用这些解，他们重构完整的规范势，并在修正球谐函数基底下展开以提取不同角动量模之间的耦合。随后通过渐近展开迭代计算静态潮汐Love张量。

Result: The master equations for magnetic polarization and gravitational perturbations reduce to exactly solvable Heun equations whose solutions are expressed in terms of hypergeometric functions. The reconstructed gauge field exhibits mode mixing: excitation of a source with angular momentum quantum number $\\ell$ induces responses with $\\ell' > \\ell$. The static tidal Love tensor encoding this mixing is computed explicitly via an iterative scheme. A near-zone approximation for the magnetic sector is also outlined.
\n\n
磁极化和引力微扰的主方程归结为精确可解的Heun方程，其解可用超几何函数表示。重构的规范场展现出模混合现象：角动量量子数为$\\ell$的源激发会诱导出$\\ell' > \\ell$的响应。刻画该混合的静态潮汐Love张量通过迭代方案被显式计算。文中还概述了磁极化部分的近区近似。

Conclusion: The static perturbations of five-dimensional Myers-Perry black holes admit exact analytic treatment due to the special structure of their Heun-type master equations. This enables precise computation of response coefficients like the tidal Love tensor and reveals nontrivial angular momentum mixing absent in four dimensions. The results open avenues for studying higher-dimensional black hole responses and may inform effective worldline descriptions in gravitational effective field theory.
\n\n
五维Myers-Perry黑洞的静态微扰因其Heun型主方程的特殊结构而允许精确解析处理。这使得潮汐Love张量等响应系数可被精确计算，并揭示了四维中不存在的非平凡角动量混合。该结果为研究高维黑洞响应开辟了新途径，并可能为引力有效场论中的有效世界线描述提供信息。

Abstract: We study the separable master equations for the electromagnetic and gravitational perturbations in five-dimensional Myers-Perry black holes. In the static limit, while the master equation for the electric polarization of the Maxwell field reduces to that of a massless scalar field, the magnetic polarization and gravitational perturbation yield Heun equations for both its angular and radial components. Remarkably, these Heun equations fall into a special class that admits exact analytic solutions in terms of hypergeometric functions. We reconstruct the gauge field using master fields and study its asymptotic behavior. When expanding the result in the basis of modified spherical harmonics, we find modes with higher angular momentum arise in response to the excitation of sources with lower angular momentum. The static tidal Love tensor that characterizes such mixing structure of the response can be computed iteratively. We also discuss the possible near zone approximation of the master equations for the magnetic polarization.

</details>

### [48] [Thermostats, Not Engines: A New Picture of Halo Gas Regulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16488)
*Hiranya V. Peiris,Andrew Pontzen,Madalina N. Tudorache,Anik Halder,Stephen Thorp,Sinan Deger,Joop Schaye,Matthieu Schaller*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper proposes that black hole feedback imposes an entropy ceiling in massive halos, causing buoyant gas to rise to the virial radius without further energy input. FLAMINGO simulations show that outflow entropy at the virial radius is mass-independent for isotropic thermal feedback but depends on jet solid angle for jet feedback. Above a critical halo mass $M_\rm{crit} \approx 10^{13.5\text{--}14}\, M_\odot$, virial shocks breach this ceiling, leading to renewed star formation in the most massive galaxies, consistent with recent low-redshift observations.
\n\n
本文提出黑洞反馈通过在大质量晕中建立熵上限来调节气体，导致浮力气团无需额外能量输入即可迁移至位力半径。FLAMINGO 模拟表明，在位力半径处，各向同性热反馈产生的外流熵与质量无关，而喷流反馈的外流熵则依赖于被直接加热气体的立体角。当晕质量超过临界值 $M_\rm{crit} \approx 10^{13.5\text{--}14}\, M_\odot$ 时，位力激波会突破该熵上限，从而预测最大质量星系中的恒星形成活动将重新激活，这与最新的低红移恒星形成率和形态学观测证据一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to understand how black hole feedback suppresses star formation in massive galaxies and why some of the most massive systems show signs of rejuvenated star formation. Traditional models often invoke continuous energy injection, but this work seeks a more energetically economical mechanism based on entropy regulation and buoyancy-driven transport.
\n\n
动机源于理解黑洞反馈如何抑制大质量星系中的恒星形成，以及为何部分最大质量系统显示出恒星形成再激活的迹象。传统模型通常假设持续的能量注入，而本文旨在寻找一种基于熵调控和浮力驱动输运的更节能机制。

Method: The authors analyze the FLAMINGO cosmological hydrodynamical simulations, comparing different black hole feedback prescriptions—specifically isotropic thermal feedback versus anisotropic jet feedback. They examine the entropy profiles of outflowing gas at the virial radius across a range of halo masses and link deviations from the entropy ceiling to the onset of virial shocks and subsequent star formation rejuvenation.
\n\n
作者分析了 FLAMINGO 宇宙学流体动力学模拟，比较了不同的黑洞反馈方案——特别是各向同性热反馈与各向异性喷流反馈。他们考察了不同晕质量下位力半径处外流气体的熵分布，并将偏离熵上限的现象与位力激波的出现及随后的恒星形成再激活联系起来。

Result: In FLAMINGO, isotropic thermal feedback produces a mass-independent entropy floor at the virial radius, consistent with an entropy ceiling model. Jet feedback yields entropy that scales with the solid angle of directly heated gas. For halos above $M_\rm{crit} \approx 10^{13.5\text{--}14}\, M_\odot$, virial shocks dominate over feedback-regulated entropy, allowing cold gas inflow and renewed star formation, which aligns with observed low-redshift star formation rates and morphologies.
\n\n
在 FLAMINGO 模拟中，各向同性热反馈在位力半径处产生与质量无关的熵下限，符合熵上限模型。喷流反馈产生的熵则随被直接加热气体的立体角变化。对于质量高于 $M_\rm{crit} \approx 10^{13.5\text{--}14}\, M_\odot$ 的晕，位力激波主导并压倒反馈调控的熵上限，允许冷气体流入并引发恒星形成的再激活，这与观测到的低红移恒星形成率和形态一致。

Conclusion: Black hole feedback can regulate hot halo gas via an entropy ceiling, with buoyancy alone driving gas to the virial radius. This mechanism naturally explains quenching in massive galaxies, while its breakdown above $M_\rm{crit}$ predicts—and observations confirm—a resurgence of star formation in the most massive systems, challenging purely energy-driven feedback paradigms.
\n\n
黑洞反馈可通过熵上限调节热晕气体，仅靠浮力即可驱动气体到达位力半径。该机制自然解释了大质量星系中的淬灭现象，而当质量超过 $M_\rm{crit}$ 时该机制失效，预测（并已被观测证实）最大质量系统中恒星形成的复苏，这对纯能量驱动的反馈范式提出了挑战。

Abstract: We propose that black hole feedback regulates gas in massive halos by establishing an entropy ceiling; the resulting buoyant gas migrates to the virial radius with no additional energy input required. The FLAMINGO simulations support this picture: at the virial radius, outflow entropy is mass-independent for isotropic thermal feedback but depends on the solid angle of directly heated gas for jet feedback. Above a critical halo mass $M_\rm{crit} \approx 10^{13.5\text{--}14}\, M_\odot$, virial shocks overwhelm the ceiling, predicting rejuvenation of star formation in the most massive galaxies, supported by new low-redshift evidence from star formation rates and morphologies.

</details>


### [49] [Constraints on Self-Interacting Fuzzy Dark Matter from the Stellar Kinematics of the Dwarf Galaxy Leo II](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17211)
*Yi Zhao,Yu-Ming Yang,Xiao-Jun Bi,Peng-Fei Yin*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper investigates self-interacting fuzzy dark matter (SI-FDM) by analyzing the stellar kinematics of the dwarf galaxy Leo II. Using a Jeans analysis, the authors constrain the two-dimensional parameter space $(m_a, f_a)$, showing that attractive self-interactions tighten the lower bound on the axion mass $m_a$, while repulsive interactions weaken it. For self-coupling strengths $f_a^{-1} \lesssim 10^{-14}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$, they find $95\%$ CL lower limits on $m_a$ in the range $(1–10)\times10^{-22}\,\mathrm{eV}$, offering a local, astrophysical constraint independent of cosmological assumptions.
\n\n
本文通过分析矮星系Leo II的恒星运动学研究了自相互作用模糊暗物质（SI-FDM）。作者利用Jeans分析约束了二维参数空间$(m_a, f_a)$，表明吸引性自相互作用会收紧轴子质量$m_a$的下限，而排斥性相互作用则会削弱该限制。对于自耦合强度$f_a^{-1} \lesssim 10^{-14}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$，他们发现$m_a$在95%置信水平下的下限位于$(1–10)\times10^{-22}\,\mathrm{eV}$范围内，提供了一种不依赖宇宙学假设的局域天体物理约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The one-parameter FDM model is increasingly disfavored by Lyman-$α$ forest data and dwarf galaxy observations. To alleviate these tensions, the authors consider self-interacting FDM—a theoretically well-motivated extension where the axion-like particle has a quartic self-coupling controlled by the decay constant $f_a$. Constraining this two-parameter model $(m_a, f_a)$ with local astrophysical data provides a complementary approach to cosmological probes.
\n\n
单参数FDM模型正受到Lyman-$α$森林数据和矮星系观测的日益严格限制。为缓解这些张力，作者考虑了自相互作用FDM——一种理论上有良好动机的扩展，其中类轴子粒子具有由衰减常数$f_a$控制的四次自耦合。利用局域天体物理数据约束这一双参数模型$(m_a, f_a)$，可为宇宙学探针提供互补方法。

Method: The authors perform a Jeans analysis of stellar kinematic data from the dwarf spheroidal galaxy Leo II to infer the underlying dark matter density profile. They compare this empirical profile with theoretical SI-FDM halo profiles that depend on both the particle mass $m_a$ and the self-interaction strength characterized by $f_a^{-1}$. By mapping the agreement between observed and predicted profiles across the $(m_a, f_a)$ plane, they derive joint constraints without invoking cosmological simulations or galaxy formation models.
\n\n
作者对矮椭球星系Leo II的恒星运动学数据进行Jeans分析，以推断其底层暗物质密度轮廓。他们将该经验轮廓与依赖于粒子质量$m_a$和由$f_a^{-1}$表征的自相互作用强度的SI-FDM晕轮廓进行比较。通过在$(m_a, f_a)$平面上评估观测与理论轮廓的一致性，他们在不依赖宇宙学模拟或星系形成模型的情况下导出了联合约束。

Result: For fixed $m_a$, attractive self-interactions ($f_a^{-1} < 0$) produce more concentrated cores, improving fit to Leo II data and strengthening the lower bound on $m_a$; repulsive interactions ($f_a^{-1} > 0$) yield more diffuse profiles, worsening the fit and weakening the bound. At self-coupling strengths $|f_a^{-1}| \lesssim 10^{-14}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$, the $95\%$ CL lower limit on $m_a$ ranges from $1\times10^{-22}\,\mathrm{eV}$ to $10\times10^{-22}\,\mathrm{eV}$, depending on statistical methodology. The analysis yields simultaneous constraints on both $m_a$ and $f_a$.
\n\n
对于固定的$m_a$，吸引性自相互作用（$f_a^{-1} < 0$）产生更集中的核心，改善对Leo II数据的拟合，从而加强$m_a$的下限；排斥性相互作用（$f_a^{-1} > 0$）导致更弥散的轮廓，拟合变差，削弱限制。当自耦合强度$|f_a^{-1}| \lesssim 10^{-14}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$时，$m_a$在95%置信水平下的下限范围为$1\times10^{-22}\,\mathrm{eV}$至$10\times10^{-22}\,\mathrm{eV}$，具体取决于所用统计方法。该分析同时约束了$m_a$和$f_a$两个参数。

Conclusion: Self-interacting FDM can reconcile tensions in the standard FDM model through modifications to the central density profile. Using local stellar kinematics in Leo II, the study provides robust, cosmology-independent constraints on the $(m_a, f_a)$ parameter space. This demonstrates that small-scale astrophysical systems serve as powerful laboratories for probing ultralight dark matter physics beyond the minimal model.
\n\n
自相互作用FDM可通过修改中心密度轮廓来缓解标准FDM模型中的张力。利用Leo II中的局域恒星运动学，本研究提供了对$(m_a, f_a)$参数空间稳健且不依赖宇宙学的约束。这表明小尺度天体物理系统是探索超越最小模型的超轻暗物质物理的强大实验室。

Abstract: The one-parameter fuzzy dark matter (FDM) model has faced increasingly stringent constraints from both Lyman-$α$ forest observations and local measurements of dwarf galaxies. A natural extension to mitigate these limits is the inclusion of FDM self-interactions. In this study, we derive constraints in the two-dimensional parameter space $(m_a, f_a)$ using the dark matter density profile inferred from a Jeans analysis of the stellar kinematics in the dwarf galaxy Leo II, which has previously been employed to constrain non-interacting FDM. We find that, for a fixed particle mass $m_a$, attractive (repulsive) self-interaction leads to a more concentrated (more diffuse) FDM density profile relative to the non-interacting case, thereby improving (worsening) agreement with the Jeans analysis results. Our results indicate that, for either attractive or repulsive SI with strength $f_a^{-1}\lesssim 10^{-14}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$, the $95\%$ confidence-level lower limits on $m_a$ lies within the range $(1-10)\times10^{-22}\,\mathrm{eV}$, although the precise bounds depend to some extent on the statistical method employed. This analysis simultaneously constrains the two parameters $(m_a, f_a)$ without relying on assumptions about cosmological or galaxy evolution histories, and thus offers a complementary probe to existing constraints.
