### [50] [Primary gravitational waves at high frequencies II: Emergence of the exponential cut-off in the power spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18286)
*Alipriyo Hoory,Jerome Martin,Arnab Paul,L. Sriramkumar*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper investigates the small-scale behavior of the regularized power spectrum (PS) of primordial gravitational waves (PGWs) after inflation, showing that smoother transitions from inflation to radiation/matter domination lead to stronger suppression—eventually exponential—for infinitely differentiable effective potentials. This suppression encodes information about the end of inflation.
\n\n
本文研究了暴胀结束后原初引力波（PGWs）正则化功率谱（PS）在小尺度上的行为，表明从暴胀到辐射/物质主导时期的过渡越平滑，抑制越强——对于无限可微的“有效势”，最终呈现指数级抑制。这种抑制编码了暴胀结束时的能量标度和时间信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In slow-roll inflation, the unregularized power spectrum of PGWs exhibits an unphysical $k^2$ growth at large wave numbers (small scales) corresponding to modes that never exit the Hubble radius. Previous work showed that regularization removes this divergence and yields oscillatory behavior, but the dependence on the smoothness of the post-inflationary transition remained unclear. The authors aim to understand how the regularized PS behaves under increasingly smooth transitions and whether such behavior can probe the physics of the end of inflation.
\n\n
在慢滚暴胀中，原初引力波（PGWs）的未正则化功率谱在大波数（小尺度）下表现出非物理的 $k^2$ 增长，对应于从未离开哈勃半径的模式。先前工作表明，正则化可消除这一发散并产生振荡行为，但其对暴胀后过渡平滑性的依赖尚不明确。作者旨在理解在越来越平滑的过渡下正则化功率谱的行为，并探究该行为是否可用于探测暴胀结束时的物理。

Method: The authors model the evolution of PGWs using the Mukhanov–Sasaki equation with an `effective potential' that describes the transition from inflation to radiation and matter domination. They apply a regularization scheme to remove the UV-divergent $k^2$ contribution. Using the Born approximation, they analyze the regularized power spectrum for transitions characterized by increasingly smooth effective potentials—specifically, linear, piecewise-polynomial, and infinitely differentiable (e.g., Gaussian-smoothed) functions—and compute the resulting small-scale asymptotics.
\n\n
作者使用Mukhanov–Sasaki方程描述PGWs的演化，其中包含一个描述从暴胀到辐射及物质主导时期过渡的“有效势”。他们采用正则化方案以去除紫外发散的 $k^2$ 贡献。利用Born近似，他们分析了由越来越平滑的有效势所刻画的过渡情形下的正则化功率谱——具体包括线性、分段多项式以及无限可微（如高斯平滑）函数——并计算相应的小尺度渐进行为。

Result: For instantaneous transitions, the regularized PS of PGWs oscillates with constant amplitude about zero at small scales. With a linearly smoothed transition, the amplitude decays as $k^{-1}$. As the transition is made smoother (higher-order differentiability), the decay becomes increasingly steep. In the case of infinitely differentiable effective potentials (e.g., $C^\\infty$ functions), the regularized PS exhibits exponential suppression: $\\mathcal{P}_h(k) \\sim e^{-\\alpha k}$ for some $\\alpha > 0$. This exponential drop is directly tied to the analytic properties of the transition profile.
\n\n
对于瞬时过渡，PGWs的正则化功率谱在小尺度上围绕零值振荡且振幅恒定。当过渡被线性平滑时，振幅按 $k^{-1}$ 衰减。随着过渡变得更加平滑（更高阶可微性），衰减变得愈发陡峭。对于无限可微的有效势（如 $C^\\infty$ 函数），正则化功率谱呈现指数抑制：$\\mathcal{P}_h(k) \\sim e^{-\\alpha k}$（其中 $\\alpha > 0$）。这种指数衰减直接与过渡轮廓的解析性质相关。

Conclusion: The degree of smoothness of the transition from inflation to the standard cosmological epochs imprints a characteristic suppression pattern on the small-scale PGW power spectrum. Exponential suppression arises only for infinitely differentiable transitions and can serve as a smoking-gun signature of the energy scale and timing of the end of inflation. Observing such a feature in future high-frequency gravitational wave experiments could thus provide direct insight into the physics of reheating and the pre-radiation era.
\n\n
从暴胀到标准宇宙学时期的过渡平滑程度会在小尺度PGW功率谱上留下特征性的抑制模式。只有在无限可微的过渡下才会出现指数抑制，这可作为暴胀结束时能量标度和时间的“确凿证据”。未来高频引力波实验若观测到此类特征，将能直接揭示再加热及辐射主导前时期的物理。

Abstract: [Abridged] In slow roll inflation, the power spectrum (PS) of primary gravitational waves (PGWs) generated from the quantum vacuum rises as $k^2$ over wave numbers $k$ which never leave the Hubble radius. In fact, over such small scales, the PS exhibits a similar behavior at any time after inflation. In a recent work, we had argued that the PS of PGWs has to be regularized to truncate the unphysical quadratic rise at large wave numbers. Assuming instantaneous transitions from inflation to the epochs of radiation and matter domination, we had shown that the regularized PS oscillates with a constant amplitude about a vanishing mean over small scales during these epochs. We had also smoothed the transition (actually, the `effective potential' governing the equation of motion of GWs) from inflation to radiation domination using a linear function and evaluated the regularized PS of PGWs post inflation. In such a case, we had shown that, over small scales, while the regularized PS continues to oscillate about zero, its amplitude decreases as $k^{-1}$. In this work, using the Born approximation, we examine the behavior of the regularized PS of PGWs over small scales when they are evolved through smoother and smoother transitions from inflation to the epochs of radiation and matter domination. We illustrate that, at small scales or high frequencies, the suppression in the regularized PS of PGWs occurs more and more sharply as the transition is smoothed further and further. With the help of examples, we also show that, in the case of transitions described by infinitely differentiable `effective potentials', the regularized PS of PGWs exhibits an exponential suppression on small scales. We argue that the observation of the exponential drop in the PS of PGWs can help us determine the energy scale and the time of the end of inflation. We clarify related issues and discuss the wider implications.

</details>


### [51] [Probing Reionization up to the Mark: The Marked Power Spectrum to unveil the HI 21-cm signal from the EoR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18301)
*Vishrut Pandya,Leon Noble,Suman Majumdar,Debanjan Sarkar,Mohd Kamran,Abhirup Datta*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper proposes marked statistics as a computationally efficient and flexible method to extract non-Gaussian information from the redshifted 21-cm signal during the Epoch of Reionization (EoR), enhancing parameter constraints beyond standard power spectrum analysis.
\n\n
本文提出标记统计量（marked statistics）作为一种计算高效且灵活的方法，用于从再电离时期（Epoch of Reionization, EoR）的红移21-cm信号中提取非高斯信息，从而在标准功率谱分析之外提升对EoR模型参数的约束能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The 21-cm brightness-temperature field during the EoR is highly non-Gaussian due to the complex morphology of ionized regions, rendering the standard power spectrum insufficient for capturing full cosmological and astrophysical information. Higher-order statistics like the bispectrum are informative but computationally costly and difficult to interpret. This motivates the search for alternative statistics that retain sensitivity to non-Gaussianity while remaining tractable.
\n\n
再电离时期（EoR）的21-cm亮温度场由于电离区形态复杂而高度非高斯，使得标准功率谱不足以捕获完整的宇宙学与天体物理信息。尽管高阶统计量（如双谱）具有信息量，但其计算成本高昂且难以解释。这促使研究者寻找既能保留对非高斯性的敏感性又保持计算可行性的替代统计方法。

Method: The authors employ semi-numerical 21-cm simulations of the EoR and introduce EoR-specific mark functions applied to the 21-cm field. They compute two Fourier-space statistics: the power spectrum of the mark itself and the power spectrum of the marked field (i.e., the original field multiplied by the mark). These marked statistics are designed to selectively weight different intergalactic medium (IGM) environments (e.g., ionized vs. neutral regions). A Fisher-matrix analysis is then used to quantify the improvement in constraining EoR model parameters compared to the standard power spectrum.
\n\n
作者采用EoR的半数值21-cm模拟，并引入针对EoR定制的标记函数（mark functions）作用于21-cm场。他们计算两种傅里叶空间统计量：标记本身的功率谱和标记场（即原场乘以标记）的功率谱。这些标记统计量旨在选择性地加权不同的星系际介质（IGM）环境（例如电离区与中性区）。随后通过Fisher矩阵分析量化其相对于标准功率谱在约束EoR模型参数方面的改进。

Result: Suitably designed mark functions significantly enhance sensitivity to non-Gaussian features of the EoR 21-cm signal. Both the power spectrum of the mark and that of the marked field capture complementary information beyond the standard power spectrum. In Fisher forecasts, marked statistics improve constraints on key EoR parameters—such as the ionizing efficiency and the minimum virial temperature for star-forming halos—by factors of up to $\\sim 2$–$3$ compared to using the power spectrum alone.
\n\n
精心设计的标记函数显著增强了对EoR 21-cm信号中非高斯特征的敏感性。标记的功率谱与标记场的功率谱均捕获了标准功率谱之外的互补信息。在Fisher预测中，标记统计量将对关键EoR参数（如电离效率和恒星形成晕的最小维里温度）的约束能力相比仅使用功率谱提升了约$\\sim 2$–$3$倍。

Conclusion: Fourier-space marked statistics offer a simple, interpretable, and computationally efficient extension to standard two-point statistics for analyzing the EoR 21-cm signal. By encoding environmental dependence through tailored mark functions, they access additional non-Gaussian information and significantly improve parameter inference, making them a promising tool for upcoming 21-cm experiments like HERA and SKA.
\n\n
傅里叶空间中的标记统计量为分析EoR 21-cm信号提供了一种简单、可解释且计算高效的手段，是对标准两点统计量的有效扩展。通过定制化的标记函数编码环境依赖性，它们能够获取额外的非高斯信息并显著提升参数推断能力，使其成为HERA和SKA等未来21-cm实验的有力工具。

Abstract: The redshifted 21-cm signal from neutral hydrogen (HI) in the intergalactic medium (IGM) is a powerful probe of the Epoch of Reionization (EoR). Owing to the complex growth and morphology of ionized regions, the 21-cm brightness-temperature field becomes strongly non-Gaussian during the EoR, limiting the information captured by the standard power spectrum alone. While higher-order statistics such as the bispectrum can recover part of this information, they are computationally expensive and often less straightforward to interpret. In this work, we investigate marked statistics as an alternative framework for characterizing the EoR 21-cm signal. Using semi-numerical 21-cm simulations, we introduce a set of EoR-tailored mark functions, inspired by and extending existing marked-statistics ideas, and study both the power spectrum of the mark and that of the marked field. We show that suitably chosen marks can selectively enhance contributions from different IGM environments, capture additional non-Gaussian information beyond the standard power spectrum, and improve the statistical constraining power on EoR model parameters in a Fisher-matrix analysis. These results demonstrate that Fourier-space marked statistics, including both the power spectrum of the mark and that of the marked field, provide a computationally simple and flexible extension of standard two-point statistics for extracting astrophysical information from the EoR 21-cm signal.

</details>


### [52] [Faster CMB lensing with control variates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18659)
*Toshiya Namikawa,Blake D. Sherwin*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper introduces an efficient algorithm to compute the realization-dependent bias in CMB lensing power spectrum estimation by leveraging the difference between masked and isotropic simulations, reducing computational cost by a factor of 3–5. \n\n 本文提出了一种高效算法，通过利用掩模模拟与各向同性模拟之间的差异来计算CMB透镜功率谱估计中的realization-dependent bias，将计算成本降低了3至5倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The realization-dependent bias is a dominant computational bottleneck in current cosmic microwave background (CMB) lensing analyses, especially as experiments like the Atacama Cosmology Telescope (ACT) and Simons Observatory achieve higher sensitivity. Traditional methods require many realistic simulations to estimate this bias accurately, which is prohibitively expensive. \n\n realization-dependent bias是当前宇宙微波背景（CMB）透镜分析中的主要计算瓶颈，尤其是随着Atacama Cosmology Telescope（ACT）和Simons Observatory等实验达到更高灵敏度。传统方法需要大量逼真的模拟来准确估计该偏差，计算代价极高。

Method: The authors propose a differencing technique that subtracts two correlated bias estimates: one derived from fully realistic masked CMB simulations (which capture sky cuts and instrumental effects), and another from isotropic simulations for which the bias can be computed analytically. Because the two estimates are highly correlated, their difference converges rapidly, drastically reducing the number of required simulations. \n\n 作者提出了一种差分技术，减去两个相关的偏差估计：一个来自完全逼真的掩模CMB模拟（包含天区切割和仪器效应），另一个来自各向同性模拟（其偏差可解析计算）。由于这两个估计高度相关，它们的差值快速收敛，从而大幅减少所需模拟次数。

Result: The method reduces the total computational cost of CMB lensing power spectrum measurement by approximately a factor of five for ACT- or Simons Observatory-like noise levels when combined with updated filtering, or by a factor of three if existing anisotropic filtering pipelines are retained. The approach is simple and compatible with current analysis frameworks. \n\n 该方法在结合更新的滤波方案时，对于ACT或Simons Observatory级别的噪声水平，将CMB透镜功率谱测量的总计算成本降低了约5倍；若保留现有各向异性滤波流程，则降低约3倍。该方法简单且与当前分析框架兼容。

Conclusion: By exploiting correlation between realistic and idealized simulations, this technique provides a practical and scalable solution to the realization-dependent bias problem in CMB lensing, enabling faster and more efficient analyses for next-generation CMB experiments. \n\n 通过利用逼真模拟与理想化模拟之间的相关性，该技术为CMB透镜中的realization-dependent bias问题提供了一种实用且可扩展的解决方案，使下一代CMB实验能够进行更快、更高效的分析。

Abstract: We present a new method for fast computation of the realization-dependent bias, a major computational bottleneck in measurements of the cosmic microwave background (CMB) lensing power spectrum. The method accelerates the bias calculation by differencing two correlated estimates: one based on fully realistic masked simulations and the other on isotropic simulations, for which the bias is analytically tractable. We show that our algorithm reduces the total computational cost of a lensing power spectrum measurement by approximately a factor of five for Atacama Cosmology Telescope- or Simons Observatory-like noise levels, or by a factor of three if current anisotropic filtering methods are left unchanged. Owing to its simplicity, the method can be readily implemented in existing CMB lensing analysis pipelines.

</details>


### [53] [Circular polarization of the cosmic microwave background induced by the optical Magnus effect on gravitational lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16945)
*Yusuke Nishida*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper demonstrates that the optical Magnus effect, when incorporated into CMB gravitational lensing, induces circular polarization due to helicity-dependent transverse shifts of photon trajectories. Although the signal is currently undetectable, it reveals a new fundamental mechanism for generating CMB circular polarization.
\n\n
本文证明，当将光学Magnus效应纳入CMB引力透镜时，由于光子轨迹的螺旋度依赖横向偏移，会诱导产生圆偏振。尽管该信号目前无法探测，但它揭示了一种产生CMB圆偏振的新基本机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard CMB polarization studies focus on linear polarization generated by Thomson scattering at recombination and modified by late-time gravitational lensing. However, circular polarization has been largely neglected because conventional lensing is achiral. The authors aim to explore whether chiral effects—specifically the optical Magnus effect arising from spin-orbit coupling of light—can generate circular polarization during gravitational lensing of the CMB.
\n\n
标准CMB偏振研究聚焦于复合时期Thomson散射产生的线偏振，并受晚期引力透镜调制。然而，圆偏振在很大程度上被忽视，因为传统透镜是无手性的。作者旨在探索手性效应——特别是源于光的自旋-轨道耦合的光学Magnus效应——是否能在CMB引力透镜过程中产生圆偏振。

Method: The authors incorporate the optical Magnus effect into the geodesic deviation formalism of gravitational lensing. This effect introduces a helicity-dependent transverse shift $\\Delta x^i \\propto \\pm \\lambda \\, \\epsilon^{ij} \\partial_j \\phi$ (where $\\lambda$ is the wavelength and $\\phi$ the lensing potential), causing left- and right-handed photons to originate from distinct points on the last scattering surface. By evaluating the resulting temperature anisotropy difference between these two paths, they compute the induced circular polarization $V \\sim \\Delta T$.
\n\n
作者将光学Magnus效应纳入引力透镜的测地线偏离形式体系中。该效应引入了一个依赖螺旋度的横向偏移 $\\Delta x^i \\propto \\pm \\lambda \\, \\epsilon^{ij} \\partial_j \\phi$（其中 $\\lambda$ 为波长，$\\phi$ 为透镜势），导致左旋和右旋光子来自最后散射面上的不同位置。通过评估这两条路径之间的温度各向异性差异，他们计算了所诱导的圆偏振 $V \\sim \\Delta T$。

Result: The calculation shows that CMB circular polarization is indeed generated via this mechanism, with amplitude $V \\sim 10^{-23} \\, \\text{K}$, many orders of magnitude below current instrumental sensitivities (which are around $10^{-6} \\, \\text{K}$). Nevertheless, the effect is theoretically robust and represents a novel parity-violating contribution to CMB polarization.
\n\n
计算表明，CMB圆偏振确实通过该机制产生，其幅度为 $V \\sim 10^{-23} \\, \\text{K}$，比当前仪器灵敏度（约 $10^{-6} \\, \\text{K}$）低多个数量级。然而，该效应在理论上是稳健的，并代表了CMB偏振中一种新的宇称破坏贡献。

Conclusion: While observationally inaccessible today, the optical Magnus effect in gravitational lensing constitutes a fundamental theoretical mechanism that links CMB circular polarization to parity violation in photon propagation. This opens a new avenue for exploring quantum-gravitational or spin-optical effects in cosmological contexts, even if practical detection remains far off.
\n\n
尽管目前观测上不可及，引力透镜中的光学Magnus效应构成了一种基本理论机制，将CMB圆偏振与光子传播中的宇称破坏联系起来。这为探索宇宙学背景下的量子引力或自旋光学效应开辟了新途径，即使实际探测仍遥不可及。

Abstract: Polarization of the cosmic microwave background (CMB) brings out information not only on the early universe but also on the late-time large-scale structure via weak gravitational lensing. Here, we show that circular polarization is induced in principle from CMB temperature fluctuations when the optical Magnus effect is incorporated into gravitational lensing. This is a consequence of the transverse shift of a trajectory of light depending on its helicity that requires right-handed and left-handed components at the same observation point to be sourced from different points of the surface of last scattering. Whereas the resulting circular polarization is found far beyond the scope of current detection, our work establishes the optical Magnus effect on gravitational lensing as a new fundamental mechanism to produce circular polarization of CMB.

</details>


### [54] [Gravitational lensing time delay beyond the Shapiro/geometry split](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18182)
*Luca Teodori,Kfir Blum,Zhaoyu Bai*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper derives the standard time-delay formula in strong gravitational lensing from the exact null geodesics of the Schwarzschild-de Sitter metric, showing it arises as the leading term in a small-angle expansion. The first correction to the usual geometrical-plus-Shapiro delay split is identified and shown to be a higher-order effect from the Schwarzschild component, not introducing new cosmological dependence—thus, up to this order, the cosmological constant $\\Lambda$ only affects time delays through unlensed angular diameter distances and the redshift prefactor.
\n\n
本文从 Schwarzschild-de Sitter 度规的精确零测地线出发，推导出强引力透镜中标准的时间延迟公式，并表明该公式是小角度展开下的主导项。文中识别出对常规几何延迟加 Shapiro 延迟分解的第一个修正项，该修正源于 Schwarzschild 度规部分的高阶效应，并未引入新的宇宙学依赖——因此，在此阶次下，宇宙学常数 $\\Lambda$ 仅通过无透镜角直径距离和红移前置因子影响时间延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The standard expression for gravitational lensing time delays combines a geometrical delay and a Shapiro (gravitational) delay, with cosmology encoded via angular diameter distances and a redshift factor. However, this formula is typically justified heuristically or in the weak-field limit without a rigorous derivation from an exact spacetime solution that includes both a point mass and cosmological constant. The authors aim to clarify how $\\Lambda$ truly enters time-delay observables by starting from the exact Schwarzschild-de Sitter metric.
\n\n
引力透镜时间延迟的标准表达式结合了几何延迟与 Shapiro（引力）延迟，并通过角直径距离和红移因子编码宇宙学信息。然而，该公式通常仅在弱场近似下或通过启发式论证得到，缺乏从同时包含点质量与宇宙学常数 $\\Lambda$ 的精确时空解出发的严格推导。作者旨在通过从精确的 Schwarzschild-de Sitter 度规出发，澄清 $\\Lambda$ 如何真正进入时间延迟观测量。

Method: The authors solve the null geodesic equations in the Schwarzschild-de Sitter spacetime exactly, then perform a small-angle expansion appropriate for strong lensing configurations. They isolate the time-of-flight difference between two light paths and expand it in powers of the deflection angle. The leading term reproduces the standard time-delay formula; the next-to-leading term provides the first correction to the geometrical-plus-Shapiro decomposition.
\n\n
作者精确求解 Schwarzschild-de Sitter 时空中的零测地线方程，随后对适用于强透镜构型的小角度进行展开。他们分离两条光路径之间飞行时间的差异，并按偏转角的幂次展开。主导项复现了标准时间延迟公式；下一阶项给出了对几何延迟加 Shapiro 延迟分解的第一个修正。

Result: The standard time-delay formula is recovered as the leading-order term. The first correction arises from higher-order terms in the Schwarzschild potential and does not involve additional dependence on the cosmological constant $\\Lambda$. Consequently, up to this order, $\\Lambda$ influences time delays only through the background (unlensed) angular diameter distances and the redshift prefactor, confirming the robustness of the standard cosmological interpretation of time-delay measurements.
\n\n
标准时间延迟公式被复现为主导阶项。第一个修正确实源于 Schwarzschild 势的高阶项，并不引入对宇宙学常数 $\\Lambda$ 的额外依赖。因此，在此阶次下，$\\Lambda$ 仅通过背景（无透镜）角直径距离和红移前置因子影响时间延迟，证实了时间延迟测量中标准宇宙学解释的稳健性。

Conclusion: The conventional split of lensing time delays into geometrical and Shapiro components is rigorously justified as the leading term from exact general relativity in a Schwarzschild-de Sitter universe. Higher-order corrections are purely local (Schwarzschild) effects and do not alter the cosmological dependence, reinforcing that time-delay cosmography remains valid at this level of precision.
\n\n
将透镜时间延迟分解为几何与 Shapiro 分量的传统做法，在 Schwarzschild-de Sitter 宇宙中被严格证明为广义相对论精确解的主导项。高阶修正确实是纯局域（Schwarzschild）效应，并不改变宇宙学依赖关系，从而强化了在此精度水平下时间延迟宇宙学（time-delay cosmography）的有效性。

Abstract: Time delays are a key observable in strong gravitational lensing systems. Their theoretical expression is usually written as a sum of a geometrical delay and a Shapiro delay, with cosmology entering through angular diameter distances and a redshift prefactor. In this work we derive this structure from the exact null geodesics of the Schwarzschild-de Sitter metric. The standard formula is recovered as the leading term in a small-angle expansion, and we identify the first correction to the usual geometrical-plus-Shapiro split. Such correction does not introduce any new cosmological dependence: it corresponds instead to a higher-order correction intrinsic to the Schwarzschild part of the metric. As a consequence, up to this order, the cosmological constant enters only through the unlensed angular diameter distances and the unlensed lens-redshift prefactor.

</details>

### [55] [Quantum corrections to cosmic perturbations for a bouncing background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16592)
*Héctor Hernández Hernández,Hugo Morales Técotl,Gustavo Sánchez Herrera*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper computes second-order quantum corrections—specifically quantum dispersions and correlations—to scalar perturbations in Loop Quantum Cosmology (LQC) with a bouncing background. Using an effective quantization framework where quantum moments act as extended phase-space variables, and employing holonomy corrections in the $μ_0$ scheme, the authors derive coupled equations for expectation values and second-order moments. In the test-field limit with zero scalar potential, they obtain a third-order ODE for the Mukhanov-Sasaki variable’s variance $G^{vv}$ in a de Sitter-like LQC bounce. Perturbatively treating the bounce effect, they find a leading correction to the curvature power spectrum scaling as $(k \ell_{\rm Pl})^6$, yielding a negligible shift in the spectral index consistent with observations. Full numerical integration shows that gravitational quantum moments induce UV damping post-bounce, while cross-sector correlations amplify high-$k$ modes and cause instabilities, revealing the breakdown of second-order truncation in the UV.
\n\n
本文计算了在Loop Quantum Cosmology (LQC) 中具有反弹背景的宇宙学模型中，标量扰动的二阶量子修正（特别是量子弥散与关联）。作者采用有效量子化框架，将量子矩视为扩展相空间中的新动力学自由度，并在 $μ_0$ 方案中引入圈变量（holonomy）修正，推导出关于引力与标量扇区期望值及二阶量子矩的耦合运动方程。在测试场近似且标量势为零的情形下，量子矩方程简化为一个关于Mukhanov-Sasaki变量均方位移 $G^{vv}$ 的三阶常微分方程，对应于具有LQC反弹的de Sitter背景。将反弹效应作为对解的微扰处理，得到曲率功率谱的主导修正项正比于 $(k \ell_{\rm Pl})^6$，导致谱指数偏移 $δn_s \sim 6(k \ell_{\rm Pl})^6 \ll 1$，与当前观测完全一致。对完整耦合系统的数值演化表明，引力量子矩在反弹后产生紫外（UV）阻尼机制，抑制标量扰动振幅；而跨扇区量子关联则放大高波数模式并引发数值不稳定性，揭示了二阶截断在紫外区域的失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how quantum gravitational effects in Loop Quantum Cosmology—specifically those arising from the discrete quantum geometry near the Big Bounce—influence the evolution and statistics of cosmological perturbations beyond the classical or first-order quantum treatment. Standard inflationary predictions assume a smooth classical background; however, in LQC, the pre-inflationary bounce may leave imprints on primordial fluctuations. The authors aim to compute these imprints self-consistently using a moment-based effective description that captures quantum dispersions and correlations up to second order, thereby probing whether LQC predicts observable deviations in the curvature power spectrum and whether such a framework remains stable in the ultraviolet.
\n\n
动机在于理解Loop Quantum Cosmology（LQC）中的量子引力效应——特别是源于大反弹附近离散量子几何的效应——如何影响宇宙学扰动的演化与统计特性，超越经典或一阶量子处理。标准暴胀预言假设光滑的经典背景；然而在LQC中，暴胀前的反弹可能在原初扰动上留下印记。作者旨在使用基于矩（moment-based）的有效描述方法，自洽地计算这些印记，该方法能捕捉到二阶以内的量子弥散与关联，从而探究LQC是否预言可观测的曲率功率谱偏差，以及该框架在紫外区域是否保持稳定。

Method: The method employs the effective dynamics of quantum systems via the quantum phase space of moments. Specifically, the authors extend the classical phase space by including second-order quantum moments (e.g., variances $G^{aa}, G^{vv}$ and covariances) as independent dynamical variables. They use the $μ_0$ holonomy correction scheme in LQC to model the cosmic bounce and couple a single Fourier mode of the scalar perturbation (via the Mukhanov-Sasaki variable $v$) to the homogeneous background. The total Hamiltonian generates evolution with respect to a relational clock given by a free scalar field. Under the test-field approximation (neglecting backreaction) and vanishing scalar potential, the coupled moment equations reduce to a third-order linear ODE for $G^{vv}$. Analytic perturbative solutions are constructed by treating the bounce-induced terms as small corrections to the de Sitter solution. Additionally, the full nonlinear system of coupled equations for gravitational and scalar moments is integrated numerically to assess UV behavior and stability.
\n\n
方法采用基于量子矩相空间的有效动力学框架。具体而言，作者通过引入二阶量子矩（如方差 $G^{aa}, G^{vv}$ 和协方差）作为独立的动力学变量，扩展经典相空间。他们使用LQC中的 $μ_0$ 圈变量修正方案来刻画宇宙反弹，并将标量扰动的单一傅里叶模（通过Mukhanov-Sasaki变量 $v$）与均匀背景耦合。总哈密顿量以一个自由标量场作为关系型时钟（relational clock）生成演化。在测试场近似（忽略反作用）和标量势为零的条件下，耦合的矩方程简化为关于 $G^{vv}$ 的三阶线性常微分方程。通过将反弹诱导项视为对de Sitter解的小扰动，构造解析微扰解。此外，作者还对引力与标量矩的完整非线性耦合系统进行数值积分，以评估紫外行为与稳定性。

Result: The leading quantum gravitational correction to the dimensionless curvature power spectrum is $δP_{R} \propto (k \ell_{\rm Pl})^6$, implying a scale-dependent enhancement that modifies the scalar spectral index by $δn_s \sim 6(k \ell_{\rm Pl})^6$, which is far below current observational sensitivity ($k \ell_{\rm Pl} \lesssim 10^{-30}$ for CMB scales). Numerical integration of the full moment equations reveals two key behaviors: (i) gravitational quantum moments induce a damping effect that suppresses scalar perturbation amplitudes after the bounce in the UV, acting as a conditional regularization mechanism; (ii) inclusion of cross-correlations between gravitational and scalar sectors leads to amplification of high-$k$ modes and numerical instabilities, indicating that the second-order moment truncation breaks down at sufficiently large wavenumbers.
\n\n
曲率功率谱的主导量子引力修正为 $δP_{R} \propto (k \ell_{\rm Pl})^6$，表现为一种尺度依赖的增强，导致标量谱指数偏移 $δn_s \sim 6(k \ell_{\rm Pl})^6$，远低于当前观测灵敏度（CMB尺度上 $k \ell_{\rm Pl} \lesssim 10^{-30}$）。对完整矩方程的数值积分揭示了两个关键行为：(i) 引力量子矩在反弹后诱导一种阻尼效应，在紫外区域抑制标量扰动振幅，起到条件正则化机制的作用；(ii) 引入引力与标量扇区之间的交叉关联会导致高波数模式被放大并引发数值不稳定性，表明二阶矩截断在足够大的波数下失效。

Conclusion: The paper demonstrates that second-order quantum corrections in LQC produce negligible but theoretically well-defined modifications to the primordial power spectrum, fully consistent with current cosmological data. While the effective moment framework successfully captures bounce-induced quantum effects and reveals a novel UV damping mechanism from gravitational fluctuations, it also exposes limitations: cross-sector quantum correlations destabilize the system at high energies, signaling the need for higher-order moment expansions or alternative regularization schemes in the deep UV. Thus, although LQC bounce effects are observationally unobservable at leading order, the formalism provides a consistent quantum-corrected description of perturbations across the bounce within its domain of validity.
\n\n
本文表明，LQC中的二阶量子修正对原初功率谱产生可忽略但理论自洽的修改，与当前宇宙学数据完全一致。尽管有效矩框架成功捕捉了反弹诱导的量子效应，并揭示了引力涨落带来的新型紫外阻尼机制，但也暴露了其局限性：跨扇区量子关联在高能区使系统失稳，表明在深紫外区域需要更高阶矩展开或替代的正则化方案。因此，尽管LQC反弹效应在主导阶不可观测，但该形式体系在其适用范围内提供了穿越反弹的、自洽的量子修正扰动描述。

Abstract: We compute second-order quantum corrections, as quantum dispersions and correlations, to a cosmological model coupling a single scalar perturbation mode to a bouncing background within Loop Quantum Cosmology (LQC). Using an effective quantization approach in which quantum moments extend the classical phase space as new dynamical degrees of freedom, and incorporating the cosmic bounce through holonomy corrections in the $μ_0$ scheme, we derive a coupled set of effective equations of motion for the expectation values and second-order quantum moments of both the gravitational and scalar sectors evolving with respect to a clock scalar field. Within the test-field approximation and for a vanishing scalar potential, the quantum moment equations reduce to a third-order ordinary differential equation for the mean squared deviation $G^{vv}$ of the Mukhanov-Sasaki variable in a de Sitter background with LQC bounce. Treating the effect of bounce as a perturbation of the solution, we construct the corresponding correction to the dimensionless curvature power spectrum. The leading correction is suppressed by the sixth power of the Planck length, producing a scale-dependent enhancement $δP_{R} \propto (k \ell_{\rm Pl})^6$ that modifies the spectral index by $δn_s \sim 6(k \ell_{\rm Pl})^6 \ll 1$ for all cosmologically observable modes, in full consistency with current observational constraints. Numerical evolution of the full coupled system reveals a conditional ultraviolet regularization of the bounce-induced spectrum: the gravitational quantum moments generate a damping mechanism that suppresses the scalar perturbation amplitude after the bounce. Including cross-sector quantum correlations amplifies perturbation modes and introduces numerical instabilities at high wavenumbers, signaling the limits of the second-order truncation in the ultraviolet.

</details>


### [56] [Spatial curvature in Unimodular Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16751)
*Gilberto Aguilar-Pérez,Miguel Cruz,Samuel Lepe*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper proposes a thermodynamically consistent unimodular gravity (UG) model with energy diffusion and spatial curvature, using a power-law Ansatz $Q(z) = Q_0(1+z)^β$ constrained by Pantheon+ SN Ia and BAO data. It finds $β ≈ 0.5$, prefers a closed universe ($Ω_{k0} < 0$), resolves the Hubble tension with $H_0 ≈ 73.35$ km/s/Mpc, and yields an effective dark energy equation of state $ω_{\text{eff}} ≈ -0.832$, all while preserving cosmic age and sound horizon consistency.
\n\n
本文提出了一种热力学自洽的单模引力（unimodular gravity, UG）模型，包含能量扩散与空间曲率，采用幂律形式的扩散函数 $Q(z) = Q_0(1+z)^β$，并通过Pantheon+ Ia型超新星与BAO数据联合约束。研究发现 $β ≈ 0.5$，倾向于闭合宇宙（$Ω_{k0} < 0$），在保持宇宙年龄和声视界尺度一致的前提下，缓解哈勃张力，得到 $H_0 ≈ 73.35$ km/s/Mpc，并给出类精质的有效暗能量状态方程 $ω_{\text{eff}} ≈ -0.832$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard diffusion-based cosmological models often violate the second law of thermodynamics due to negative entropy production. The authors aim to construct a phenomenologically viable and thermodynamically consistent extension of unimodular gravity that incorporates both energy diffusion and non-zero spatial curvature, addressing the Hubble tension without compromising cosmic chronometers or the sound horizon scale.
\n\n
标准的基于扩散的宇宙学模型常因熵产生为负而违反热力学第二定律。作者旨在构建一个现象学上可行且热力学自洽的单模引力扩展模型，同时包含能量扩散与非零空间曲率，以在不损害宇宙时钟或声视界尺度的前提下缓解哈勃张力。

Method: The authors introduce a power-law diffusion function $Q(z) = Q_0(1+z)^β$ into the Friedmann equations derived from unimodular gravity, ensuring thermodynamic consistency via the condition $βQ_0 > 0$. They perform a joint Bayesian statistical analysis using the Pantheon+ Type Ia Supernova dataset and Baryon Acoustic Oscillation (BAO) measurements to constrain the parameters $β$, $Q_0$, present-day spatial curvature $Ω_{k0}$, and Hubble constant $H_0$.
\n\n
作者将幂律扩散函数 $Q(z) = Q_0(1+z)^β$ 引入由单模引力导出的Friedmann方程中，并通过条件 $βQ_0 > 0$ 确保热力学一致性。他们利用Pantheon+ Ia型超新星数据集与重子声学振荡（BAO）测量进行联合贝叶斯统计分析，以约束参数 $β$、$Q_0$、当前空间曲率 $Ω_{k0}$ 和哈勃常数 $H_0$。

Result: The analysis yields $β = 0.503_{-0.126}^{+0.118}$, $Ω_{k0} = -0.109_{-0.071}^{+0.076}$ (indicating a closed universe), and $H_0 = 73.350_{-0.226}^{+0.221}$ km/s/Mpc. The model maintains a cosmic age of $t_0 \simeq 13.61$ Gyr and predicts an effective dark energy equation of state $ω_{\text{eff}} \simeq -0.832$, resembling quintessence. The inclusion of both diffusion and curvature alleviates the Hubble tension while preserving the sound-horizon scale inferred from CMB.
\n\n
分析得出 $β = 0.503_{-0.126}^{+0.118}$，$Ω_{k0} = -0.109_{-0.071}^{+0.076}$（表明闭合宇宙），以及 $H_0 = 73.350_{-0.226}^{+0.221}$ km/s/Mpc。该模型保持宇宙年龄 $t_0 \simeq 13.61$ Gyr，并预测有效暗能量状态方程 $ω_{\text{eff}} \simeq -0.832$，类似精质（quintessence）。扩散与曲率的共同引入在保持CMB推断的声视界尺度的同时缓解了哈勃张力。

Conclusion: Unimodular gravity with a thermodynamically consistent power-law energy diffusion and non-zero spatial curvature provides a viable alternative to ΛCDM. It naturally resolves the Hubble tension, favors a closed universe, and mimics quintessence-like dark energy, all while satisfying entropy constraints and maintaining agreement with cosmic age and sound-horizon measurements.
\n\n
具有热力学自洽的幂律能量扩散与非零空间曲率的单模引力为ΛCDM提供了一个可行的替代方案。它自然地缓解哈勃张力，倾向于闭合宇宙，并模拟类精质暗能量，同时满足熵增约束，并与宇宙年龄及声视界观测保持一致。

Abstract: We investigate the cosmological implications of unimodular gravity (UG) featuring energy diffusion and spatial curvature. While standard diffusion models often suffer from thermodynamic inconsistencies, we propose a phenomenologically viable power-law Ansatz for the diffusion function, $Q(z) = Q_0(1+z)^β$, which strictly satisfies the second law of thermodynamics by demanding positive entropy production ($βQ_0 > 0$). Using a joint statistical analysis with the Pantheon+ Type Ia Supernova compilation and Baryon Acoustic Oscillation (BAO) measurements, we tightly constrain the parameter space. We find a diffusion exponent of $β= 0.503_{-0.126}^{+0.118}$ and a slight preference for a closed spatial geometry with $Ω_{k0} = -0.109_{-0.071}^{+0.076}$ at present time. Remarkably, the consideration of spatial curvature and diffusion naturally alleviates the Hubble tension, yielding $H_0 = 73.350_{-0.226}^{+0.221}$ km/s/Mpc while maintaining a consistent cosmic age of $t_0 \simeq 13.61$ Gyr. Furthermore, the constrained diffusion scales as a stable, quintessence-like effective dark energy ($ω_{\text{eff}} \simeq -0.832$). Thus, unimodular diffusion provides a thermodynamically consistent phenomenological alternative that can alleviate the Hubble tension while preserving both the cosmic age and the sound-horizon scale, with a preference for a closed spatial geometry.

</details>


### [57] [Gauge-invariant cosmological perturbations in Type 3 New General Relativity and background-hierarchy bounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16869)
*Kyosuke Tomonari,Daniel Blixt,Sebastian Bahamonde*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies background-hierarchy bounds in Type~3 of New General Relativity (NGR), a metric-affine gauge theory with two free parameters that preserves spatial rotations and diffeomorphism invariance but breaks Lorentz-boost symmetry. The authors derive constraints on the parameter space by requiring that background evolution contributions do not dominate over quadratic kinetic terms in the perturbed Lagrangian for scalar, vector, and tensor modes around a flat FLRW background, thereby identifying viable regions for cosmological applications.
\n\n
本文研究了New General Relativity（NGR）Type~3中的background-hierarchy bounds。该理论是一种具有两个自由参数的metric-affine规范引力理论，保持空间旋转对称性和diffeomorphism不变性，但破坏Lorentz-boost不变性。作者通过要求背景演化项在扰动拉格朗日量中不超过二次动能项，推导出围绕平坦FLRW背景的标量、矢量和张量模的约束条件，从而确定适用于宇宙学应用的参数空间区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from ensuring the validity of linear perturbation theory in Type~3 NGR for cosmological scenarios. When the background spacetime evolution dominates over the kinetic terms of perturbations—i.e., when background-hierarchy bounds are violated—the perturbative expansion breaks down, rendering predictions unreliable. Thus, identifying the parameter regime where such dominance does not occur is essential for meaningful cosmological modeling within this Lorentz-boost-violating gravity framework.
\n\n
动机源于确保Type~3 NGR在线性扰动理论下对宇宙学场景的有效性。当背景时空演化项主导扰动的动能项时（即违反background-hierarchy bounds），微扰展开失效，导致预测不可靠。因此，在这一破坏Lorentz-boost对称性的引力框架中，识别不发生此类主导的参数区域对于构建有意义的宇宙学模型至关重要。

Method: The authors first revisit the structure of Type~3 NGR, emphasizing gauge choices informed by symmetry considerations in both Dirac--Bergmann constraint analysis and linear perturbation theory for theories with Weitzenböck connection. They then perform a perturbative expansion of the action around a flat Friedmann–Lemaître–Robertson–Walker (FLRW) background, decomposing perturbations into scalar, transverse-vector, and tensor modes. Without restricting to purely gauge-invariant variables, they correctly identify propagating degrees of freedom and extract the quadratic kinetic terms. Background-hierarchy bounds are derived by imposing that coefficients of time-derivative-squared terms in the background-evolution sector remain subdominant compared to those in the kinetic sector for each mode.
\n\n
作者首先回顾Type~3 NGR的结构，强调在Dirac--Bergmann约束分析和线性扰动理论中，基于Weitzenböck联络理论的对称性所指导的规范选择。随后，他们在平坦Friedmann–Lemaître–Robertson–Walker（FLRW）背景上对作用量进行扰动展开，并将扰动分解为标量、横向矢量和张量模。即使不局限于纯规范不变变量，他们也能正确识别传播自由度并提取二次动能项。通过要求背景演化部分中时间导数平方项的系数在每种模下均弱于动能部分的对应系数，推导出background-hierarchy bounds。

Result: The paper successfully derives explicit background-hierarchy bounds for scalar, transverse-vector, and tensor perturbations in Type~3 NGR. These bounds constrain the two free parameters of the theory, delineating a region in parameter space where the kinetic terms dominate over background-evolution contributions. Within this region, linear perturbation theory remains self-consistent and suitable for cosmological applications, despite the absence of Lorentz-boost invariance.
\n\n
本文成功推导出Type~3 NGR中标量、横向矢量和张量扰动的显式background-hierarchy bounds。这些约束限制了该理论的两个自由参数，划定了参数空间中动能项主导背景演化贡献的区域。在此区域内，尽管缺乏Lorentz-boost不变性，线性扰动理论仍保持自洽，适用于宇宙学应用。

Conclusion: Type~3 of New General Relativity can support a consistent linear cosmological perturbation theory provided its two parameters lie within the region defined by the derived background-hierarchy bounds. The analysis confirms that propagating modes can be reliably identified even without using exclusively gauge-invariant variables, and underscores the importance of background-kinetic balance as a viability criterion in Lorentz-boost-violating gravitational theories.
\n\n
New General Relativity的Type~3只要其两个参数位于所推导的background-hierarchy bounds定义的区域内，就能支持自洽的线性宇宙学扰动理论。分析证实，即使不完全使用规范不变变量，也能可靠地识别传播模，并强调了在破坏Lorentz-boost对称性的引力理论中，背景项与动能项之间的平衡是理论可行性的关键判据。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate background-hierarchy bounds in Type~3 of New General Relativity (NGR). These bounds arise when the contribution associated with the evolution of the background spacetime exceeds that of the quadratic kinetic term in the perturbed Lagrangian. Type~3 of NGR has two free parameters and preserves diffeomorphism invariance and spatial rotations, while breaking Lorentz-boost invariance. We first review Type~3 and identify preferable gauge choices for metric-affine gauge theories of gravity with Weitzenböck connection, including NGR, from the viewpoint of symmetry in both Dirac--Bergmann analysis and linear perturbation theory. We then revisit the perturbative analysis of Type~3 and show that the propagating modes are correctly identified even when the perturbed Lagrangian is not written solely in terms of gauge-invariant variables. Finally, we derive the background-hierarchy bounds for the scalar, transverse-vector, and tensor modes around a flat FLRW background, and identify the region of parameter space in which the linear perturbation theory of Type~3 remains viable for cosmological applications.

</details>


### [58] [Boson Stars surrounded by Polish Doughnuts in Scalar-Tensor Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17078)
*Kristian Gjorgjieski,Maxim Rose,Burkhard Kleihaus,Jutta Kunz,Petya Nedkova*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper studies thick accretion disks (Polish Doughnuts) around rotating boson stars in general relativity (GR) and scalar-tensor theories, showing that spontaneous scalarization qualitatively alters spacetime geometry, leading to more compact, strongly bound disks—sometimes without innermost stable circular orbits (ISCOs) or even exhibiting two-centered structures—offering potential observational signatures of modified gravity in strong-field regimes.
\n\n
本文研究了广义相对论（GR）和标量-张量理论中标量化旋转玻色星周围的厚吸积盘（Polish Doughnuts），表明自发标量化会定性地改变时空几何结构，导致更致密、束缚更强的吸积盘——有时甚至不存在最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO），或呈现双中心结构——为强场区域中修改引力理论提供了潜在的观测特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore how spontaneous scalarization in alternative theories of gravity (specifically scalar-tensor theories) modifies the strong-field spacetime geometry around compact objects like boson stars, and how these modifications imprint on observable properties of accretion disks. Understanding such effects can provide smoking-gun signatures to distinguish GR from modified gravity using astrophysical observations of accretion flows.
\n\n
动机在于探索替代理论（特别是标量-张量理论）中的自发标量化如何改变玻色星等致密天体周围的强场时空几何，并研究这些改变如何影响吸积盘的可观测性质。理解此类效应可为利用吸积流的天文观测区分广义相对论与修改引力理论提供决定性证据。

Method: The authors construct equilibrium models of thick accretion disks with constant specific angular momentum $l = l_0$ around rotating boson stars in both GR and scalar-tensor theories. They focus on spontaneously scalarized solutions and compare them with their GR counterparts across the parameter space of boson star mass and compactness. The analysis involves solving the Einstein–Klein–Gordon equations for the boson star background and then computing the relativistic hydrodynamics of the disk in that fixed spacetime, examining orbital structure (e.g., existence of ISCOs) and disk morphology.
\n\n
作者构建了在广义相对论和标量-张量理论中围绕旋转玻色星的具有恒定比角动量 $l = l_0$ 的厚吸积盘平衡模型。他们聚焦于自发标量化解，并在玻色星质量和致密度参数空间中将其与对应的广义相对论解进行比较。分析包括求解爱因斯坦–克莱因–戈登场方程以获得玻色星背景时空，然后在此固定时空中计算吸积盘的相对论流体力学，考察轨道结构（如ISCO的存在性）和盘的形态。

Result: Scalarization dramatically reshapes the spacetime: some scalarized boson stars lack innermost stable circular orbits (ISCOs), permitting stable geodesic motion down to the origin and supporting quasi-spherical, highly compact disks. For the most massive scalarized configurations, the specific angular momentum profile becomes non-monotonic, enabling two-centered Polish Doughnuts connected by a cusp. In all cases, disks around scalarized boson stars are more compact and possess deeper gravitational binding than their GR analogs.
\n\n
标量化显著重塑了时空结构：某些标量化玻色星缺乏最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO），允许稳定测地线运动直达中心，从而支持准球形且高度致密的吸积盘。对于质量最大的标量化构型，其比角动量剖面呈现非单调性，使得吸积盘可形成由尖点连接的双中心Polish Doughnuts结构。在所有情形中，标量化玻色星周围的吸积盘都比其广义相对论对应物更致密、引力束缚更深。

Conclusion: The distinctive morphological features of accretion disks around spontaneously scalarized boson stars—such as the absence of ISCOs, quasi-spherical compactness, and multi-centered structures—provide clear theoretical predictions for observational tests of strong-field gravity. These features could serve as discriminators between GR and scalar-tensor theories in future high-resolution observations of accreting compact objects.
\n\n
自发标量化玻色星周围吸积盘的独特形态特征——如ISCO缺失、准球形致密性以及多中心结构——为强场引力的观测检验提供了明确的理论预言。这些特征可在未来对吸积致密天体的高分辨率观测中用作区分广义相对论与标量-张量理论的判据。

Abstract: We investigate thick accretion disks (Polish Doughnuts) around rotating self-interacting boson stars in general relativity and scalar-tensor theories, focusing on spontaneously scalarized solutions and their general relativistic counterparts. Using equilibrium models with constant specific angular momentum, we analyze disk structures across the parameter space, with emphasis on the phase transition between GR and scalarized configurations. We find that scalarization induces qualitative changes in the spacetime that significantly affect disk morphology. In particular, scalarized boson stars can lack innermost circular orbits, allowing stable motion down to the center and enabling highly compact, quasi-spherical disks. For the most massive scalarized solutions, a non-monotonic angular momentum profile further permits two-centered disk configurations connected by a cusp. Overall, disks around scalarized boson stars are more compact and more strongly bound than those in general relativity, highlighting distinctive features that may serve as observational signatures of alternative gravity theories in the strong-field regime.

</details>


### [59] [Dynamic Aspects of Bumblebee Gravity: Post-Newtonian Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17516)
*Jie Zhu,Hao Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper analyzes Bumblebee gravity using the parameterized post-Newtonian (PPN) formalism, showing that self-consistency up to 1.5PN order requires $\\lambda = -\\xi/2$, implying a direct coupling between the Bumblebee field $B_\\mu$ and the Einstein tensor. Tachyonic stability demands $V''(0)=0$. This setup leads to non-zero PPN parameters $\\alpha_1$, $\\alpha_2$, and a new logarithmically growing potential $U_B$, indicating preferred-frame effects due to Lorentz violation. Observational bounds from pulsar timing constrain $|\\ell| \\lesssim 1.6\\times 10^{-9}$.
\n\n
本文利用参数化后牛顿（PPN）方法分析了Bumblebee引力理论，表明在1.5PN阶下自洽性要求$\\lambda = -\\xi/2$，这对应于Bumblebee场$B_\\mu$与Einstein张量的直接耦合。快子稳定性要求势函数满足$V''(0)=0$。在此条件下，PPN度规给出非零的参数$\\alpha_1$、$\\alpha_2$以及一个具有对数渐进行为的新PPN势$U_B$，反映出由Lorentz对称性破缺导致的优先参考系效应。脉冲星计时观测进一步限制$|\\ell| \\lesssim 1.6\\times 10^{-9}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the phenomenological viability and theoretical consistency of Bumblebee gravity—a model of spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking—by embedding it within the well-established PPN framework, which allows comparison with precision solar system and binary pulsar tests of gravity.
\n\n
动机在于通过将Bumblebee引力（一种自发Lorentz对称性破缺模型）嵌入成熟的参数化后牛顿（PPN）框架中，以评估其现象学可行性和理论自洽性，从而与高精度太阳系及双脉冲星引力实验进行比较。

Method: The authors apply the parameterized post-Newtonian (PPN) expansion to the action of Bumblebee gravity, systematically solving the field equations up to 1.5 post-Newtonian order. They impose self-consistency conditions and tachyonic stability ($V''(0)=0$) on the Bumblebee potential $V(B_\\mu B^\\mu \\pm b^2)$, and derive the resulting PPN metric potentials and parameters.
\n\n
作者将参数化后牛顿（PPN）展开应用于Bumblebee引力的作用量，系统地求解场方程至1.5PN阶。他们对Bumblebee势$V(B_\\mu B^\\mu \\pm b^2)$施加自洽性条件和快子稳定性条件（$V''(0)=0$），并推导出相应的PPN度规势和参数。

Result: The analysis yields that PPN self-consistency at 1.5PN requires $\\lambda = -\\xi/2$, leading to non-vanishing preferred-frame parameters $\\alpha_1$ and $\\alpha_2$, and a new PPN potential $U_B$ with logarithmic asymptotics. The vanishing of $U_B$ further requires $\\xi = \\kappa/2$ or $V^{(3)}(0) = 0$. In the small-$\\ell$ limit, $\\alpha_2 \\simeq -\\ell_2$, giving the observational bound $|\\ell| \\lesssim 1.6 \\times 10^{-9}$ from pulsar timing.
\n\n
分析表明，在1.5PN阶下PPN自洽性要求$\\lambda = -\\xi/2$，导致非零的优先参考系参数$\\alpha_1$和$\\alpha_2$，以及一个具有对数渐进行为的新PPN势$U_B$。若要求$U_B$消失，则需额外满足$\\xi = \\kappa/2$或$V^{(3)}(0) = 0$。在小$\\ell$极限下，$\\alpha_2 \\simeq -\\ell_2$，由此脉冲星计时观测给出约束$|\\ell| \\lesssim 1.6 \\times 10^{-9}$。

Conclusion: Bumblebee gravity exhibits observable preferred-frame effects through non-zero PPN parameters $\\alpha_1$ and $\\alpha_2$, confirming its departure from General Relativity due to Lorentz violation. The tight constraint on $\\ell$ demonstrates that such Lorentz-breaking models are highly restricted by current gravitational experiments, unless fine-tuned to suppress $U_B$.
\n\n
Bumblebee引力通过非零的PPN参数$\\alpha_1$和$\\alpha_2$展现出可观测的优先参考系效应，证实了其因Lorentz对称性破缺而偏离广义相对论。对$\\ell$的严格限制表明，除非通过精细调节抑制$U_B$，否则此类Lorentz破缺模型已被当前引力实验高度限制。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the dynamic aspects of Bumblebee gravity via the parameterized post-Newtonian method. We find that the PPN framework is self-consistent up to 1.5PN order if and only if $λ= -ξ/2$, which corresponds to a direct coupling between the Bumblebee field $B_μ$ and the Einstein tensor. The requirement of tachyonic stability restricts the Bumblebee potential to satisfy $V''(0)=0$. In the specific case where $λ= -ξ/2$, the resulting PPN metric yields non-vanishing values for the parameters $α_1$ and $α_2$, as well as a novel PPN potential $U_B$ that exhibits a logarithmic asymptotic growth. The vanishing of the potential $U_B$ necessitates the additional constraints $ξ= κ/2$ or $V^{(3)}(0) = 0$. These results signify the presence of preferred-frame effects, a direct consequence of the Lorentz symmetry breaking in the model. In the limit of small $\ell$, we obtain $α_2 \simeq -\ell_2$, which yields a constraint of $|\ell| \lesssim 1.6\times 10^{-9}$ based on pulsar timing observations.

### [60] [Impact of the axion-like self-interactions in gravitational atoms for LISA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17589)
*Samuel Gómez Gómez,Xisco Jimenez Forteza,Carlos Palenzuela Luque*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates how ultralight self-interacting bosonic halos (e.g., axion-like particles) around massive black holes affect gravitational wave signals from extreme- and intermediate-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs/IMRIs). It shows that LISA can detect the resulting waveform dephasing due to dynamical friction, thereby constraining boson mass $m_\mathrm{dm} \sim 10^{-17}$–$10^{-15}\,\mathrm{eV}$ and decay constant $f_a \sim 10^{10}$–$3.2 \times 10^{12}\,\mathrm{GeV}$, even without couplings to Standard Model fields.
\n\n
本文研究了大质量黑洞周围的超轻自相互作用玻色子晕（如类轴子粒子）对极端质量和中等质量比旋进（EMRI/IMRI）引力波信号的影响。研究表明，LISA 可以通过动力学摩擦引起的波形相位偏移探测此类效应，从而限制玻色子质量 $m_\mathrm{dm} \sim 10^{-17}$–$10^{-15}\,\mathrm{eV}$ 和衰变常数 $f_a \sim 10^{10}$–$3.2 \times 10^{12}\,\mathrm{GeV}$，且无需依赖与标准模型场的额外耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ultralight bosons like axion-like particles are compelling dark matter candidates that can form macroscopic Bose-Einstein condensates—so-called gravitational atoms—around compact objects. While previous studies often assumed static halo profiles, this work employs a recently proposed dynamical formation mechanism, offering a more realistic description of the halo structure. The motivation is to assess whether future space-based gravitational wave observatories like LISA can probe the particle physics parameters of such dark matter candidates through their gravitational influence alone, especially via dynamical friction effects on inspiraling compact objects.
\n\n
类轴子等超轻玻色子是引人注目的暗物质候选者，可在致密天体周围形成宏观玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚态（即所谓“引力原子”）。以往研究多采用静态晕轮廓假设，而本文采用近期提出的动力学形成机制，能更真实地描述晕结构。其动机在于评估未来空间引力波探测器（如 LISA）能否仅通过引力效应（特别是对旋进致密天体的动力学摩擦）来探测此类暗物质候选者的粒子物理参数。

Method: The authors model the gravitational atom using a dynamical halo formation scenario consistent with axion-like particle physics, incorporating both gravitational potential and repulsive self-interactions characterized by the decay constant $f_a$. They compute the dynamical friction force exerted by the halo on an inspiraling secondary compact object in EMRI/IMRI systems. This modifies the orbital evolution and induces dephasing in the gravitational waveform relative to vacuum GR predictions. Using Fisher matrix analysis, they estimate LISA’s ability to measure deviations in the signal for various boson masses $m_\mathrm{dm}$, decay constants $f_a$, dark matter densities $\rho_\mathrm{dm}$, and total binary masses $M$, assuming signal-to-noise ratios up to $\sim 100$.
\n\n
作者采用符合类轴子粒子物理的动力学晕形成模型，同时包含引力势和由衰变常数 $f_a$ 表征的排斥性自相互作用。他们计算了该晕对 EMRI/IMRI 系统中旋进次级致密天体施加的动力学摩擦力，该力会改变轨道演化并在引力波形中引入相对于真空广义相对论预测的相位偏移。通过 Fisher 矩阵分析，他们在不同玻色子质量 $m_\mathrm{dm}$、衰变常数 $f_a$、暗物质密度 $\rho_\mathrm{dm}$ 和总质量 $M$ 下，评估 LISA 在信噪比最高约 $\sim 100$ 时探测此类偏差的能力。

Result: For conservative dark matter densities based on Navarro-Frenk-White (NFW) profile central values, LISA can probe $m_\mathrm{dm} \sim 10^{-17}$–$10^{-15}\,\mathrm{eV}$ and $f_a \sim 10^{10}$–$3.2 \times 10^{12}\,\mathrm{GeV}$ using binaries with total mass $M \sim 10^4$–$10^5\,M_\odot$. With higher densities ($\rho_\mathrm{dm} = 10^3\,\mathrm{GeV/cm^3}$) and SNR $\sim 20$, a benchmark point at $m_\mathrm{dm} \sim 2.5 \times 10^{-16}\,\mathrm{eV}$ and $f_a \sim 6.3 \times 10^{10}\,\mathrm{GeV}$ maximizes dephasing and allows recovery of particle parameters at the percent level. Crucially, these constraints rely solely on gravitational interactions, requiring no couplings to Standard Model fields.
\n\n
在基于 Navarro-Frenk-White（NFW）轮廓中心值的保守暗物质密度下，LISA 利用总质量 $M \sim 10^4$–$10^5\,M_\odot$ 的双星系统可探测 $m_\mathrm{dm} \sim 10^{-17}$–$10^{-15}\,\mathrm{eV}$ 和 $f_a \sim 10^{10}$–$3.2 \times 10^{12}\,\mathrm{GeV}$。当密度更高（$\rho_\mathrm{dm} = 10^3\,\mathrm{GeV/cm^3}$）且信噪比 $\sim 20$ 时，基准点 $m_\mathrm{dm} \sim 2.5 \times 10^{-16}\,\mathrm{eV}$ 和 $f_a \sim 6.3 \times 10^{10}\,\mathrm{GeV}$ 使相位偏移最大化，并可在百分之一精度恢复粒子参数。关键的是，这些限制仅依赖引力相互作用，无需与标准模型场耦合。

Conclusion: LISA will be capable of probing ultralight axion-like dark matter through purely gravitational signatures in EMRI/IMRI waveforms. By measuring dephasing induced by dynamical friction in self-interacting bosonic halos, it can constrain both the boson mass and self-coupling strength (via $f_a$) over a wide parameter range. This provides a novel, model-independent avenue to test fundamental particle physics beyond the Standard Model using gravitational wave astronomy.
\n\n
LISA 将能够通过 EMRI/IMRI 波形中的纯引力信号探测超轻类轴子暗物质。通过测量自相互作用玻色子晕中动力学摩擦引起的相位偏移，可在宽广参数范围内同时限制玻色子质量和自耦合强度（通过 $f_a$）。这为利用引力波天文学检验超出标准模型的基本粒子物理提供了一条新颖且模型无关的途径。

Abstract: Ultralight bosons with self-interactions, such as axion-like particles, can form astrophysical Bose-Einstein condensates around stars or compact objects, often referred to as gravitational atoms. In this work, we adopt a recently proposed dynamical formation mechanism for these halos and estimate their impact on extreme- and intermediate-mass-ratio inspirals when present around the primary black hole. We show that, for signal-to-noise ratios $\lesssim 100$, LISA can distinguish gravitational waveforms from binaries embedded in such halo overdensities. Our analysis indicates that LISA can probe boson masses $m_\mathrm{dm}\sim10^{-17}$-$10^{-15}\,\mathrm{eV}$ and decay constants $f_a\sim10^{10}$-$3.2 \times 10^{12}\,\mathrm{GeV}$ using binaries with total masses $M\sim10^4$-$10^5\,M_\odot$, assuming conservative DM densities consistent with the central values of Navarro-Frenk-White profiles. Allowing for higher background densities and different extreme-mass-ratio configurations further extends the accessible parameter space. Moreover, we find that for a binary configuration with $M\sim10^4\,M_\odot$, $ρ_\mathrm{dm} = 10^3\,\mathrm{GeV/cm^3}$, and signal-to-noise ratio $\mathrm{SNR}\sim20$, a particle mass of $m_\mathrm{dm}\sim2.5\times10^{-16}\,\mathrm{eV}$ and decay constant $f_a\sim6.3\times10^{10}\,\mathrm{GeV}$ maximize the dephasing due to dynamical friction, enabling the recovery of the particle parameters at the percent level. These results demonstrate that LISA can place constraints on axion-like particle masses and self-interactions without requiring additional couplings to Standard Model fields.

</details>


### [61] [Constraints on non-canonical chaotic inflation from ACT DR6 and BICEP/Keck data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16772)
*Wei Yang,Chen-Hao Wu,Ya-Peng Hu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper demonstrates that chaotic inflation models with non-canonical kinetic terms can be made viable by constraining the non-canonical parameter $α$ using high-precision CMB data and equilateral non-Gaussianity limits. For potential indices $n = 1/3, 2/3, 1$, tight bounds on $α$ are derived, and the required e-folding number naturally settles near $N \simeq 54$.
\n\n
本文表明，通过利用高精度宇宙微波背景（CMB）数据和对等边非高斯性 $f_{\rm NL}^{\rm equil}$ 的限制，可以约束非标准动能项中的参数 $α$，从而使原本被排除的混沌暴胀模型重新变得可行。对于势函数指数 $n = 1/3, 2/3, 1$，分别给出了 $α$ 的严格限制，且所需的 e-fold 数自然收敛到 $N \simeq 54$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard chaotic inflation with canonical kinetic terms is strongly disfavored by Planck/BICEP data for simple monomial potentials (e.g., $V(ϕ) ∝ ϕ^n$ with $n ≥ 1$). This work explores whether introducing a non-canonical kinetic term—parameterized by $α$—can reconcile these models with current cosmological observations, particularly through constraints from equilateral non-Gaussianity and CMB power spectra.
\n\n
标准混沌暴胀模型在具有正则动能项的情况下，对于简单的单项式势（如 $V(ϕ) ∝ ϕ^n$ 且 $n ≥ 1$）已被 Planck/BICEP 数据强烈排除。本研究旨在探索引入由参数 $α$ 描述的非正则动能项是否能通过等边非高斯性及 CMB 功率谱的观测约束，使这些模型与当前宇宙学数据重新兼容。

Method: The authors adopt a non-canonical scalar field action with kinetic term $\\mathcal{L}_{\\rm kin} ∝ (X/M_{\\rm Pl}^4)^α$, where $X = -\\frac{1}{2}∂_μϕ∂^μϕ$. They apply the slow-roll approximation to derive background evolution and perturbation equations. Primordial power spectra and bispectra (for $f_{\\rm NL}^{\\rm equil}$) are computed numerically. Parameter inference is performed via Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) using the joint P-ACT-LB-BK18 dataset, which combines Planck, ACT, SPT, and BICEP/Keck data.
\n\n
作者采用一个非正则标量场作用量，其动能项为 $\\mathcal{L}_{\\rm kin} ∝ (X/M_{\\rm Pl}^4)^α$，其中 $X = -\\frac{1}{2}∂_μϕ∂^μϕ$。他们应用慢滚近似推导背景演化和扰动方程，并数值求解原初功率谱和双谱（用于计算 $f_{\\rm NL}^{\\rm equil}$）。参数推断通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法完成，使用联合的 P-ACT-LB-BK18 数据集（包含 Planck、ACT、SPT 和 BICEP/Keck 数据）。

Result: For chaotic potentials with $n = 1/3$, $2/3$, and $1$, the non-canonical parameter is constrained at $1σ$ to $α = 8.8^{+1.6}_{-2.8}$, $11.7^{+1.7}_{-2.6}$, and $16.4^{+3.7}_{-7.0}$, respectively. The required number of e-folds converges naturally to $N ≃ 54$ without fine-tuning. These results place previously excluded chaotic models within the $1σ$ observational allowed region when non-canonical kinetics are included.
\n\n
对于 $n = 1/3$、$2/3$ 和 $1$ 的混沌势，非正则参数 $α$ 在 $1σ$ 置信水平下分别被限制为 $8.8^{+1.6}_{-2.8}$、$11.7^{+1.7}_{-2.6}$ 和 $16.4^{+3.7}_{-7.0}$。所需的 e-fold 数自然收敛到 $N ≃ 54$，无需精细调节。这些结果表明，当引入非正则动能项后，原先被排除的混沌暴胀模型可重新落入观测数据的 $1σ$ 允许区域内。

Conclusion: Non-canonical kinetic terms provide a theoretically viable mechanism to rescue otherwise ruled-out chaotic inflation scenarios. The interplay between the potential index $n$ and the kinetic exponent $α$ allows compatibility with high-precision CMB data, while simultaneously predicting observable levels of equilateral non-Gaussianity and a natural e-folding number around 54.
\n\n
非正则动能项为拯救原本被排除的混沌暴胀模型提供了一种理论可行的机制。势函数指数 $n$ 与动能指数 $α$ 之间的相互作用使得模型能够与高精度 CMB 数据兼容，同时预言可观测水平的等边非高斯性以及自然的 e-fold 数（约 54）。

Abstract: In this study, we precisely evaluated the feasibility of the chaotic inflation model within a non-canonical kinetic framework. By applying the slow-roll approximation and imposing constraints on the equilateral non-Gaussianity $f_{\rm NL}^{\rm equil}$, we imposed constraints on the feasible range of the potential index $n$. We established physical bounds for the non-canonical parameter $α$. To obtain precise parameter constraints, we solved the primordial perturbation equations numerically and conducted a rigorous MCMC analysis by using a comprehensive joint P-ACT-LB-BK18 dataset. For these potentials $n=1/3$, $2/3$, and $1$, our results respectively tightly limit $α$ to the levels of $8.8^{+1.6}_{-2.8}$, $11.7^{+1.7}_{-2.6}$, and $16.4^{+3.7}_{-7.0}$, within the corresponding $1σ$ confidence intervals. Meanwhile, the required number of $e$-foldings naturally converges to $N \simeq 54$, without the need for fine-tuning. These findings confirm that non-standard mechanisms can resurrect excluded chaotic inflation models within the $1σ$ allowed regions of high-precision cosmological data.

</details>


### [62] [Junction Conditions and Gravitational Collapse in Scalar-Tensor-Vector Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17615)
*Debanjan Debnath,Anant Badal,Kaushik Bhattacharya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper derives junction conditions for Scalar-Tensor-Vector Gravity (STVG/MOG) and applies them to model gravitational collapse by matching an interior FLRW spacetime (with baryonic matter and dark energy) to an exterior Reissner–Nordström (RN)-like spacetime across a charged shell. It demonstrates that RN-like black holes—both extremal and sub-extremal—can form in finite proper time.
\n\n
本文推导了标量-张量-矢量引力理论（Scalar-Tensor-Vector Gravity, STVG/MOG）的连接条件，并将其应用于引力坍缩模型：通过一个携带STVG电荷的壳层，将内部包含重子物质和暗能量的FLRW时空与外部静态球对称的类Reissner–Nordström（RN）时空进行匹配。研究表明，在有限固有时内可形成类RN黑洞，包括极端和次极端情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard General Relativity (GR) faces challenges in explaining galactic rotation curves and cosmological observations without invoking dark matter. Scalar-Tensor-Vector Gravity (STVG/MOG), proposed by J. W. Moffat, offers a modified gravity framework that can account for these phenomena through additional fields: a scalar field $G(x)$, a massive vector field $\\phi_\\mu$, and auxiliary scalar fields. However, the mathematical structure of STVG—particularly its junction conditions across boundaries—had not been rigorously formulated. Understanding gravitational collapse in this theory requires consistent matching between interior and exterior spacetimes, which motivates the derivation of these junction conditions.
\n\n
广义相对论（GR）在不引入暗物质的情况下难以解释星系旋转曲线和宇宙学观测。J. W. Moffat提出的标量-张量-矢量引力理论（STVG/MOG）通过引入额外场——标量场 $G(x)$、有质量矢量场 $\\phi_\\mu$ 和辅助标量场——提供了一种修改引力的框架以解释这些现象。然而，STVG理论中跨边界区域的连接条件尚未被严格建立。要研究该理论中的引力坍缩过程，必须在内部与外部时空之间建立自洽的匹配条件，这构成了本文推导连接条件的核心动机。

Method: Starting from the full STVG action, the authors perform a variational principle with a timelike hypersurface separating two spacetime regions. They derive generalized Israel–Darmois junction conditions adapted to STVG by ensuring continuity of the induced metric and accounting for possible distributional sources on the shell. The matching is applied between an interior FLRW metric containing baryonic matter and dark energy, and an exterior static, spherically symmetric RN-like solution of STVG characterized by mass $M$ and STVG-charge $Q_{\\text{STVG}}$. The dynamics of the shell are governed by conservation laws derived from the field equations, leading to effective equations of motion analogous to those in GR but modified by STVG contributions.
\n\n
作者从完整的STVG作用量出发，在分隔两个时空区域的类时超曲面上应用变分原理，推导出适用于STVG的广义Israel–Darmois连接条件：要求诱导度规连续，并考虑壳层上可能存在的分布源。他们将这一匹配应用于内部包含重子物质和暗能量的FLRW度规与外部由质量 $M$ 和STVG电荷 $Q_{\\text{STVG}}$ 表征的静态球对称类RN解之间。壳层的动力学由场方程导出的守恒律决定，从而得到类似于GR但受STVG修正的有效运动方程。

Result: Two explicit collapse models are constructed: (1) a scenario where the collapsing system evolves into an extremal RN-like black hole with $M = |Q_{\\text{STVG}}|$, and (2) another where it approaches a sub-extremal RN-like configuration with $M > |Q_{\\text{STVG}}|$. In both cases, horizon formation occurs in finite proper time as measured by comoving observers inside the collapsing region. The asymptotic observer sees the collapse proceed toward horizon formation without violation of cosmic censorship within the STVG framework.
\n\n
本文构建了两个明确的坍缩模型：(1) 坍缩系统演化为极端类RN黑洞（满足 $M = |Q_{\\text{STVG}}|$）；(2) 系统趋向于次极端类RN构型（满足 $M > |Q_{\\text{STVG}}|$）。在这两种情形中，共动观测者测得的固有时内均会发生视界形成。远处渐近观测者看到坍缩朝向视界形成进行，且在STVG框架内未违反宇宙监督假设。

Conclusion: The successful formulation of junction conditions in STVG enables a consistent treatment of gravitational collapse in this modified gravity theory. The results demonstrate that RN-like black holes—central objects in STVG phenomenology—can form dynamically from realistic collapse scenarios involving standard matter and dark energy. This provides a theoretical foundation for studying compact object formation and black hole physics beyond General Relativity within the STVG/MOG framework.
\n\n
STVG中连接条件的成功建立使得在此修改引力理论中对引力坍缩进行自洽处理成为可能。结果表明，作为STVG唯象学核心的类RN黑洞，能够从包含标准物质和暗能量的现实坍缩过程中动态形成。这为在STVG/MOG框架下研究致密天体形成及广义相对论之外的黑洞物理奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: We formulate the junction conditions for Scalar-Tensor-Vector Gravity (STVG/MOG), proposed by J.~W.~Moffat. Using these conditions, the theory of gravitational collapse is constructed. In the collapsing process, an interior Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) spacetime with baryonic matter and dark energy is matched with an exterior static, spherically symmetric Reissner--Nordström (RN)-like spacetime through a shell that carries STVG-charge. Starting from the standard STVG action, we derive the junction conditions across a boundary that relate the values of the various field quantities and their derivatives across the matching surface. Using the matching conditions and the nature of the collapsing shell, it is shown that a gravitational collapse can proceed in the present situation, and one can have RN-like horizon formation in finite proper time. We present two simplified models of gravitational collapse in this article: one ends up as an extremal RN-like black hole, and the other tends to collapse towards a sub-extremal RN-like black hole, as observed by an asymptotic observer at an infinite distance away from the collapsing system.

</details>


### [63] [Scattering, absorption and greybody factor of scalar particles by Lorentz-violating charged black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17647)
*F. M. Belchior*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies the scattering and absorption of spin-0 particles by electrically charged black holes in two Lorentz-violating (LV) gravity models: the bumblebee model with a vector field acquiring a vacuum expectation value (VEV), and a model with a self-interacting Kalb-Ramond field coupled to gravity. Using the partial wave method, the authors compute scattering cross sections, absorption probabilities, and greybody factors (GFs), highlighting how both the LV parameter and black hole charge affect these observables.
\n\n
本文研究了在两种洛伦兹对称性自发破缺（LV）的引力模型中，自旋为0的粒子被带电黑洞散射和吸收的问题：其一是矢量场获得真空期望值（VEV）的“大黄蜂”（bumblebee）模型，其二是与引力耦合的自相互作用Kalb-Ramond场模型。作者采用分波法计算了散射截面、吸收概率和灰体因子（GFs），揭示了LV参数和黑洞电荷对这些可观测量的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from exploring quantum-gravitational effects through effective field theories that incorporate spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking (LSB). Such frameworks—like the bumblebee and Kalb-Ramond models—offer testable deviations from general relativity in strong-field regimes. By analyzing how scalar fields interact with charged black holes in these settings, the authors aim to uncover observational signatures of LSB encoded in scattering and absorption phenomena, particularly via greybody factors which modulate Hawking radiation spectra.
\n\n
该研究的动机源于通过包含洛伦兹对称性自发破缺（LSB）的有效场论来探索量子引力效应。诸如大黄蜂模型和Kalb-Ramond模型等框架在强引力场区域提供了广义相对论的可观测偏离。通过分析标量场在这些背景下与带电黑洞的相互作用，作者旨在揭示编码于散射和吸收现象中的LSB观测信号，特别是通过调制霍金辐射谱的灰体因子（greybody factors）。

Method: The authors employ the partial wave decomposition method to solve the Klein-Gordon equation for a minimally coupled spin-0 field in the background of electrically charged black hole solutions derived from two distinct Lorentz-violating gravity models. They impose appropriate boundary conditions at the event horizon and spatial infinity to compute the absorption probability $|T_{\\ell}|^2$ for each angular momentum mode $\\ell$, from which the total absorption cross section and greybody factors are obtained. Scattering amplitudes are constructed from phase shifts $\\delta_{\\ell}$, yielding the differential and total scattering cross sections.
\n\n
作者采用分波展开方法，在由两种不同洛伦兹破缺引力模型导出的带电黑洞背景中求解最小耦合自旋-0场的Klein-Gordon方程。他们在事件视界和空间无穷远处施加适当的边界条件，计算每个角动量模 $\\ell$ 的吸收概率 $|T_{\\ell}|^2$，进而得到总吸收截面和灰体因子。散射振幅由相移 $\\delta_{\\ell}$ 构造，从而获得微分和总散射截面。

Result: The results show that both the Lorentz violation (LV) parameter and the black hole electric charge significantly modify the greybody factors, absorption cross sections, and scattering patterns. Specifically, increasing the LV parameter generally enhances absorption at low frequencies, while electric charge tends to suppress it. The interplay between these parameters leads to nontrivial distortions in the angular distribution of scattered waves and alters the frequency dependence of the GFs compared to standard Reissner-Nordström black holes.
\n\n
结果表明，洛伦兹破缺（LV）参数和黑洞电荷均显著改变了灰体因子、吸收截面和散射模式。具体而言，增大LV参数通常在低频下增强吸收，而电荷则倾向于抑制吸收。这些参数之间的相互作用导致散射波角分布出现非平凡畸变，并使灰体因子的频率依赖性相较于标准Reissner-Nordström黑洞发生改变。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking in gravitational theories leaves imprints on black hole scattering and absorption processes. The computed greybody factors provide a potential observational window into Lorentz-violating physics through modifications to Hawking radiation or accretion disk emissions. This work thus bridges effective field theory approaches to quantum gravity with phenomenological black hole physics.
\n\n
该研究表明，引力理论中的自发洛伦兹对称性破缺会在黑洞散射和吸收过程中留下可观测印记。所计算的灰体因子为通过霍金辐射或吸积盘辐射的修正来探测洛伦兹破缺物理提供了潜在的观测窗口。因此，本工作将量子引力的有效场论方法与黑洞现象学联系起来。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the scattering and absorption of spin 0 particles for electrically charged black holes in two gravity models with spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking. The first one is the so-called bumblebee model that involves a vector field with a nonvanishing vacuum expectation value (VEV), while the second one involves a self-interacting Kalb-Ramond field coupled to gravity. For our purpose, we employ the partial waves method to compute the scattering cross-section and the absorption for these charged black holes. Moreover, we calculate the greybody factors (GFs) for spin 0 particles, showing the influence of both the LV parameter and electric charge.
