### [64] [Warm inflation in Weyl geometric gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16884)
*Runhua Huang,Tiberiu Harko,Shi-Dong Liang,Hong-Hao Zhang,Lei Ming*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper constructs a warm inflationary model within Weyl geometric gravity, where the $\tilde{R}^2$ action is recast as a linear theory with an extra scalar degree of freedom. By including radiation, an inflaton with quartic potential, and a Weyl vector, and adopting a linear dissipation coefficient, the authors numerically demonstrate a viable warm inflation scenario that naturally reheats into a radiation-dominated era, with predictions consistent with ACT observational data.
\n\n
本文在Weyl几何引力理论中构建了一个warm inflation（暖暴胀）模型，其中$\tilde{R}^2$作用量被等价地重构为带有额外标量自由度的线性理论。通过引入辐射、具有四次势的inflaton场以及Weyl矢量，并采用线性耗散系数，作者通过数值计算展示了可行的warm inflation场景，该场景能自然过渡到辐射主导时期，其预言与ACT观测数据一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from exploring alternative gravitational frameworks beyond General Relativity to address early Universe cosmology. Specifically, Weyl geometric gravity offers a conformally invariant foundation, and its $\tilde{R}^2$ extension naturally introduces new degrees of freedom. Warm inflation—where dissipative processes generate radiation during inflation—avoids the need for a separate reheating phase. The paper aims to unify these ideas by embedding warm inflation into Weyl geometry to study how the Weyl vector modifies inflationary dynamics and observables.
\n\n
动机源于探索广义相对论之外的替代理论以研究早期宇宙学。具体而言，Weyl几何引力提供了共形不变的基础，其$\tilde{R}^2$推广自然引入新的自由度。Warm inflation（暖暴胀）通过耗散过程在暴胀期间产生辐射，从而避免了单独的reheating（再加热）阶段。本文旨在将warm inflation嵌入Weyl几何中，研究Weyl矢量如何修正暴胀动力学和可观测量。

Method: The authors start from the conformally invariant gravitational action in Weyl geometry augmented by a $\tilde{R}^2$ term, which they reformulate via variational methods into an equivalent linear theory with an auxiliary scalar field arising from higher-order curvature. They then construct a warm inflationary setup involving three components: the inflaton (with a quartic potential $V(\\phi) \\propto \\phi^4$), radiation, and the Weyl vector field. Dissipation is modeled using the standard linear ansatz $\\Gamma \\propto T$, where $\\Gamma$ is the dissipation coefficient and $T$ is the radiation temperature. The coupled Boltzmann–Friedmann equations are solved numerically for different coupling forms between the Weyl vector and other fields. Cosmological observables (e.g., scalar spectral index $n_s$, tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$) are computed and compared with ACT (Atacama Cosmology Telescope) data.
\n\n
作者从Weyl几何中共形不变的引力作用量出发，加入$\tilde{R}^2$项，并通过变分方法将其重构为等效的线性理论，其中高阶曲率项引入一个辅助标量场。随后构建包含三个组分的warm inflation框架：inflaton场（具有四次势$V(\\phi) \\propto \\phi^4$）、辐射和Weyl矢量场。耗散过程采用标准线性假设$\\Gamma \\propto T$，其中$\\Gamma$为耗散系数，$T$为辐射温度。针对Weyl矢量与其他场的不同耦合形式，数值求解耦合的Boltzmann–Friedmann方程，并计算宇宙学可观测量（如标量谱指数$n_s$、张量-标量比$r$），与ACT（阿塔卡马宇宙学望远镜）数据进行比较。

Result: The numerical analysis shows that inclusion of the Weyl vector modifies the effective friction and potential terms in the inflaton equation of motion, thereby altering the slow-roll dynamics. For appropriate couplings, the model achieves sufficient e-folds of warm inflation and smoothly transitions to a radiation-dominated era without a separate reheating phase. The predicted values of $n_s$ and $r$ fall within the observational bounds set by the latest ACT data, demonstrating phenomenological viability.
\n\n
数值分析表明，引入Weyl矢量会修改inflaton运动方程中的有效摩擦项和势能项，从而改变慢滚动力学。对于合适的耦合形式，该模型可实现足够的e-fold数的warm inflation，并平滑过渡到辐射主导时期，无需单独的reheating阶段。所预言的$n_s$和$r$值落在最新ACT数据的观测限制范围内，证明了其现象学可行性。

Conclusion: The study successfully demonstrates that warm inflation can be consistently realized in Weyl geometric gravity with a $\tilde{R}^2$ correction. The Weyl vector plays a nontrivial role in shaping inflationary dynamics and enables a natural exit to radiation domination. The agreement with ACT constraints suggests that such modified gravity frameworks remain viable candidates for early Universe cosmology and merit further investigation, particularly regarding the nature of the Weyl vector and its possible connections to particle physics or dark sectors.
\n\n
本研究成功证明，在带有$\tilde{R}^2$修正的Weyl几何引力中可以自洽地实现warm inflation。Weyl矢量在塑造暴胀动力学中起着非平凡作用，并使宇宙能自然过渡到辐射主导时期。与ACT观测约束的一致性表明，此类修改引力框架仍是早期宇宙学的可行候选者，值得进一步研究，尤其是Weyl矢量的本质及其与粒子物理或暗区可能的联系。

Abstract: We investigate the warm inflationary scenario in the Weyl geometric gravity theory, in which the action is constructed by adding matter to the simplest conformally invariant gravitational action in Weyl geometry. The $\tilde{R}^2$ theory can be formulated equivalently as a linear theory supplemented by an additional scalar degree of freedom originating from higher-order curvature terms, with the equations of motion obtained via variational methods. We investigate the cosmological implications of the theory by considering the warm inflationary scenario of the early evolution of the Universe, in which radiation, the inflaton field, and the Weyl vector coexist. We consider the widely studied linear dissipation coefficient model along with a quartic potential, and investigate the influence of the Weyl vector term on the dynamics. We have performed numerical computations for different coupling models, and we have successfully developed a warm inflationary model in which the Universe transitions naturally from an inflationary epoch to a radiation-dominated era. The relevant cosmological observables have been calculated and compared with the latest observational constraints from the ACT data.

</details>


### [65] [Positive Running of the Spectral Index for Scalar Theory and Modified Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17813)
*S. D. Odintsov,V. K. Oikonomou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates whether a positive running of the spectral index ($\\alpha_s = dn_s/d\\ln k$) can be realized in viable inflationary models. While standard minimally coupled scalar field and $F(R)$ gravity models struggle to produce positive $\\alpha_s$ consistent with observations, certain nuanced scalar scenarios and Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet (EGB) gravity—compatible with GW170817—can naturally yield positive running while satisfying current CMB constraints.
\n\n
本文研究了在可行的暴胀模型中实现谱指数正跑动（$\\alpha_s = dn_s/d\\ln k$）的可能性。标准的极小耦合标量场和$F(R)$引力模型难以产生与观测一致的正$\\alpha_s$，但某些精细调整的标量场场景以及与GW170817事件相容的Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet（EGB）引力理论可以自然地产生正跑动，同时满足当前CMB约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent ACT data mildly favor a positive running of the spectral index ($\\alpha_s > 0$), which, if confirmed by future CMB experiments, would challenge or rule out many popular inflationary models that predict negative or negligible running. The authors aim to explore whether such a positive $\\alpha_s$ can arise within theoretically well-motivated frameworks: minimally coupled scalar field inflation, $F(R)$ gravity, and Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet (EGB) gravity—especially the latter due to its string theory origins and compatibility with gravitational wave speed constraints from GW170817.
\n\n
近期ACT数据显示谱指数跑动可能为正（$\\alpha_s > 0$），若未来CMB实验确认这一点，将挑战或排除许多预测负或可忽略跑动的流行暴胀模型。作者旨在探索这种正$\\alpha_s$是否能在理论上动机明确的框架中出现：极小耦合标量场暴胀、$F(R)$引力和Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet（EGB）引力——尤其是后者因其弦论起源及与GW170817引力波速度约束的相容性。

Method: The authors analyze three classes of inflationary models: (1) canonical single-field inflation with a minimally coupled scalar, (2) $F(R)$ gravity (treated via conformal transformation to scalar-tensor form), and (3) Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet (EGB) gravity with a scalar field non-minimally coupled to the Gauss-Bonnet invariant. They compute the inflationary observables—spectral index $n_s$, tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$, and running $\\alpha_s$—using the slow-roll approximation. For EGB models, they impose the constraint from GW170817 that the scalar propagation speed equals the speed of light, which fixes the relation between the scalar coupling function and the Gauss-Bonnet coupling. They then examine parameter regimes where $\\alpha_s > 0$ while maintaining compatibility with Planck and ACT bounds on $n_s$ and $r$.
\n\n
作者分析了三类暴胀模型：(1) 极小耦合的正则单标量场暴胀，(2) $F(R)$引力（通过共形变换处理为标量-张量形式），(3) 标量场与Gauss-Bonnet不变量非极小耦合的Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet（EGB）引力。他们利用慢滚近似计算暴胀观测量——谱指数$n_s$、张标比$r$和跑动$\\alpha_s$。对于EGB模型，他们施加GW170817对引力波速度的约束（要求标量扰动传播速度等于光速），从而固定标量耦合函数与Gauss-Bonnet耦合之间的关系。随后，他们考察在满足Planck和ACT对$n_s$与$r$限制的前提下，$\\alpha_s > 0$的参数区域。

Result: For canonical scalar field and $F(R)$ gravity models, achieving $\\alpha_s > 0$ typically requires violating slow-roll conditions or producing observationally disfavored values of $n_s$ or $r$, making them largely incompatible with a positive running scenario under current data. However, finely tuned scalar potentials (e.g., with features or inflection points) can marginally accommodate $\\alpha_s > 0$. In contrast, Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity—when constrained by GW170817—naturally allows for $\\alpha_s > 0$ within a viable slow-roll inflationary regime that simultaneously satisfies Planck and ACT observational bounds.
\n\n
对于正则标量场和$F(R)$引力模型，实现$\\alpha_s > 0$通常需要破坏慢滚条件或导致与观测不符的$n_s$或$r$值，因此在当前数据下基本无法兼容正跑动情形。然而，精细调整的标量势（如具有特征结构或拐点）可勉强容纳$\\alpha_s > 0$。相比之下，在GW170817约束下的Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet引力理论可在满足慢滚条件的可行暴胀机制中自然产生$\\alpha_s > 0$，同时符合Planck和ACT的观测限制。

Conclusion: A confirmed positive running of the spectral index would strongly disfavor standard single-field slow-roll inflation and $F(R)$ gravity as viable paradigms. However, it would provide indirect support for modified gravity theories with higher-curvature corrections, particularly Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity of string-theoretic origin. Future high-precision CMB measurements of $\\alpha_s$ could thus serve as a discriminant between fundamental inflationary frameworks.
\n\n
若谱指数正跑动被证实，将严重削弱标准单场慢滚暴胀和$F(R)$引力作为可行范式的地位。然而，这将间接支持具有高阶曲率修正的修改引力理论，特别是源于弦论的Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet引力。因此，未来对$\\alpha_s$的高精度CMB测量可作为区分不同基本暴胀框架的关键判据。

Abstract: In this work we address the possibility of having a positive running of the spectral index in inflationary theories. The recent ACT data indicate mildly that the running of the spectral index might be positive, and several other physical indications point out this possibility. If the running of the spectral index is confirmed to be positive by future cosmic microwave background experiments, this can rule out quite popular inflationary scenarios. We investigate how it is possible to obtain a positive running of the spectral index in the context of minimally coupled scalar field gravity and modified gravity. For the modified gravity we choose two mainstream and of string origin candidate theories, $F(R)$ gravity and Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity. In the case of scalar field inflation and $F(R)$ gravity inflation, we demonstrate the difficulties for obtaining a positive running of the spectral index for a viable inflationary regime, so scalar theories and $F(R)$ gravity are mostly compatible with the Planck data. But nuanced scalar field scenarios can be compatible with the ACT data and produce a positive running of the spectral index. In the context of Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet theories which are compatible with the GW170817 event, the running of the spectral index can easily be positive while in parallel having a viable inflationary era.

</details>


### [66] [Pole Skipping, Avoided Crossing, and Resonant Excitation in Kerr Quasinormal Modes near Algebraically Special Frequencies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17840)
*Kei-ichiro Kubota,Hayato Motohash*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Kerr quasinormal modes near algebraically special frequencies display anomalous features—bifurcation, disappearance, and nonsmooth Schwarzschild limits. The paper resolves these by analyzing pole-zero dynamics of Green-function components across Riemann sheets: bifurcation arises from avoided crossing with resonant excitation, and disappearance results from pole skipping via cancellation of a quasinormal-mode pole by a Matsubara-mode zero.
\n\n
Kerr 准正规模（quasinormal modes）在代数特殊频率（algebraically special frequencies）附近表现出异常行为——包括表观分岔、消失以及与 Schwarzschild 极限的非光滑连接。本文通过分析 Green 函数构建块在不同 Riemann 面上的极点（pole）与零点（zero）动力学，揭示了这些现象的物理起源：分岔源于伴随共振激发的避免交叉（avoided crossing），而消失则是由于准正规模极点被 Matsubara 模零点抵消所导致的极点跳跃（pole skipping）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The anomalous behavior of Kerr quasinormal modes near algebraically special frequencies—such as apparent bifurcation, mode disappearance, and nonsmooth connection to the Schwarzschild limit—has lacked a clear physical explanation for decades. Understanding these phenomena is crucial for black hole perturbation theory, gravitational-wave physics, and the analytic structure of black hole Green functions.
\n\n
Kerr 准正规模在代数特殊频率附近的异常行为（如表观分岔、模式消失以及与 Schwarzschild 极限的非光滑连接）数十年来缺乏清晰的物理解释。理解这些现象对于黑洞微扰理论、引力波物理以及黑洞 Green 函数的解析结构至关重要。

Method: The authors perform a complex-frequency analysis of the Green function for Teukolsky's equation in the Kerr spacetime, tracking the movement of poles (associated with quasinormal modes) and zeros (including Matsubara modes) across multiple Riemann sheets. They identify interactions between poles and zeros that lead to avoided crossings and pole-zero cancellations, thereby diagnosing the mechanisms behind the observed anomalies.
\n\n
作者对 Kerr 时空下 Teukolsky 方程的 Green 函数进行了复频率分析，追踪了与准正规模相关的极点和包括 Matsubara 模在内的零点在多个 Riemann 面上的运动。他们识别出极点与零点之间的相互作用，这些作用导致避免交叉和极零抵消，从而诊断出观测到的异常现象背后的机制。

Result: The study demonstrates that the apparent bifurcation of quasinormal modes stems from an avoided crossing between nearby poles accompanied by resonant excitation, while their disappearance is due to pole skipping: a quasinormal-mode pole is exactly canceled by a coincident Matsubara-mode zero. This provides a unified resolution to long-standing puzzles regarding the behavior of Kerr quasinormal modes near algebraically special frequencies.
\n\n
研究表明，准正规模的表观分岔源于附近极点之间的避免交叉并伴随共振激发，而其消失则是由于极点跳跃（pole skipping）：一个准正规模极点被重合的 Matsubara 模零点精确抵消。这为 Kerr 准正规模在代数特殊频率附近行为的长期难题提供了统一解释。

Conclusion: The anomalies in Kerr quasinormal-mode spectra near algebraically special frequencies are not pathologies but arise from subtle analytic structures involving pole-zero interactions in the complex frequency plane. This insight clarifies the connection between quasinormal modes, hydrodynamic modes (Matsubara modes), and the global analytic properties of black hole Green functions.
\n\n
Kerr 准正规模谱在代数特殊频率附近的异常并非病态行为，而是源于复频率平面上极点与零点相互作用所导致的精细解析结构。这一见解澄清了准正规模、流体动力学模（Matsubara 模）与黑洞 Green 函数整体解析性质之间的联系。

Abstract: Kerr quasinormal modes near algebraically special frequencies exhibit anomalous behavior, including apparent bifurcation, disappearance, and a nonsmooth connection to the Schwarzschild limit, which has remained puzzling for decades. Tracking poles and zeros of Green-function building blocks across different Riemann sheets, we show that the bifurcation is due to an avoided crossing accompanied by resonant excitation, while the disappearance is due to pole skipping caused by cancellation of a quasinormal-mode pole by a Matsubara-mode zero. This resolves the physical origin of these long-standing anomalies.

</details>


### [67] [Potential Space Symmetries in Ernst-like Formulations of Einstein-Maxwell/ModMax-Scalar field Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17843)
*Leonel Bixano,Tonatiuh Matos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper completes the classification of visible, hidden, sectorial, and discrete symmetries in stationary, axisymmetric Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar Field (EMSF) and Einstein-ModMax-Scalar Field (EMMSF) theories using an Ernst-like real potential space $(f,ε,ψ,χ,κ)$. It identifies the solvable Lie algebra of visible symmetries, characterizes hidden symmetries (Ehlers and Harrison transformations) on invariant subspaces, and shows how EMSF symmetries deform in the frozen ModMax regime. The work also develops a Hamiltonian formulation with Noether charges and Casimir invariants, derives quadratures for metric and gauge potentials via harmonic functions, and applies these transformations to generate new charged and rotating solutions from Weyl scalar--acuum seeds.
\n\n
本文完成了在定态轴对称的 Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar Field (EMSF) 和 Einstein-ModMax-Scalar Field (EMMSF) 理论中，基于 Ernst 型实势空间 $(f,ε,ψ,χ,κ)$ 的可见、隐藏、扇区及离散对称性的完整分类。文章确定了可见对称性的可解 Lie 代数，刻画了不变子空间上的隐藏对称性（Ehlers 变换作用于引力-转动扇区，Harrison 变换作用于静电/静磁扇区），并展示了在冻结 ModMax 区域 ($v=v_0, w=w_0$) 中 EMSF 扇区变换如何变形。研究还构建了扇区代数的 Hamiltonian 表述，包含 Noether 荷与 Casimir 不变量，并通过调和函数导出度规与规范势的求积表达式。最后，这些变换被应用于具有独立引力与标量调和函数的 Weyl 标量真空种子解，生成带电与转动的新解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to fully understand the symmetry structure—both manifest and hidden—of stationary, axisymmetric solutions in coupled gravitational-electromagnetic-scalar systems, particularly extending known integrability techniques from Einstein-Maxwell theory to include scalar fields and the recently proposed ModMax electrodynamics. Such symmetries are crucial for solution generation, integrability, and uncovering hidden conservation laws in nonlinear field theories.
\n\n
动机在于全面理解引力-电磁-标量耦合系统中定态轴对称解的对称性结构（包括显式与隐藏对称性），特别是将 Einstein-Maxwell 理论中已知的可积性技术推广至包含标量场和新近提出的 ModMax 电动力学的情形。这类对称性对于解的生成、可积性分析以及揭示非线性场论中的隐藏守恒律至关重要。

Method: The authors work in a real five-dimensional potential space $(f,ε,ψ,χ,κ)$ analogous to the Ernst formalism. They identify visible symmetries as point transformations forming a solvable Lie algebra. Hidden symmetries are analyzed via their action on invariant subspaces: Ehlers transformation in the gravito-rotational sector and electric/magnetic Harrison transformations in electromagnetic sectors. In the frozen EMMSF limit ($v = v_0$, $w = w_0$), they study deformation of EMSF symmetries. A Hamiltonian framework is constructed where the affine geodesic energy governs the quadrature for the metric function $k$, while Noether charges associated with Killing directions of $ε$ and $χ$ yield $ω$ and $A_\varphi$ via dual harmonic functions. Discrete symmetries are examined through a Lewis-Weyl-Papapetrou frame map. Solution generation is demonstrated by applying sectorial transformations to harmonic Weyl scalar--acuum seeds.
\n\n
作者采用一个五维实势空间 $(f,ε,ψ,χ,κ)$，类比于 Ernst 形式。他们将可见对称性识别为构成可解 Lie 代数的点变换。隐藏对称性通过其在不变子空间上的作用进行分析：Ehlers 变换作用于引力-转动扇区，电/磁 Harrison 变换作用于电磁扇区。在冻结 EMMSF 极限 ($v = v_0$, $w = w_0$) 下，研究 EMSF 对称性的变形。构建了一个 Hamiltonian 框架，其中仿射测地线能量控制度规函数 $k$ 的求积，而与 $ε$ 和 $χ$ 的 Killing 方向相关的 Noether 荷通过共轭调和函数给出 $ω$ 和 $A_\varphi$。离散对称性通过 Lewis-Weyl-Papapetrou 标架映射进行考察。通过将扇区变换应用于调和 Weyl 标量真空种子解，演示了解的生成。

Result: The paper establishes: (1) the complete solvable Lie algebra of visible symmetries in the $(f,ε,ψ,χ,κ)$ space; (2) characterization of hidden symmetries—Ehlers and Harrison—as acting on distinct invariant sectors; (3) in frozen ModMax, coexistence of electric and magnetic Harrison transformations enforces $d w = 0$ and $d[(v^2 + w^2)/w] = 0$, uniquely selecting the frozen sector; (4) a Hamiltonian formulation where $k$ is determined by the affine-geodesic Hamiltonian, and $ω$, $A_\varphi$ are expressed via Noether charges and dual harmonic functions; (5) a discrete symmetry mapping $κ \mapsto κ^{-1}$, $ψ \leftrightarrow χ$ (with sign), $ε \mapsto ε - ψχ$; (6) explicit generation of new charged (via Harrison) and rotating (via Ehlers) solutions from Weyl scalar--acuum seeds, with full quadratures provided for all metric and gauge functions.
\n\n
本文取得以下成果：(1) 在 $(f,ε,ψ,χ,κ)$ 势空间中建立了完整的可见对称性可解 Lie 代数；(2) 将隐藏对称性——Ehlers 与 Harrison 变换——刻画为作用于不同不变扇区；(3) 在冻结 ModMax 情形下，电与磁 Harrison 变换的共存要求 $d w = 0$ 与 $d[(v^2 + w^2)/w] = 0$，从而唯一确定冻结扇区；(4) 构建了 Hamiltonian 表述，其中 $k$ 由仿射测地 Hamiltonian 决定，而 $ω$ 与 $A_\varphi$ 通过 Noether 荷及共轭调和函数表达；(5) 发现一个离散对称性映射：$κ \mapsto κ^{-1}$，$ψ \mapsto χ$，$χ \mapsto -ψ$，$ε \mapsto ε - ψχ$；(6) 从 Weyl 标量真空种子解出发，明确生成了新的带电解（通过 Harrison 映射）与转动态（通过 Ehlers 映射），并给出了所有度规与规范势函数的完整求积表达式。

Conclusion: The symmetry structure of stationary, axisymmetric EMSF and EMMSF theories is richer than previously known, with a unified framework encompassing visible, hidden, sectorial, and discrete symmetries. The frozen ModMax sector emerges naturally from consistency conditions of dual Harrison transformations. The Hamiltonian approach links geometric quantities to conserved Noether charges, enabling systematic solution generation. This provides a powerful toolkit for constructing exact solutions in generalized Einstein-Maxwell-scalar theories with nonlinear electrodynamics.
\n\n
定态轴对称 EMSF 与 EMMSF 理论的对称性结构比以往所知更为丰富，本文提供了一个统一框架，涵盖可见、隐藏、扇区及离散对称性。冻结 ModMax 扇区自然地由对偶 Harrison 变换的一致性条件导出。Hamiltonian 方法将几何量与守恒的 Noether 荷联系起来，从而实现系统化解的生成。这为在包含非线性电动力学的广义 Einstein-Maxwell-标量理论中构造精确解提供了强大工具箱。

Abstract: We complete the visible, hidden, sectorial, and discrete symmetries of Ernst-like potential spaces in stationary, axisymmetric Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar Field (EMSF) and Einstein-ModMax-Scalar Field (EMMSF) theories. In the real potential space \((f,ε,ψ,χ,κ)\), we determine the exact visible symmetries and their solvable Lie algebra. We characterize the hidden symmetries on invariant subspaces: Ehlers acts in the gravito-rotational sector, while electric and magnetic Harrison transformations act in static electromagnetic sectors.
  In the frozen EMMSF regime, \(v=v_0,\ w=w_0\), we show how EMSF sectorial transformations are deformed in ModMax theory. We also show that coexistence of electric and magnetic sectorial Harrison transformations imposes \(d w=0\) and \(d[(v^2+w^2)/w]=0\), selecting precisely the frozen ModMax sector.
  We study the Hamiltonian formulation, Noether charges, and Casimir invariants of the sectorial algebras. In harmonic branches of the \(A,B,C\) one-forms, the affine geodesic energy is constant, so the quadrature for \(k\) is controlled by the affine-geodesic Hamiltonian. The functions \(ω\) and \(A_\varphi\) follow from Noether charges along the Killing directions of \(ε\) and \(χ\), and are written using dual harmonic functions.
  We examine the electric and magnetic Lewis-Weyl-Papapetrou frames and their discrete map, which sends \(κ\mapstoκ^{-1}\), \(ψ\mapstoχ\), \(χ\mapsto-ψ\), and \(ε\mapstoε-ψχ\). Finally, we apply the sectorial transformations to harmonic scalar--acuum Weyl seeds with independent gravitational and scalar harmonics. Frozen-ModMax Harrison maps generate charged branches, while Ehlers generates the gravito-rotational branch. For these solutions we give the final quadratures for \(k\), \(ω\), and \(A_\varphi\).

</details>


### [68] [Cosmological perturbations of TDiff fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18424)
*Antonio L. Maroto,Prado Martín-Moruno,Diego Tessainer*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates scalar field theories in cosmological backgrounds where diffeomorphism invariance is broken down to transverse diffeomorphisms via the matter sector. It develops cosmological perturbation theory for both single- and multi-field setups, analyzes pressure perturbations and adiabaticity, explores interaction-induced corrections in multi-field models due to symmetry breaking, and examines perturbative stability through the effective speed of sound, identifying phenomenologically viable models.
\n\n
本文研究了宇宙学背景下通过物质部分将微分同胚不变性破缺至横截微分同胚子群的标量场理论。文章针对单场和多场模型发展了相应的宇宙学微扰理论，分析了压强微扰的不同贡献、绝热性，以及由于对称性破缺在多场情形中相互作用引起的微扰系数修正，并通过有效声速考察了微扰的稳定性，提出了具有现象学意义的具体模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from exploring cosmological models where spacetime symmetries are partially broken by the matter content—specifically, where full diffeomorphism invariance is reduced to transverse diffeomorphisms. Understanding such symmetry-breaking patterns is crucial for constructing alternative theories of inflation or dark energy that deviate from standard single-clock paradigms, especially in multi-field contexts where new interaction structures and non-adiabatic effects can arise.
\n\n
动机源于探索由物质内容部分破缺时空对称性的宇宙学模型——特别是将完整的微分同胚不变性缩减为横截微分同胚的情形。理解此类对称性破缺模式对于构建偏离标准单时钟范式的暴胀或暗能量替代理论至关重要，尤其在多场情形中可能产生新的相互作用结构和非绝热效应。

Method: The authors formulate cosmological perturbation theory for scalar field models with matter-induced breaking of diffeomorphism invariance down to transverse diffeomorphisms. They decompose the pressure perturbation $\\delta p$ into adiabatic and non-adiabatic components, compute perturbation coefficients in both single- and multi-field scenarios, and analyze the effective speed of sound $c_s^2 = \\delta p / \\delta \\rho$ to assess gradient instabilities. Specific Lagrangian examples respecting the residual symmetry are constructed to illustrate phenomenological viability.
\n\n
作者针对由物质诱导将微分同胚不变性破缺至横截微分同胚的标量场模型，建立了宇宙学微扰理论。他们将压强微扰 $\\delta p$ 分解为绝热与非绝热成分，在单场和多场情形下计算微扰系数，并通过有效声速 $c_s^2 = \\delta p / \\delta \\rho$ 分析梯度不稳定性。文中还构造了满足剩余对称性的具体拉格朗日量实例以展示其现象学可行性。

Result: The paper identifies how symmetry breaking to transverse diffeomorphisms modifies the structure of pressure perturbations, introduces new interaction terms in multi-field models, and alters the adiabatic sound speed. It shows that non-adiabatic contributions arise naturally in multi-field settings due to misalignment between field space trajectories and the symmetry-breaking direction. Stable models require $c_s^2 > 0$, which constrains the form of allowed interactions. Several explicit models satisfying these conditions are presented.
\n\n
论文揭示了破缺至横截微分同胚如何改变压强微扰的结构，在多场模型中引入新的相互作用项，并修正绝热声速。研究表明，由于场空间轨迹与对称性破缺方向之间的错位，非绝热贡献在多场情形中自然出现。稳定模型要求 $c_s^2 > 0$，这限制了允许的相互作用形式。文中给出了若干满足这些条件的具体模型。

Conclusion: Scalar field theories with matter-sector breaking of diffeomorphism invariance to transverse diffeomorphisms provide a consistent framework for cosmological perturbations, yielding rich phenomenology in multi-field contexts through non-adiabatic pressure perturbations and modified sound speeds. The requirement of perturbative stability selects a restricted class of interactions, offering testable signatures for early- and late-time cosmology.
\n\n
物质部分将微分同胚不变性破缺至横截微分同胚的标量场理论为宇宙学微扰提供了自洽框架，在多场情形下通过非绝热压强微扰和修正的声速展现出丰富的现象学。微扰稳定性的要求筛选出一类受限的相互作用，为早期和晚期宇宙学提供了可检验的信号。

Abstract: We study scalar field theories that break diffeomorphism invariance down to the subgroup of transverse diffeomorphisms through the matter sector in cosmological backgrounds. We focus on single- and multi-field models and develop the corresponding cosmological perturbation theory. We analyze the different contributions to the pressure perturbation, discussing the adiabaticity and the effects in the perturbation coefficients of the interactions that arise in the multi-field case as a consequence of the symmetry breaking. We also consider the stability of the perturbations in terms of the effective speed of sound and present particular models that could be of phenomenological interest.

### [69] [Rotating black holes with primary hair in five-dimensional generalized Proca theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17870)
*Mokhtar Hassaine,Ulises Hernandez-Vera*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper constructs exact rotating black hole solutions in five-dimensional generalized Proca theories using a Kerr-Schild ansatz aligned with a null geodesic congruence, yielding analytic metrics with primary hair and two independent angular momenta while preserving the Myers-Perry Kerr-Schild structure augmented by a Proca self-tensor term.
\n\n
本文在五维广义Proca理论中，利用沿零测地线汇的Kerr-Schild ansatz构造了精确的旋转黑洞解，所得度规具有主发（primary hair）和两个独立角动量，并保持Myers-Perry的Kerr-Schild形式，额外增加了由Proca 1-形式自身张量积构成的项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the scarcity of exact analytic black hole solutions in higher-dimensional modified gravity theories with vector fields, especially those exhibiting primary hair—hair not determined solely by conserved charges. Generalized Proca theories offer a theoretically consistent framework for massive vector fields with derivative self-interactions, but their non-linearities typically obstruct closed-form solutions. This work aims to overcome this barrier by exploiting geometric constraints that simplify the field equations.
\n\n
动机源于高维修改引力理论中带有矢量场的精确解析黑洞解极为稀少，尤其是那些具有主发（即发参数不由守恒荷唯一确定）的解。广义Proca理论为具有导数自相互作用的有质量矢量场提供了理论自洽的框架，但其非线性通常阻碍闭式解的获得。本文旨在通过利用能简化场方程的几何约束来克服这一障碍。

Method: The authors employ a Kerr-Schild ansatz for the metric: $g_{\mu\nu} = \bar{g}_{\mu\nu} + H k_\mu k_\nu$, where $\bar{g}_{\mu\nu}$ is the background (e.g., (A)dS), and $k^\mu$ is a null geodesic vector. The Proca field is set as $A_\mu = q(\psi) k_\mu$, with $q$ an arbitrary function of the non-Killing angular coordinate $\psi$. This configuration enforces $A_\mu A^\mu = 0$ on-shell. Substituting into the generalized Proca field equations yields three master equations governing $H$, $q$, and the theory’s coupling functions. Consistency requires these couplings to be discrete constants, leading to algebraically defined solution branches.
\n\n
作者采用Kerr-Schild度规ansatz：$g_{\mu\nu} = \\bar{g}_{\\mu\\nu} + H k_\\mu k_\\nu$，其中$\\bar{g}_{\\mu\\nu}$为背景度规（如(A)dS），$k^\\mu$为零测地线矢量。Proca场设为$A_\\mu = q(\\psi) k_\\mu$，其中$q$是非Killing角坐标$\\psi$的任意函数。该构型保证在壳层上满足$A_\\mu A^\\mu = 0$。将其代入广义Proca场方程后，得到三个控制$H$、$q$及理论耦合函数的主方程。一致性条件要求这些耦合为离散常数，从而导出由代数关系定义的若干解分支。

Result: The paper derives new exact, asymptotically (A)dS rotating black hole solutions in five dimensions with two independent rotation parameters. The metric retains the standard Myers-Perry Kerr-Schild form plus an extra term $A_\mu A_\nu$. The Proca field carries primary hair through an arbitrary function $q(\psi)$, and the allowed theories are restricted to specific branches where the generalized Proca coupling constants satisfy algebraic constraints (e.g., $G_4 = -2G_5/(3r_c)$). These solutions generalize the vacuum Myers-Perry family to include dynamical vector hair.
\n\n
本文导出了五维中新的一类精确、渐近(A)dS的旋转黑洞解，具有两个独立转动参数。度规保持标准Myers-Perry的Kerr-Schild形式，并附加一项$A_\\mu A_\\nu$。Proca场通过任意函数$q(\\psi)$携带主发，且允许的理论被限制在若干分支上，其中广义Proca耦合常数满足代数约束（例如$G_4 = -2G_5/(3r_c)$）。这些解将真空Myers-Perry族推广至包含动力学矢量发的情形。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates that geometrically motivated ansätze can yield fully analytic black hole solutions with primary hair in higher-dimensional generalized Proca theories. The preservation of the Kerr-Schild structure despite the presence of a non-trivial Proca field highlights a hidden integrability. The results significantly extend the known solution space beyond Einstein gravity and provide a new arena for studying hairy black holes, stability, and holographic applications in five dimensions.
\n\n
本文表明，基于几何动机的ansatz可在高维广义Proca理论中产生具有主发的全解析黑洞解。尽管存在非平凡Proca场，Kerr-Schild结构仍得以保持，揭示了一种隐藏的可积性。该结果显著拓展了爱因斯坦引力之外的已知解空间，为研究五维中有发黑洞、稳定性及全息应用提供了新平台。

Abstract: This work presents a new class of exact analytic rotating black hole solutions within five-dimensional generalized Proca theories. Through a Kerr-Schild ansatz where the Proca field is set along a null geodesic congruence, the non-linear field equations reduce to a consistent set of three master equations. This geometric configuration ensures that the vector field remains light-like on-shell, effectively restricting the theory's functional couplings to discrete constants and allowing for a fully analytic treatment. The resulting solutions, incorporating a cosmological constant and two independent angular momenta, exhibit primary hair given by an arbitrary function of the non-Killing angular coordinate. We identify several solution branches defined by specific algebraic relations between the Proca coupling constants, providing a significant generalization of the Myers-Perry family. Notably, the metric retains a Kerr-Schild form identical to the Myers-Perry representation, with an additional contribution constructed from the tensor product of the Proca one-form with itself.

</details>


### [70] [The problem of time: a path integral view](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17935)
*Juan Manuel Diaz,Alejandro Perez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper demonstrates that time evolution in a timeless nonrelativistic closed quantum system emerges via the path integral when a clock subsystem is prepared in a semiclassical `good-clock state'. The same mechanism resolves the `cosine problem'—the appearance of both $\exp(iS/\hbar)$ and $\exp(-iS/\hbar)$ terms—in generally covariant theories like quantum gravity, showing it stems from time-reversal symmetry and time-neutral boundary conditions rather than a flaw requiring modification.
\n\n
本文表明，在一个无时间的非相对论性封闭量子系统中，当通过路径积分方法将某个子系统识别为时钟并置于半经典“好时钟态”时，时间演化便会自然涌现。同样的机制解决了广义协变理论（如量子引力）中的“余弦问题”——即跃迁振幅中同时出现 $\exp(iS/\hbar)$ 与 $\exp(-iS/\hbar)$ 项的现象，指出这是时间反演对称性与时中性边界条件的自然结果，而非需要修正基本动力学的缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how time evolution arises in fundamentally timeless quantum systems, particularly in the context of generally covariant theories like quantum gravity where the Hamiltonian vanishes identically. The operator formalism struggles with this emergence, while the path integral offers a clearer perspective. Additionally, the paper aims to address the so-called `cosine problem' in spin foam models and other path integral regularizations of quantum gravity, where transition amplitudes contain both forward and backward propagating phases, leading some to propose ad hoc modifications.
\n\n
动机在于理解时间演化如何从本质上无时间的量子系统中产生，尤其是在广义协变理论（如量子引力）中，其哈密顿量恒为零。算符/希尔伯特空间形式对此难以处理，而路径积分方法提供了更清晰的视角。此外，本文旨在解决自旋泡沫模型及其他量子引力路径积分正则化中的所谓“余弦问题”——跃迁振幅包含前向与后向传播相位，导致一些研究者提出临时性修正方案。

Method: The authors employ the path integral formulation of a simple nonrelativistic closed quantum system that mimics features of generally covariant theories (e.g., vanishing total Hamiltonian). They identify a subsystem as a `clock' and analyze transition amplitudes between time-neutral boundary states. By preparing the clock in a semiclassical `good-clock state'—a narrow wavepacket peaked around a classical trajectory—they show how interference selects only the forward-propagating phase $\exp(iS/\hbar)$. This approach is then generalized to generally covariant systems with action $S$, linking the emergence of time to the breaking of time-reversal symmetry via the clock’s state, not via modification of dynamics.
\n\n
作者采用一个模拟广义协变理论特征（如总哈密顿量为零）的简单非相对论封闭量子系统的路径积分表述。他们将某子系统识别为“时钟”，并分析时中性边界态之间的跃迁振幅。通过将时钟制备为半经典的“好时钟态”——即在经典轨迹附近尖锐局域的波包——他们展示了干涉如何仅选择前向传播相位 $\exp(iS/\hbar)$。该方法随后被推广至作用量为 $S$ 的广义协变系统，将时间的涌现归因于时钟态对时间反演对称性的破缺，而非对基本动力学的修改。

Result: The key result is that Schrödinger time evolution emerges naturally from a timeless path integral once a clock degree of freedom is introduced and prepared in a semiclassical good-clock state. Furthermore, the `cosine problem'—the presence of both $\exp(\pm iS/\hbar)$ in transition amplitudes—is shown to be a consequence of time-reversal invariance combined with time-neutral boundary conditions. The good-clock state breaks this symmetry effectively, selecting only the forward-propagating amplitude $\exp(iS/\hbar)$ without altering the fundamental path integral measure or dynamics.
\n\n
核心结果是：一旦在无时间的路径积分中引入时钟自由度并将其制备为半经典好时钟态，薛定谔时间演化便会自然涌现。此外，“余弦问题”——即跃迁振幅中同时存在 $\exp(\pm iS/\hbar)$——被证明是时间反演不变性与时中性边界条件共同作用的结果。好时钟态有效破缺该对称性，仅选出前向传播振幅 $\exp(iS/\hbar)$，而无需修改基本路径积分测度或动力学。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that time is not fundamental but emergent in quantum theories with general covariance. The apparent `cosine problem' in approaches like loop quantum gravity is not a pathology but a natural feature reflecting time-reversal symmetry; it is resolved by recognizing the role of semiclassical clock states in defining a time arrow. This reinforces the view that canonical quantum gravity is fundamentally timeless, and time evolution arises only conditionally through relational dynamics involving a physical clock.
\n\n
本文得出结论：在具有广义协变性的量子理论中，时间并非基本概念，而是涌现的。“余弦问题”在圈量子引力等方法中并非病态，而是反映时间反演对称性的自然特征；通过认识到半经典时钟态在定义时间箭头中的作用，该问题得以解决。这强化了如下观点：正则量子引力本质上是无时间的，时间演化仅在涉及物理时钟的关系动力学条件下才出现。

Abstract: We show that the emergence of time evolution in an otherwise timeless nonrelativistic closed quantum system -- viewed as a poor man's model of generally covariant quantum theory -- can be understood from the perspective of the path integral representation. As often happens in the functional integral approach, this viewpoint offers a more intuitive account of features that become cumbersome in the operator/Hilbert-space formulation. We show how Schrödinger evolution emerges once a clock degree of freedom is identified and placed in a suitable semiclassical `good-clock state'.
  Our analysis has a consequence that extends to path integral formulations of generally covariant systems with action $S$ (including gravity). In such theories certain transition amplitudes take the form $\exp(iS/\hbar)+\exp(-iS/\hbar)$ rather than the expected `forward propagating' $\exp(iS/\hbar)$. This feature, known as the {\em cosine problem}, appears in concrete regularizations of the path integral, for example in the spin foam representation defining the physical inner product between spin network states in loop quantum gravity. Both formally and in explicit regularizations, this apparent difficulty has led some authors to seek modifications of the basic amplitudes to eliminate backward propagation.
  Our model shows that the cosine problem is instead a natural consequence of time-reversal invariance of the fundamental dynamics together with the time-neutral boundary states commonly used in transition amplitudes. When a suitable clock system is identified and placed in a semiclassical `good-clock state', it introduces a time arrow selecting the `forward propagating' $\exp(iS/\hbar)$, without modifying the fundamental dynamics.
  The analysis clarifies how time emerges under suitable conditions and emphasizes that, in the canonical formulation, quantum gravity is fundamentally timeless.

</details>


### [71] [Slow-roll inflation in (dual) Kaniadakis cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18070)
*Leila Liravi,Ahmad Sheykhi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies slow-roll inflation in Kaniadakis and dual Kaniadakis cosmology, where entropy is generalized via a deformation parameter $κ$. Modified Friedmann equations lead to $κ$-corrected inflationary predictions for $n_s$, $r$, and the scalar power spectrum. Observational constraints from Planck tightly bound $κ$, yet viable inflationary scenarios exist, suggesting testable links between non-extensive thermodynamics and early-universe physics.
\n\n
本文研究了Kaniadakis和dual Kaniadakis宇宙学框架下的慢滚暴胀，其中熵通过变形参数$κ$被推广。修正的Friedmann方程导致对$n_s$、$r$和标量功率谱的$κ$修正预言。Planck观测数据对$κ$施加了严格限制，但仍存在可行的暴胀场景，表明非广延热力学与早期宇宙物理之间可能存在可观测的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from exploring how generalized statistical mechanics—specifically Kaniadakis entropy, which introduces a deformation parameter $κ$ encoding deviations from standard Boltzmann-Gibbs statistics—affects early-universe cosmology. By embedding this non-extensive thermodynamic framework into inflationary dynamics, the authors aim to uncover whether such modifications yield observationally viable predictions and potentially detectable signatures in primordial perturbations.
\n\n
动机源于探索广义统计力学——特别是引入变形参数$κ$以刻画对标准Boltzmann-Gibbs统计偏离的Kaniadakis熵——如何影响早期宇宙宇宙学。通过将这种非广延热力学框架嵌入暴胀动力学，作者旨在揭示此类修正是否能产生观测上可行的预言，并在原初扰动中留下潜在可探测的印记。

Method: The authors derive modified Friedmann equations using the first law of thermodynamics with Kaniadakis entropy $S_κ ∝ \\arcsinh(κ S_{BG})/κ$, leading to $κ$-dependent corrections in the Hubble flow. They then compute slow-roll parameters, scalar and tensor power spectra, and associated observables ($n_s$, $r$) within both standard and dual Kaniadakis formulations. These predictions are confronted with Planck 2018 data to constrain $κ$.
\n\n
作者利用带有Kaniadakis熵$S_κ ∝ \\arcsinh(κ S_{BG})/κ$的热力学第一定律推导出修正的Friedmann方程，从而在Hubble流中引入依赖于$κ$的修正。随后，他们在标准和dual Kaniadakis两种形式下计算慢滚参数、标量与张量功率谱及相关观测量（$n_s$、$r$），并将这些预言与Planck 2018数据对比以约束$κ$。

Result: For standard Kaniadakis cosmology, viable slow-roll inflation consistent with Planck bounds on $n_s$ and $r$ exists only for highly suppressed $|κ| \\lesssim \\mathcal{O}(10^{-2})$. In dual Kaniadakis cosmology, certain ranges of $κ$ allow the scalar spectral index to remain within observational limits. The predicted scalar power spectrum in both frameworks aligns with Planck measurements when $κ$ is sufficiently small, indicating that $κ$-corrections are constrained but not ruled out.
\n\n
在标准Kaniadakis宇宙学中，只有当$|κ| \\lesssim \\mathcal{O}(10^{-2})$时，慢滚暴胀才能与Planck对$n_s$和$r$的限制相容。在dual Kaniadakis宇宙学中，某些$κ$取值范围可使标量谱指数保持在观测允许范围内。当$κ$足够小时，两种框架预言的标量功率谱均与Planck测量一致，表明$κ$修正虽受强约束但未被排除。

Conclusion: Kaniadakis and dual Kaniadakis cosmologies provide theoretically consistent extensions of standard inflation that incorporate non-extensive thermodynamics. While current data impose tight bounds on the deformation parameter $κ$, they do not exclude it entirely, leaving room for potentially observable imprints in primordial fluctuations. This establishes a phenomenological bridge between generalized statistical mechanics and early-universe cosmology.
\n\n
Kaniadakis和dual Kaniadakis宇宙学为纳入非广延热力学的标准暴胀提供了理论自洽的扩展。尽管当前数据对变形参数$κ$施加了严格限制，但并未完全排除其可能性，仍为原初涨落中潜在可观测的印记留有空间。这建立了广义统计力学与早期宇宙宇宙学之间的现象学桥梁。

Abstract: We investigate slow-roll inflation within the framework of Kaniadakis and dual Kaniadakis cosmology, where the usual entropy formalism is generalized through a deformation parameter $κ$. By deriving the modified Friedmann equations and the corresponding inflationary dynamics induced by Kaniadakis entropy, we analyze the deviations from standard inflation arising from $κ$-corrections. We compute the scalar and tensor spectral indices, the tensor-to-scalar ratio, and examine the observational constraints on the deformation parameter. Our results show that consistency with current observational data imposes stringent bounds on the deformation parameter $κ$. In the standard Kaniadakis formulation, viable slow-roll inflationary scenarios compatible with the Planck constraints on the scalar spectral index $n_s$ and the tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$ can be obtained, although the allowed values of $κ$ are strongly suppressed. For the dual Kaniadakis formulation, we find that the primordial power spectrum of scalar perturbations can remain consistent with observational data within certain parameter regions. We also verify the compatibility of the predicted scalar power spectrum with the latest Planck results and discuss the phenomenological implications of the $κ$-induced corrections. These findings suggest that Kaniadakis cosmology may leave potentially observable imprints on primordial perturbations, providing a possible connection between non-extensive thermodynamics and the physics of the early universe.

### [72] [Effects of formation channels and gravitational lensing on stochastic gravitational wave background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18097)
*Xin-yi Lin,Zhengxiang Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper uses Hierarchical Bayesian Inference (HBI) on GWTC-4 data to constrain primordial black hole (PBH) population parameters, computes separate stochastic gravitational-wave backgrounds (SGWBs) for astrophysical black holes (ABHs) and PBHs including gravitational lensing effects, and shows that both LIGO and the Einstein Telescope (ET) can distinguish between ABH and PBH formation models in certain frequency bands—with ET offering broader discriminatory power across parameter space.
\n\n
本文利用分层贝叶斯推断（Hierarchical Bayesian Inference, HBI）方法对GWTC-4数据进行分析，以约束原初黑洞（Primordial Black Holes, PBHs）的种群超参数；分别计算了天体物理黑洞（Astrophysical Black Holes, ABHs）和PBHs产生的随机引力波背景（Stochastic Gravitational-Wave Backgrounds, SGWBs），并考虑了引力透镜效应对SGWB应变振幅的修正；结果表明，LIGO和爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope, ET）均可在特定频率范围内区分这两种黑洞形成模型，其中ET在更广阔的参数空间中具备更强的区分能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to observationally distinguish between two competing black hole formation scenarios—astrophysical (from stellar collapse) versus primordial (from early-Universe density fluctuations)—by leveraging their distinct imprints on the stochastic gravitational-wave background (SGWB). Since PBHs can form at very high redshifts ($z \\gg 10$), before the first stars, their merger history and resulting SGWB differ significantly from those of ABHs. Current and future gravitational-wave detectors offer a unique probe of these differences, especially when lensing effects—which alter SGWB strain—are properly accounted for.
\n\n
该研究的动机源于需要通过观测手段区分两种竞争性的黑洞形成机制：天体物理起源（由大质量恒星坍缩形成）与原初起源（由早期宇宙密度涨落直接形成）。由于原初黑洞（PBHs）可在极高红移（$z \\gg 10$）时期、即第一代恒星形成之前产生，其并合历史及由此产生的随机引力波背景（SGWB）与天体物理黑洞（ABHs）存在显著差异。当前及未来的引力波探测器为探测这些差异提供了独特途径，尤其是在正确计入引力透镜效应（可改变SGWB应变振幅）的情况下。

Method: The authors apply Hierarchical Bayesian Inference (HBI) to the GWTC-4 catalog to infer hyperparameters characterizing the PBH mass and redshift distribution. They then model the SGWB spectra $\\Omega_{\\text{GW}}(f)$ separately for ABHs and PBHs, integrating over cosmic merger rates and accounting for gravitational lensing, which modifies the observed strain via magnification probability distributions. The resulting SGWB predictions are compared against the power-law integrated (PI) sensitivity curves of LIGO and the Einstein Telescope (ET) to assess model distinguishability in frequency space.
\n\n
作者将分层贝叶斯推断（HBI）应用于GWTC-4目录，以推断刻画原初黑洞（PBH）质量和红移分布的种群超参数。随后，他们分别对天体物理黑洞（ABHs）和原初黑洞（PBHs）建模其随机引力波背景谱 $\\Omega_{\\text{GW}}(f)$，通过对宇宙并合率进行积分，并计入引力透镜效应——后者通过放大率概率分布修正观测到的应变。最终，将所得SGWB预测与LIGO和爱因斯坦望远镜（ET）的幂律积分（Power-Law Integrated, PI）灵敏度曲线进行比较，以评估在频率空间中区分两种模型的能力。

Result: The analysis shows that both LIGO and ET can distinguish between ABH- and PBH-originated SGWBs within specific frequency windows. However, LIGO’s ability is limited to a single discrimination method and is sensitive to the inclusion of lensing, which shifts the effective frequency band for model separation. In contrast, the Einstein Telescope exhibits robust discrimination capability across a wider range of PBH population parameters and frequencies, even when lensing effects are included.
\n\n
分析表明，LIGO和爱因斯坦望远镜（ET）均可在特定频率窗口内区分源自天体物理黑洞（ABHs）与原初黑洞（PBHs）的随机引力波背景（SGWB）。然而，LIGO的区分能力仅限于单一判别方法，且对是否计入透镜效应敏感——透镜效应会改变模型可区分的有效频段。相比之下，即使计入透镜效应，爱因斯坦望远镜在更广泛的PBH种群参数和频率范围内仍展现出稳健的模型区分能力。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates that stochastic gravitational-wave background measurements, particularly with next-generation detectors like the Einstein Telescope, provide a powerful tool to test the origin of black holes. Accounting for gravitational lensing is essential for accurate SGWB modeling, and future observations will significantly constrain or potentially identify a primordial component in the black hole population.
\n\n
本研究表明，随机引力波背景（SGWB）的测量——尤其是借助爱因斯坦望远镜等下一代探测器——是检验黑洞起源的有力工具。准确建模SGWB必须计入引力透镜效应，而未来的观测将能显著限制、甚至可能识别黑洞种群中的原初成分。

Abstract: Two primary formation channels for black holes have been proposed: the astrophysical channel, driven by the collapse of massive stars, and the primordial channel, involving their direct formation from density fluctuations in the early Universe. The key distinction between astrophysical black holes (ABHs) and primordial black holes (PBHs) is that PBHs can form at very high redshifts, before any stars have formed, leading to different stochastic gravitational-wave backgrounds (SGWBs). These SGWBs arise from the superposition of unresolved gravitational-wave signals accumulated over all redshifts. In this work, we employ the Hierarchical Bayesian Inference (HBI) framework and the publicly available GWTC-4 data to infer the population hyperparameters of PBHs. We then compute the SGWBs from ABHs and PBHs separately, accounting for the lensing effect, which can modify the strain amplitude of the SGWBs. By comparing the resulting SGWBs with the power-law integrated (PI) sensitivity curves of ground-based gravitational-wave detectors -- LIGO and the Einstein Telescope (ET) -- we find that both detectors can distinguish between these two black hole formation models within specific frequency ranges. However, LIGO is limited to a single method for distinguishing these models, and the lensing effect alters the frequency range over which discrimination is possible. In contrast, ET is capable of distinguishing ABHs from PBHs across a broader parameter space.
