### [73] [The impact of seasonality over the sensitivity of Einstein Telescope and the SNR of CBC signals at the Sardinia candidate site](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18135)
*Matteo Di Giovanni,Davide Rozza,Giovanni Diaferia,Andrea Contu,Rosario De Rosa,Carlo Giunchi,Luca Naticchioni,Marco Olivieri,Annalisa Allocca,Enrico Calloni,Giovanni Luca Cardello,Luciano Errico,Giovanni Losurdo,Irene Molinari,Lucia Trozzo,Domenico D'Urso*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper analyzes seasonal seismic noise variations at the Sardinia candidate site for the Einstein Telescope (ET), showing that even in worst-case months, Newtonian noise causes only minor (~few percent) degradation in signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) for compact binary coalescences, affirming the site’s suitability for ET’s low-frequency science goals.
\n\n
本文分析了爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope, ET）撒丁岛候选台址的季节性地震噪声变化，结果表明即使在最不利的月份，牛顿噪声（Newtonian noise）对致密双星并合信号的信噪比（SNR）造成的退化也仅有几个百分点，从而确认该台址适合实现ET的低频科学目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The low-frequency sensitivity of third-generation gravitational-wave detectors like the Einstein Telescope is limited by Newtonian noise—gravity gradients induced by ambient seismic fluctuations. Seasonal variations in seismic activity could therefore affect detector performance and the detectability of compact binary coalescences. This work aims to quantify such effects specifically at the Sardinia candidate site using real borehole seismic data.
\n\n
第三代引力波探测器（如爱因斯坦望远镜）的低频灵敏度受限于牛顿噪声——由环境地震涨落引起的引力梯度扰动。因此，地震活动的季节性变化可能影响探测器性能及致密双星并合事件的可探测性。本研究旨在利用真实的深孔地震数据，定量评估撒丁岛候选台址此类效应的具体影响。

Method: The authors analyze seismic data from 2022–2025 collected in deep boreholes at the Sardinia site to characterize monthly noise spectra. They select July (best case) and December (worst case) as representative months. These spectra are used to compute Newtonian noise in the 2–10 Hz band, which is then incorporated into modified ET sensitivity curves. A simulation framework evaluates the resulting impact on SNR for binary neutron star (BNS) and intermediate-mass black hole (IMBH) signals under the triangular ET configuration, without active Newtonian noise cancellation.
\n\n
作者分析了2022–2025年在撒丁岛台址深孔中采集的地震数据，以刻画逐月噪声谱，并选取7月（最佳情况）和12月（最差情况）作为代表性月份。利用这些谱计算2–10 Hz频段内的牛顿噪声，并将其纳入修正后的ET灵敏度曲线。在未采用主动牛顿噪声抑制的情况下，通过模拟框架评估三角形ET构型下双中子星（BNS）和中等质量黑洞（IMBH）信号的信噪比（SNR）变化。

Result: The Sardinia site exhibits low seismic noise overall, leading to only modest seasonal variations in Newtonian noise. The resulting SNR variation for compact binary signals is limited to a few percent between best and worst months. Even in the worst-case scenario (December), the degradation in low-frequency sensitivity remains small, confirming robust performance across seasons.
\n\n
撒丁岛台址整体地震噪声水平较低，导致牛顿噪声的季节性变化微弱。致密双星信号的信噪比在最佳与最差月份之间的变化仅限于几个百分点。即使在最差情况（12月），低频灵敏度的退化仍然很小，表明全年性能稳定。

Conclusion: Seasonal environmental fluctuations at the Sardinia candidate site have negligible impact on the Einstein Telescope’s ability to detect compact binary coalescences in the early inspiral phase. The site’s intrinsically low seismic noise ensures that Newtonian noise remains subdominant, validating Sardinia as a suitable location for achieving ET’s design sensitivity at low frequencies.
\n\n
撒丁岛候选台址的季节性环境波动对爱因斯坦望远镜在旋近早期阶段探测致密双星并合的能力影响可忽略。该台址固有的低地震噪声确保牛顿噪声保持次主导地位，从而验证了撒丁岛作为实现ET低频设计灵敏度的合适选址。

Abstract: This work investigates the impact of seasonal variations in seismic noise on the low-frequency performance of the Einstein Telescope (ET) at the Sardinia candidate site, focusing on implications for compact binary coalescence observations. Using seismic data collected between 2022 and 2025 in deep boreholes, we characterize monthly noise variations and identify representative best and worst case scenarios, corresponding to July and December. The measured seismic spectra are used to estimate the Newtonian noise contribution in the 2-10 Hz band and to derive modified ET sensitivity curves. These are implemented in a simulation framework to evaluate their effect on the signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) of binary neutron star and intermediate mass black hole signals, assuming the triangular ET configuration. We find that the low seismic noise of the Sardinia site results in only minor seasonal variations in detector sensitivity. The corresponding impact on SNR is limited to a few percent, even without including Newtonian noise mitigation. These results indicate that seasonal environmental fluctuation have a minor effect on the early inspired detectability of compact binaries, confirming the suitability of the Sardinia site for achieving ET low-frequency sensitivity goals.

</details>


### [74] [The Case for Astrons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18186)
*Claudio Corianò,Paul H. Frampton,Leonardo Torcellini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates a hypothetical population of primordial, supermassive, electrically charged compact objects ("astrons") with $M_A \sim 10^{12} M_\odot$ and enormous charge $Q_A \sim 4 \times 10^{32}\,\mathrm{C}$, exploring their theoretical viability, physical constraints (e.g., plasma screening, super-extremality), and potential cosmological implications. It concludes that standard homogeneous cosmology cannot accommodate them as dark energy sources, and any viable role requires solving an inhomogeneous Einstein–Maxwell averaging problem.
\n\n
本文研究了一类假设的原初超大质量带电致密天体（“astrons”），其质量 $M_A \sim 10^{12} M_\odot$，电荷 $Q_A \sim 4 \times 10^{32}\,\mathrm{C}$，探讨了其理论可行性、物理限制（如等离子体屏蔽、超极端性）及可能的宇宙学意义。结论指出，标准均匀宇宙学无法将其作为暗能量来源，任何可行的角色都需解决超出均匀近似的非均匀 Einstein–Maxwell 平均问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore whether a sparse population of primordial, highly charged compact objects—distinct from standard black holes or dark matter candidates—could have observable astrophysical signatures (e.g., via Lyman-$α$ absorption or lensing) or play a nontrivial role in cosmology, such as contributing to late-time acceleration, despite their exotic nature and strong theoretical constraints.
\n\n
动机是探索一类稀疏分布的原初高电荷致密天体（不同于标准黑洞或暗物质候选者）是否具有可观测的天体物理信号（例如通过 Lyman-$α$ 吸收或引力透镜），或在宇宙学中扮演非平凡角色（如贡献于晚期加速膨胀），尽管其具有奇异性质和强理论限制。

Method: The authors perform a multi-faceted theoretical analysis: (1) assess charge generation mechanisms and argue the fiducial charge must be primordial; (2) evaluate accretion saturation limits and show ordinary processes cannot yield such high charges; (3) analyze plasma screening and neutralization in ionized media; (4) study spacetime geometry in Reissner–Nordström and Kerr–Newman regimes, noting the super-extremal nature ($Q > M$ in natural units); (5) consider observational probes like Lyman-$α$ forest distortions; and (6) examine cosmological backreaction by comparing the $a^{-4}$ scaling of electromagnetic interaction energy to standard FLRW components.
\n\n
作者进行了多方面的理论分析：(1) 评估电荷产生机制，并论证所设电荷必须是原初的；(2) 考察吸积饱和极限，表明普通过程无法产生如此高电荷；(3) 分析电离介质中的等离子体屏蔽与中和效应；(4) 研究 Reissner–Nordström 和 Kerr–Newman 时空几何，指出其处于超极端状态（自然单位下 $Q > M$）；(5) 考虑 Lyman-$α$ 森林畸变等观测探针；(6) 通过将电磁相互作用能的 $a^{-4}$ 标度与标准 FLRW 组分对比，考察宇宙学反作用。

Result: Key results include: (i) the fiducial astron parameters imply a super-extremal Reissner–Nordström geometry lacking a photon sphere; (ii) plasma screening and neutralization pose severe obstacles to charge persistence; (iii) the electromagnetic energy density of a homogeneous charged population scales as radiation ($\\propto a^{-4}$), precluding late-time cosmic acceleration in standard FLRW cosmology; (iv) formation at $\\sim$months after Big Bang suggests only indirect links to early JWST structures via baryonic assembly around dark seeds.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(i) 所设 astron 参数对应超极端 Reissner–Nordström 几何，无光子球；(ii) 等离子体屏蔽与中和对电荷持久性构成严峻障碍；(iii) 均匀带电群体的电磁能量密度按辐射标度（$\\propto a^{-4}$），在标准 FLRW 宇宙学中无法导致晚期加速；(iv) 在大爆炸后约数月形成，暗示其与 JWST 观测到的早期结构仅通过重子围绕暗种子组装存在间接联系。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that while astrons are theoretically conceivable as primordial relics, their extreme charge introduces insurmountable challenges within standard cosmological frameworks. A viable cosmological role would require going beyond homogeneous FLRW models to solve the inhomogeneous Einstein–Maxwell averaging problem—a formidable theoretical task with no current solution. Thus, astrons are unlikely to explain cosmic acceleration or serve as dominant dark components without new physics.
\n\n
论文结论认为，尽管 astrons 可被视为理论上可能的原初遗迹，但其极端电荷在标准宇宙学框架内带来难以克服的挑战。若要赋予其可行的宇宙学角色，必须超越均匀 FLRW 模型，求解非均匀 Einstein–Maxwell 平均问题——这是一个目前尚无解的艰巨理论任务。因此，除非引入新物理，astrons 不太可能解释宇宙加速膨胀或作为主导的暗成分。

Abstract: We examine a proposed population of primordial, electrically charged compact objects, which we call astrons, with fiducial parameters \(M_A\sim10^{12}M_\odot\), \(Q_A\sim4\times10^{32}\,\mathrm{C}\), and megaparsec-scale separations. We analyze charge generation, ordinary accretion saturation, charge persistence in an ionized medium, plasma screening, the Reissner--Nordström and Kerr--Newman geometric regimes, lensing, and the possible use of Lyman-\(α\) absorption as a probe of astron electric fields, and the cosmological interpretation of a sparse charged population. The large-charge branch is not obtained from ordinary accretion saturation; it should be treated as a primordial or early-universe charge-concentration hypothesis. A horizon-mass estimate places a \(10^{12}M_\odot\) primordial object at times of order months after the Big Bang, so any relation to the early structures observed by the James Webb Space Telescope would be indirect, through later baryonic assembly around dark seeds. The main constraints are severe: plasma screening and neutralization must be avoided, the fiducial charge drives the exterior into a super-extremal regime without a Reissner--Nordström photon sphere, and the homogeneous interaction energy of a charged population scales as \(a^{-4}\). Thus the simplest FLRW perfect-fluid reduction does not generate asymptotic late-time acceleration. Any viable cosmological role for astrons must instead come from a controlled inhomogeneous Einstein--Maxwell averaging problem beyond the homogeneous approximation.

</details>


### [75] [Natural modification of quantum uncertainty, modified gravity, and cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18203)
*Christian G. Boehmer,Eissa Al-Nasrallah*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates that seemingly 'natural' extensions of physical theories—such as adding higher-order terms—are not universally natural across different theoretical frameworks. Using the flat FLRW cosmological equations, it links the generalized uncertainty principle (GUP) to modified gravity theories and finds that only Born-Infeld gravity remains consistently natural in both contexts.
\n\n
本文表明，看似“自然”的物理理论扩展（例如添加高阶项）在不同理论框架中并非普遍自然。通过平坦FLRW宇宙学方程，将广义不确定性原理（GUP）与修改引力理论联系起来，并发现只有Born-Infeld引力在这两种情境下都保持一致性地自然。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the widespread practice in theoretical physics of extending models by including 'natural' higher-order corrections or non-linearities, often without verifying whether such extensions preserve naturalness across dual or related formulations. The authors aim to expose hidden inconsistencies by examining the interplay between quantum-gravitational corrections (via GUP) and classical modifications of gravity within cosmology.
\n\n
动机源于理论物理中普遍采用的做法：通过引入“自然”的高阶修正或非线性项来扩展模型，却往往未验证此类扩展在对偶或相关表述中是否仍保持自然性。作者旨在通过考察量子引力修正（通过GUP）与宇宙学中经典引力修改之间的相互作用，揭示其中隐藏的不一致性。

Method: The authors employ the flat Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) metric to derive cosmological evolution equations under two perspectives: (1) incorporating corrections from the generalized uncertainty principle (GUP), which introduces a minimal length scale and modifies the energy density–Hubble parameter relation; and (2) considering generic modified gravity theories, expressed via an effective gravitational action $S = \\int d^4x \\sqrt{-g} f(R, R_{\\mu\\nu}R^{\\mu\\nu}, \\dots)$. They map the GUP-modified Friedmann equation onto the modified gravity framework and analyze which $f$-theories reproduce the same dynamics without introducing pathological higher-derivative terms or fine-tuning.
\n\n
作者采用平坦Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker（FLRW）度规，从两个角度推导宇宙演化方程：(1) 引入广义不确定性原理（GUP）的修正，该修正引入最小长度尺度并修改能量密度与Hubble参数的关系；(2) 考虑一般的修改引力理论，其作用量表示为 $S = \\int d^4x \\sqrt{-g} f(R, R_{\\mu\\nu}R^{\\mu\\nu}, \\dots)$。他们将GUP修正后的Friedmann方程映射到修改引力框架中，并分析哪些 $f$-理论能在不引入病态高阶导数项或精细调节的情况下重现相同动力学。

Result: A simple quadratic correction in the GUP-modified Friedmann equation—arising from a minimal length—translates into highly non-linear and complicated field equations in generic modified gravity theories. However, the Born-Infeld-type gravity models, characterized by an action of the form $\\mathcal{L}_{\\text{BI}} \\propto \\sqrt{\\det(g_{\\mu\\nu} + \\lambda R_{\\mu\\nu})}$, uniquely yield a consistent and structurally simple correspondence with the GUP framework. All other common modifications (e.g., $f(R)$, Gauss-Bonnet, etc.) fail to maintain naturalness in both descriptions simultaneously.
\n\n
GUP修正的Friedmann方程中的一个简单二次修正项（源于最小长度）在一般修改引力理论中会转化为高度非线性且复杂的场方程。然而，Born-Infeld型引力模型——其拉格朗日量形式为 $\\mathcal{L}_{\\text{BI}} \\propto \\sqrt{\\det(g_{\\mu\\nu} + \\lambda R_{\\mu\\nu})}$——是唯一能与GUP框架建立一致且结构简洁对应关系的理论。所有其他常见修改（如 $f(R)$、Gauss-Bonnet等）均无法同时在两种描述中保持自然性。

Conclusion: The notion of 'naturalness' in theoretical extensions is context-dependent and not invariant under theoretical dualities or reformulations. The identification of Born-Infeld gravity as the unique model preserving naturalness across both quantum-motivated (GUP) and classical geometric (modified gravity) frameworks suggests it may play a privileged role in quantum gravity phenomenology and early-universe cosmology.
\n\n
理论扩展中的“自然性”概念依赖于具体语境，并不在理论对偶性或重新表述下保持不变。Born-Infeld引力被识别为唯一能在量子启发（GUP）与经典几何（修改引力）框架中同时保持自然性的模型，这表明它可能在量子引力唯象学和早期宇宙学中扮演特殊角色。

Abstract: A common approach in physics and mathematics is to extend and modify theories and frameworks by considering what is often described as a `natural' extension or modification by including higher-order terms or by introducing other non-linearities. We show that such an approach must be taken with care as physical models can be connected in indirect ways. What looks like a natural approach in one setting will likely not be natural in another. We use the flat Friedmann-Lemaitre-Robertson-Walker equations of cosmology to connect the generalized uncertainty principle to modified theories of gravity. A simple additional term in one setting leads to enormous complications in the other. We identify Born-Infeld models as the only ones which appear natural in both settings.

</details>


### [76] [Kerr-like black holes shadow surrounded by dark matter halos: Comparison between various dark matter profiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18205)
*Malihe Heydari-Fard,Mohaddese Heydari-Fard*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates the shadows of rotating black holes embedded in King, Hernquist, and Moore dark matter halo profiles. Using the Newman-Janis algorithm to generate rotating solutions from static ones, the authors analyze how dark matter parameters affect horizons, ergoregions, and shadow radii. They find that while the shadow radius slightly increases relative to Kerr black holes, the overall size and shape changes are negligible across all considered halo types—cuspy or cored—suggesting black hole shadows cannot reliably distinguish between different dark matter distributions.
\n\n
本文研究了嵌入King、Hernquist和Moore暗物质晕轮廓中的旋转黑洞的阴影。作者利用Newman-Janis算法从静态解生成旋转解，分析暗物质特征密度、特征半径和自旋参数对视界、能层和阴影半径的影响。研究发现，尽管相对于无暗物质的Kerr黑洞，阴影半径略有增大，但在所有考虑的晕轮廓（无论是cusp型还是cored型）中，阴影的大小和形状变化均可忽略，表明黑洞阴影无法有效区分星系中心不同类型的暗物质分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the growing interest in using black hole shadows—observable via very-long-baseline interferometry (e.g., EHT)—as probes of spacetime geometry near supermassive black holes, particularly in environments where dark matter may significantly alter gravitational fields. The authors aim to assess whether different dark matter halo profiles (King, Hernquist, Moore) imprint detectable signatures on black hole shadows, which could in principle reveal the nature of dark matter distribution in galactic nuclei.
\n\n
动机源于近年来利用黑洞阴影（可通过甚长基线干涉测量技术如EHT观测）作为探测超大质量黑洞附近时空几何的工具的兴趣日益增长，尤其是在暗物质可能显著改变引力场的环境中。作者旨在评估不同的暗物质晕轮廓（King、Hernquist、Moore）是否会在黑洞阴影上留下可观测的印记，从而原则上揭示星系核中暗物质分布的性质。

Method: The authors start with known static black hole solutions immersed in three spherically symmetric dark matter halo profiles: King, Hernquist, and Moore. They apply the Newman-Janis algorithm—a complex coordinate transformation technique—to generate corresponding rotating (Kerr-like) black hole metrics. They then compute key geometric features: inner and outer event horizons, ergoregion boundaries, and photon sphere properties to determine the shadow radius as observed by a distant observer. The dependence of these quantities on the dark matter characteristic density $\\rho_0$, characteristic radius $r_0$, and black hole spin $a$ is systematically analyzed and compared against the vacuum Kerr solution.
\n\n
作者从已知的嵌入三种球对称暗物质晕轮廓（King、Hernquist和Moore）中的静态黑洞解出发，应用Newman-Janis算法（一种复坐标变换技术）生成相应的旋转（Kerr-like）黑洞度规。随后计算关键几何特征：内/外事件视界、能层边界以及光子球性质，以确定遥远观测者所见的阴影半径。系统分析了这些量对暗物质特征密度$\\rho_0$、特征半径$r_0$和黑洞自旋参数$a$的依赖性，并与真空Kerr解进行比较。

Result: The presence of dark matter increases the shadow radius slightly compared to the Kerr black hole without dark matter. However, this effect is extremely small for all three halo models (King, Hernquist, Moore), regardless of whether the profile is cuspy (e.g., Moore) or cored (e.g., King). The modifications to the horizon structure and ergoregion are similarly minimal. Crucially, the shape of the shadow remains nearly identical to that of Kerr, with deviations too small to be observationally distinguishable with current or near-future instruments.
\n\n
暗物质的存在会使阴影半径相比无暗物质的Kerr黑洞略有增大。然而，对于所有三种晕模型（King、Hernquist、Moore），无论其轮廓是cuspy型（如Moore）还是cored型（如King），这种效应都极其微弱。视界结构和能层的修正同样微小。关键的是，阴影形状几乎与Kerr黑洞一致，偏差小到当前或近期仪器无法观测区分。

Conclusion: For Kerr-like black holes embedded in standard astrophysical dark matter halos (including both cuspy and cored profiles), the black hole shadow is robust against variations in the dark matter distribution. Consequently, shadow observations alone cannot serve as a diagnostic tool to infer the specific form of the dark matter density profile in galactic centers. Alternative observational strategies or complementary probes (e.g., stellar dynamics, gravitational lensing) remain necessary to constrain dark matter properties near black holes.
\n\n
对于嵌入标准天体物理暗物质晕（包括cuspy型和cored型轮廓）中的Kerr-like黑洞，其阴影对暗物质分布的变化具有鲁棒性。因此，仅靠阴影观测无法作为诊断工具来推断星系中心暗物质密度轮廓的具体形式。要约束黑洞附近暗物质的性质，仍需依赖其他观测策略或互补探针（如恒星动力学、引力透镜）。

Abstract: The study of shadows of static and rotating black holes immersed in various dark matter halo profiles has gained significant attention in recent years. In this paper, we consider the static black hole solution immersed in three dark matter halo profiles (King, Hernquist, and Moore) and, by using the Newman-Janis algorithm, obtain the corresponding rotating black hole solutions. The main goal of the paper is to study the influence of the characteristic density, characteristic radius, and the spin parameter on the inner and outer horizons, the ergoregion, and the shadow radius, and to compare the results with Kerr black holes and other dark matter profiles. Our findings indicate that the shadow radius of rotating black holes immersed in dark matter increases compared to that of the Kerr black hole in the absence of dark matter; however, the impact on the size and shape of the shadow is negligible for King, Hernquist, and Moore profiles, and for all other dark matter halo profiles considered, and is independent of whether the halo is cuspy or cored. Therefore, at least for these Kerr-like black holes, the black hole shadow is not a suitable tool for distinguishing the nature of the dark matter distribution in galactic centers.

</details>


### [77] [Short-Range Tests of the Gravitational Inverse-Square Law](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18212)
*Jiro Murata,Takuhiro Fujiie,Sae Suzuki*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper reviews and updates experimental constraints on deviations from the gravitational inverse-square law at short distances over the past decade, using a unified formalism to enable direct comparison with theoretical extensions of general relativity. It compares different model parametrizations—such as extra-dimensional scenarios—and contrasts results from tabletop experiments with those from high-energy colliders for both Yukawa and power-law potential modifications.
\n\n
本文回顾并更新了过去十年中在短距离上对引力平方反比定律偏离的实验限制，采用统一的形式体系，以便与广义相对论的理论扩展进行直接比较。文章比较了不同的模型参数化方法（如额外维度模型），并将桌面实验结果与高能对撞机实验结果在Yukawa势和幂律势修正情形下进行了对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to test general relativity at short ranges where quantum gravity or extra-dimensional effects might manifest as deviations from the inverse-square law. A consistent framework is required to compare diverse experimental results (from tabletop to collider scales) with various beyond-GR models, enabling meaningful constraints on new physics.
\n\n
动机源于在短程尺度上检验广义相对论的需求，因为在这些尺度上量子引力或额外维度效应可能表现为对平方反比定律的偏离。需要一个一致的框架来将多样化的实验结果（从桌面实验到对撞机尺度）与各种超越广义相对论（beyond-GR）的模型进行比较，从而对新物理施加有意义的限制。

Method: The authors employ a consistent theoretical formalism to reinterpret and compile experimental bounds across length scales. They analyze deviations parameterized as Yukawa-type potentials ($V(r) \\propto e^{-r/\\lambda}/r$) and power-law corrections ($V(r) \\propto 1/r^{2+\\alpha}$), comparing constraints derived from precision short-range gravity experiments (e.g., torsion balances, Casimir force measurements) with those inferred from high-energy collider data under assumptions of extra dimensions or other effective field theory frameworks.
\n\n
作者采用一致的理论形式体系重新解释并汇编了跨越不同长度尺度的实验限制。他们分析了以Yukawa型势（$V(r) \\propto e^{-r/\\lambda}/r$）和幂律修正（$V(r) \\propto 1/r^{2+\\alpha}$）参数化的偏离，并将精密短程引力实验（如扭秤、Casimir力测量）得出的约束与基于额外维度或其他有效场论（EFT）框架假设下从高能对撞机数据推断的约束进行比较。

Result: Updated exclusion limits are provided for the strength and range of Yukawa and power-law deviations from Newtonian gravity. The analysis shows that tabletop experiments dominate constraints at sub-millimeter scales, while collider experiments provide complementary bounds at much shorter distance scales (≲10⁻¹⁹ m). Consistency across parametrizations reveals which theoretical models (e.g., large extra dimensions) are most tightly constrained.
\n\n
文章给出了Yukawa势和幂律偏离牛顿引力的强度与作用范围的最新排除界限。分析表明，桌面实验在亚毫米尺度上占据主导约束地位，而对撞机实验则在更短的距离尺度（≲10⁻¹⁹ m）上提供互补限制。不同参数化方案之间的一致性揭示了哪些理论模型（如大额外维度）受到最严格的限制。

Conclusion: A unified analysis framework enables robust cross-experiment and cross-model comparisons, strengthening the empirical foundation for testing gravity beyond general relativity. Future improvements in both low-energy precision experiments and high-energy probes will further narrow the window for new gravitational physics at short distances.
\n\n
统一的分析框架使得跨实验和跨模型的比较更加可靠，从而加强了检验广义相对论之外引力理论的经验基础。未来低能精密实验和高能探针的改进将进一步缩小短距离上新引力物理的可能性窗口。

Abstract: Experimental constraints on the gravitational inverse-square law at short range are presented, employing a consistent formalism across a wide range of length scales. We provide comprehensive updates from the past decade, building upon our previous review. This work facilitates the direct comparison of experimental results with theoretical models that extend general relativity. Furthermore, a comparison between various model parametrizations, including extra-dimensional models, is introduced. Finally, results from tabletop experiments are compared with those from high-energy collider experiments for both Yukawa and power-law potentials.

</details>


### [78] [Quasinormal modes of a rotating loop quantum black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18249)
*Zhongzhinan Dong,Shulan Li,Dan Zhang,Jian-Pin Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We compute quasinormal modes of a massless scalar field on an effective rotating loop quantum black hole spacetime using the continued fraction method. Quantum corrections universally lower both real and imaginary parts of fundamental mode frequencies, while rotation introduces nontrivial modulations—crossover behavior in spherically symmetric perturbations and enhanced oscillation with reduced damping when azimuthal dependence is included. Overtone modes retain characteristic loop quantum gravity signatures like outbursts and non-monotonicity, shifted by rotation to weaker quantum regimes; orbital angular momentum suppresses outbursts, whereas azimuthal coupling induces spectral inversions among higher overtones.
\n\n
我们使用连分式方法计算了有效旋转圈量子黑洞时空上无质量标量场的准正规模。量子修正普遍降低基模频率的实部和虚部，而旋转引入了非平凡调制——球对称扰动中出现交叉行为，当包含方位角依赖时则增强振荡并减弱阻尼。高阶泛音模式保留了圈量子引力的典型特征（如爆发和非单调演化），旋转将这些现象移至更弱的量子修正区域；轨道角动量抑制爆发，而方位自由度则在更高阶泛音间引发谱反转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to probe observable imprints of Loop Quantum Gravity (LQG) in black hole dynamics through quasinormal mode (QNM) spectroscopy. While non-rotating LQG-inspired black holes exhibit distinctive quantum signatures (e.g., overtone outbursts), it remains unclear how these features persist or transform under rotation—a crucial astrophysical ingredient. The motivation is to construct a physically plausible rotating LQG black hole model via the improved Newman-Janis algorithm and systematically study how quantum corrections, spin, and angular structure of perturbations jointly shape the QNM spectrum, thereby providing testable predictions for gravitational-wave astronomy.
\n\n
本文旨在通过准正规模（QNM）谱学探测圈量子引力（Loop Quantum Gravity, LQG）在黑洞动力学中的可观测印记。尽管非旋转的LQG启发黑洞展现出独特的量子特征（如泛音爆发），但尚不清楚这些特征在旋转（一个关键的天体物理要素）下如何保持或转变。其动机是通过改进的Newman-Janis算法构建一个物理上合理的旋转LQG黑洞模型，并系统研究量子修正、自旋以及扰动的角结构如何共同塑造QNM谱，从而为引力波天文学提供可检验的预言。

Method: The authors employ an effective rotating black hole metric derived from a covariant spherical LQG model using the improved Newman-Janis algorithm. They consider linear perturbations of a massless scalar field $\\Phi$ governed by the Klein-Gordon equation $\\Box \\Phi = 0$ on this background. After separating variables via $\\Phi(t,r,\\theta,\\phi) = e^{-i\\omega t} R(r) Y_{\\ell m}(\\theta,\\phi)$, they obtain a radial master equation with an effective potential dependent on the quantum correction parameter $\\delta$, black hole spin $a$, and angular numbers $(\\ell, m)$. The quasinormal frequencies $\\omega = \\omega_R + i \\omega_I$ are computed using the continued fraction method (Leaver’s algorithm), which enforces outgoing-wave boundary conditions at the horizon and infinity. Systematic scans over $\\delta$, $a$, $\\ell$, and $m$ reveal dependencies of both fundamental ($n=0$) and overtone ($n \\geq 1$) modes.
\n\n
作者采用一种有效旋转黑洞度规，该度规源自协变球对称LQG模型并通过改进的Newman-Janis算法构造。他们考虑无质量标量场$\\Phi$在此背景上的线性微扰，由Klein-Gordon方程$\\Box \\Phi = 0$描述。通过变量分离$\\Phi(t,r,\\theta,\\phi) = e^{-i\\omega t} R(r) Y_{\\ell m}(\\theta,\\phi)$，得到一个径向主方程，其有效势依赖于量子修正参数$\\delta$、黑洞自旋$a$以及角量子数$(\\ell, m)$。准正规模频率$\\omega = \\omega_R + i \\omega_I$通过连分式方法（Leaver算法）计算，该方法在视界和无穷远处施加出射波边界条件。通过对$\\delta$、$a$、$\\ell$和$m$进行系统扫描，揭示了基模（$n=0$）和泛音模（$n \\geq 1$）的依赖关系。

Result: Key results include: (1) For all fundamental modes, increasing the quantum correction $\\delta$ monotonically decreases both $\\omega_R$ (oscillation frequency) and $|\\omega_I|$ (damping rate), implying slower, longer-lived ringdown. (2) Rotation induces a crossover in $\\omega_R$ vs. $a$ for $\\ell = m = 0$, absent for $\\ell > 0$; nonzero $m$ enhances $\\omega_R$ and further suppresses damping. (3) Overtone modes exhibit “overtone outbursts” (sudden spikes in $|\\omega_I|$) and non-monotonic $\\omega(\\delta)$ evolution—hallmarks of LQG—even in the rotating case, though shifted to smaller $\\delta$. (4) Nonzero $\\ell$ suppresses outbursts, while $m \\neq 0$ boosts $\\omega_R$, leading to spectral inversions where higher overtones cross in frequency. These findings demonstrate that rotation preserves core LQG spectral features while enriching them with angular structure.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(1) 对所有基模，增大量子修正参数$\\delta$单调降低$\\omega_R$（振荡频率）和$|\\omega_I|$（阻尼率），意味着更慢、更持久的铃宕（ringdown）。(2) 对于$\\ell = m = 0$，旋转在$\\omega_R$随$a$的变化中诱导出交叉行为，而$\\ell > 0$时该行为消失；非零$m$增强$\\omega_R$并进一步抑制阻尼。(3) 泛音模即使在旋转情形下仍表现出“泛音爆发”（$|\\omega_I|$的突然尖峰）和$\\omega(\\delta)$的非单调演化——这是LQG的标志性特征，尽管被旋转移至更小的$\\delta$区域。(4) 非零$\\ell$抑制爆发，而$m \\neq 0$提升$\\omega_R$，导致谱反转，即更高阶泛音在频率上发生交叉。这些发现表明，旋转在保留LQG核心谱特征的同时，通过角结构使其更加丰富。

Conclusion: The effective rotating loop quantum black hole retains robust quantum gravitational signatures in its quasinormal spectrum, confirming the physical relevance of the improved Newman-Janis construction. The interplay between quantum corrections, rotation, and angular momentum generates a rich phenomenology—including frequency crossovers, overtone outbursts, and spectral inversions—that distinguishes LQG predictions from classical or other quantum gravity models. These features provide concrete theoretical templates for black hole spectroscopy with next-generation gravitational-wave detectors, offering a pathway to empirically test quantum geometry effects in strong-field gravity.
\n\n
有效的旋转圈量子黑洞在其准正规模谱中保留了稳健的量子引力印记，证实了改进的Newman-Janis构造的物理相关性。量子修正、旋转与角动量之间的相互作用产生了丰富的现象学特征——包括频率交叉、泛音爆发和谱反转——这些特征将LQG预言与经典或其他量子引力模型区分开来。这些特征为下一代引力波探测器开展黑洞谱学研究提供了具体的理论模板，为在强场引力中经验性检验量子几何效应开辟了路径。

Abstract: We investigate the quasinormal modes of a massless scalar field on an effective rotating loop quantum black hole background, constructed from a covariant spherical model via an improved Newman-Janis algorithm. Using the continued fraction method, we compute the spectrum for both fundamental and overtone modes, and systematically analyze how the frequencies depend on the quantum correction, spin, and angular structure of the perturbation. For all fundamental modes, increasing the quantum gravity correction monotonically reduces both the oscillation frequency and the damping rate, signaling slower oscillations and prolonged decay. Rotation imprints a nontrivial modulation: for a spherically symmetric perturbation, the real frequency displays a crossover as the spin grows, whereas this feature is suppressed once angular momentum is turned on; further activating the azimuthal component enhances the frequency and reduces the damping even more strongly. In the overtone sector, the rotating solution retains the hallmark quantum gravitational signatures of the spherical case - overtone outbursts and non-monotonic evolution - with rotation shifting these phenomena to weaker quantum corrections. Nonzero orbital angular momentum suppresses the outbursts, while the azimuthal degree of freedom boosts the frequency, giving rise to novel spectral inversions among higher overtones. Our results confirm that the effective rotating metric captures essential loop quantum gravity features, providing clear theoretical benchmarks for black hole spectroscopy and future gravitational-wave observations.

</details>


### [79] [Dyonic Black Holes in Lorentz-Violating Gravity with a Background Kalb--Ramond Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18371)
*Yu-Xuan Lin,Jia-Zhou Liu,Yu-Xiao Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper constructs an exact four-dimensional static, spherically symmetric dyonic black hole solution in Lorentz-violating gravity by introducing a nonminimal coupling between the Kalb–Ramond field and the electromagnetic field. It analyzes geodesic motion to compute observable features like the photon sphere and shadow radius, and studies thermodynamics in the extended phase space, revealing a first-order phase transition sensitive to Lorentz violation and dyonic charges.
\n\n
本文通过引入Kalb–Ramond场与电磁场之间的非最小耦合，在洛伦兹破缺引力中构造了一个精确的四维静态球对称dyonic黑洞解。文章分析了测地线运动以计算光子球和阴影半径等可观测量，并在扩展相空间中研究了热力学性质，揭示了一阶相变，其结构强烈依赖于洛伦兹破缺参数和dyonic电荷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore how Lorentz symmetry violation—induced by a background Kalb–Ramond field—affects black hole solutions, particularly dyonic ones carrying both electric and magnetic charges. The authors aim to understand modifications to spacetime geometry, particle dynamics, and thermodynamic behavior due to this Lorentz-violating framework.
\n\n
动机在于探索由背景Kalb–Ramond场引起的洛伦兹对称性破缺如何影响黑洞解，特别是同时携带电荷和磁荷的dyonic黑洞。作者旨在理解在此洛伦兹破缺框架下时空几何、粒子动力学和热力学行为的修正。

Method: The authors introduce a nonminimal coupling term between the Kalb–Ramond field $H_{\mu\nu\rho}$ and the electromagnetic field strength $F_{\mu\nu}$ in the action of a Lorentz-violating gravitational theory. They solve the field equations to obtain an exact static, spherically symmetric dyonic black hole metric. Geodesic equations for null and timelike particles are analyzed to determine the photon-sphere radius, black hole shadow, and innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO). In the extended phase space (where the cosmological constant is treated as pressure), they compute thermodynamic quantities such as temperature, entropy, and volume, and verify the first law and Smarr relation. Phase transitions are studied via Gibbs free energy.
\n\n
作者在洛伦兹破缺引力理论的作用量中引入Kalb–Ramond场$H_{\mu\nu\rho}$与电磁场强度$F_{\mu\nu}$之间的非最小耦合项，求解场方程得到一个精确的静态球对称dyonic黑洞度规。通过分析零测地线和类时测地线，确定光子球半径、黑洞阴影和最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）。在扩展相空间（将宇宙学常数视为压强）中，计算温度、熵和体积等热力学量，并验证热力学第一定律和Smarr关系。通过Gibbs自由能研究相变行为。

Result: The solution exhibits a genuine curvature singularity at $r=0$, confirmed by curvature invariants. Both the Lorentz-violating parameter and dyonic charges significantly alter the photon-sphere radius, shadow size, and ISCO location. Thermodynamically, the black hole satisfies the first law and Smarr formula in the extended phase space. A first-order small–large black hole phase transition occurs, with critical behavior modulated by the Lorentz-violating parameter and dyonic charges.
\n\n
该解在$r=0$处存在真实的曲率奇点，由曲率不变量证实。洛伦兹破缺参数和dyonic电荷显著改变了光子球半径、阴影大小和ISCO位置。在热力学方面，该黑洞在扩展相空间中满足热力学第一定律和Smarr公式。系统展现出小黑洞与大黑洞之间的一阶相变，其临界行为受洛伦兹破缺参数和dyonic电荷调控。

Conclusion: The interplay between Lorentz violation (via a background Kalb–Ramond field) and dyonic charge enriches black hole physics, leading to observable deviations in shadow and orbital dynamics, as well as novel thermodynamic phase structure. This demonstrates that Lorentz-violating extensions of general relativity can yield physically distinct black hole solutions with testable phenomenological signatures.
\n\n
洛伦兹破缺（通过背景Kalb–Ramond场）与dyonic电荷的相互作用丰富了黑洞物理，导致阴影和轨道动力学的可观测偏差，以及新颖的热力学相结构。这表明广义相对论的洛伦兹破缺推广可产生具有可观测现象学特征的物理上不同的黑洞解。

Abstract: By introducing a nonminimal coupling between the Kalb--Ramond field and the electromagnetic field, we construct an exact four-dimensional static, spherically symmetric dyonic black hole solution in Lorentz-violating gravity with a background Kalb--Ramond field. The curvature invariants show that the spacetime retains a genuine curvature singularity at $r=0$. We then analyze the geodesic motion of null and timelike particles and obtain the photon-sphere radius, the shadow radius, and the innermost stable circular orbit, demonstrating that both the Lorentz-violating parameter and the dyonic charges can appreciably modify the shadow size and the domain of stable circular motion. In the extended phase space, we derive the thermodynamic quantities and verify the first law of black hole thermodynamics together with the Smarr relation. The system also exhibits a first-order phase transition between small and large black holes, and its phase structure is strongly influenced by the Lorentz-violating parameter and the dyonic charges.

</details>


### [80] [Traversable Wormholes with Non-Exotic Matter: The Role of Higher Curvature Corrections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18376)
*M Daniel Ranjan,Soumya Chakrabarti,Sanjit Das*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates traversable wormhole solutions in a higher-derivative gravity theory described by an $f(R,\\Box R)$ action. It shows that curvature corrections involving the d'Alembertian of the Ricci scalar can reduce or even eliminate the need for exotic matter typically required to satisfy wormhole geometry constraints.
\n\n
本文研究了由 $f(R,\\Box R)$ 作用量描述的高阶导数引力理论中的可穿越虫洞解。研究表明，包含 Ricci 标量的 d'Alembertian 的曲率修正项可以减少甚至完全消除通常为满足虫洞几何约束所需的奇异物质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the desire to understand whether quantum-motivated modifications to general relativity—specifically $f(R,\\Box R)$ gravity, which includes higher-derivative terms like $\\Box R$—can support traversable wormholes without requiring large amounts of exotic matter that violates classical energy conditions.
\n\n
动机源于理解量子启发的广义相对论修正——特别是包含高阶导数项（如 $\\Box R$）的 $f(R,\\Box R)$ 引力理论——是否能在不依赖大量违反经典能量条件的奇异物质的情况下支持可穿越虫洞。

Method: The authors derive the modified gravitational field equations from an $f(R,\\Box R)$ action for a static, spherically symmetric spacetime ansatz suitable for wormhole geometries. They analyze these equations both analytically and numerically, focusing on the effective stress-energy tensor induced by higher-curvature terms and its implications for the null, weak, and strong energy conditions at the wormhole throat.
\n\n
作者从适用于虫洞几何的静态球对称时空假设出发，推导出 $f(R,\\Box R)$ 作用量下的修正引力场方程，并通过解析和数值方法分析这些方程，重点关注由高阶曲率项诱导的有效应力-能量张量及其对虫洞喉部处零能量条件、弱能量条件和强能量条件的影响。

Result: The study finds that the higher-derivative contributions from the $\\Box R$ term act as an effective geometric source in the field equations, mimicking exotic matter. This allows for wormhole solutions that either significantly reduce or completely avoid the violation of classical energy conditions, thereby lessening or eliminating the need for external exotic matter.
\n\n
研究发现，来自 $\\Box R$ 项的高阶导数贡献在场方程中表现为一种有效的几何源，模拟奇异物质的作用。这使得虫洞解能够显著减少甚至完全避免违反经典能量条件，从而减轻或消除对外部奇异物质的需求。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that $f(R,\\Box R)$ gravity provides a viable theoretical framework in which traversable wormholes can exist with minimal or no exotic matter, suggesting that quantum-inspired higher-derivative gravity may resolve long-standing issues in wormhole physics related to energy condition violations.
\n\n
本文得出结论：$f(R,\\Box R)$ 引力提供了一个可行的理论框架，在此框架下可穿越虫洞可以在极少甚至无需奇异物质的情况下存在，表明受量子启发的高阶导数引力理论可能解决虫洞物理中与能量条件破坏相关的长期难题。

Abstract: In this paper, we explore wormhole solutions in a higher-derivative theory of gravity where the action depends not only on the Ricci scalar \(R\), but also on its d'Alembertian, \(\Box R\). Such \(f(R,\Box R)\) models are motivated by quantum corrections to general relativity and naturally extend the space of possible gravitational geometries. Our goal is to examine whether traversable wormholes can exist in this framework and to understand the role of higher-order curvature terms in supporting them. We derive the field equations for a static, spherically symmetric wormhole and study their solutions using both analytical arguments and numerical methods. Particular attention is given to the classical energy conditions, which are usually violated in wormhole physics. We find that the higher-derivative corrections can effectively contribute to the stress-energy tensor, reducing the amount of exotic matter required at the throat, and in some cases eliminating the need for it altogether.

### [81] [Probing (sub-)solar-mass black holes and superspinars with current and next-generation gravitational-wave observatories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18428)
*K. S. Sruthy,N. V. Krishnendu,Chandrachur Chakraborty,Nami Uchikata*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper explores the detectability of (sub-)solar-mass black hole and superspinar binaries using current and future gravitational-wave detectors. It finds that third-generation observatories like Einstein Telescope and Cosmic Explorer can significantly improve detection sensitivity and parameter estimation—especially spin measurements—with precision $Δχ_{1z} \sim 10^{-4}–10^{-3}$, enabling discrimination between near-extremal black holes and superspinars.
\n\n
本文探讨了利用当前和未来引力波探测器对（亚）太阳质量黑洞和超旋星双星系统的可探测性。研究发现，爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）和宇宙探索者（Cosmic Explorer）等第三代观测站可显著提升探测灵敏度和参数估计精度——尤其是自旋测量精度可达 $Δχ_{1z} \sim 10^{-4}–10^{-3}$，从而能够区分近极端黑洞与超旋星（superspinars）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the theoretical possibility that (sub-)solar-mass compact objects—such as primordial black holes or exotic superspinars—could exist and provide unique probes of early-universe physics and strong-field gravity beyond general relativity. Detecting such systems would test fundamental aspects of black hole formation, cosmic history, and potential deviations from Kerr geometry in extreme regimes.
\n\n
动机源于（亚）太阳质量致密天体（如原初黑洞或奇异的超旋星）在理论上可能存在的可能性，它们可作为早期宇宙物理和广义相对论之外强场引力的独特探针。探测此类系统将检验黑洞形成、宇宙历史以及极端条件下偏离Kerr几何的基本物理。

Method: The authors model gravitational-wave signals from inspiraling binaries using the frequency-domain post-Newtonian waveform TaylorF2, truncated at the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) to exclude merger and ringdown contributions. They evaluate detectability by computing signal-to-noise ratios (SNRs) using the noise power spectral densities of Advanced LIGO, Einstein Telescope, and Cosmic Explorer. Fisher matrix analysis is employed to estimate measurement uncertainties, particularly for the primary component’s dimensionless spin parameter $χ_{1z}$.
\n\n
作者使用频域后牛顿（post-Newtonian）波形模型 TaylorF2 对旋近双星的引力波信号进行建模，并在最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）处截断信号以排除并合与铃宕阶段的影响。他们通过计算信噪比（SNR），结合 Advanced LIGO、爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）和宇宙探索者（Cosmic Explorer）的噪声功率谱密度来评估可探测性，并采用 Fisher 矩阵分析估算参数测量误差，特别是主成分无量纲自旋参数 $χ_{1z}$ 的不确定性。

Result: Third-generation detectors dramatically outperform current ones: they achieve SNRs of $\sim 100–350$ for binaries in the mass range $0.1~M_\odot–2~M_\odot$, thanks to enhanced low-frequency sensitivity and longer observable inspiral. This enables spin measurements with precision $Δχ_{1z} \sim 10^{-4}–10^{-3}$, sufficient to distinguish near-extremal Kerr black holes ($χ \lesssim 1$) from superspinars ($χ > 1$).
\n\n
第三代探测器性能远超当前设备：得益于增强的低频灵敏度和更长的可观测旋近阶段，对于质量范围为 $0.1~M_\odot–2~M_\odot$ 的双星系统，其信噪比可达 $\sim 100–350$。这使得自旋测量精度达到 $Δχ_{1z} \sim 10^{-4}–10^{-3}$，足以区分近极端Kerr黑洞（$χ \lesssim 1$）与超旋星（$χ > 1$）。

Conclusion: Future third-generation gravitational-wave observatories will open a new window into the population of low-mass compact objects and enable stringent tests of strong-field gravity. The high-precision spin measurements they facilitate could confirm or rule out exotic compact objects like superspinars, thereby probing physics beyond classical black hole paradigms.
\n\n
未来的第三代引力波观测站将为低质量致密天体族群研究开辟新窗口，并实现对强场引力的严格检验。其所实现的高精度自旋测量有望证实或排除超旋星等奇异致密天体，从而探索超越经典黑洞范式的物理。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave observations provide a powerful probe of compact objects and strong-field gravity. In this work, we investigate the detectability of binaries containing (sub-)solar-mass black holes and superspinars with current and next-generation gravitational-wave observatories. Such objects may arise from primordial formation channels or from more exotic high-energy scenarios, and their detection would provide important insights into the population of low-mass compact objects and the physics of extreme gravitational fields. We model the gravitational-wave signals using the frequency-domain post-Newtonian inspiral waveform model TaylorF2, and truncate the signal at the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) to avoid contamination from the post-inspiral regime. We assess the observability of these systems using the sensitivities of current detectors such as Advanced LIGO and upcoming third-generation observatories including the Einstein Telescope and Cosmic Explorer. Our results show that while current detectors have limited reach for very low-mass binaries, third-generation observatories can enhance both detection capability and parameter-estimation precision. Their improved strain sensitivity and extended low-frequency coverage allow these observatories to track the inspiral phase over a substantially larger number of gravitational-wave cycles. As a result, they achieve considerably higher signal-to-noise ratios and provide dramatically improved constraints on binary parameters. In particular, it is possible to measure the primary spin parameter with precision $Δχ_{1z}~\sim~10^{-4}-10^{-3}$, potentially allowing clear observational discrimination between near-extremal black holes and superspinars in the mass range $0.1~M_\odot-2~M_\odot$ and with signal-to-noise ratio of $\sim 100-350$.

### [82] [Scalar$-$Tensor Gravity as a Probe of Generalized Black Hole Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18551)
*Hussain Gohar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper constructs a geometric framework linking generalized black hole entropy functionals (e.g., Barrow, Tsallis–Cirto, quantum/entanglement corrections) to scalar–tensor gravity via the Misner–Sharp mass and Wald entropy, yielding scale-dependent gravitational couplings and specific Einstein-frame scalar potentials that produce testable cosmological scenarios.
\n\n
本文构建了一个几何框架，通过Misner–Sharp质量与Wald熵将广义黑洞熵泛函（如Barrow熵、Tsallis–Cirto熵、量子/纠缠修正）与标量–张量引力理论联系起来，导出了依赖于尺度的有效引力耦合以及特定的Einstein-frame标量势，从而产生可观测的宇宙学情景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a geometric and field-theoretic foundation for various information-theoretic proposals of generalized black hole entropy by embedding them into consistent scalar–tensor theories of gravity, thereby connecting quantum/statistical entropy corrections to observable gravitational and cosmological phenomena.
\n\n
动机是为各种信息论导向的广义黑洞熵提案（如Barrow熵、Tsallis熵等）提供一个几何与场论基础，将其嵌入自洽的标量–张量引力理论中，从而将量子/统计熵修正与可观测的引力及宇宙学现象联系起来。

Method: The authors identify a correspondence between generalized entropy functionals $S_{\text{gen}}$ and the Misner–Sharp quasilocal mass $M_{\text{MS}}$, then use the Wald Noether-charge formalism in scalar–tensor theories to derive an effective gravitational coupling $G_{\text{eff}}(r)$ that depends on entropy parameters. They perform a conformal transformation to the Einstein frame and compute the resulting scalar potential $V(\phi)$ for specific entropy models.
\n\n
作者建立了广义熵泛函 $S_{\text{gen}}$ 与Misner–Sharp准局域质量 $M_{\text{MS}}$ 的对应关系，然后在标量–张量理论中利用Wald Noether-荷形式导出依赖于熵参数的有效引力耦合 $G_{\text{eff}}(r)$。通过共形变换到Einstein frame，计算了特定熵模型对应的标量势 $V(\phi)$。

Result: For Barrow entropy, they obtain a steep exponential potential; for Tsallis–Cirto entropy, an exponential potential controlled by the nonextensivity parameter $\\delta$; and for quantum-gravity or entanglement-induced corrections, an approximately linear potential. These lead to distinct cosmological behaviors—such as inflation, dark energy, or non-singular bounces—and satisfy solar-system, BBN, and pulsar-timing constraints.
\n\n
对于Barrow熵，得到一个陡峭的指数势；对于Tsallis–Cirto熵，得到由非广延参数 $\\delta$ 控制的指数势；对于量子引力或纠缠诱导的修正，则得到近似线性的势。这些势导致不同的宇宙学行为——如暴胀、暗能量或无奇点反弹——并满足太阳系、大爆炸核合成（BBN）和脉冲星计时观测的限制。

Conclusion: The work establishes a unified, geometrically rigorous link between information-theoretic black hole entropy corrections and modified gravity, demonstrating that such entropy proposals naturally induce scalar potentials with rich and testable cosmological implications within viable scalar–tensor frameworks.
\n\n
该工作建立了信息论黑洞熵修正与修改引力之间统一且几何严谨的联系，表明这类熵提案在可行的标量–张量框架内自然诱导出具有丰富且可检验宇宙学含义的标量势。

Abstract: We develop a geometric realization of a broad class of generalized black hole entropy functionals by establishing their direct correspondence with the Misner$-$Sharp quasilocal mass and the Wald Noether$-$charge entropy in scalar$-$tensor theories of gravity. The resulting models feature a scale-dependent effective gravitational coupling, whose functional dependence is determined by the underlying entropy parameters. Within this framework, we derive explicit Einstein-frame scalar potentials: for Barrow entropy, a steep exponential potential; for Tsallis$-$Cirto entropy, an exponential potential governed by the nonextensivity parameter; and for quantum-gravity and entanglement$-$induced corrections, an approximately linear potential. These distinct potentials generate characteristic cosmological phenomenology, with implications for inflationary dynamics, late-time dark-energy behavior, and non-singular bouncing cosmologies. The framework is compatible with current constraints from solar-system tests, big-bang nucleosynthesis, and pulsar-timing observations, and it yields predictions that can be probed by forthcoming observational surveys. In this way, the analysis establishes a unified and geometrically grounded connection between information$-$theoretic entropy proposals and gravitational field theory.

</details>


### [83] [Particle Dynamics, Shadow and Hawking Sparsity of a Kalb-Ramond Black Hole Coupled to Nonlinear Electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16461)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Ahmad Al-Badawi,İzzet Sakallı*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates the geodesic structure and observational signatures of a static, spherically symmetric black hole sourced by a Kalb–Ramond (KR) field coupled to nonlinear electrodynamics (NED), characterized by mass $M$, magnetic monopole charge $q$, and Lorentz-violating parameters $(γ,λ)$. It derives analytic expressions for particle orbits, photon sphere, black hole shadow, and quasinormal modes via the Lyapunov exponent. EHT constraints on M87$^\ast$ and Sgr~A$^\ast$ are used to bound $(q,γ)$, and thermodynamic quantities including Hawking temperature, horizon area, and the Gray–Visser sparsity parameter are computed—showing a significant increase in sparsity relative to Schwarzschild.
\n\n
本文研究了一种由Kalb–Ramond（KR）场与非线性电动力学（NED）耦合所支撑的静态球对称黑洞的测地线结构和观测特征，该时空由质量 $M$、磁单极荷 $q$ 和洛伦兹破缺参数 $(γ,λ)$ 表征。文中推导了粒子轨道、光子球、黑洞阴影及通过Lyapunov指数得到的准正规模的解析表达式。利用事件视界望远镜（EHT）对M87$^\ast$和Sgr~A$^\ast$的观测约束了 $(q,γ)$ 参数空间，并计算了霍金温度、视界面积和Gray–Visser稀疏性参数——结果表明其稀疏性显著高于Schwarzschild情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore how exotic matter sources—specifically a Kalb–Ramond (KR) antisymmetric tensor field coupled to nonlinear electrodynamics (NED)—modify black hole geometry, geodesic dynamics, and observable signatures such as the shadow and quasinormal modes. Additionally, the authors aim to confront theoretical predictions with Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) data and examine implications for Hawking radiation through the sparsity parameter.
\n\n
动机在于探索奇异物质源——特别是与非线性电动力学（NED）耦合的Kalb–Ramond（KR）反对称张量场——如何改变黑洞几何、测地线动力学以及阴影和准正规模等可观测量。此外，作者旨在将理论预言与事件视界望远镜（EHT）数据进行对照，并通过稀疏性参数考察其对霍金辐射的影响。

Method: The authors solve for timelike and null geodesics in a static, spherically symmetric metric sourced by KR + NED fields. They derive closed-form expressions for the effective potential $V_{\rm eff}(r)$, specific energy $E$, and angular momentum $L$ for circular massive particle orbits. The photon sphere is obtained from unstable null circular geodesics, and the Lyapunov exponent $λ_L$ is computed to determine eikonal quasinormal-mode frequencies via $ω_{\rm eik}=(\ell+1/2)\,Ω_c-i(n+1/2)\,|λ_L|$. The shadow radius is compared with EHT observations of M87$^\ast$ and Sgr~A$^\ast$ to constrain $(q,γ)$. Thermodynamic quantities—Hawking temperature $T_H$, horizon area $A_H$, and Gray–Visser sparsity parameter $η = A_H / (4π T_H^2)$—are analytically evaluated.
\n\n
作者在由KR+NED场支撑的静态球对称度规中求解类时和类光测地线，推导出有效势 $V_{\rm eff}(r)$、圆轨道上大质量粒子的比能量 $E$ 和角动量 $L$ 的解析表达式。通过不稳定类光圆轨道确定光子球，并计算Lyapunov指数 $λ_L$ 以通过公式 $ω_{\rm eik}=(\ell+1/2)\,Ω_c-i(n+1/2)\,|λ_L|$ 确定几何光学极限下的准正规模频率。将阴影半径与EHT对M87$^\ast$和Sgr~A$^\ast$的观测结果对比，以约束参数 $(q,γ)$。同时解析计算了热力学量——霍金温度 $T_H$、视界面积 $A_H$ 和Gray–Visser稀疏性参数 $η = A_H / (4π T_H^2)$。

Result: Key results include: (i) analytic expressions for $E$, $L$, and $V_{\rm eff}$ for circular orbits; (ii) identification of the photon sphere and associated Lyapunov exponent yielding eikonal QNM frequencies; (iii) EHT-compatible shadow radii across most of the allowed $(q,γ)$ parameter space; (iv) viable region in $(q,γ)$ consistent with $1σ$ EHT bounds; and (v) a dramatic increase in the Gray–Visser sparsity parameter from the Schwarzschild value $16π^3 \simeq 496$ to $\sim 1.7\times10^3$, indicating a much sparser Hawking cascade.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(i) 圆轨道的比能量 $E$、角动量 $L$ 和有效势 $V_{\rm eff}$ 的解析表达式；(ii) 光子球的确定及其对应的Lyapunov指数，用于给出几何光学极限下的准正规模频率；(iii) 在大部分物理允许的 $(q,γ)$ 参数范围内，黑洞阴影半径与EHT观测一致；(iv) 符合EHT $1σ$ 置信区间的 $(q,γ)$ 可行区域；(v) Gray–Visser稀疏性参数从Schwarzschild值 $16π^3 \simeq 496$ 显著增至约 $1.7\times10^3$，表明霍金辐射级联更加稀疏。

Conclusion: The combined influence of the Kalb–Ramond field and magnetic monopole charge in nonlinear electrodynamics leads to black hole solutions that remain observationally viable per EHT constraints while exhibiting markedly enhanced Hawking radiation sparsity. This suggests that exotic matter sectors can significantly alter quantum emission properties without violating current astrophysical bounds on shadow size.
\n\n
Kalb–Ramond场与非线性电动力学中磁单极荷的共同作用导致的黑洞解在满足EHT观测约束的同时，展现出显著增强的霍金辐射稀疏性。这表明奇异物质成分可在不违反当前黑洞阴影观测限制的前提下，显著改变量子辐射特性。

Abstract: We study the timelike and null geodesic structure of a static, spherically symmetric black hole sourced by a Kalb--Ramond (KR) field coupled to nonlinear electrodynamics (NED). The geometry is characterized by the mass $M$, the magnetic monopole charge $q$, and the Lorentz-violating parameters $(γ,λ)$. Closed-form expressions are derived for the effective potential, as well as the specific energy and angular momentum of massive particles on circular orbits. We further analyze the photon sphere, black hole shadow, and the Lyapunov exponent associated with unstable null circular geodesics. The latter determines the eikonal quasinormal-mode frequencies through $ω_{\rm eik}=(\ell+1/2)\,Ω_c-i(n+1/2)\,|λ_L|$. The shadow radius is compared with the Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) observations of M87$^\ast$ and Sgr~A$^\ast$, allowing us to identify the viable region in the $(q,γ)$ parameter space. Finally, we compute the Hawking temperature, horizon area, and the Gray--Visser sparsity parameter. We demonstrate that the combined effects of the KR field and magnetic monopole charge increase the sparsity parameter from the Schwarzschild value $16π^3 \simeq 496$ to nearly $1.7\times10^3$. This indicates a significantly sparser Hawking cascade compared to the Schwarzschild case, while the photon ring remains consistent with the EHT $1σ$ observational bounds across most of the physically allowed parameter range.

</details>


### [84] [Impact of sky localization uncertainty on ringdown inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18595)
*Kallol Dey,Enrico Barausse,Marco Crisostomi,Roberto Trotta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: As gravitational-wave ringdown signals become stronger, accurate inference of quasinormal modes requires proper handling of extrinsic parameters like sky location, inclination, and polarization. Fixing these to point estimates from earlier analyses artificially reduces uncertainties and may bias amplitude measurements. The paper proposes two improved approaches: (1) using uninformative priors on extrinsics sampled jointly with intrinsic parameters, and (2) using informed sky priors from the full inspiral-merger-ringdown posterior. Both yield unbiased amplitude posteriors with larger uncertainties than standard methods, while amplitude ratios—key for Kerr spectroscopy—remain stable. A fast, publicly available pipeline enables full parameter sampling in tens of minutes on a laptop. Applied to GW250114 and GW190521, it robustly confirms the $(2,2,1)$ overtone in the former and finds only mild evidence for the $(3,3,0)$ mode in the latter.
\n\n
随着引力波铃宕（ringdown）信号越来越强，准正规模（quasinormal-mode）的推断越来越依赖于对外在参数（如天空定位、倾角和偏振）的恰当处理。标准分析将这些外在参数固定为来自先前完整波形（inspiral-merger-ringdown）分析的点估计值，人为破坏了参数简并性，并低估了模式振幅的真实不确定性。本文测试了两种替代方案：(1) 对外在参数使用无信息先验，并与残余质量、自旋、模式振幅和相位联合采样；(2) 使用来自完整信号后验的天空位置信息先验。前者导致振幅后验边缘分布更宽，而两种方法均避免了因固定天空定位而引入的潜在偏差。相比之下，模式振幅比在不同方法下保持一致，使其成为Kerr谱学（Kerr spectroscopy）的稳健观测量。作者公开了一个快速铃宕分析流程，可在笔记本电脑上于数十分钟内完成全参数采样。将其应用于GW250114和GW190521事件，该方法稳健地确认了GW250114中$(2,2,1)$泛音的存在，而对于GW190521仅发现$(3,3,0)$模式的微弱证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard ringdown analyses often fix extrinsic parameters (sky position, inclination, polarization) to point estimates derived from the full inspiral-merger-ringdown signal, which artificially breaks degeneracies between these parameters and the quasinormal-mode amplitudes. This leads to underestimated uncertainties in amplitude posteriors and potential biases in tests of general relativity via Kerr spectroscopy. The motivation is to develop more statistically consistent inference frameworks that properly account for extrinsic-parameter uncertainty without sacrificing computational feasibility.
\n\n
标准铃宕分析通常将外在参数（天空位置、倾角、偏振）固定为从完整inspiral-merger-ringdown信号中导出的点估计值，这人为破坏了这些参数与准正规模振幅之间的简并性，导致振幅后验的不确定性被低估，并可能在通过Kerr谱学检验广义相对论时引入偏差。本文的动机是开发一种在统计上更自洽的推断框架，在不牺牲计算可行性的前提下，恰当地考虑外在参数的不确定性。

Method: The authors implement two Bayesian inference strategies for ringdown analysis: (i) joint sampling of all parameters—including remnant mass $M_f$, spin $\chi_f$, mode amplitudes $A_{\\ell m n}$, phases $\phi_{\\ell m n}$, and extrinsic parameters (sky location, inclination $\iota$, polarization $\psi$)—using uninformative (flat) priors on the extrinsics; and (ii) using an informed prior on sky position derived from the full IMR posterior, while still sampling other extrinsic and intrinsic parameters. They employ a fast time-domain ringdown likelihood and efficient MCMC or nested sampling to achieve full inference in $\\mathcal{O}(10)$ minutes on a laptop. The pipeline is made publicly available.
\n\n
作者实现了两种用于铃宕分析的贝叶斯推断策略：(i) 联合采样所有参数——包括残余质量$M_f$、自旋$\chi_f$、模式振幅$A_{\\ell m n}$、相位$\phi_{\\ell m n}$以及外在参数（天空位置、倾角$\iota$、偏振$\psi$）——对外在参数采用无信息（均匀）先验；(ii) 使用从完整IMR后验导出的天空位置信息先验，同时仍对其他外在和内禀参数进行采样。他们采用快速的时域铃宕似然函数和高效的MCMC或嵌套采样算法，在笔记本电脑上实现约数十分钟量级的全参数推断。该流程已公开发布。

Result: Using uninformative extrinsic priors yields significantly broader marginal posteriors for individual mode amplitudes compared to standard fixed-extrinsic analyses, reflecting more realistic uncertainties. However, ratios of mode amplitudes (e.g., $A_{221}/A_{220}$) remain consistent across all methods, demonstrating their robustness as observables for Kerr spectroscopy. Applied to real events: GW250114 shows strong evidence for the $(2,2,1)$ overtone under all tested approaches; GW190521 shows only mild (non-significant) evidence for the $(3,3,0)$ mode, suggesting previous claims may be sensitive to prior choices or over-constrained modeling.
\n\n
使用无信息外在先验得到的单个模式振幅边缘后验显著宽于标准固定外在参数的分析结果，反映了更真实的不确定性。然而，模式振幅比（例如$A_{221}/A_{220}$）在所有方法中保持一致，证明其作为Kerr谱学观测量的稳健性。应用于真实事件：GW250114在所有测试方法下均显示出对$(2,2,1)$泛音的强证据；而GW190521仅显示出对$(3,3,0)$模式的微弱（不显著）证据，表明此前的相关声称可能对先验选择或过度约束的建模敏感。

Conclusion: Proper treatment of extrinsic-parameter uncertainty is essential for unbiased and reliable ringdown inference. Fixing these parameters to point estimates should be avoided in favor of joint sampling with either uninformative or informed priors. While absolute mode amplitudes are highly prior- and degeneracy-sensitive, amplitude ratios provide a robust basis for testing the Kerr nature of black hole remnants. The developed fast pipeline enables routine full-parameter ringdown analyses, enhancing the rigor of future gravitational-wave spectroscopy.
\n\n
恰当地处理外在参数的不确定性对于无偏且可靠的铃宕推断至关重要。应避免将这些参数固定为点估计值，而应采用联合采样策略，配合无信息或信息先验。尽管绝对模式振幅对先验和参数简并高度敏感，但振幅比为检验黑洞残余是否符合Kerr解提供了稳健基础。所开发的快速分析流程使得全参数铃宕分析可常规化，提升了未来引力波谱学研究的严谨性。

Abstract: As gravitational-wave ringdown signals grow louder, quasinormal-mode inference depends increasingly on the treatment of extrinsic parameters. Standard analyses fix sky localization - and sometimes also polarization and inclination - to point estimates from a prior inspiral-merger-ringdown analysis, artificially breaking degeneracies and underestimating the true uncertainty of mode-amplitude values. We test two alternatives: uninformative priors on the extrinsic parameters, sampled jointly with the remnant mass, spin, mode amplitudes, and phases; and informed priors on sky position from the full signal posterior. The former yields wider marginal constraints on amplitude posteriors, and both avoid potential bias introduced by fixing the sky localization. In contrast, mode amplitude ratios remain consistent across approaches, making them a robust observable for Kerr spectroscopy. Our publicly available pipeline enables fast ringdown analyses capable of sampling all parameters, requiring tens of minutes on a laptop for a full inference. Applied to GW250114 and GW190521, our methods confirm the robust detection of the $(2,2,1)$ overtone in GW250114, and, for GW190521, find only mild evidence for the $(3,3,0)$ mode.

</details>


### [85] [Bouncing singularities in Schwarzschild: a geometric origin of the QNM convergence region](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16489)
*Paolo Arnaudo,Benjamin Withers*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates that the convergence of the quasinormal mode (QNM) expansion of the retarded Green's function in Schwarzschild spacetime is governed by a complex-time singularity with a geometric origin: a 'bouncing singularity' arising from a null geodesic reflecting off the black hole singularity. This explains the observed boundary of QNM convergence at real times and also accounts for the annular convergence region of the Matsubara mode sum near the horizon.
\n\n
本文证明了Schwarzschild时空推迟Green函数的quasinormal mode（QNM）展开的收敛性由复时间平面上的一个奇点决定，该奇点具有几何起源：在AdS/CFT文献中称为“bouncing singularity”，由从黑洞奇点反弹的null geodesic引起。这解释了实时间下QNM收敛区域为何被一个看似平凡点（$r_* = 0$）处散射的null ray所限制，并且同一组奇点也导致了靠近视界处Matsubara模求和的环形收敛区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the long-standing puzzle regarding the limited domain of convergence of the quasinormal mode (QNM) expansion for the retarded Green's function in Schwarzschild spacetime. Previous numerical and semi-analytical studies observed that the QNM series converges only within a finite time interval bounded by a specific null geodesic, but lacked a clear analytical explanation rooted in complex analysis or spacetime geometry. The authors aim to uncover the precise analytic structure—specifically, the nature and origin of singularities in the complex time plane—that governs this convergence behavior.
\n\n
动机源于Schwarzschild时空中推迟Green函数的quasinormal mode（QNM）展开收敛域有限这一长期未解之谜。先前的数值和半解析研究表明，QNM级数仅在由特定null geodesic界定的有限时间区间内收敛，但缺乏基于复分析或时空几何的清晰解析解释。作者旨在揭示控制该收敛行为的精确解析结构——特别是复时间平面上奇点的本质与起源。

Method: The authors employ complex analysis of the retarded Green's function in Schwarzschild spacetime, focusing on its analytic continuation into the complex time plane. They identify singularities by examining the behavior of null geodesics in the extended spacetime geometry, particularly those that interact with the black hole curvature singularity. Using techniques inspired by AdS/CFT—specifically the concept of 'bouncing singularities' arising from geodesics that reflect off singular boundaries—they analytically locate the dominant singularity responsible for limiting the QNM expansion's radius of convergence. They further connect this singularity to the convergence properties of the Matsubara mode sum via contour deformation arguments in the complex frequency/time plane.
\n\n
作者采用对Schwarzschild时空推迟Green函数的复分析方法，重点研究其在复时间平面上的解析延拓。他们通过考察延拓时空几何中null geodesic的行为（尤其是与黑洞曲率奇点相互作用的测地线）来识别奇点。借助AdS/CFT中的技术——特别是由从奇点边界反射的测地线引起的“bouncing singularities”概念——他们解析地定位了主导QNM展开收敛半径的奇点。此外，他们通过复频率/时间平面上的围道形变论证，将该奇点与Matsubara模求和的收敛性质联系起来。

Result: The key result is the identification of a specific complex-time singularity—the 'bouncing singularity'—as the analytic origin of the finite convergence radius of the QNM expansion. This singularity arises from a null geodesic that originates near the horizon, travels inward, reflects off the $r=0$ curvature singularity, and returns outward. Its location in the complex time plane ($t = \pm i\pi/2\kappa + \dots$, with $\kappa$ the surface gravity) determines the boundary of convergence at real times, which coincides with the arrival time of the null ray scattered at $r_* = 0$. The same singularity structure explains the annular region of convergence for the Matsubara mode sum describing early-time near-horizon dynamics.
\n\n
核心结果是识别出一个特定的复时间奇点——“bouncing singularity”——作为QNM展开有限收敛半径的解析起源。该奇点源于一条null geodesic：它从视界附近出发，向内传播，在$r=0$曲率奇点处反射后向外返回。其在复时间平面中的位置（$t = \\pm i\\pi/2\\kappa + \\dots$，其中$\\kappa$为表面引力）决定了实时间下收敛区域的边界，该边界恰好对应于在$r_* = 0$处散射的null ray的到达时间。相同的奇点结构也解释了描述视界附近早期动力学的Matsubara模求和的环形收敛区域。

Conclusion: The convergence properties of both the quasinormal mode expansion and the Matsubara mode sum in Schwarzschild spacetime are universally governed by geometric singularities in the complex time plane associated with null geodesics interacting with the black hole singularity. This provides a unified geometric and analytic explanation for previously observed convergence limits and establishes a direct link between classical spacetime structure (geodesic incompleteness at $r=0$) and the analytic structure of quantum or linear perturbative correlators.
\n\n
Schwarzschild时空中quasinormal mode展开和Matsubara模求和的收敛性质均由复时间平面上与null geodesic和黑洞奇点相互作用相关的几何奇点统一支配。这为先前观测到的收敛极限提供了统一的几何与解析解释，并建立了经典时空结构（$r=0$处的测地不完备性）与量子或线性微扰关联函数解析结构之间的直接联系。

Abstract: We show analytically that the convergence of the QNM expansion of the retarded Green's function of the Schwarzschild spacetime is set by a singularity in the complex time plane. The singularity has a simple geometric origin: it is an example of a `bouncing singularity' in the language of AdS/CFT literature, caused by a null geodesic which bounces from the black hole singularity. Our work explains why the QNM convergence region at real times is bounded by null ray which scatters from the gravitational potential at a seemingly unremarkable point ($r_* = 0$ in the conventions of previous work) -- this ray is the same distance from the origin as the bouncing singularity in the relevant complex plane. The same set of singularities are responsible for an annular region of convergence for the Matsubara mode sum which describes the early time behaviour of the Schwarzschild Green's function for perturbations close to the horizon.

</details>


### [86] [Emergent Thiemann coherent states in the near-kernel sector of quantum reduced loop gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18625)
*Ilkka Mäkinen,Hanno Sahlmann,Waleed Sherif*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates near-kernel states of the Hamiltonian constraint in quantum reduced loop gravity using neural quantum states and variational Monte Carlo. Three classes of solutions emerge: non-factorized at low spin cutoffs, and two distinct factorized branches at high cutoffs—one matching reduced Thiemann coherent states with near-unit fidelity, suggesting semiclassical emergence, and another strongly factorized but not describable by those coherent states.
\n\n
本文利用神经量子态和变分蒙特卡洛方法研究了量子约化圈引力中哈密顿约束算符的近核（near-kernel）区域。研究发现三类解：在低自旋截断下为非因子化解；在高截断下出现两个不同的因子化分支——其中一个与约化Thiemann相干态以接近单位保真度匹配，暗示半经典结构的涌现，另一个虽强因子化但无法用该相干态族描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the physical content of the Hamiltonian constraint in loop quantum gravity (LQG) is essential for identifying semiclassical states and recovering general relativity in the low-energy limit. The one-vertex model of quantum reduced loop gravity provides a simplified yet nontrivial setting to explore the kernel (or near-kernel) of the constraint operator. Traditional analytical methods struggle with the complexity of the full constraint; thus, numerical approaches like variational Monte Carlo with neural quantum states offer a promising route to characterize its low-energy spectrum and structure.
\n\n
理解圈量子引力（LQG）中哈密顿约束的物理内涵对于识别半经典态并在低能极限下恢复广义相对论至关重要。量子约化圈引力的单顶点模型为探索约束算符的核（或近核）提供了一个简化但非平凡的框架。传统解析方法难以处理完整约束的复杂性，因此采用神经量子态的变分蒙特卡洛等数值方法为刻画其低能谱和结构提供了有效途径。

Method: The authors employ variational Monte Carlo (VMC) with neural quantum states to minimize the positive semi-definite operator $\\hat{\\mathcal Q} = \\hat C \\hat C^\\dagger$, where $\\hat C$ is the symmetric Hamiltonian constraint containing both Euclidean and Lorentzian terms. The Hilbert space is truncated by imposing a maximum spin cutoff $j_{\\mathrm{max}}$ up to 1001 on the three edges incident to the single vertex. Neural networks parametrize trial wavefunctions, and stochastic optimization is used to find states that minimize $\\langle \\hat{\\mathcal Q} \\rangle$, thereby approximating near-kernel states of $\\hat C$. Factorization properties and overlaps with reduced Thiemann coherent states are then analyzed.
\n\n
作者采用神经量子态的变分蒙特卡洛（VMC）方法，对正半定算符 $\\hat{\\mathcal Q} = \\hat C \\hat C^\\dagger$ 进行极小化，其中 $\\hat C$ 是包含欧几里得项和洛伦兹项的对称哈密顿约束。希尔伯特空间通过对单顶点所连三条边施加最大自旋截断 $j_{\\mathrm{max}} \\leq 1001$ 而被截断。神经网络参数化试探波函数，并通过随机优化寻找使 $\\langle \\hat{\\mathcal Q} \\rangle$ 最小的状态，从而逼近 $\\hat C$ 的近核态。随后分析这些态的因子化性质及其与约化Thiemann相干态的重叠。

Result: Three qualitatively distinct classes of near-kernel states are identified. For low $j_{\\mathrm{max}}$, states are non-factorized across the three edge degrees of freedom. For large $j_{\\mathrm{max}}$, two factorized branches emerge: (i) one branch is accurately described as a product of one-edge wavefunctions and matches reduced Thiemann coherent states with near-unit fidelity, indicating emergent semiclassical behavior; (ii) the other branch is also strongly factorized but its one-edge components deviate significantly from the Thiemann coherent-state ansatz.
\n\n
研究识别出三类定性不同的近核态。在低 $j_{\\mathrm{max}}$ 时，态在三条边自由度上是非因子化的；在高 $j_{\\mathrm{max}}$ 时，出现两个因子化分支：(i) 一个分支可高精度地表示为单边波函数的乘积，并与约化Thiemann相干态以接近单位保真度匹配，表明半经典行为的涌现；(ii) 另一分支同样强因子化，但其单边分量显著偏离Thiemann相干态形式。

Conclusion: The near-kernel sector of the Hamiltonian constraint in quantum reduced loop gravity exhibits rich structure, including both non-factorized and factorized solutions. The emergence of a branch closely aligned with reduced Thiemann coherent states supports the idea that semiclassical geometries can arise from the quantum dynamics encoded in the constraint. However, the existence of another robust factorized branch not captured by standard coherent states suggests additional physical sectors or limitations of current semiclassical tools, warranting further investigation.
\n\n
量子约化圈引力中哈密顿约束的近核区域展现出丰富结构，包括非因子化与因子化解。其中一个分支与约化Thiemann相干态高度一致，支持“半经典几何可从约束所编码的量子动力学中涌现”这一观点。然而，另一未被标准相干态捕捉到的稳健因子化分支的存在，暗示可能存在额外的物理扇区或当前半经典工具的局限性，值得进一步研究。

Abstract: We study the near-kernel sector of the Hamiltonian constraint operator in the one-vertex model of quantum reduced loop gravity using variational Monte Carlo methods with neural quantum states. The analysis is based on the symmetric Hamiltonian containing both Euclidean and Lorentzian contributions, and on the variational minimization of the positive quadratic operator $\hat{\mathcal Q}=\hat C \hat C^\dagger$ in truncated Hilbert spaces with spin cutoff up to $j_{\mathrm{max}}=1001$. The resulting near-kernel states are found to organize into three qualitatively distinct classes. At low cutoffs, we find solutions that do not factorize across the three edge degrees of freedom. At larger cutoffs, we find two different factorized branches, both described to very high accuracy by products of one-edge wavefunctions but localized in different spin regimes. One of these branches is matched with near-unit fidelity by reduced Thiemann coherent states, providing evidence for an emergent semiclassical organization of the near-kernel sector. The other is likewise strongly factorized, but its one-edge factors are not well described by the same coherent-state family.

### [87] [Dynamical quasinormal mode excitation II: propagation and convergence in Schwarzschild](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16492)
*Marina De Amicis,Enrico Cannizzaro,Gregorio Carullo,Adrien Kuntz,Laura Sberna*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We refine the description of quasinormal mode (QNM) excitation during black hole plunge by identifying the bounce radius $r_*=0$ as a key feature governing QNM propagation. Using an improved high-frequency analysis of Leaver's solutions and the formalism from Paper I, we derive a first-principles QNM signal that accurately captures post-peak waveform oscillations. The signal transitions from destructive interference of overtones (quasi-resonant regime) to coherent summation (free-oscillator regime) as the particle crosses $r_*=0$, offering a physical picture of ringdown dynamics.
\n\n
我们通过识别反弹半径 $r_*=0$ 作为控制准正规模（QNM）传播的关键特征，改进了黑洞并合阶段 QNM 激发的描述。利用对 Leaver 解的高频行为的改进分析以及 Paper I 中的形式体系，我们推导出一个基于第一性原理的 QNM 信号，能精确捕捉波形峰值之后的振荡成分。当粒子穿越 $r_*=0$ 时，信号从高次泛音相消干涉的准共振态过渡到相干叠加的自由振子态，为铃宕（ringdown）动力学提供了清晰的物理解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to resolve ambiguities in how quasinormal modes are dynamically excited during the late plunge phase of a particle into a Schwarzschild black hole. Prior models lacked a precise prescription for QNM propagation in the time domain, especially near the transition from inspiral to ringdown. Recent suggestions of a "bounce radius" at $r_*=0$ motivate a deeper investigation into its role in shaping the observed gravitational waveform.
\n\n
本文旨在解决粒子落入 Schwarzschild 黑洞晚期并合阶段中准正规模（QNM）如何被动态激发的问题。以往模型缺乏对时域中 QNM 传播的精确描述，特别是在旋近到铃宕的过渡区域。近期文献提出在 $r_*=0$ 处存在一个“反弹半径”，这促使作者深入研究其在引力波形形成中的作用。

Method: The authors extend the framework of Paper I by analyzing the high-frequency asymptotics of Leaver’s exact QNM solutions in the Regge–Wheeler tortoise coordinate $r_*$. They identify $r_*=0$ as a scattering point that separates two propagation regimes: left-moving (direct light-cone propagation) and right-moving (scattering before reaching the observer). They apply this refined propagation rule to compute the dynamical QNM response to an inspiralling particle trajectory, tracking overtone contributions across the bounce radius crossing.
\n\n
作者通过分析 Regge–Wheeler 龟坐标 $r_*$ 下 Leaver 精确 QNM 解的高频渐近行为，扩展了 Paper I 的框架。他们将 $r_*=0$ 识别为一个散射点，分隔两种传播机制：左侧为直接沿光锥传播，右侧为在到达观测者前发生散射。他们将这一改进的传播规则应用于计算沿旋近轨道运动粒子所激发的动态 QNM 响应，并追踪粒子穿越反弹半径时各阶泛音的贡献。

Result: The refined model yields a QNM signal that matches the oscillatory part of the full numerical waveform immediately after the peak amplitude. Crucially, the authors observe a dynamical transition at $r_*=0$: for $r_*>0$, successive QNM overtones are driven out of phase, causing destructive interference; for $r_*<0$, they align in phase, leading to rapid convergence of the overtone sum. This explains the emergence of a clean ringdown signal post-plunge.
\n\n
改进后的模型所得到的 QNM 信号与全数值波形在峰值之后的振荡部分高度吻合。关键发现是：在 $r_*=0$ 处存在动力学转变——当 $r_*>0$ 时，连续的 QNM 泛音被反相驱动，导致相消干涉；当 $r_*<0$ 时，泛音同相叠加，使泛音级数快速收敛。这解释了并合后清晰铃宕信号的出现机制。

Conclusion: The identification of $r_*=0$ as the bounce radius provides a robust physical mechanism for QNM excitation during plunge. The transition from quasi-resonant to free-oscillator behavior clarifies the collective dynamics of overtones and validates a first-principles approach to ringdown modelling. This work establishes a theoretical foundation for accurate, physically motivated templates in gravitational-wave data analysis.
\n\n
将 $r_*=0$ 确定为反弹半径，为并合阶段 QNM 激发提供了坚实的物理机制。从准共振态到自由振子态的转变阐明了泛音的集体动力学行为，并验证了基于第一性原理的铃宕建模方法。本工作为引力波数据分析中构建精确且物理动机明确的模板奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: We study the dynamical excitation of quasinormal modes (QNMs) during the plunge of a particle into a Schwarzschild black hole, building on the framework of Phys. Rev. D 113 (2026) 2, 024048 (Paper I). Investigating the high-frequency behavior of Leaver's QNM solutions, we obtain a more accurate and general prescription for their propagation. We confirm the existence of a new "characteristic radius" for QNM excitation, the bounce radius $r_*=0$, in agreement with recent literature. To its right, the QNM signal scatters off this point before reaching the observer; to its left, it propagates directly on the light-cone. Applying the formalism of Paper I to inspiralling particles, and using this refined prescription, we obtain a QNM signal that accurately reproduces the oscillatory component of the waveform after the bounce crossing, yielding an essentially complete first-principles description of the waveform from shortly after the signal peak. The dynamical QNM signal undergoes a transition as the particle crosses the bounce radius: from a quasi-resonant regime, where successive overtones are driven in counter-phase and interfere destructively, to a free-oscillator one, where they are in phase and the QNM sum converges rapidly. These results provide a clear physical interpretation of the collective QNM behavior during the plunge, and a firm theoretical foundation for accurate ringdown modelling.
