### [88] [The spacetime Penrose inequality under a quasi final state hypothesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18730)
*Ahmed Ellithy*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper proves the spacetime Penrose inequality under a new, weaker late-time assumption called the quasi final state hypothesis, using a novel spacetime-based method involving tangentially maximal hypersurfaces that reduce the problem to the Riemannian Penrose inequality.
\n\n
本文在一种新的、更弱的晚期假设——“准终态假设”（quasi final state hypothesis）下证明了时空Penrose不等式，采用了一种基于时空的新方法，引入“切向极大超曲面”（tangentially maximal hypersurface），将问题约化为Riemann型Penrose不等式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Penrose’s original heuristic for the spacetime Penrose inequality relies on the black hole final state conjecture, which is strong and unproven. The authors aim to replace this with a precise, substantially weaker late-time condition that is physically plausible and mathematically tractable, thereby providing a rigorous proof of the inequality without assuming full black hole settling.
\n\n
Penrose最初对时空Penrose不等式的启发式论证依赖于黑洞终态猜想（black hole final state conjecture），该猜想较强且未经证明。作者旨在用一个精确且显著更弱的晚期条件来替代它，该条件在物理上合理且数学上可处理，从而在不假设黑洞完全弛豫的前提下严格证明该不等式。

Method: The authors introduce the quasi final state hypothesis—a late-time decay condition on the shift vector’s normal component and the ratio of timelike to spacelike mean curvature, plus convergence of horizon cross-sectional areas. They construct tangentially maximal hypersurfaces foliated by spacelike spheres with vanishing timelike mean curvature. These hypersurfaces satisfy a quasilinear inward-parabolic PDE; the authors develop its a priori estimates and prove global existence. On such hypersurfaces, the spacetime Hawking mass coincides with the Riemannian Hawking mass, and the dominant energy condition implies nonnegative scalar curvature, allowing application of the Riemannian Penrose inequality together with area laws for dynamical and isolated horizons.
\n\n
作者提出“准终态假设”——对移位矢量法向分量和类时与类空平均曲率之比的晚期衰减条件，以及视界横截面积收敛到有限极限。他们构造了由类空球面叶状结构组成的“切向极大超曲面”，其类时平均曲率为零。这些超曲面满足一个拟线性内向抛物型偏微分方程（quasilinear inward-parabolic PDE）；作者发展了其先验估计并证明了整体存在性。在此类超曲面上，时空Hawking质量退化为Riemann型Hawking质量，而主能量条件（dominant energy condition）给出非负数量曲率，从而可结合动力学与孤立视界的面积定律应用Riemann型Penrose不等式。

Result: Under the quasi final state hypothesis and the dominant energy condition, every asymptotically flat initial data set with boundary given by a marginally outer trapped surface (MOTS) cross-section of the apparent horizon tube $H_{app}$ satisfies the spacetime Penrose inequality: $M_{\text{ADM}} \geq \sqrt{\frac{A}{16\pi}}$, where $A$ is the area of the MOTS.
\n\n
在准终态假设和主能量条件下，任意渐近平直初值数据集，若其边界为表观视界管 $H_{app}$ 的边缘外陷获面（MOTS）横截面，则满足时空Penrose不等式：$M_{\text{ADM}} \geq \sqrt{\frac{A}{16\pi}}$，其中 $A$ 为MOTS的面积。

Conclusion: The spacetime Penrose inequality can be rigorously established without invoking the full black hole final state conjecture, using a physically motivated and mathematically precise late-time condition. The introduction of tangentially maximal hypersurfaces provides a new geometric framework that bridges spacetime geometry and Riemannian methods, opening avenues for further applications in general relativity.
\n\n
时空Penrose不等式可在不依赖完整的黑洞终态猜想的情况下被严格建立，仅需一个物理上有动机且数学上精确的晚期条件。“切向极大超曲面”的引入提供了一个连接时空几何与Riemann方法的新几何框架，为广义相对论中的进一步应用开辟了道路。

Abstract: Penrose's original heuristic for his eponymous spacetime inequality -- a conjectured lower bound on the ADM mass in terms of the area of a horizon cross-section -- relies on the black hole final state conjecture. In this paper we isolate a substantially weaker but precise late-time condition, which we call the quasi final state hypothesis and prove the spacetime Penrose inequality under this hypothesis. More precisely, for an asymptotically flat globally hyperbolic spacetime with a black-hole-type apparent horizon tube ${H}_{app}$ satisfying the dominant energy condition and the quasi final state hypothesis, we show that every asymptotically flat initial data set whose boundary is a MOTS cross-section of ${H}_{app}$ satisfies the spacetime Penrose inequality. The quasi final state hypothesis requires only a late-time decay condition on the normal component of the shift and the ratio of timelike to spacelike mean curvature, together with convergence of the cross-sectional areas of ${H}_{app}$ to a finite limit.
  Our approach is new and formulated directly in spacetime. The main geometric object is what we call a \emph{tangentially maximal} hypersurface, carrying a foliation by spacelike spheres whose timelike mean curvature vanishes. We show that these hypersurfaces are governed by a quasilinear inward-parabolic PDE, and we develop the corresponding a priori theory and prove global existence. On these hypersurfaces, the spacetime Hawking mass reduces to the Riemannian Hawking mass, and the dominant energy condition gives nonnegative scalar curvature. The Riemannian Penrose inequality, combined with the area laws for dynamical and isolated horizons, then yields the result.

</details>


### [89] [Quantum-statistical constraints on Kerr-anti-de Sitter thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16536)
*T. L. Campos,M. C. Baldiotti,C. Molina*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper constructs a unified framework to interpret the multiple thermodynamic descriptions of Kerr-anti de Sitter (KadS) black holes, showing that only a restricted subclass—selected by quantum statistical relations and geometric consistency—is physically meaningful, with unique descriptions emerging in specific limits or gauge choices.
\n\n
本文构建了一个统一框架，用于解释Kerr-anti de Sitter（KadS）黑洞的多种热力学描述，表明只有通过量子统计关系和几何一致性所选出的一个受限子类才具有物理意义，并在特定极限或规范选择下涌现出唯一描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The existence of an infinite family of thermodynamic formulations for KadS black holes—each satisfying the first law and homogeneity but differing in definitions of mass, volume, and pressure—poses a conceptual ambiguity. The authors aim to resolve this by identifying physical criteria (from semiclassical Euclidean methods and quantum statistical relations) that select physically admissible descriptions and clarify the role of observers.
\n\n
KadS黑洞存在无限多种热力学表述——每种都满足热力学第一定律和齐次性，但在质量、体积和压强的定义上有所不同——这带来了概念上的模糊性。作者旨在通过识别物理判据（来自半经典欧几里得方法和量子统计关系）来解决这一问题，从而筛选出物理上可接受的描述并澄清观测者的作用。

Method: The authors employ the Euclidean path integral formalism to identify temperature $T$ and angular velocity $\Omega$ as kinematic quantities fixed by the Killing vector generating the horizon. They treat the pressure-volume term $P\delta V$ as dynamical, requiring gauge fixing of the potential conjugate variables (mass and volume). They impose the quantum statistical relation $I = \beta (M - TS - \Omega J)$—where $I$ is the on-shell Euclidean action—to constrain the allowed thermodynamic descriptions, and analyze limits ($\Lambda \to 0$, $J \to 0$) and special conditions (e.g., co-rotation with infinity, equality of thermodynamic and geometric volumes).
\n\n
作者采用欧几里得路径积分形式，将温度$T$和角速度$\Omega$识别为由生成视界的Killing矢量所固定的运动学量。他们将压强-体积项$P\delta V$视为动力学项，需对共轭变量（质量和体积）进行规范固定。他们施加量子统计关系$I = \beta (M - TS - \Omega J)$（其中$I$为壳层上欧几里得作用量）以约束允许的热力学描述，并分析极限情形（$\Lambda \to 0$、$J \to 0$）及特殊条件（例如与无穷远共转、热力学体积与几何体积重合）。

Result: The quantum statistical relation restricts the infinite family of KadS thermodynamics to a physically admissible subclass that correctly reduces to Schwarzschild-AdS and standard Kerr thermodynamics in appropriate limits. Two unique descriptions are identified: (1) the one associated with an observer co-rotating with infinity, and (2) the one where thermodynamic volume equals geometric volume. The observer’s frame is encoded in the horizon-generating Killing vector.
\n\n
量子统计关系将KadS热力学的无限族限制为一个物理上可接受的子类，该子类在适当极限下正确还原为Schwarzschild-AdS和标准Kerr热力学。文中识别出两种唯一描述：(1) 与无穷远共转的观测者对应的描述；(2) 热力学体积等于几何体积的描述。观测者的参考系被编码在生成视界的Killing矢量中。

Conclusion: The paper resolves the ambiguity in KadS black hole thermodynamics by unifying geometric, semiclassical, and quantum-statistical perspectives. It establishes that physically meaningful thermodynamic descriptions are not arbitrary but are selected by consistency with the Euclidean path integral and boundary conditions, leading to uniqueness in key physical scenarios.
\n\n
本文通过统一几何、半经典和量子统计视角，解决了KadS黑洞热力学中的模糊性。研究表明，物理上有意义的热力学描述并非任意，而是由与欧几里得路径积分及边界条件的一致性所选定，从而在关键物理情形下导致唯一性。

Abstract: We develop a general framework for interpreting the thermodynamic descriptions of Kerr-anti de Sitter black holes (KadS). These descriptions satisfy a first law and respect the homogeneity required by scaling properties. Additionally, they are subject to restrictions from semiclassical arguments. We show that temperature and angular velocity are kinematic quantities tied to a reference frame, identified through the Euclidean formalism. However, the pressure-volume contribution is a dynamical term that requires a gauge fixing of the potential mass and volume. It is established that the observer associated with a given thermodynamic description is directly encoded in the Killing vector that generates the horizon. We demonstrate that the quantum statistical relation restricts the infinite family of KadS descriptions to a subclass that reduces to Schwarzschild-adS and Kerr thermodynamics in the limits of vanishing cosmological constant and angular momentum. Furthermore, we establish the uniqueness of both the description associated with a frame co-rotating with infinity, and the description whose thermodynamic and geometric volumes coincide. Thus, our framework provides a coherent interpretation of the variety of KadS thermodynamics, reconciling geometric and quantum-statistical considerations.

### [90] [Joule-Thomson effect and Efficiency of deformed AdS-Schwarzschild black hole in presence of quintessence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17476)
*Dhruba Jyoti Gogoi,Ronit Karmakar,Jyatsnasree Bora,Pohar Buragohain,Chandika Gogoi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates the Joule-Thomson expansion and extended thermodynamics of a modified black hole with parameters $α$, $β$, and $σ$. It finds that $α$ and $β$ strongly enhance cooling effects and thermal stability, while $σ$ has a milder impact; efficiency of a heat engine is increased by $α$ but decreased by $β$ and $σ$, indicating that geometric deformation and quintessence jointly shape the black hole’s thermodynamic behavior.
\n\n
本文研究了具有参数 $α$、$β$ 和 $σ$ 的修正黑洞的焦耳-汤姆逊膨胀与扩展热力学。结果表明，$α$ 和 $β$ 显著增强冷却效应和热稳定性，而 $σ$ 的影响较弱；热机效率因 $α$ 提高，但随 $β$ 和 $σ$ 增大而降低，表明几何形变与quintessence共同决定了黑洞的热力学结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how geometric deformation (encoded in $α$) and quintessence-like fields (controlled by $β$ and $σ$) alter the extended thermodynamic properties—particularly Joule-Thomson expansion and heat-engine performance—of black holes beyond standard general relativity solutions.
\n\n
动机在于理解几何形变（由 $α$ 编码）和类quintessence场（由 $β$ 和 $σ$ 控制）如何改变黑洞的扩展热力学性质——特别是焦耳-汤姆逊膨胀和热机性能——超越标准广义相对论解的情形。

Method: The authors compute the Hawking temperature, derive the Joule-Thomson coefficient $\\mu = \\left( \\frac{\\partial T}{\\partial P} \\right)_H$, determine inversion curves from $\\mu = 0$, and analyze isenthalpic trajectories in the $T$–$P$ plane. They also evaluate heat-engine efficiency using the Carnot-like cycle within extended black hole thermodynamics, where pressure $P$ is identified with the cosmological constant.
\n\n
作者计算了Hawking温度，推导出焦耳-汤姆逊系数 $\\mu = \\left( \\frac{\\partial T}{\\partial P} \\right)_H$，通过 $\\mu = 0$ 确定反转曲线，并在 $T$–$P$ 平面中分析等焓轨迹。他们还在扩展黑洞热力学框架下，将压强 $P$ 视为宇宙学常数，利用类Carnot循环评估热机效率。

Result: The deformation parameter $α$ and control parameter $β$ shift the minimum temperature upward, expand the cooling region in the inversion diagram, and increase the inversion temperature. Parameter $σ$ exerts a weaker but consistent influence. In heat-engine analysis, $α$ boosts efficiency, while larger $β$ and $σ$ suppress it. These results confirm that both spacetime geometry ($α$) and quintessence ($β$, $σ$) co-determine thermodynamic behavior.
\n\n
形变参数 $α$ 和控制参数 $β$ 使最低温度上移，扩大反转图中的冷却区域，并提高反转温度；参数 $σ$ 的影响较弱但一致。在热机分析中，$α$ 提升效率，而较大的 $β$ 和 $σ$ 则抑制效率。这些结果证实时空几何（$α$）与quintessence（$β$, $σ$）共同决定热力学行为。

Conclusion: The unified thermodynamic structure of the modified black hole is governed jointly by geometric deformation and quintessence background. This demonstrates that extended thermodynamics provides a robust framework to probe how exotic matter and spacetime modifications influence black hole thermal processes like Joule-Thomson expansion and energy extraction via heat engines.
\n\n
该修正黑洞的统一热力学结构由几何形变与quintessence背景共同支配。这表明扩展热力学为探究奇异物质和时空修正如何影响黑洞的热过程（如焦耳-汤姆逊膨胀及通过热机提取能量）提供了稳健框架。

Abstract: We study the Joule-Thomson expansion and extended thermodynamics of a modified black hole characterised by the parameters $α$, $β$, and $σ$. Analysis of the Hawking temperature, Joule-Thomson coefficient, inversion curves, and isenthalpic trajectories shows that these parameters significantly modify the heating-cooling behaviour and thermal stability of the system. The deformation parameter $α$ and control parameter $β$ shift the temperature minimum, enlarge the cooling region, and raise the inversion temperature, while $σ$ produces a weaker but consistent influence. The heat-engine analysis reveals that $α$ enhances efficiency, whereas higher $β$ and $σ$ reduce it. Overall, the results demonstrate that geometric deformation and quintessence jointly govern the unified thermodynamic structure of the black hole.

</details>
